   1 | # Changelog
   2 | 
   3 | All notable changes to this project will be documented in this file.
   4 | 
   5 | ## [0.2.0] - 2024-03-01
   6 | 
   7 | ### Added
   8 | - Structured logging with tracing and log file rotation
   9 | - CLI `--version` flag
  10 | - Proper error handling instead of panics on startup
  11 | - CI test and clippy checks before build
  12 | 
  13 | ### Fixed
  14 | - Replaced all `expect()`/`unwrap()` with proper error handling
  15 | - Standardized logging with tracing (replaced eprintln!/println!)
  16 | - Pinned litchi git dependency for reproducible builds
  17 | - NSIS uninstall hook now properly removes PATH entry
  18 | 
  19 | ### Changed
  20 | - Updated version from 0.1.0 to 0.2.0
  21 | - Added tracing-appender for log rotation
  22 | 
  23 | ## [0.1.0] - 2024-01-01
  24 | 
  25 | ### Added
  26 | - Initial release
  27 | - Full-text search with Tantivy
  28 | - File metadata database with redb
  29 | - Iced-based UI
  30 | - Multiple file format parsers (PDF, DOCX, EPUB, etc.)
  31 | - File system watcher for live indexing
```

### File: `CONTRIBUTING.md`

```markdown
   1 | # Contributing to Flash Search
   2 | 
   3 | Thank you for your interest in contributing to Flash Search!
   4 | 
   5 | ## Development Setup
   6 | 
   7 | ```bash
   8 | # Install Rust
   9 | curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh
  10 | 
  11 | # Clone and setup
  12 | git clone https://github.com/yourusername/flash-search.git
  13 | cd flash-search
  14 | 
  15 | # Run development server
  16 | cargo run
  17 | ```
  18 | 
  19 | ## Building
  20 | 
  21 | ```bash
  22 | # Debug build
  23 | cargo build
  24 | 
  25 | # Release build
  26 | cargo build --release
  27 | 
  28 | # Run tests
  29 | cargo test
  30 | ```
  31 | 
  32 | ## Code Style
  33 | 
  34 | - Use `cargo fmt` before committing
  35 | - Use `cargo clippy` to catch common mistakes
  36 | - Follow existing code conventions
  37 | 
  38 | ## Pull Request Process
  39 | 
  40 | 1. Fork the repository
  41 | 2. Create a feature branch
  42 | 3. Make your changes
  43 | 4. Run tests and formatting
  44 | 5. Submit a pull request
  45 | 
  46 | ## Reporting Issues
  47 | 
  48 | Please include:
  49 | - Steps to reproduce
  50 | - Expected vs actual behavior
  51 | - System information
  52 | 
  53 | ## License
  54 | 
  55 | By contributing, you agree that your contributions will be licensed under GPLv3.
```

```markdown
   1 | <h1 align="center">Flash Search</h1>
   2 | 
   3 | <p align="center">
   4 |   <img src="assets/logo.png" alt="Flash Search Logo" width="120">
   5 | </p>
   6 | 
   7 | <p align="center">
   8 |   <b>Ultrafast local full-text search with minimal resource footprint</b>
   9 | </p>
  10 | 
  11 | <p align="center">
  12 |   <a href="#features">Features</a> •
  13 |   <a href="#installation">Installation</a> •
  14 |   <a href="#usage">Usage</a> •
  15 |   <a href="#tech-stack">Tech Stack</a> •
  16 |   <a href="#performance">Performance</a> •
  17 |   <a href="#roadmap">Roadmap</a>
  18 | </p>
  19 | 
  20 | <p align="center">
  21 |   <img src="https://img.shields.io/badge/Rust-000000?style=flat&logo=rust&logoColor=white" alt="Rust">
  22 |   <img src="https://img.shields.io/badge/Iced-0.14-blue?style=flat&logo=rust&logoColor=white" alt="Iced">
  23 |   <img src="https://img.shields.io/badge/License-GPL--3.0-blue.svg" alt="License">
  24 | </p>
  25 | 
  26 | ---
  27 | 
  28 | <h2 align="center">🚀 Features</h2>
  29 | 
  30 | - **⚡ Blazing Fast**: Sub-50ms search results across millions of documents
  31 | - **📂 Filename Search**: Instant filename-only search mode for ultra-fast navigation
  32 | - **💾 Minimal Footprint**: <30MB RAM usage at idle (vs 200MB+ for Electron apps)
  33 | - **📄 Universal Format Support**: Native support for **75+ formats** (PDF, Office, Images, Archives, Ebooks, etc.)
  34 | - **🔍 Full-Text Search**: BM25 scoring, boolean queries, exact phrase matching
  35 | - **📸 Integrated OCR**: Search text within images and scanned PDFs via Kreuzberg
  36 | - **📊 Advanced Filters**: Filter by size (`size:>1MB`), extension (`ext:rs`), or path (`path:src`)
  37 | - **🔄 Live Indexing**: Automatic file watching and incremental updates
  38 | - **🎯 Smart Filtering**: .gitignore support, custom exclude patterns
  39 | - **🌙 Native UI**: Beautiful dark/light themes using Iced's high-performance renderer.
  40 | - **🔄 Auto-Update**: Seamlessly checks for and installs new updates in the background.
  41 | - **🚀 Auto-Launch**: Configurable to launch quietly on system startup so search is always ready.
  42 | 
  43 | 
  44 | <h2 align="center">📥 Installation</h2>
  45 | 
  46 | <h3 align="center">Prerequisites</h3>
  47 | 
  48 | - **Windows**: Windows 10/11
  49 | - **macOS**: macOS 10.15+
  50 | - **Linux**: Vulkan-compatible drivers & development tools (pkg-config, libfontconfig1-dev)
  51 | 
  52 | <h3 align="center">Install via Terminal</h3>
  53 | 
  54 | **Windows (PowerShell):**
  55 | ```powershell
  56 | irm https://github.com/SV-stark/FindAll/releases/latest/download/flash-search-installer.ps1 | iex
  57 | ```
  58 | 
  59 | **macOS & Linux:**
  60 | ```bash
  61 | curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -LsSf https://github.com/SV-stark/FindAll/releases/latest/download/flash-search-installer.sh | sh
  62 | ```
  63 | 
  64 | Or manually download the pre-built binaries for your platform from the [Releases](https://github.com/SV-stark/FindAll/releases) page.
  65 | 
  66 | *Note: The installed application binary is called `flash-search`.*
  67 | 
  68 | <h3 align="center">Build from Source</h3>
  69 | 
  70 | ```bash
  71 | # Clone the repository
  72 | git clone https://github.com/SV-stark/FindAll.git
  73 | cd FindAll
  74 | 
  75 | # Build the application
  76 | cargo build --release
  77 | 
  78 | # Run in development mode
  79 | cargo run
  80 | ```
  81 | 
  82 | <h2 align="center">🎮 Usage</h2>
  83 | 
  84 | <h3 align="center">First Launch</h3>
  85 | 
  86 | 1.  **Initial Setup**: Select folders to index on first launch
  87 | 2.  **Indexing**: The app will scan and index your files (this may take a few minutes for large directories)
  88 | 3.  **Search**: Press `Alt+Space` (or your custom hotkey) to open the search bar from anywhere
  89 | 
  90 | <h3 align="center">Search Syntax</h3>
  91 | 
  92 | | Query | Description |
  93 | |:---|:---|
  94 | | `rust tutorial` | Find documents containing both words |
  95 | | `"exact phrase"` | Find exact phrase matches |
  96 | | `rust OR python` | Boolean OR operator |
  97 | | `code -python` | Exclude documents with "python" |
  98 | | `title:api` | Search only in document titles |
  99 | | `ext:pdf` | Filter by file extension |
 100 | | `path:docs` | Filter by folder path |
 101 | | `size:>5MB` | Filter by file size (KB, MB, GB) |
 102 | 
 103 | <h3 align="center">Keyboard Shortcuts</h3>
 104 | 
 105 | | Shortcut | Action |
 106 | |:---|:---|
 107 | | `Alt+Space` | Toggle search window (Global Hotkey, configurable in Settings) |
 108 | | `Ctrl+Enter` | Open selected file |
 109 | | `Ctrl+C` | Copy file path |
 110 | | `Esc` | Close search window |
 111 | | `↑/↓` | Navigate results |
 112 | 
 113 | <h3 align="center">Command-Line Interface</h3>
 114 | 
 115 | Flash Search includes a CLI mode for terminal-based querying and scripting:
 116 | 
 117 | ```bash
 118 | # Basic terminal text search
 119 | flash-search --cli "query"
 120 | 
 121 | # Output as JSON 
 122 | flash-search --cli "query" --json
 123 | ```
 124 | 
 125 | <h3 align="center">App Data & Logs</h3>
 126 | 
 127 | Flash Search automatically manages its index database and rolling background logs (retained up to 30 days) locally in the `com.flashsearch` data directory:
 128 | - **Windows**: `%AppData%\com.flashsearch` or `%LocalAppData%\com.flashsearch`
 129 | - **macOS/Linux**: `~/.local/share/com.flashsearch` or `~/.config/com.flashsearch`
 130 | 
 131 | <h2 align="center">🏗️ Tech Stack</h2>
 132 | 
 133 | <h3 align="center">Core Architecture</h3>
 134 | 
 135 | | Component | Technology | Purpose |
 136 | |:---|:---|:---|
 137 | | **Language** | Rust | Zero-overhead, memory-safe core |
 138 | | **GUI** | Iced | High-performance, cross-platform UI framework (<30MB RAM) |
 139 | | **Search Engine** | Tantivy | Full-text indexing with BM25 scoring |
 140 | | **Document Intelligence** | [Kreuzberg](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg) | Universal text extraction (75+ formats) + OCR |
 141 | | **Metadata DB** | redb | Pure Rust key-value storage |
 142 | | **Concurrency** | Rayon + Tokio | Parallel processing + async I/O |
 143 | 
 144 | <h3 align="center">Supported File Formats</h3>
 145 | 
 146 | | Category | Supported Formats | OCR |
 147 | |:---|:---|:---:|
 148 | | **Digital Documents** | PDF (Native & Scanned), XPS, OXPS, PS, EPS | ✅ |
 149 | | **MS Office** | DOC, DOCX, XLS, XLSX, PPT, PPTX (incl. Macro/Template variations) | ❌ |
 150 | | **Images** | JPG, PNG, WEBP, BMP, GIF, TIFF, JP2, PNM, PBM, PGM, PPM | ✅ |
 151 | | **Text & Markup** | MD, TXT, RTF, HTML, HTM, XML, SVG, LaTeX (TEX), RST, ORG | ❌ |
 152 | | **E-books & Comics** | EPUB, FB2, MOBI, AZW3, CHM, CBZ, CBR | ❌ |
 153 | | **Archives** | ZIP, 7Z, TAR, TGZ, GZ, RAR | ❌ |
 154 | | **Data & Emails** | JSON, YAML, TOML, CSV, ODS, EML, MSG | ❌ |
 155 | 
 156 | <h2 align="center">📊 Performance</h2>
 157 | 
 158 | <div align="center">
 159 | 
 160 | Flash Search leverages **[Kreuzberg](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg)**'s Rust-native text extraction engine to bypass traditional parsing bottlenecks. 
 161 | 
 162 | Benchmarks on standard desktop hardware (e.g., AMD Ryzen 7 / Apple M-series):
 163 | 
 164 | </div>
 165 | 
 166 | | Metric | Value | Notes |
 167 | |:---|:---|:---|
 168 | | **Text Extraction Speed** | Up to **9x-40x** faster | Compared to traditional Python-based parsers (e.g. Unstructured) |
 169 | | **Indexing Throughput** | **~50-100 MB/s** | Highly parallelized via Rayon |
 170 | | **Search Latency (p50)** | **< 15ms** | Instant retrieval on million-document datasets |
 171 | | **Search Latency (p99)** | **< 50ms** | Thanks to Tantivy's optimized index |
 172 | | **Idle RAM Usage** | **~25-30 MB** | Minimal background footprint securely controlled via Rust |
 173 | | **Peak RAM (Indexing)** | **~150-200 MB** | Gracefully bounded by streaming architecture and zero-copy patterns |
 174 | 
 175 | <h3 align="center">Comparison</h3>
 176 | 
 177 | <div align="center">
 178 | 
 179 | | Feature | Flash Search | AnyTXT | Windows Search | Recoll |
 180 | |:---|:---|:---|:---|:---|
 181 | | Startup Time | **Instant** | ~2s | System | ~3s |
 182 | | Memory Overhead | **~30MB** | ~80MB | ~150MB+ | ~120MB |
 183 | | Fast PDF Extraction | ✅ **(Kreuzberg)** | ✅ | ⚠️ | ✅ |
 184 | | Integrated OCR | ✅ **(Multi-Backend)** | ✅ | ❌ | ⚠️ |
 185 | | Supported Formats | ✅ **(75+)** | ✅ | ❌ | ⚠️ |
 186 | | Live Updates | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ |
 187 | | Cross-Platform | ✅ | ⚠️ | ❌ | ✅ |

 191 | <h2 align="center">🗺️ Roadmap</h2>
 192 | 
 193 | ### Phase 1: Foundation (Completed ✅)
 194 | - [x] High-performance core with **Rust**
 195 | - [x] Efficient UI framework with **Iced**
 196 | - [x] Basic file parsers for PDF, DOCX, and TXT
 197 | - [x] Parallel filesystem scanning and incremental indexing
 198 | 
 199 | ### Phase 2: Polish & UX (Completed ✅)
 200 | - [x] Advanced search filters (date, size, extension)
 201 | - [x] Global "Spotlight-style" search bar (Alt+Space)
 202 | - [x] Real-time file indexing and system tray integration
 203 | - [x] Fast filename-only search mode for instant navigation
 204 | - [x] Optimized result preview and metadata retrieval
 205 | - [x] **Network Discovery**: Support for enterprise SMB/CIFS and NAS drives
 206 | 
 207 | ### Phase 3: Advanced Intelligence (In Progress 🚧)
 208 | - [x] **Universal Text Extraction**: 75+ formats supported via **Kreuzberg**
 209 | - [x] **Integrated OCR**: Native support for scanned PDFs and images
 210 | - [x] **Pinned Results**: Favorite important files for instant access
 211 | - [ ] **Semantic Search**: Vector embeddings for context-aware queries
 212 | - [ ] **Natural Language Queries**: "files from last week about taxes"
 213 | 
 214 | ### Phase 4: Expansion & Connectivity (Future 🔮)
 215 | - [ ] **Plugin System**: Community-built parsers and search extensions
 216 | - [ ] **Cloud Indexing**: Optional encrypted metadata sync across devices
 217 | - [ ] **Developer API**: Headless search service for other applications

  30 | use crate::settings::{AppSettings, SettingsManager};
  31 | use crate::watcher::WatcherManager;
  32 | use arc_swap::ArcSwap;
  33 | use parking_lot::Mutex;
  34 | use std::sync::Arc;
  35 | use tokio::sync::mpsc;
  36 | 
  37 | pub struct AppState {
  38 |     pub indexer: Arc<IndexManager>,
  39 |     pub metadata_db: Arc<MetadataDb>,
  40 |     pub settings_manager: Arc<SettingsManager>,
  41 |     pub settings_cache: ArcSwap<AppSettings>,
  42 |     pub watcher: Mutex<WatcherManager>,
  43 |     pub filename_index: Option<Arc<FilenameIndex>>,
  44 |     pub progress_tx: mpsc::Sender<crate::scanner::ProgressEvent>,
  45 |     pub scanner: Arc<crate::scanner::Scanner>,
  46 |     pub indexing_handle: Mutex<Option<tokio::task::JoinHandle<()>>>,
  47 | }
  48 | 
  49 | #[bon::bon]
  50 | impl AppState {
  51 |     #[builder]
  52 |     pub fn new(
  53 |         indexer: Arc<IndexManager>,
  54 |         metadata_db: Arc<MetadataDb>,
  55 |         settings_manager: SettingsManager,
  56 |         watcher: WatcherManager,
  57 |         filename_index: Option<Arc<FilenameIndex>>,
  58 |         progress_tx: mpsc::Sender<crate::scanner::ProgressEvent>,
  59 |         scanner: Arc<crate::scanner::Scanner>,
  60 |     ) -> Self {
  61 |         let cache = settings_manager.load().unwrap_or_else(|e| {
  62 |             tracing::warn!("Failed to load settings (using defaults): {}", e);
  63 |             AppSettings::default()
  64 |         });
  65 |         let mut watcher = watcher;
  66 |         let _ = watcher.update_watch_list(&cache.index_dirs);
  67 |         Self {
  68 |             indexer,
  69 |             metadata_db,
  70 |             settings_manager: Arc::new(settings_manager),
  71 |             settings_cache: ArcSwap::from_pointee(cache),
  72 |             watcher: Mutex::new(watcher),
  73 |             filename_index,
  74 |             progress_tx,
  75 |             scanner,
  76 |             indexing_handle: Mutex::new(None),
  77 |         }
  78 |     }
  79 | }
  80 | 
  81 | #[cfg(test)]
  82 | mod tests {
  83 |     use super::*;
  84 |     use crate::indexer::searcher::SearchResult;
  85 |     use tempfile::tempdir;
  86 | 
  87 |     #[test]
  88 |     fn test_export_csv() {
  89 |         let temp_dir = tempdir().unwrap();
  90 |         let csv_path = temp_dir.path().join("test.csv");
  91 |         let results = vec![
  92 |             SearchResult::builder()
  93 |                 .file_path("test.txt".to_string())
  94 |                 .score(1.0)
  95 |                 .matched_terms(vec![])
  96 |                 .snippets(vec![])
  97 |                 .build(),
  98 |         ];
  99 | 
 100 |         export_results_csv(&results, csv_path.to_str().unwrap()).unwrap();
 101 |         let content = std::fs::read_to_string(csv_path).unwrap();

 103 |         assert!(content.contains("1,test.txt,"));
 104 |     }
 105 | }

   1 | use crate::commands::AppState;
   2 | use crate::commands::{
   3 |     get_file_preview_highlighted_internal, search_filenames_internal, search_query_internal,
   4 | };
   5 | use crate::error::FlashError;
   6 | use crate::indexer::searcher::{SearchParams, SearchResult};
   7 | use crate::scanner::ProgressEvent;
   8 | use crate::settings::AppSettings;
   9 | use compact_str::CompactString;
  10 | use iced::futures::SinkExt;
  11 | use iced::widget::Id;
  12 | use iced::{Element, Subscription, Task};
  13 | use parking_lot::Mutex;
  14 | use std::sync::Arc;
  15 | use tokio::sync::mpsc;
  16 | 
  17 | pub mod icons;
  18 | pub mod search;
  19 | pub mod settings;
  20 | pub mod theme;
  21 | 
  22 | #[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]
  23 | pub enum Tab {
  24 |     Search,
  25 |     Settings,
  26 | }
  27 | 
  28 | #[derive(Debug, Clone)]
  29 | pub struct FileItem {
  30 |     pub score: f32,
  31 |     pub path: String,
  32 |     pub title: String,
  33 |     pub extension: Option<CompactString>,
  34 |     pub size: Option<u64>,
  35 |     pub modified: Option<u64>,
  36 |     pub snippets: Vec<String>,
  37 | }
  38 | 
  39 | impl From<SearchResult> for FileItem {
  40 |     fn from(r: SearchResult) -> Self {
  41 |         let path_clone = r.file_path.clone();
  42 |         Self {
  43 |             score: r.score,
  44 |             path: r.file_path,
  45 |             title: r.title.as_ref().map_or_else(
  46 |                 || {
  47 |                     std::path::Path::new(&path_clone)
  48 |                         .file_name()
  49 |                         .and_then(|n| n.to_str())
  50 |                         .unwrap_or(&path_clone)
  51 |                         .to_string()
  52 |                 },
  53 |                 std::string::ToString::to_string,
  54 |             ),
  55 |             extension: r.extension,
  56 |             size: r.size,
  57 |             modified: r.modified,
  58 |             snippets: r.snippets,
  59 |         }
  60 |     }
  61 | }
  62 | 
  63 | impl From<crate::models::FilenameSearchResult> for FileItem {
  64 |     fn from(r: crate::models::FilenameSearchResult) -> Self {
  65 |         let path_clone = r.file_path.clone();
  66 |         Self {
  67 |             score: 1.0,
  68 |             path: r.file_path,
  69 |             title: r.file_name.to_string(),
  70 |             extension: std::path::Path::new(&path_clone)
  71 |                 .extension()
  72 |                 .and_then(|e| e.to_str())
  73 |                 .map(CompactString::from),
  74 |             size: None,
  75 |             modified: None,
  76 |             snippets: Vec::new(),
  77 |         }
  78 |     }
  79 | }
  80 | 
  81 | #[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Default, serde::Serialize, serde::Deserialize)]
  82 | pub enum DateFilter {
  83 |     #[default]
  84 |     Anytime,
  85 |     Today,
  86 |     Last7Days,
  87 |     Last30Days,
  88 | }

  90 | #[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Default, serde::Serialize, serde::Deserialize)]
  91 | pub enum SearchMode {
  92 |     #[default]
  93 |     FullText,
  94 |     Filename,
  95 | }
  96 | 
  97 | pub fn get_search_input_id() -> Id {
  98 |     static ID: std::sync::OnceLock<Id> = std::sync::OnceLock::new();
  99 |     ID.get_or_init(Id::unique).clone()
 100 | }
 101 | 
 102 | pub fn get_progress_subscription_id() -> Id {
 103 |     static ID: std::sync::OnceLock<Id> = std::sync::OnceLock::new();
 104 |     ID.get_or_init(Id::unique).clone()
 105 | }
 106 | 
 107 | pub fn format_size(bytes: u64) -> String {
 108 |     const KB: u64 = 1024;
 109 |     const MB: u64 = 1024 * 1024;
 110 |     const GB: u64 = 1024 * 1024 * 1024;
 111 | 
 112 |     if bytes >= GB {
 113 |         format!("{:.2} GB", bytes as f64 / GB as f64)
 114 |     } else if bytes >= MB {
 115 |         format!("{:.1} MB", bytes as f64 / MB as f64)
 116 |     } else if bytes >= KB {
 117 |         format!("{:.1} KB", bytes as f64 / KB as f64)
 118 |     } else {
 119 |         format!("{bytes} B")
 120 |     }
 121 | }
 122 | 
 123 | /// # Panics
 124 | ///
 125 | /// Panics if the timestamp is out of range for the system's local time.
 126 | pub fn format_date(timestamp: u64) -> String {
 127 |     jiff::Timestamp::from_second(i64::try_from(timestamp).unwrap_or(i64::MAX))
 128 |         .unwrap_or_else(|_| jiff::Timestamp::from_second(0).unwrap())
 129 |         .to_zoned(jiff::tz::TimeZone::system())
 130 |         .strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M")
 131 |         .to_string()
 132 | }

 142 |     ItemHovered(Option<usize>),

 144 |     OpenFolder(String),
 145 |     CopyPath(String),
 146 |     ShowContextMenu(usize),
 147 |     // Filters

 149 |     ToggleFilterExtension(String),
 150 |     MinSizeChanged(String),
 151 |     MaxSizeChanged(String),
 152 |     SizeUnitChanged(String),
 153 |     DateFilterChanged(DateFilter),
 154 |     SearchModeChanged(SearchMode),
 155 |     ToggleCaseSensitive(bool),
 156 |     ToggleWholeWord(bool),
 157 |     ClearFilters,
 158 |     // Settings

 160 |     ExcludePatternsChanged(String),
 161 |     CustomExtensionsChanged(String),
 162 |     GlobalHotkeyChanged(String),
 163 |     AddFolder,
 164 |     RemoveFolder(usize),
 165 |     ToggleMinimizeToTray(bool),
 166 |     ToggleAutoStart(bool),
 167 |     ToggleContextMenu(bool),
 168 |     ToggleTheme,

 177 |     FontSizeChanged(crate::settings::FontSize),

 182 |     IndexRebuilt,

 191 |     ExportResults(String), // format: "csv" or "json"
 192 |     WindowIdCaptured(iced::window::Id),
 193 |     DismissError,

 200 | pub struct App {
 201 |     pub(crate) state: Option<Arc<AppState>>,
 202 |     pub(crate) error: Option<String>,
 203 |     pub(crate) search_error: Option<String>,
 204 |     pub(crate) active_tab: Tab,
 205 |     pub(crate) search_query: String,
 206 |     pub(crate) results: Vec<FileItem>,
 207 |     pub(crate) selected_index: Option<usize>,
 208 |     pub(crate) hovered_item_index: Option<usize>,
 209 |     pub(crate) is_searching: bool,
 210 |     pub(crate) search_id: usize,
 211 |     pub(crate) filter_extension: String,
 212 |     pub(crate) filter_extensions: std::collections::HashSet<String>,
 213 |     pub(crate) min_size: String,
 214 |     pub(crate) max_size: String,
 215 |     pub(crate) size_unit: String,
 216 |     pub(crate) date_filter: DateFilter,
 217 |     pub(crate) search_mode: SearchMode,
 218 |     pub(crate) filter_size: String,
 219 |     pub(crate) files_indexed: i32,
 220 |     pub(crate) index_size: String,
 221 |     pub(crate) rebuild_status: Option<String>,
 222 |     pub(crate) rebuild_progress: Option<f32>,
 223 |     pub(crate) is_dark: bool,
 224 |     pub(crate) sidebar_collapsed: bool,
 225 |     pub(crate) settings: AppSettings,
 226 |     pub(crate) new_index_dir: String,
 227 |     pub(crate) new_exclude_pattern: String,
 228 |     pub(crate) preview_result: Option<crate::models::PreviewResult>,
 229 |     pub(crate) is_loading_preview: bool,
 230 |     #[allow(dead_code)]
 231 |     pub(crate) tray_icon: Option<tray_icon::TrayIcon>,
 232 |     pub(crate) window_id: Option<iced::window::Id>,
 233 |     pub(crate) progress_rx: Option<Arc<Mutex<tokio::sync::mpsc::Receiver<ProgressEvent>>>>,

 235 | 
 236 | #[derive(Debug, Clone)]
 237 | struct SubscriptionData {
 238 |     rx: Arc<Mutex<tokio::sync::mpsc::Receiver<ProgressEvent>>>,
 239 | }
 240 | 
 241 | impl std::hash::Hash for SubscriptionData {
 242 |     fn hash<H: std::hash::Hasher>(&self, state: &mut H) {
 243 |         Arc::as_ptr(&self.rx).hash(state);
 244 |     }
 245 | }
 246 | 
 247 | impl PartialEq for SubscriptionData {
 248 |     fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {
 249 |         Arc::ptr_eq(&self.rx, &other.rx)
 250 |     }
 251 | }
 252 | 
 253 | impl Eq for SubscriptionData {}
 254 | 
 255 | impl Default for App {
 256 |     fn default() -> Self {
 257 |         Self {
 258 |             state: None,
 259 |             error: None,
 260 |             search_error: None,
 261 |             active_tab: Tab::Search,
 262 |             search_query: String::new(),
 263 |             results: Vec::new(),
 264 |             selected_index: None,
 265 |             hovered_item_index: None,
 266 |             is_searching: false,
 267 |             search_id: 0,
 268 |             filter_extension: String::new(),
 269 |             filter_extensions: std::collections::HashSet::new(),
 270 |             min_size: String::new(),
 271 |             max_size: String::new(),
 272 |             size_unit: "MB".to_string(),
 273 |             date_filter: DateFilter::Anytime,
 274 |             search_mode: SearchMode::FullText,
 275 |             filter_size: String::new(),
 276 |             files_indexed: 0,
 277 |             index_size: "0 MB".to_string(),
 278 |             rebuild_status: None,
 279 |             rebuild_progress: None,
 280 |             is_dark: false,
 281 |             sidebar_collapsed: false,
 282 |             settings: AppSettings::default(),
 283 |             new_index_dir: String::new(),
 284 |             new_exclude_pattern: String::new(),
 285 |             preview_result: None,
 286 |             is_loading_preview: false,
 287 |             tray_icon: None,
 288 |             window_id: None,
 289 |             progress_rx: None,
 290 |         }
 291 |     }
 292 | }
 293 | 
 294 | impl App {
 295 |     fn new(
 296 |         state: Result<Arc<AppState>, String>,
 297 |         progress_rx: Option<mpsc::Receiver<ProgressEvent>>,
 298 |     ) -> Self {
 299 |         match state {
 300 |             Ok(state) => {
 301 |                 let settings = state.settings_manager.load().unwrap_or_default();
 302 |                 let index_stats = state.indexer.get_statistics().unwrap_or_default();
 303 |                 let index_size = format!(
 304 |                     "{:.1} MB",
 305 |                     (index_stats.total_size_bytes as f64) / 1_048_576.0
 306 |                 );
 307 |                 let is_dark = matches!(settings.theme, crate::settings::Theme::Dark);
 308 | 
 309 |                 let mut app = Self {
 310 |                     state: Some(state),
 311 |                     settings: settings.clone(),
 312 |                     files_indexed: i32::try_from(index_stats.total_documents).unwrap_or(i32::MAX),
 313 |                     index_size,
 314 |                     is_dark,
 315 |                     progress_rx: progress_rx.map(|rx| Arc::new(Mutex::new(rx))),
 316 |                     ..Default::default()
 317 |                 };
 318 | 
 319 |                 for ext in &settings.default_filters.file_types {
 320 |                     app.filter_extensions.insert(ext.clone());
 321 |                 }
 322 | 
 323 |                 app
 324 |             }
 325 |             Err(e) => Self {
 326 |                 error: Some(e),
 327 |                 progress_rx: progress_rx.map(|rx| Arc::new(Mutex::new(rx))),
 328 |                 ..Default::default()
 329 |             },
 330 |         }
 331 |     }
 332 | 
 333 |     fn parse_size_filter(size_str: &str) -> (Option<u64>, Option<u64>) {
 334 |         if size_str.is_empty() {
 335 |             return (None, None);
 336 |         }
 337 | 
 338 |         let size_str = size_str.trim();
 339 |         let (op, num_str) = size_str.strip_prefix(">=").map_or_else(
 340 |             || {
 341 |                 size_str.strip_prefix("<=").map_or_else(
 342 |                     || {
 343 |                         size_str.strip_prefix(">").map_or_else(
 344 |                             || {
 345 |                                 size_str
 346 |                                     .strip_prefix("<")
 347 |                                     .map_or_else(|| (">=", size_str), |stripped| ("<", stripped))
 348 |                             },
 349 |                             |stripped| (">", stripped),
 350 |                         )
 351 |                     },
 352 |                     |stripped| ("<=", stripped),
 353 |                 )
 354 |             },
 355 |             |stripped| (">=", stripped),
 356 |         );
 357 | 
 358 |         let num_str = num_str.trim();
 359 |         let mut multiplier: u64 = 1;
 360 |         let mut clean_num = num_str;
 361 | 
 362 |         if num_str.to_uppercase().ends_with("GB") {
 363 |             multiplier = 1024 * 1024 * 1024;
 364 |             clean_num = num_str[..num_str.len() - 2].trim();
 365 |         } else if num_str.to_uppercase().ends_with("MB") {
 366 |             multiplier = 1024 * 1024;
 367 |             clean_num = num_str[..num_str.len() - 2].trim();
 368 |         } else if num_str.to_uppercase().ends_with("KB") {
 369 |             multiplier = 1024;
 370 |             clean_num = num_str[..num_str.len() - 2].trim();
 371 |         } else if num_str.to_uppercase().ends_with('B') {
 372 |             multiplier = 1;
 373 |             clean_num = num_str[..num_str.len() - 1].trim();
 374 |         }
 375 | 
 376 |         let Ok(val) = clean_num.parse::<f64>() else {
 377 |             return (None, None);
 378 |         };
 379 | 
 380 |         #[allow(clippy::cast_possible_truncation, clippy::cast_sign_loss)]
 381 |         let bytes = (val * multiplier as f64) as u64;
 382 | 
 383 |         match op {
 384 |             ">" => (Some(bytes + 1), None),
 385 |             "<" => (None, Some(bytes.saturating_sub(1))),
 386 |             "<=" => (None, Some(bytes)),
 387 |             _ => (Some(bytes), None),
 388 |         }
 389 |     }
 390 | 
 391 |     fn get_min_modified(&self) -> Option<u64> {
 392 |         match self.date_filter {
 393 |             DateFilter::Anytime => None,
 394 |             DateFilter::Today => Some(
 395 |                 #[allow(clippy::cast_sign_loss)]
 396 |                 {
 397 |                     jiff::Zoned::now()
 398 |                         .with()
 399 |                         .hour(0)
 400 |                         .minute(0)
 401 |                         .second(0)
 402 |                         .build()
 403 |                         .unwrap()
 404 |                         .timestamp()
 405 |                         .as_second() as u64
 406 |                 },
 407 |             ),
 408 |             DateFilter::Last7Days => Some(
 409 |                 #[allow(clippy::cast_sign_loss)]
 410 |                 {
 411 |                     jiff::Zoned::now()
 412 |                         .checked_sub(jiff::SignedDuration::from_secs(7 * 24 * 3600))
 413 |                         .unwrap()
 414 |                         .timestamp()
 415 |                         .as_second() as u64
 416 |                 },
 417 |             ),
 418 |             DateFilter::Last30Days => Some(
 419 |                 #[allow(clippy::cast_sign_loss)]
 420 |                 {
 421 |                     jiff::Zoned::now()
 422 |                         .checked_sub(jiff::SignedDuration::from_secs(30 * 24 * 3600))
 423 |                         .unwrap()
 424 |                         .timestamp()
 425 |                         .as_second() as u64
 426 |                 },
 427 |             ),
 428 |         }
 429 |     }
 430 | 
 431 |     fn perform_search(&mut self) -> Task<Message> {
 432 |         let state = match &self.state {
 433 |             Some(s) => s.clone(),
 434 |             None => return Task::none(),
 435 |         };
 436 | 
 437 |         let mut query = self.search_query.clone();
 438 | 
 439 |         if self.settings.whole_word
 440 |             && !query.starts_with('"')
 441 |             && !query.ends_with('"')
 442 |             && !query.contains(':')
 443 |         {
 444 |             query = format!("\"{query}\"");
 445 |         }
 446 | 
 447 |         let max_results = self.settings.max_results;
 448 |         let mode = self.search_mode;
 449 | 
 450 |         let mut extensions: ahash::AHashSet<String> = self
 451 |             .filter_extension
 452 |             .split(',')
 453 |             .map(|s| s.trim().to_lowercase())
 454 |             .filter(|s| !s.is_empty())
 455 |             .collect();
 456 | 
 457 |         for ext in &self.filter_extensions {
 458 |             extensions.insert(ext.clone());
 459 |         }
 460 | 
 461 |         let extension: Option<Vec<String>> = if extensions.is_empty() {
 462 |             None
 463 |         } else {
 464 |             Some(extensions.into_iter().collect())
 465 |         };
 466 | 
 467 |         let multiplier: u64 = match self.size_unit.as_str() {
 468 |             "KB" => 1024,
 469 |             "GB" => 1024 * 1024 * 1024,
 470 |             _ => 1024 * 1024,
 471 |         };
 472 | 
 473 |         let min_size = self
 474 |             .min_size
 475 |             .trim()
 476 |             .parse::<u64>()
 477 |             .ok()
 478 |             .map(|n| n * multiplier);
 479 |         let max_size = self
 480 |             .max_size
 481 |             .trim()
 482 |             .parse::<u64>()
 483 |             .ok()
 484 |             .map(|n| n * multiplier);
 485 | 
 486 |         let (min_size, max_size) = if min_size.is_none() && max_size.is_none() {
 487 |             Self::parse_size_filter(&self.filter_size)
 488 |         } else {
 489 |             (min_size, max_size)
 490 |         };
 491 | 
 492 |         let min_modified = self.get_min_modified();
 493 | 
 494 |         self.is_searching = true;
 495 |         self.results.clear();
 496 |         self.preview_result = None;
 497 |         self.search_id += 1;
 498 |         let current_search_id = self.search_id;
 499 |         let case_sensitive = self.settings.case_sensitive;
 500 | 
 501 |         Task::future(async move {
 502 |             match mode {
 503 |                 SearchMode::Filename => {
 504 |                     match search_filenames_internal(query.clone(), max_results, &state).await {
 505 |                         Ok(results) => {
 506 |                             let items: Vec<FileItem> =
 507 |                                 results.into_iter().map(FileItem::from).collect();
 508 |                             Message::SearchResultsReceived(current_search_id, items)
 509 |                         }
 510 |                         Err(e) => Message::SearchError(FlashError::search(&query, e)),
 511 |                     }
 512 |                 }
 513 |                 SearchMode::FullText => {
 514 |                     match search_query_internal(
 515 |                         SearchParams::builder()
 516 |                             .query(&query)
 517 |                             .limit(max_results)
 518 |                             .maybe_min_size(min_size)
 519 |                             .maybe_max_size(max_size)
 520 |                             .maybe_min_modified(min_modified)
 521 |                             .maybe_file_extensions(extension.as_deref())
 522 |                             .case_sensitive(case_sensitive)
 523 |                             .build(),
 524 |                         &state,
 525 |                     )
 526 |                     .await
 527 |                     {
 528 |                         Ok(results) => {
 529 |                             let items: Vec<FileItem> =
 530 |                                 results.into_iter().map(FileItem::from).collect();
 531 |                             Message::SearchResultsReceived(current_search_id, items)
 532 |                         }
 533 |                         Err(e) => Message::SearchError(FlashError::search(&query, e)),
 534 |                     }
 535 |                 }
 536 |             }
 537 |         })
 538 |     }
 539 | 
 540 |     fn save_settings(&self) -> Task<Message> {
 541 |         if let Some(state) = &self.state {
 542 |             let settings = self.settings.clone();
 543 |             let state = state.clone();
 544 |             return Task::perform(
 545 |                 async move {
 546 |                     let _ = state.settings_manager.save(&settings);
 547 |                     let mut watcher = state.watcher.lock();
 548 |                     let _ = watcher.update_watch_list(&settings.index_dirs);
 549 |                 },
 550 |                 |()| Message::NoOp,
 551 |             );
 552 |         }
 553 |         Task::none()
 554 |     }
 555 | }
 556 | 
 557 | #[allow(clippy::too_many_lines)]
 558 | pub fn update(app: &mut App, message: Message) -> Task<Message> {
 559 |     match message {
 560 |         Message::TabChanged(tab) => {
 561 |             app.active_tab = tab;
 562 |             Task::none()
 563 |         }
 564 |         Message::SearchQueryChanged(q) => {
 565 |             app.search_query = q;
 566 |             Task::none()
 567 |         }
 568 |         Message::SearchSubmitted => app.perform_search(),
 569 |         Message::SearchResultsReceived(id, results) => {
 570 |             if id == app.search_id {
 571 |                 app.results = results;
 572 |                 app.is_searching = false;
 573 |                 app.selected_index = None;
 574 |             }
 575 |             Task::none()
 576 |         }
 577 |         Message::SearchError(e) => {
 578 |             app.is_searching = false;
 579 |             app.search_error = Some(e.to_string());
 580 |             Task::none()
 581 |         }
 582 |         Message::ResultSelected(idx) => {
 583 |             app.selected_index = Some(idx);
 584 |             if app.settings.show_preview_panel {
 585 |                 let item = app.results[idx].clone();
 586 |                 let query = app.search_query.clone();
 587 |                 if let Some(state) = &app.state {
 588 |                     let state = state.clone();
 589 |                     app.is_loading_preview = true;
 590 |                     return Task::future(async move {
 591 |                         match get_file_preview_highlighted_internal(item.path, query, &state).await
 592 |                         {
 593 |                             Ok(preview) => Message::PreviewLoaded(preview),
 594 |                             Err(e) => Message::StatusUpdate(format!("Preview error: {e}")),
 595 |                         }
 596 |                     });
 597 |                 }
 598 |             }
 599 |             Task::none()
 600 |         }
 601 |         Message::PreviewLoaded(preview) => {
 602 |             app.preview_result = Some(preview);
 603 |             app.is_loading_preview = false;
 604 |             Task::none()
 605 |         }
 606 |         Message::ItemHovered(idx) => {
 607 |             app.hovered_item_index = idx;
 608 |             Task::none()
 609 |         }
 610 |         Message::OpenFile(path) => {
 611 |             let _ = opener::open(std::path::Path::new(&path));
 612 |             Task::none()
 613 |         }
 614 |         Message::OpenFolder(path) => {
 615 |             let _ = crate::commands::open_folder_internal(&path);
 616 |             Task::none()
 617 |         }
 618 |         Message::CopyPath(path) => {
 619 |             let _ = crate::commands::copy_to_clipboard_internal(&path);
 620 |             Task::none()
 621 |         }
 622 |         Message::FilterExtensionChanged(ext) => {
 623 |             app.filter_extension = ext;
 624 |             Task::none()
 625 |         }
 626 |         Message::ToggleFilterExtension(ext) => {
 627 |             if app.filter_extensions.contains(&ext) {
 628 |                 app.filter_extensions.remove(&ext);
 629 |             } else {
 630 |                 app.filter_extensions.insert(ext);
 631 |             }
 632 |             Task::none()
 633 |         }
 634 |         Message::MinSizeChanged(s) => {
 635 |             app.min_size = s;
 636 |             Task::none()
 637 |         }
 638 |         Message::MaxSizeChanged(s) => {
 639 |             app.max_size = s;
 640 |             Task::none()
 641 |         }
 642 |         Message::SizeUnitChanged(u) => {
 643 |             app.size_unit = u;
 644 |             Task::none()
 645 |         }
 646 |         Message::DateFilterChanged(d) => {
 647 |             app.date_filter = d;
 648 |             Task::none()
 649 |         }
 650 |         Message::SearchModeChanged(m) => {
 651 |             app.search_mode = m;
 652 |             Task::none()
 653 |         }
 654 |         Message::ToggleCaseSensitive(b) => {
 655 |             app.settings.case_sensitive = b;
 656 |             Task::none()
 657 |         }
 658 |         Message::ToggleWholeWord(b) => {
 659 |             app.settings.whole_word = b;
 660 |             Task::none()
 661 |         }
 662 |         Message::ClearFilters => {
 663 |             app.filter_extension.clear();
 664 |             app.filter_extensions.clear();
 665 |             app.min_size.clear();
 666 |             app.max_size.clear();
 667 |             app.date_filter = DateFilter::Anytime;
 668 |             Task::none()
 669 |         }
 670 |         Message::MaxResultsChanged(s) => {
 671 |             if let Ok(n) = s.parse::<usize>() {
 672 |                 app.settings.max_results = n;
 673 |             }
 674 |             Task::none()
 675 |         }
 676 |         Message::ExcludePatternsChanged(s) => {
 677 |             app.settings.exclude_patterns = s
 678 |                 .split(',')
 679 |                 .map(|p| p.trim().to_string())
 680 |                 .filter(|p| !p.is_empty())
 681 |                 .collect();
 682 |             Task::none()
 683 |         }
 684 |         Message::CustomExtensionsChanged(s) => {
 685 |             app.settings.custom_extensions = s;
 686 |             Task::none()
 687 |         }
 688 |         Message::GlobalHotkeyChanged(s) => {
 689 |             app.settings.global_hotkey = s;
 690 |             Task::none()
 691 |         }
 692 |         Message::AddFolder => Task::done(Message::PickFolder),
 693 |         Message::ToggleMinimizeToTray(b) => {
 694 |             app.settings.minimize_to_tray = b;
 695 |             Task::none()
 696 |         }
 697 |         Message::ToggleAutoStart(b) => {
 698 |             app.settings.auto_start_on_boot = b;
 699 |             Task::none()
 700 |         }
 701 |         Message::ToggleContextMenu(b) => {
 702 |             app.settings.context_menu_enabled = b;
 703 |             Task::none()
 704 |         }
 705 |         Message::ToggleTheme => {
 706 |             app.is_dark = !app.is_dark;
 707 |             app.settings.theme = if app.is_dark {
 708 |                 crate::settings::Theme::Dark
 709 |             } else {
 710 |                 crate::settings::Theme::Light
 711 |             };
 712 |             Task::none()
 713 |         }
 714 |         Message::RebuildIndex => {
 715 |             if let Some(state) = &app.state {
 716 |                 let state = state.clone();
 717 |                 return Task::future(async move {
 718 |                     let _ = state
 719 |                         .scanner
 720 |                         .scan_directory(std::path::PathBuf::from("C:\\"), vec![])
 721 |                         .await;
 722 |                     Message::IndexRebuilt
 723 |                 });
 724 |             }
 725 |             Task::none()
 726 |         }
 727 |         Message::IndexDirAdded(dir) => {
 728 |             if !dir.is_empty() && !app.settings.index_dirs.contains(&dir) {
 729 |                 app.settings.index_dirs.push(dir);
 730 |                 app.new_index_dir.clear();
 731 |             }
 732 |             Task::none()
 733 |         }
 734 |         Message::ExcludePatternAdded(p) => {
 735 |             if !p.is_empty() && !app.settings.exclude_patterns.contains(&p) {
 736 |                 app.settings.exclude_patterns.push(p);
 737 |                 app.new_exclude_pattern.clear();
 738 |             }
 739 |             Task::none()
 740 |         }
 741 |         Message::SaveSettings => app.save_settings(),
 742 |         Message::ResetSettings => {
 743 |             app.settings = AppSettings::default();
 744 |             Task::none()
 745 |         }
 746 |         Message::ThemeChanged(t) => {
 747 |             app.settings.theme = t;
 748 |             Task::none()
 749 |         }
 750 |         Message::FontSizeChanged(f) => {
 751 |             app.settings.font_size = f;
 752 |             Task::none()
 753 |         }
 754 |         Message::PollProgressResult(Some(event)) => {
 755 |             match event.ptype {
 756 |                 crate::scanner::ProgressType::Content => {
 757 |                     app.files_indexed = i32::try_from(event.processed).unwrap_or(i32::MAX);
 758 |                     app.rebuild_progress = if event.total > 0 {
 759 |                         Some(event.processed as f32 / event.total as f32)
 760 |                     } else {
 761 |                         None
 762 |                     };
 763 |                     app.rebuild_status = Some(event.status);
 764 |                 }
 765 |                 crate::scanner::ProgressType::Filename => {
 766 |                     app.rebuild_status = Some(event.status);
 767 |                 }
 768 |             }
 769 |             Task::none()
 770 |         }
 771 |         Message::IndexRebuilt => {
 772 |             let stats = app
 773 |                 .state
 774 |                 .as_ref()
 775 |                 .map(|s| s.indexer.get_statistics().unwrap_or_default())
 776 |                 .unwrap_or_default();
 777 |             app.files_indexed = i32::try_from(stats.total_documents).unwrap_or(i32::MAX);
 778 |             app.index_size = format!("{:.1} MB", (stats.total_size_bytes as f64) / 1_048_576.0);
 779 |             app.rebuild_progress = None;
 780 |             app.rebuild_status = None;
 781 |             Task::none()
 782 |         }
 783 |         Message::StatusUpdate(s) => {
 784 |             app.rebuild_status = Some(s);
 785 |             Task::none()
 786 |         }
 787 |         Message::WindowIdCaptured(id) => {
 788 |             if app.window_id.is_none() {
 789 |                 app.window_id = Some(id);
 790 |             }
 791 |             Task::none()
 792 |         }
 793 |         Message::DismissError => {
 794 |             app.error = None;
 795 |             app.search_error = None;
 796 |             Task::none()
 797 |         }
 798 |         Message::Quit => app.window_id.map_or_else(Task::none, iced::window::close),
 799 |         Message::PickFolder => Task::future(async move {
 800 |             let handle = rfd::AsyncFileDialog::new()
 801 |                 .set_title("Select Folder to Index")
 802 |                 .pick_folder()
 803 |                 .await;
 804 |             Message::FolderPicked(handle.map(|h| h.path().to_string_lossy().to_string()))
 805 |         }),
 806 |         Message::FolderPicked(Some(path)) => {
 807 |             if !app.settings.index_dirs.contains(&path) {
 808 |                 app.settings.index_dirs.push(path);
 809 |             }
 810 |             Task::none()
 811 |         }
 812 |         Message::ToggleSidebar => {
 813 |             app.sidebar_collapsed = !app.sidebar_collapsed;
 814 |             Task::none()
 815 |         }
 816 |         Message::RemoveFolder(i) | Message::RemoveIndexDir(i) => {
 817 |             if i < app.settings.index_dirs.len() {
 818 |                 app.settings.index_dirs.remove(i);
 819 |             }
 820 |             Task::none()
 821 |         }
 822 |         Message::RemoveExcludePattern(i) => {
 823 |             if i < app.settings.exclude_patterns.len() {
 824 |                 app.settings.exclude_patterns.remove(i);
 825 |             }
 826 |             Task::none()
 827 |         }
 828 |         _ => Task::none(),
 829 |     }
 830 | }
 831 | 
 832 | pub fn view(app: &App) -> Element<'_, Message> {
 833 |     match app.active_tab {
 834 |         Tab::Search => search::search_view(app),
 835 |         Tab::Settings => settings::settings_view(app),

 839 | pub fn subscription(app: &App) -> Subscription<Message> {
 840 |     app.progress_rx
 841 |         .as_ref()
 842 |         .map_or_else(Subscription::none, |rx| {
 843 |             Subscription::run_with(SubscriptionData { rx: rx.clone() }, |data| {
 844 |                 let rx = data.rx.clone();
 845 |                 iced::stream::channel(
 846 |                     100,
 847 |                     move |mut output: iced::futures::channel::mpsc::Sender<Message>| {
 848 |                         let rx = rx.clone();
 849 |                         async move {
 850 |                             loop {
 851 |                                 let event = {
 852 |                                     let mut rx_lock = rx.lock();
 853 |                                     rx_lock.try_recv().ok()
 854 |                                 };
 855 | 
 856 |                                 if let Some(event) = event {
 857 |                                     let _ =
 858 |                                         output.send(Message::PollProgressResult(Some(event))).await;
 859 |                                 } else {
 860 |                                     // Check if disconnected
 861 |                                     {
 862 |                                         let mut rx_lock = rx.lock();
 863 |                                         if matches!(
 864 |                                             rx_lock.try_recv(),
 865 |                                             Err(mpsc::error::TryRecvError::Disconnected)
 866 |                                         ) {
 867 |                                             break;
 868 |                                         }
 869 |                                     }
 870 |                                     tokio::time::sleep(std::time::Duration::from_millis(100)).await;
 871 |                                 }
 872 |                             }
 873 |                         }
 874 |                     },
 875 |                 )
 876 |             })
 877 |         })
 878 | }
 879 | 
 880 | pub const fn app_theme(app: &App) -> iced::Theme {
 881 |     if app.is_dark {
 882 |         iced::Theme::Dark
 883 |     } else {
 884 |         iced::Theme::Light
 885 |     }
 886 | }

 890 |         || "Flash Search".to_string(),
 891 |         |status| format!("Flash Search - {status}"),
 892 |     )
 893 | }

 895 | /// # Panics
 896 | ///
 897 | /// Panics if the application fails to run.
 898 | pub fn run_ui(
 899 |     state: &Result<std::sync::Arc<AppState>, String>,
 900 |     progress_rx: mpsc::Receiver<ProgressEvent>,
 901 | ) {
 902 |     let state_clone = state.clone();
 903 |     let progress_rx = Arc::new(Mutex::new(Some(progress_rx)));
 904 |     if let Err(e) = iced::application(
 905 |         move || {
 906 |             let rx = progress_rx.lock().take();
 907 |             (App::new(state_clone.clone(), rx), Task::none())
 908 |         },
 909 |         update,
 910 |         view,
 911 |     )
 912 |     .title(app_title)
 913 |     .theme(app_theme)
 914 |     .subscription(subscription)
 915 |     .run()
 916 |     {
 917 |         tracing::error!("Iced application failed to run: {e}");
 918 |         panic!("Iced application failed to run: {e}");
 919 |     }
 920 | }

 937 |             .score(0.95)
 938 |             .maybe_title(Some(CompactString::from("My File")))

 941 |             .snippets(Vec::new())

 945 |         assert_eq!(fi.path, "C:\\path\\to\\file.txt");
 946 |         assert!((fi.score - 0.95).abs() < f32::EPSILON);
 947 |         assert_eq!(fi.extension.as_deref(), Some("txt"));
 948 |     }

  17 | /// Current schema version - bump this when schema changes
  18 | pub const SCHEMA_VERSION: &str = "1.3.0";
  19 | 
  20 | fn get_schema_version_path(index_path: &Path) -> PathBuf {
  21 |     index_path.join(".schema_version")
  22 | }
  23 | 
  24 | fn read_schema_version(index_path: &Path) -> Option<String> {
  25 |     std::fs::read_to_string(get_schema_version_path(index_path))
  26 |         .ok()
  27 |         .map(|s| s.trim().to_string())
  28 | }
  29 | 
  30 | fn write_schema_version(index_path: &Path, version: &str) -> Result<()> {
  31 |     std::fs::write(get_schema_version_path(index_path), version)
  32 |         .map_err(|e| FlashError::Io(std::sync::Arc::new(e)))
  33 | }
  34 | 
  35 | /// Central manager for the Tantivy search index
  36 | pub struct IndexManager {
  37 |     #[allow(dead_code)]
  38 |     index: Index,
  39 |     writer: IndexWriterManager,
  40 |     searcher: Arc<IndexSearcher>,
  41 | }
  42 | 
  43 | impl IndexManager {
  44 |     fn rebuild_index_internal(index_path: &Path) -> Result<()> {
  45 |         // Try to backup the index before destroying it
  46 |         let backup_path = index_path.with_extension("backup");
  47 |         if let Err(e) = std::fs::remove_dir_all(&backup_path)
  48 |             && e.kind() != std::io::ErrorKind::NotFound
  49 |         {
  50 |             warn!("Failed to remove old backup at {:?}: {}", backup_path, e);
  51 |         }
  52 |         if let Err(e) = copy_dir(index_path, &backup_path) {
  53 |             warn!("Failed to backup index to {:?}: {}", backup_path, e);
  54 |         }
  55 | 
  56 |         if let Err(e) = std::fs::remove_dir_all(index_path) {
  57 |             error!(
  58 |                 "Failed to remove corrupted index at {:?}: {}",
  59 |                 index_path, e
  60 |             );
  61 |             return Err(FlashError::Io(std::sync::Arc::new(e)));
  62 |         }
  63 | 
  64 |         if let Err(e) = std::fs::create_dir_all(index_path) {
  65 |             error!(
  66 |                 "Failed to re-create index directory at {:?}: {}",
  67 |                 index_path, e
  68 |             );
  69 |             return Err(FlashError::Io(std::sync::Arc::new(e)));
  70 |         }
  71 |         write_schema_version(index_path, SCHEMA_VERSION)?;
  72 |         Ok(())
  73 |     }
  74 | 
  75 |     /// Open or create index at the specified path
  76 |     pub fn open(index_path: &Path, memory_limit_mb: u32) -> Result<Self> {
  77 |         let schema = create_schema();
  78 | 
  79 |         // Ensure directory exists
  80 |         if !index_path.exists() {
  81 |             std::fs::create_dir_all(index_path)
  82 |                 .map_err(|e| FlashError::Io(std::sync::Arc::new(e)))?;
  83 |         }
  84 | 
  85 |         // Check schema version - if mismatch, rebuild index
  86 |         let stored_version = read_schema_version(index_path);
  87 |         if let Some(ref ver) = stored_version {
  88 |             if ver != SCHEMA_VERSION {
  89 |                 warn!(
  90 |                     "Schema version mismatch: stored={}, current={}. Rebuilding index...",
  91 |                     ver, SCHEMA_VERSION
  92 |                 );
  93 |                 Self::rebuild_index_internal(index_path)?;
  94 |             }
  95 |         } else if index_path.join("meta.json").exists() {
  96 |             // Old index without version - rebuild
  97 |             warn!("No schema version found. Rebuilding index...");
  98 |             Self::rebuild_index_internal(index_path)?;
  99 |         } else {
 100 |             // New index - write version
 101 |             write_schema_version(index_path, SCHEMA_VERSION)?;
 102 |         }
 103 | 
 104 |         let directory = MmapDirectory::open(index_path)
 105 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::index(format!("Failed to open index directory: {e}")))?;
 106 | 
 107 |         let index = match Index::open_or_create(directory, schema.clone()) {
 108 |             Ok(idx) => idx,
 109 |             Err(e) => {
 110 |                 // Check if it's a schema mismatch error
 111 |                 let err_str = e.to_string();
 112 |                 if err_str.contains("Schema error") || err_str.contains("Inconsistent") {
 113 |                     warn!(
 114 |                         "Tantivy detected schema mismatch: {}. Forcing index rebuild...",
 115 |                         err_str
 116 |                     );
 117 | 
 118 |                     Self::rebuild_index_internal(index_path)?;
 119 | 
 120 |                     let new_directory = MmapDirectory::open(index_path).map_err(|e| {
 121 |                         FlashError::index(format!("Failed to re-open index directory: {e}"))
 122 |                     })?;
 123 |                     Index::open_or_create(new_directory, schema).map_err(|e| {
 124 |                         FlashError::index(format!("Failed to create new index after reset: {e}"))
 125 |                     })?
 126 |                 } else {
 127 |                     return Err(FlashError::index(format!(
 128 |                         "Failed to open or create index: {e}"
 129 |                     )));
 130 |                 }
 131 |             }
 132 |         };
 133 | 
 134 |         info!(
 135 |             "Opened index at {} with schema version {}",
 136 |             index_path.display(),
 137 |             SCHEMA_VERSION
 138 |         );
 139 | 
 140 |         let writer = IndexWriterManager::new(&index, memory_limit_mb)?;
 141 |         let searcher = IndexSearcher::new(&index, index_path.to_path_buf())?;
 142 | 
 143 |         Ok(Self {
 144 |             index,
 145 |             writer,
 146 |             searcher: Arc::new(searcher),
 147 |         })
 148 |     }
 149 |

 203 | 
 204 | fn copy_dir(src: &Path, dst: &Path) -> std::io::Result<()> {
 205 |     std::fs::create_dir_all(dst)?;
 206 |     for entry in ignore::WalkBuilder::new(src)
 207 |         .hidden(false)
 208 |         .git_ignore(false)
 209 |         .ignore(false)
 210 |         .parents(false)
 211 |         .build()
 212 |         .skip(1)
 213 |     {
 214 |         let entry = entry.map_err(std::io::Error::other)?;
 215 |         let ty = entry.file_type().ok_or_else(|| {
 216 |             std::io::Error::new(std::io::ErrorKind::NotFound, "Could not get file type")
 217 |         })?;
 218 |         let path = entry.path();
 219 |         let relative = path.strip_prefix(src).map_err(std::io::Error::other)?;
 220 |         let target = dst.join(relative);
 221 |         if ty.is_dir() {
 222 |             std::fs::create_dir_all(target)?;
 223 |         } else {
 224 |             std::fs::copy(path, target)?;
 225 |         }
 226 |     }
 227 |     Ok(())
 228 | }

  88 |                 error!("Failed to open filename index: {}", e);
  89 |                 None
  90 |             }
  91 |         };
  92 | 
  93 |     // Initialize watcher
  94 |     let watcher = watcher::WatcherManager::new(
  95 |         indexer_shared.clone(),
  96 |         metadata_db_shared.clone(),
  97 |         settings.get_allowed_extensions().clone(),
  98 |     );
  99 | 
 100 |     let (progress_tx, progress_rx) = tokio::sync::mpsc::channel(100);
 101 | 
 102 |     let scanner = Arc::new(crate::scanner::Scanner::new(
 103 |         indexer_shared.clone(),
 104 |         metadata_db_shared.clone(),
 105 |         filename_index.clone(),
 106 |         Some(progress_tx.clone()),
 107 |         settings,
 108 |     ));
 109 | 
 110 |     let state = Arc::new(
 111 |         AppState::builder()
 112 |             .indexer(indexer_shared)
 113 |             .metadata_db(metadata_db_shared)
 114 |             .settings_manager(settings_manager)
 115 |             .watcher(watcher)
 116 |             .maybe_filename_index(filename_index)
 117 |             .progress_tx(progress_tx)
 118 |             .scanner(scanner)
 119 |             .build(),
 120 |     );
 121 | 
 122 |     Ok((state, progress_rx))
 123 | }
 124 | 
 125 | /// Main entry point for the Iced GUI
 126 | ///
 127 | /// # Errors
 128 | ///
 129 | /// Returns a `FlashError` if the GUI fails to initialize or run.
 130 | pub fn run_ui() -> std::result::Result<(), FlashError> {
 131 |     let (state_res, rx) = match setup_app() {
 132 |         Ok((state, rx)) => (Ok(state), rx),
 133 |         Err(e) => (Err(e.to_string()), tokio::sync::mpsc::channel(1).1),
 134 |     };
 135 | 
 136 |     iced_ui::run_ui(&state_res, rx);
 137 |     Ok(())
 138 | }
 139 | 
 140 | pub async fn run_cli(
 141 |     query: Option<String>,
 142 |     is_json: bool,
 143 |     _index_path: Option<String>,
 144 | ) -> crate::error::Result<()> {
 145 |     if let Some(query_str) = query {
 146 |         let (state, _) = setup_app()?;
 147 |         let results = state
 148 |             .indexer
 149 |             .search(
 150 |                 SearchParams::builder()
 151 |                     .query(&query_str)
 152 |                     .limit(20)
 153 |                     .case_sensitive(false)
 154 |                     .build(),
 155 |             )
 156 |             .await?;
 157 | 
 158 |         if is_json {
 159 |             let json_results: Vec<serde_json::Value> = results
 160 |                 .into_iter()
 161 |                 .map(|res| {
 162 |                     serde_json::json!({
 163 |                         "score": res.score,
 164 |                         "path": res.file_path,
 165 |                         "title": res.title
 166 |                     })
 167 |                 })
 168 |                 .collect();
 169 |             println!(
 170 |                 "{}",
 171 |                 serde_json::to_string_pretty(&json_results).unwrap_or_default()
 172 |             );
 173 |         } else {
 174 |             for res in results {
 175 |                 println!("{} | {}", res.score, res.file_path);
 176 |             }
 177 |         }
 178 |     } else {
 179 |         println!("Usage: flash-search --cli <query> [--json]");
 180 |     }
 181 |     Ok(())
 182 | }

  43 | fn prune_old_logs(log_dir: &std::path::Path) {
  44 |     let thirty_days_ago =
  45 |         std::time::SystemTime::now() - std::time::Duration::from_secs(30 * 24 * 3600);
  46 | 
  47 |     if let Ok(entries) = std::fs::read_dir(log_dir) {
  48 |         for entry in entries.flatten() {
  49 |             if let Ok(metadata) = entry.metadata()
  50 |                 && let Ok(modified) = metadata.modified()
  51 |                 && modified < thirty_days_ago
  52 |             {
  53 |                 let _ = std::fs::remove_file(entry.path());
  54 |             }
  55 |         }
  56 |     }
  57 | }

  84 | fn main() {
  85 |     let app_dir = dirs::data_local_dir()
  86 |         .unwrap_or_else(|| std::path::PathBuf::from("."))
  87 |         .join("com.flashsearch");
  88 |     std::fs::create_dir_all(&app_dir).ok();
  89 |     let lock_path = app_dir.join("app.lock");
  90 | 
  91 |     let lock_file = match std::fs::OpenOptions::new()
  92 |         .write(true)
  93 |         .create(true)
  94 |         .truncate(true)
  95 |         .open(&lock_path)
  96 |     {
  97 |         Ok(file) => file,
  98 |         Err(e) => {
  99 |             eprintln!(
 100 |                 "Error: Failed to open lock file at {}.",
 101 |                 lock_path.display()
 102 |             );
 103 |             eprintln!("Details: {e}");
 104 |             std::process::exit(1);
 105 |         }
 106 |     };
 107 | 
 108 |     let mut lock = fd_lock::RwLock::new(lock_file);
 109 |     if lock.try_write().is_err() {
 110 |         // App is already running - just exit
 111 |         // In a real app, we might want to signal the existing instance to show itself
 112 |         std::process::exit(0);
 113 |     }
 114 | 
 115 |     init_logging(&app_dir);
 116 | 
 117 |     let rt = tokio::runtime::Builder::new_multi_thread()
 118 |         .enable_all()
 119 |         .build()
 120 |         .expect("Failed to create tokio runtime");
 121 | 
 122 |     let _guard = rt.enter();
 123 | 
 124 |     spawn_update_checker();
 125 | 
 126 |     // Set up graceful shutdown
 127 |     ctrlc::set_handler(|| {
 128 |         info!("Shutdown signal received, committing index...");
 129 |         flash_search::SHUTDOWN_FLAG.store(true, Ordering::SeqCst);
 130 |     })
 131 |     .expect("Error setting Ctrl-C handler");
 132 | 
 133 |     // Run the UI
 134 |     if let Err(e) = flash_search::run_ui() {
 135 |         error!("Application error: {}", e);
 136 |         std::process::exit(1);
 137 |     }

   1 | use crate::error::{FlashError, Result};
   2 | use std::path::{Path, PathBuf};
   3 | 
   4 | pub mod memory_map;
   5 | 
   6 | use compact_str::CompactString;
   7 | 
   8 | #[derive(Debug, Clone, serde::Serialize, serde::Deserialize)]
   9 | pub struct ParsedDocument {
  10 |     pub path: String,
  11 |     pub content: String,
  12 |     pub title: Option<CompactString>,
  13 |     pub language: Option<CompactString>,
  14 |     pub keywords: Option<String>,
  15 |     pub layout: Option<String>,
  16 |     pub code_metadata: Option<String>,
  17 |     pub embeddings: Option<Vec<f32>>,
  18 | }
  19 | 
  20 | /// Detect file type and route to appropriate parser using Kreuzberg
  21 | pub fn parse_file(path: &Path) -> Result<ParsedDocument> {
  22 |     // Log the file extension for debugging
  23 |     let extension = path.extension().and_then(|e| e.to_str()).unwrap_or("none");
  24 |     tracing::debug!(
  25 |         "Parsing file: {} (extension: {})",
  26 |         path.display(),
  27 |         extension
  28 |     );
  29 | 
  30 |     let mime = kreuzberg::detect_mime_type(path, true).ok();
  31 | 
  32 |     // Disable cache to prevent unbounded memory growth during deep directory scans.
  33 |     let config = kreuzberg::ExtractionConfig {
  34 |         use_cache: false,
  35 |         ..Default::default()
  36 |     };
  37 | 
  38 |     let result = kreuzberg::extract_file_sync(path, mime.as_deref(), &config).map_err(|e| {
  39 |         tracing::error!("Failed to extract file {}: {}", path.display(), e);
  40 |         FlashError::parse(path, format!("Extraction failed: {e}"))
  41 |     })?;
  42 | 
  43 |     tracing::debug!("Successfully parsed file: {}", path.display());
  44 | 
  45 |     Ok(map_extraction_result(path, result))
  46 | }
  47 | 
  48 | /// Process a batch of files using Kreuzberg's native async concurrent batch extraction.
  49 | ///
  50 | /// This is `async` — it must be called from within a Tokio async context. Kreuzberg
  51 | /// manages its own semaphore-gated `JoinSet` internally, scaling concurrency to
  52 | /// `(num_cpus * 1.5).ceil()` by default — no manual Rayon pools needed.
  53 | pub async fn parse_files_batch(paths: &[PathBuf]) -> Result<Vec<Result<ParsedDocument>>> {
  54 |     tracing::debug!("Async batch parsing {} files via kreuzberg", paths.len());
  55 | 
  56 |     let config = kreuzberg::ExtractionConfig {
  57 |         use_cache: false,
  58 |         ..Default::default()
  59 |     };
  60 | 
  61 |     let batched_paths: Vec<(PathBuf, Option<kreuzberg::FileExtractionConfig>)> =
  62 |         paths.iter().map(|p| (p.clone(), None)).collect();
  63 | 
  64 |     let batch_results = kreuzberg::batch_extract_file(batched_paths, &config)
  65 |         .await
  66 |         .map_err(|e| {
  67 |             tracing::error!("Kreuzberg async batch extraction failed entirely: {}", e);
  68 |             FlashError::parse(Path::new("batch"), format!("Batch extraction crashed: {e}"))
  69 |         })?;
  70 | 
  71 |     let results = batch_results
  72 |         .into_iter()
  73 |         .zip(paths.iter())
  74 |         .map(|(extraction_result, path)| Ok(map_extraction_result(path, extraction_result)))
  75 |         .collect();
  76 | 
  77 |     Ok(results)
  78 | }
  79 | 
  80 | /// Maps a `kreuzberg::ExtractionResult` into a `ParsedDocument`.
  81 | fn map_extraction_result(path: &Path, result: kreuzberg::ExtractionResult) -> ParsedDocument {
  82 |     let language = result
  83 |         .detected_languages
  84 |         .as_ref()
  85 |         .and_then(|langs| langs.first().map(CompactString::from));
  86 | 
  87 |     let keywords = result.extracted_keywords.as_ref().map(|kws| {
  88 |         kws.iter()
  89 |             .map(|k| k.text.as_str())
  90 |             .collect::<Vec<_>>()
  91 |             .join(" ")
  92 |     });
  93 | 
  94 |     ParsedDocument {
  95 |         path: path.to_string_lossy().to_string(),
  96 |         content: result.content,
  97 |         title: result.metadata.title.map(CompactString::from),
  98 |         language,
  99 |         keywords,
 100 |         layout: result.structured_output.map(|l| format!("{l:?}")),
 101 |         code_metadata: result.annotations.map(|c| format!("{c:?}")),
 102 |         embeddings: result
 103 |             .chunks
 104 |             .and_then(|c| c.into_iter().find_map(|chunk| chunk.embedding)),
 105 |     }
 106 | }
 107 |

```rust
   1 | pub mod drive_scanner;
   2 | 
   3 | use crate::error::Result;
   4 | use crate::indexer::IndexManager;
   5 | use crate::metadata::MetadataDb;
   6 | use crate::parsers::{ParsedDocument, parse_file};
   7 | use blake3;

  10 | use std::sync::Arc;
  11 | use std::sync::atomic::AtomicUsize;
  12 | use std::sync::atomic::Ordering;
  13 | use std::time::Instant;
  14 | use tokio::sync::mpsc;
  15 | use tracing::{info, instrument, warn};
  16 | 
  17 | #[derive(Clone, Debug, serde::Serialize)]
  18 | pub enum ProgressType {
  19 |     Content,
  20 |     Filename,
  21 | }
  22 | 
  23 | #[derive(Clone, Debug, serde::Serialize)]
  24 | pub struct ProgressEvent {
  25 |     pub total: usize,
  26 |     pub processed: usize,
  27 |     pub current_file: String,
  28 |     pub status: String,
  29 |     pub ptype: ProgressType,
  30 |     pub files_per_second: f64,
  31 |     pub eta_seconds: u64,
  32 |     pub current_folder: String,
  33 | }

  35 | const BATCH_SIZE: usize = 1000;
  36 | 
  37 | #[derive(Debug)]
  38 | struct IndexTask {
  39 |     doc: ParsedDocument,
  40 |     modified: u64,
  41 |     size: u64,
  42 |     content_hash: [u8; 32],
  43 | }

  57 |         metadata_db: Arc<MetadataDb>,
  58 |         filename_index: Option<Arc<crate::indexer::filename_index::FilenameIndex>>,

  71 |     fn get_scanner() -> Box<dyn DriveScanner> {
  72 |         #[cfg(target_os = "windows")]
  73 |         {
  74 |             Box::new(drive_scanner::WindowsDriveScanner)
  75 |         }
  76 |         #[cfg(target_os = "macos")]
  77 |         {
  78 |             Box::new(drive_scanner::MacDriveScanner)
  79 |         }
  80 |         #[cfg(target_os = "linux")]
  81 |         {
