```rust
  83 |         }
  84 |         #[cfg(not(any(target_os = "windows", target_os = "macos", target_os = "linux")))]
  85 |         {
  86 |             Box::new(drive_scanner::DefaultDriveScanner)
  87 |         }
  88 |     }
  89 | 
  90 |     #[instrument(skip(self, tx))]
  91 |     pub fn watch_drive(
  92 |         &self,
  93 |         root: PathBuf,
  94 |         tx: mpsc::Sender<(PathBuf, crate::watcher::WatcherAction)>,
  95 |     ) -> Result<()> {
  96 |         let scanner = Self::get_scanner();
  97 |         scanner.watch(root, tx)
  98 |     }
  99 | 
 100 |     fn process_writer_loop(
 101 |         task_rx: &crossbeam_channel::Receiver<IndexTask>,
 102 |         filename_index: Option<&Arc<crate::indexer::filename_index::FilenameIndex>>,
 103 |         indexer: &Arc<IndexManager>,
 104 |         metadata_db: &Arc<MetadataDb>,
 105 |         progress_tx: Option<&mpsc::Sender<ProgressEvent>>,
 106 |         total_files: &Arc<AtomicUsize>,
 107 |     ) {
 108 |         info!("Stage 2b: Batch Writing");
 109 |         let start = Instant::now();
 110 |         let mut doc_batch: Vec<(crate::parsers::ParsedDocument, u64, u64)> =
 111 |             Vec::with_capacity(BATCH_SIZE);
 112 |         let mut meta_batch: Vec<(String, u64, u64, [u8; 32])> = Vec::with_capacity(BATCH_SIZE);
 113 |         let mut processed: usize = 0;
 114 | 
 115 |         for task in task_rx {
 116 |             // Add to filename index
 117 |             if let Some(f_index) = filename_index {
 118 |                 let path = std::path::Path::new(&task.doc.path);
 119 |                 if let Some(name) = path.file_name().and_then(|n| n.to_str()) {
 120 |                     let _ = f_index.add_file(&task.doc.path, name);
 121 |                 }
 122 |             }
 123 | 
 124 |             // Clone path before moving doc
 125 |             let doc_path = task.doc.path.clone();
 126 |             doc_batch.push((task.doc, task.modified, task.size));
 127 |             meta_batch.push((doc_path, task.modified, task.size, task.content_hash));
 128 |             processed += 1;
 129 | 
 130 |             // Flush batch when full
 131 |             if doc_batch.len() >= BATCH_SIZE {
 132 |                 let _ = indexer.add_documents_batch(&doc_batch);
 133 |                 let _ = indexer.commit();
 134 |                 indexer.invalidate_cache();
 135 |                 let _ = metadata_db.batch_update_metadata(&meta_batch);
 136 |                 doc_batch.clear();
 137 |                 meta_batch.clear();
 138 |             }
 139 | 
 140 |             // Progress update
 141 |             if processed.is_multiple_of(10) {
 142 |                 let current_total = total_files.load(Ordering::Relaxed);
 143 |                 let elapsed = start.elapsed().as_secs_f64();
 144 |                 let rate = if elapsed > 0.0 {
 145 |                     processed as f64 / elapsed
 146 |                 } else {
 147 |                     0.0
 148 |                 };
 149 | 
 150 |                 // Batch summary every 1000 files
 151 |                 if processed.is_multiple_of(1000) {
 152 |                     info!(
 153 |                         "Indexed {} / {} files ({:.1} files/s)",
 154 |                         processed, current_total, rate
 155 |                     );
 156 |                 }
 157 | 
 158 |                 if let Some(tx) = progress_tx {
 159 |                     let _ = tx.try_send(ProgressEvent {
 160 |                         ptype: ProgressType::Content,
 161 |                         current_file: String::new(),
 162 |                         current_folder: String::new(),
 163 |                         processed,
 164 |                         total: current_total,
 165 |                         status: "Indexing contents...".to_string(),
 166 |                         eta_seconds: if rate > 0.0 {
 167 |                             #[allow(clippy::cast_possible_truncation, clippy::cast_sign_loss)]
 168 |                             {
 169 |                                 (current_total.saturating_sub(processed) as f64 / rate).round()
 170 |                                     as u64
 171 |                             }
 172 |                         } else {
 173 |                             0
 174 |                         },
 175 |                         files_per_second: rate,
 176 |                     });
 177 |                 }
 178 |             }
 179 |         }
 180 | 
 181 |         // Flush remaining items (B1: always commit at end)
 182 |         if !doc_batch.is_empty() {
 183 |             let _ = indexer.add_documents_batch(&doc_batch);
 184 |             let _ = indexer.commit();
 185 |             indexer.invalidate_cache();
 186 |             let _ = metadata_db.batch_update_metadata(&meta_batch);
 187 |         }
 188 | 
 189 |         // Final progress
 190 |         if let Some(tx) = progress_tx {
 191 |             let _ = tx.try_send(ProgressEvent {
 192 |                 ptype: ProgressType::Content,
 193 |                 current_file: String::new(),
 194 |                 current_folder: String::new(),
 195 |                 processed,
 196 |                 total: processed,
 197 |                 status: "All files indexed".to_string(),
 198 |                 eta_seconds: 0,
 199 |                 files_per_second: 0.0,
 200 |             });
 201 |         }
 202 | 
 203 |         info!(
 204 |             "Indexed {} files in {:.2}s",
 205 |             processed,
 206 |             start.elapsed().as_secs_f64()
 207 |         );
 208 |     }
 209 | 
 210 |     #[allow(clippy::too_many_lines)]
 211 |     #[instrument(skip(self, exclude_patterns), fields(root = %root.display()))]
 212 |     pub async fn scan_directory(&self, root: PathBuf, exclude_patterns: Vec<String>) -> Result<()> {
 213 |         info!("Starting directory scan for {}", root.display());
 214 | 
 215 |         let (path_tx, path_rx) = crossbeam_channel::unbounded::<PathBuf>();
 216 | 
 217 |         let root_clone = root.clone();
 218 |         let tx_clone = self.progress_tx.clone();
 219 |         let scanner = Self::get_scanner();
 220 |         let total = Arc::new(AtomicUsize::new(0));
 221 |         let total_for_scan = total.clone();
 222 | 
 223 |         let walker_handle = tokio::task::spawn_blocking(move || {
 224 |             scanner.scan(
 225 |                 root_clone,
 226 |                 exclude_patterns,
 227 |                 path_tx,
 228 |                 tx_clone,
 229 |                 total_for_scan,
 230 |             )
 231 |         });
 232 | 
 233 |         // --- Stage 2: Content Indexing (Async Batched) ---
 234 |         //
 235 |         // Architecture:
 236 |         //   - path_rx (crossbeam, sync) is drained in a spawn_blocking task.
 237 |         //   - Valid, filtered file paths are grouped into chunks of CHUNK_SIZE and
 238 |         //     sent through an async mpsc channel (chunk_tx -> chunk_rx).
 239 |         //   - An async Tokio task receives chunks and awaits parse_files_batch(),
 240 |         //     which uses kreuzberg's native JoinSet-based concurrency internally —
 241 |         //     no manual Rayon pool needed.
 242 |         //   - Parsed IndexTasks are forwarded to a sync writer via crossbeam.
 243 |         const CHUNK_SIZE: usize = 200;
 244 | 
 245 |         let (task_tx, task_rx) = crossbeam_channel::bounded::<IndexTask>(BATCH_SIZE * 8);
 246 |         // Async channel for sending path-chunks from the blocking walker to the async parser.
 247 |         let (chunk_tx, mut chunk_rx) = tokio::sync::mpsc::channel::<Vec<(PathBuf, u64, u64)>>(32);
 248 | 
 249 |         let metadata_db_for_filter = self.metadata_db.clone();
 250 |         let metadata_db_for_writer = self.metadata_db.clone();
 251 |         let indexer_clone = self.indexer.clone();
 252 |         let filename_index_clone = self.filename_index.clone();
 253 |         let progress_tx_clone = self.progress_tx.clone();
 254 |         let total_files = total.clone();
 255 | 
 256 |         let file_size_limit_mb = self.settings.index_file_size_limit_mb;
 257 |         let allowed_extensions: Arc<std::collections::HashSet<String>> = Arc::new(
 258 |             self.settings
 259 |                 .get_allowed_extensions()
 260 |                 .iter()
 261 |                 .map(|e| e.to_lowercase())
 262 |                 .collect(),
 263 |         );
 264 | 
 265 |         // --- Stage 2a: Blocking path receiver + filter ---
 266 |         // Drains path_rx (crossbeam), applies extension/size/metadata filters,
 267 |         // checks the metadata DB for staleness, then sends chunks over chunk_tx.
 268 |         let filter_handle = tokio::task::spawn_blocking(move || {
 269 |             info!("Stage 2a: Path filtering and chunking");
 270 |             let limit_bytes = u64::from(file_size_limit_mb) * 1024 * 1024;
 271 |             let mut chunk: Vec<(PathBuf, u64, u64)> = Vec::with_capacity(CHUNK_SIZE);
 272 | 
 273 |             for path in path_rx {
 274 |                 // Extension filter
 275 |                 let Some(ext) = path.extension().and_then(|e| e.to_str()) else {
 276 |                     continue;
 277 |                 };
 278 |                 if !allowed_extensions.contains(&ext.to_ascii_lowercase()) {
 279 |                     continue;
 280 |                 }
 281 | 
 282 |                 // Stat the file
 283 |                 let Ok(meta) = std::fs::metadata(&path) else {
 284 |                     continue;
 285 |                 };
 286 |                 let size = meta.len();
 287 |                 if size > limit_bytes {
 288 |                     warn!(
 289 |                         "Skipping large file: {} ({} bytes > {} bytes limit)",
 290 |                         path.display(),
 291 |                         size,
 292 |                         limit_bytes
 293 |                     );
 294 |                     continue;
 295 |                 }
 296 |                 let modified = meta
 297 |                     .modified()
 298 |                     .unwrap_or(std::time::SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH)
 299 |                     .duration_since(std::time::SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH)
 300 |                     .unwrap_or_default()
 301 |                     .as_secs();
 302 | 
 303 |                 chunk.push((path, modified, size));
 304 | 
 305 |                 if chunk.len() >= CHUNK_SIZE {
 306 |                     // Batch-check staleness against the metadata DB before sending.
 307 |                     let entries: Vec<_> = chunk
 308 |                         .iter()
 309 |                         .map(|(p, m, s)| (p.to_string_lossy().to_string(), *m, *s))
 310 |                         .collect();
 311 |                     let needs: Vec<bool> = metadata_db_for_filter
 312 |                         .batch_needs_reindex(&entries)
 313 |                         .unwrap_or_else(|_| vec![true; entries.len()]);
 314 |                     let current_chunk = std::mem::take(&mut chunk);
 315 |                     let stale: Vec<_> = current_chunk
 316 |                         .into_iter()
 317 |                         .zip(needs)
 318 |                         .filter_map(|(item, need)| need.then_some(item))
 319 |                         .collect();
 320 |                     if !stale.is_empty() {
 321 |                         let _ = chunk_tx.blocking_send(stale);
 322 |                     }
 323 |                     chunk.clear();
 324 |                 }
 325 |             }
 326 | 
 327 |             // Flush remainder
 328 |             if !chunk.is_empty() {
 329 |                 let entries: Vec<_> = chunk
 330 |                     .iter()
 331 |                     .map(|(p, m, s)| (p.to_string_lossy().to_string(), *m, *s))
 332 |                     .collect();
 333 |                 let needs: Vec<bool> = metadata_db_for_filter
 334 |                     .batch_needs_reindex(&entries)
 335 |                     .unwrap_or_else(|_| vec![true; entries.len()]);
 336 |                 let stale: Vec<_> = chunk
 337 |                     .into_iter()
 338 |                     .zip(needs)
 339 |                     .filter_map(|(item, need)| need.then_some(item))
 340 |                     .collect();
 341 |                 if !stale.is_empty() {
 342 |                     let _ = chunk_tx.blocking_send(stale);
 343 |                 }
 344 |             }
 345 |             // chunk_tx drops here, closing chunk_rx.
 346 |         });
 347 | 
 348 |         // --- Stage 2b: Async Kreuzberg batch parser ---
 349 |         // Receives chunks over the mpsc channel and awaits kreuzberg's native
 350 |         // concurrent JoinSet-based batch extractor directly on the Tokio runtime.
 351 |         let task_tx_for_parser = task_tx.clone();
 352 |         let parser_handle = tokio::spawn(async move {
 353 |             info!("Stage 2b: Async Kreuzberg batch parsing");
 354 |             while let Some(chunk) = chunk_rx.recv().await {
 355 |                 let just_paths: Vec<PathBuf> = chunk.iter().map(|(p, _, _)| p.clone()).collect();
 356 | 
 357 |                 match crate::parsers::parse_files_batch(&just_paths).await {
 358 |                     Ok(results) => {
 359 |                         for (parsed_res, (path, modified, size)) in
 360 |                             results.into_iter().zip(chunk.into_iter())
 361 |                         {
 362 |                             match parsed_res {
 363 |                                 Ok(parsed) => {
 364 |                                     let content_hash =
 365 |                                         blake3::hash(parsed.content.as_bytes()).into();
 366 |                                     let _ = task_tx_for_parser.send(IndexTask {
 367 |                                         doc: parsed,
 368 |                                         modified,
 369 |                                         size,
 370 |                                         content_hash,
 371 |                                     });
 372 |                                 }
 373 |                                 Err(e) => {
 374 |                                     warn!("Failed to parse file {:?}: {}", path, e);
 375 |                                 }
 376 |                             }
 377 |                         }
 378 |                     }
 379 |                     Err(e) => {
 380 |                         // Batch-level crash: fall back to individual sync parsing.
 381 |                         warn!("Async batch crashed ({e}), falling back to per-file sync parsing");
 382 |                         for (path, modified, size) in chunk {
 383 |                             if let Ok(parsed) = parse_file(&path) {
 384 |                                 let content_hash = blake3::hash(parsed.content.as_bytes()).into();
 385 |                                 let _ = task_tx_for_parser.send(IndexTask {
 386 |                                     doc: parsed,
 387 |                                     modified,
 388 |                                     size,
 389 |                                     content_hash,
 390 |                                 });
 391 |                             } else {
 392 |                                 warn!("Failed to parse file {:?}", path);
 393 |                             }
 394 |                         }
 395 |                     }
 396 |                 }
 397 |             }
 398 |             // Drop task_tx clone so the writer sees EOF once filter also drops.
 399 |             drop(task_tx_for_parser);
 400 |         });
 401 | 
 402 |         // --- Stage 2c: Sequential batch writer (sync) ---
 403 |         // Tantivy writes must be sequential; this separate thread drains task_rx.
 404 |         let writer_handle = tokio::task::spawn_blocking(move || {
 405 |             Self::process_writer_loop(
 406 |                 &task_rx,
 407 |                 filename_index_clone.as_ref(),
 408 |                 &indexer_clone,
 409 |                 &metadata_db_for_writer,
 410 |                 progress_tx_clone.as_ref(),
 411 |                 &total_files,
 412 |             );
 413 |         });
 414 | 
 415 |         // Wait for all stages to complete
 416 |         walker_handle
 417 |             .await
 418 |             .map_err(|e| crate::error::FlashError::index(format!("Walk task failed: {e}")))?
 419 |             .map_err(|e| crate::error::FlashError::index(format!("Walk logic failed: {e}")))?;
 420 |         filter_handle
 421 |             .await
 422 |             .map_err(|e| crate::error::FlashError::index(format!("Filter task failed: {e}")))?;
 423 |         parser_handle
 424 |             .await
 425 |             .map_err(|e| crate::error::FlashError::index(format!("Parse task failed: {e}")))?;
 426 |         // Drop the original task_tx so the writer sees the channel close.
 427 |         drop(task_tx);
 428 |         writer_handle
 429 |             .await
 430 |             .map_err(|e| crate::error::FlashError::index(format!("Write task failed: {e}")))?;
 431 | 
 432 |         // Commit filename index to disk
 433 |         if let Some(f_index) = &self.filename_index {
 434 |             let _ = f_index.commit();
 435 |         }
 436 | 
 437 |         Ok(())
 438 |     }
 439 | }
 440 | 
 441 | #[cfg(test)]

 443 |     use super::*;
 444 |     use crate::indexer::IndexManager;
 445 |     use crate::metadata::MetadataDb;
 446 |     use crate::settings::AppSettings;
```

```rust
   1 | use std::io::Result;
   2 | 
   3 | fn main() -> Result<()> {
   4 |     #[cfg(windows)]
   5 |     {
   6 |         use std::path::Path;
   7 |         let icon_path = Path::new("assets/icon.ico");
   8 |         let logo_path = Path::new("assets/logo.png");
   9 | 
  10 |         // Generate icon if it doesn't exist (or is empty) and logo exists
  11 |         if (!icon_path.exists() || std::fs::metadata(icon_path).map_or(0, |m| m.len()) == 0)
  12 |             && logo_path.exists()
  13 |         {
  14 |             println!("cargo:warning=Generating icon from logo.png...");
  15 |             if let Ok(img) = image::open(logo_path) {
  16 |                 // Resize to 256x256 for a high-quality icon that isn't massive
  17 |                 let resized = img.resize(256, 256, image::imageops::FilterType::Lanczos3);
  18 |                 if let Err(e) = resized.save_with_format(icon_path, image::ImageFormat::Ico) {
  19 |                     println!("cargo:warning=Failed to save icon.ico: {e}");
  20 |                 } else {
  21 |                     println!("cargo:warning=Successfully generated icon.ico");
  22 |                 }
  23 |             } else {
  24 |                 println!("cargo:warning=Failed to open assets/logo.png");
  25 |             }
  26 |         }
  27 | 
  28 |         if icon_path.exists() && std::fs::metadata(icon_path).map_or(0, |m| m.len()) > 0 {
  29 |             let mut res = winres::WindowsResource::new();
  30 |             res.set_icon(icon_path.to_str().unwrap());
  31 |             res.compile()?;
  32 |         } else {
  33 |             println!("cargo:warning=No valid icon found at assets/icon.ico - skipping embedding");
  34 |         }
  35 |     }
  36 | 
  37 |     Ok(())
  38 | }
```

```rust
   1 | #[cfg(target_os = "windows")]
   2 | pub fn set_auto_start(enable: bool, app_name: &str, exe_path: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
   3 |     use winreg::RegKey;
   4 |     use winreg::enums::{HKEY_CURRENT_USER, KEY_ALL_ACCESS};
   5 | 
   6 |     let hkcu = RegKey::predef(HKEY_CURRENT_USER);
   7 |     let run_key = hkcu
   8 |         .open_subkey_with_flags(
   9 |             r"Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Run",
  10 |             KEY_ALL_ACCESS,
  11 |         )
  12 |         .map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
  13 | 
  14 |     if enable {
  15 |         run_key
  16 |             .set_value(app_name, &exe_path)
  17 |             .map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
  18 |     } else {
  19 |         let _ = run_key.delete_value(app_name);
  20 |     }
  21 |     Ok(())
  22 | }
  23 | 
  24 | #[cfg(target_os = "windows")]
  25 | pub fn is_auto_start_enabled(app_name: &str) -> Result<bool, String> {
  26 |     use winreg::RegKey;
  27 |     use winreg::enums::HKEY_CURRENT_USER;
  28 | 
  29 |     let hkcu = RegKey::predef(HKEY_CURRENT_USER);
  30 |     let run_key = hkcu
  31 |         .open_subkey(r"Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Run")
  32 |         .map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
  33 | 
  34 |     match run_key.get_value::<String, _>(app_name) {
  35 |         Ok(_) => Ok(true),
  36 |         Err(_) => Ok(false),
  37 |     }
  38 | }
  39 |

  44 |
```

```rust
   1 | use crate::commands::AppState;
   2 | use crate::indexer::searcher::IndexStatistics;
   3 | use crate::models::{IndexStatus, RecentFile};
   4 | use std::path::PathBuf;
   5 | use std::sync::Arc;
   6 | use tracing::error;
   7 | 
   8 | /// Starts the indexing process.
   9 | ///
  10 | /// # Errors
  11 | ///
  12 | /// Returns an error if the indexing task cannot be spawned or fails.
  13 | pub async fn start_indexing_internal(path: String, state: Arc<AppState>) -> Result<(), String> {
  14 |     let path = PathBuf::from(path);
  15 |     let mut handle_guard = state.indexing_handle.lock();
  16 | 
  17 |     // Abort previous indexing if still running
  18 |     if let Some(handle) = handle_guard.take() {
  19 |         handle.abort();
  20 |     }
  21 | 
  22 |     let state_clone = state.clone();
  23 |     let handle = tokio::spawn(async move {
  24 |         let settings = state_clone.settings_cache.load();
  25 |         let mut exclude_patterns = settings.exclude_patterns.clone();
  26 |         for folder in &settings.exclude_folders {
  27 |             exclude_patterns.push(folder.clone());
  28 |         }
  29 | 
  30 |         if let Err(e) = state_clone
  31 |             .scanner
  32 |             .scan_directory(path, exclude_patterns)
  33 |             .await
  34 |         {
  35 |             error!("Indexing error: {}", e);
  36 |         }
  37 |     });
  38 | 
  39 |     *handle_guard = Some(handle);
  40 |     drop(handle_guard);
  41 |     Ok(())
  42 | }
  43 | 
  44 | /// Gets the current status of the indexer.
  45 | ///
  46 | /// # Errors
  47 | ///
  48 | /// Returns an error if the index statistics cannot be retrieved.
  49 | pub async fn get_index_status_internal(state: &Arc<AppState>) -> Result<IndexStatus, String> {
  50 |     let is_running = {
  51 |         let mut handle_guard = state.indexing_handle.lock();
  52 |         let finished = handle_guard
  53 |             .as_ref()
  54 |             .is_some_and(tokio::task::JoinHandle::is_finished);
  55 |         if finished {
  56 |             *handle_guard = None;
  57 |             false
  58 |         } else {
  59 |             handle_guard.is_some()
  60 |         }
  61 |     };
  62 | 
  63 |     let status = if is_running {
  64 |         "indexing".to_string()
  65 |     } else {
  66 |         "idle".to_string()
  67 |     };
  68 | 
  69 |     let index_stats = state.indexer.get_statistics().map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
  70 | 
  71 |     Ok(IndexStatus {
  72 |         status,
  73 |         files_indexed: index_stats.total_documents,
  74 |     })
  75 | }
  76 | 
  77 | /// Gets the current index statistics.
  78 | ///
  79 | /// # Errors
  80 | ///
  81 | /// Returns an error if the indexer statistics are unavailable.
  82 | pub async fn get_index_statistics_internal(
  83 |     state: &Arc<AppState>,
  84 | ) -> Result<IndexStatistics, String> {
  85 |     state.indexer.get_statistics().map_err(|e| e.to_string())
  86 | }
  87 | 
  88 | /// Gets a list of recently indexed files.

  90 | /// # Errors

  92 | /// Returns an error if the database query fails.
  93 | pub async fn get_recent_files_internal(
```

```rust
   1 | use crate::commands::AppState;
   2 | use crate::indexer::searcher::{SearchParams, SearchResult};
   3 | use crate::models::{FilenameIndexStats, FilenameSearchResult, PreviewResult};

   7 | use std::time::Duration;
   8 | 
   9 | static PREVIEW_CACHE: OnceLock<Cache<(String, u64), String>> = OnceLock::new();
  10 | 
  11 | fn get_preview_cache() -> &'static Cache<(String, u64), String> {
  12 |     PREVIEW_CACHE.get_or_init(|| {
  13 |         Cache::builder()
  14 |             .max_capacity(100)
  15 |             .time_to_live(Duration::from_secs(600))
  16 |             .build()
  17 |     })
  18 | }
  19 | 
  20 | /// Performs a search query against the index.
  21 | ///
  22 | /// # Errors
  23 | ///
  24 | /// Returns an error if the search query fails.
  25 | pub async fn search_query_internal(
  26 |     params: SearchParams<'_>,
  27 |     state: &Arc<AppState>,
  28 | ) -> Result<Vec<SearchResult>, String> {
  29 |     state
  30 |         .indexer
  31 |         .search(params)
  32 |         .await
  33 |         .map_err(|e| e.to_string())
  34 | }
  35 | 
  36 | /// Gets a preview of the file content.
  37 | ///
  38 | /// # Errors
  39 | ///
  40 | /// Returns an error if the file cannot be read or parsed.
  41 | pub async fn get_file_preview_internal(path: String) -> Result<String, String> {
  42 |     let path_buf = std::path::PathBuf::from(&path);
  43 |     let modified = std::fs::metadata(&path_buf)
  44 |         .and_then(|m| m.modified())
  45 |         .map(|t| {
  46 |             t.duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)
  47 |                 .unwrap_or_default()
  48 |                 .as_secs()
  49 |         })
  50 |         .unwrap_or(0);
  51 | 
  52 |     let cache = get_preview_cache();
  53 |     let cache_key = (path.clone(), modified);
  54 | 
  55 |     if let Some(cached) = cache.get(&cache_key) {
  56 |         return Ok(cached);
  57 |     }
  58 | 
  59 |     let result = tokio::task::spawn_blocking(move || parse_file(&path_buf))
  60 |         .await
  61 |         .map_err(|e| format!("Preview task failed: {e}"))?;
  62 | 
  63 |     match result {
  64 |         Ok(doc) => {
  65 |             let content = doc.content[..std::cmp::min(doc.content.len(), 10000)].to_string();
  66 |             cache.insert(cache_key, content.clone());
  67 |             Ok(content)
  68 |         }
  69 |         Err(e) => Err(e.to_string()),
  70 |     }
  71 | }
  72 | 
  73 | /// Gets a highlighted preview of the file content.
  74 | ///
  75 | /// # Errors
  76 | ///
  77 | /// Returns an error if the preview generation fails.
  78 | pub async fn get_file_preview_highlighted_internal(
  79 |     path: String,
  80 |     query: String,
  81 |     state: &Arc<AppState>,
  82 | ) -> Result<PreviewResult, String> {
  83 |     use crate::indexer::query_parser::extract_highlight_terms;
  84 |     let case_sensitive = state.settings_cache.load().case_sensitive;
  85 |     let matched_terms = extract_highlight_terms(&query, case_sensitive);
  86 | 
  87 |     let content = get_file_preview_internal(path).await?;
  88 |     Ok(PreviewResult {
  89 |         content,
  90 |         matched_terms,
  91 |     })
  92 | }
  93 | 
  94 | /// Searches for filenames in the filename index.
  95 | ///
  96 | /// # Errors
  97 | ///
  98 | /// Returns an error if the filename index is not initialized or the search fails.
  99 | pub async fn search_filenames_internal(
 100 |     query: String,
 101 |     limit: usize,
 102 |     state: &Arc<AppState>,
 103 | ) -> Result<Vec<FilenameSearchResult>, String> {
 104 |     state.filename_index.as_ref().map_or_else(
 105 |         || Err("Filename index not initialized".to_string()),
 106 |         |filename_index| {
 107 |             filename_index
 108 |                 .search(&query, limit)
 109 |                 .map(|results| {
 110 |                     results
 111 |                         .into_iter()
 112 |                         .map(|r| FilenameSearchResult {
 113 |                             file_path: r.file_path,
 114 |                             file_name: r.file_name,
 115 |                         })
 116 |                         .collect()
 117 |                 })
 118 |                 .map_err(|e| e.to_string())
 119 |         },
 120 |     )
 121 | }
 122 | 
 123 | /// Gets statistics for the filename index.
 124 | ///
 125 | /// # Errors
 126 | ///
 127 | /// Returns an error if the filename index is not initialized or stats cannot be retrieved.
 128 | pub async fn get_filename_index_stats_internal(
 129 |     state: &Arc<AppState>,
 130 | ) -> Result<FilenameIndexStats, String> {
 131 |     if let Some(ref filename_index) = state.filename_index {
 132 |         let index_stats = filename_index.get_stats().map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
 133 |         Ok(FilenameIndexStats {
 134 |             total_files: index_stats.total_files,
 135 |             index_size_bytes: index_stats.index_size_bytes,
 136 |         })
 137 |     } else {
 138 |         Err("Filename index not initialized".to_string())
 139 |     }
 140 | }
```

```rust
  64 | pub fn add_search_history_internal(query: String, state: &Arc<AppState>) -> Result<(), String> {
  65 |     let mut cache = state.settings_cache.load().as_ref().clone();
  66 | 
  67 |     let mut history = cache.search_history.clone();
  68 | 
  69 |     let mut found = false;
  70 |     for item in &mut history {
  71 |         if item.query == query {
  72 |             item.frequency += 1;
  73 |             item.last_used = std::time::SystemTime::now()
  74 |                 .duration_since(std::time::SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH)
  75 |                 .unwrap_or_default()
  76 |                 .as_secs();
  77 |             found = true;
  78 |             break;
  79 |         }
  80 |     }
  81 | 
  82 |     if !found {
  83 |         history.insert(
  84 |             0,
  85 |             crate::settings::SearchHistoryItem {
  86 |                 query,
  87 |                 frequency: 1,
  88 |                 last_used: std::time::SystemTime::now()
  89 |                     .duration_since(std::time::SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH)
  90 |                     .unwrap_or_default()
  91 |                     .as_secs(),
  92 |             },
  93 |         );
  94 |     }
  95 | 
  96 |     history.sort_by(|a, b| b.frequency.cmp(&a.frequency));
  97 |     history.truncate(50);
  98 | 
  99 |     cache.search_history = history;
 100 |     state
 101 |         .settings_manager
 102 |         .save(&cache)
 103 |         .map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
 104 | 
 105 |     state.settings_cache.store(Arc::new(cache));
 106 |     Ok(())
 107 | }

 119 | pub fn pin_file_internal(path: String, state: &Arc<AppState>) -> Result<(), String> {
 120 |     let mut cache = state.settings_cache.load().as_ref().clone();
 121 | 
 122 |     if !cache.pinned_files.contains(&path) {
 123 |         cache.pinned_files.push(path);
 124 |         state
 125 |             .settings_manager
 126 |             .save(&cache)
 127 |             .map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
 128 |         state.settings_cache.store(Arc::new(cache));
 129 |     }
 130 |     Ok(())
 131 | }
```

```rust
   1 | use std::path::PathBuf;
   2 | use std::sync::Arc;
   3 | use thiserror::Error;
   4 | 
   5 | pub use anyhow::Context;
   6 | 
   7 | #[derive(Error, Debug, Clone)]
   8 | pub enum FlashError {
   9 |     #[error("IO error: {0}")]
  10 |     Io(Arc<std::io::Error>),
  11 | 
  12 |     #[error("Parse error in {path}: {cause}")]
  13 |     Parse { path: PathBuf, cause: String },
  14 | 
  15 |     #[error("Index error: {msg}")]
  16 |     Index { msg: String, field: Option<String> },
  17 | 
  18 |     #[error("Database error: {operation} on {key}: {cause}")]
  19 |     Database {
  20 |         operation: String,
  21 |         key: String,
  22 |         cause: String,
  23 |     },
  24 | 
  25 |     #[error("Unsupported file format: {format}")]
  26 |     UnsupportedFormat { format: String, extension: String },
  27 | 
  28 |     #[error("File corrupted or encrypted: {path}")]
  29 |     CorruptedFile { path: PathBuf, operation: String },
  30 | 
  31 |     #[error("Search error: query '{query}' failed: {cause}")]
  32 |     Search { query: String, cause: String },
  33 | 
  34 |     #[error("Config error: {key}: {cause}")]
  35 |     Config { key: String, cause: String },
  36 | 
  37 |     #[error("Archive error: {archive_type} - {operation}: {cause}")]
  38 |     Archive {
  39 |         archive_type: String,
  40 |         operation: String,
  41 |         cause: String,
  42 |     },
  43 | 
  44 |     #[error("Lock poisoned: {lock_name}")]
  45 |     PoisonedLock { lock_name: String },
  46 | 
  47 |     #[error("Not found: {resource} '{identifier}'")]
  48 |     NotFound {
  49 |         resource: String,
  50 |         identifier: String,
  51 |     },
  52 | }
  53 | 
  54 | impl From<std::io::Error> for FlashError {
  55 |     fn from(e: std::io::Error) -> Self {
  56 |         Self::Io(Arc::new(e))
  57 |     }
  58 | }
  59 | 
  60 | pub type Result<T> = std::result::Result<T, FlashError>;
  61 | 
  62 | // Helper constructors for common error patterns
  63 | impl FlashError {
  64 |     pub fn parse<P: Into<PathBuf>, S: Into<String>>(path: P, cause: S) -> Self {
  65 |         Self::Parse {
  66 |             path: path.into(),
  67 |             cause: cause.into(),
  68 |         }
  69 |     }
  70 | 
  71 |     pub fn index<S: Into<String>>(msg: S) -> Self {
  72 |         Self::Index {
  73 |             msg: msg.into(),
  74 |             field: None,
  75 |         }
  76 |     }
  77 | 
  78 |     pub fn index_field<S: Into<String>>(field: S, msg: S) -> Self {
  79 |         Self::Index {
  80 |             msg: msg.into(),
  81 |             field: Some(field.into()),
  82 |         }
  83 |     }
  84 |

  87 |             operation: operation.into(),
  88 |             key: key.into(),
  89 |             cause: cause.into(),
  90 |         }
  91 |     }
  92 |

  94 |         Self::UnsupportedFormat {
  95 |             format: format.into(),
  96 |             extension: extension.into(),
  97 |         }
  98 |     }
  99 | 
 100 |     pub fn corrupted_file<P: Into<PathBuf>, S: Into<String>>(path: P, operation: S) -> Self {
 101 |         Self::CorruptedFile {
 102 |             path: path.into(),
 103 |             operation: operation.into(),
 104 |         }
 105 |     }
 106 | 
 107 |     pub fn search<S1: Into<String>, S2: Into<String>>(query: S1, cause: S2) -> Self {
 108 |         Self::Search {
 109 |             query: query.into(),
 110 |             cause: cause.into(),
 111 |         }
 112 |     }
 113 | 
 114 |     pub fn config<S1: Into<String>, S2: Into<String>>(key: S1, cause: S2) -> Self {
 115 |         Self::Config {
 116 |             key: key.into(),
 117 |             cause: cause.into(),
 118 |         }
 119 |     }
 120 | 
 121 |     pub fn archive<S1: Into<String>, S2: Into<String>, S3: Into<String>>(
 122 |         archive_type: S1,
 123 |         operation: S2,
 124 |         cause: S3,
 125 |     ) -> Self {

 129 |             cause: cause.into(),
 130 |         }
 131 |     }
 132 |

 134 |         Self::PoisonedLock {
 135 |             lock_name: lock_name.into(),
 136 |         }
 137 |     }
 138 |

 142 |             identifier: identifier.into(),

 144 |     }
```

```rust
   1 | use iced::Element;
   2 | use iced::widget::{Text, text};
   3 | 
   4 | pub const FONT: iced::Font = iced::Font::with_name("lucide");
   5 | 
   6 | // Load the pre-built Lucide font from assets
   7 | pub const FONT_BYTES: &[u8] = include_bytes!("../../assets/lucide.ttf");
   8 | 
   9 | /// Icon name to Unicode character mapping for Lucide font
  10 | pub fn get_icon_char(name: &str) -> char {
  11 |     match name {
  12 |         "magnifying-glass" | "search" => '\u{e151}',
  13 |         "magnifying-glass-plus" => '\u{e1b6}',
  14 |         "magnifying-glass-minus" => '\u{e1b7}',
  15 |         "gear" | "settings" => '\u{e154}',
  16 |         "trash" => '\u{e18d}',
  17 |         "file" => '\u{e0c0}',
  18 |         "file-text" | "text" => '\u{e0cc}',
  19 |         "folder" => '\u{e0d7}',
  20 |         "folder-open" => '\u{e247}',
  21 |         "info" => '\u{e0f9}',
  22 |         "warning" => '\u{e193}',
  23 |         "check" => '\u{e06c}',
  24 |         "x" => '\u{e1b2}',
  25 |         "plus" => '\u{e13d}',
  26 |         "minus" => '\u{e11c}',
  27 |         "arrow-right" => '\u{e049}',
  28 |         "arrow-left" => '\u{e048}',
  29 |         "arrow-up" => '\u{e04a}',
  30 |         "arrow-down" => '\u{e042}',
  31 |         "download" => '\u{e0b2}',
  32 |         "copy" => '\u{e09e}',
  33 |         "database" => '\u{e0ad}',
  34 |         "star" => '\u{e176}',
  35 |         _ => {
  36 |             tracing::warn!("icon '{}' not found", name);
  37 |             '\u{003f}' // Question mark as fallback
  38 |         }
  39 |     }
  40 | }
  41 | 
  42 | /// Helper function to create an iced Text widget containing the given icon unicode.
  43 | #[must_use]
  44 | pub fn icon<'a>(name: &str) -> Text<'a> {
  45 |     text(get_icon_char(name).to_string()).font(FONT)
  46 | }
  47 | 
  48 | /// For the old `load_icon` helper signature
  49 | #[must_use]
  50 | pub fn load_icon<'a>(name: &str) -> Element<'a, super::Message> {
  51 |     icon(name).size(16).into()
  52 | }
  53 | 
  54 | #[must_use]
  55 | pub fn load_icon_size<'a>(name: &str, size: f32) -> Element<'a, super::Message> {
  56 |     icon(name).size(size).into()
  57 | }
```

```rust
  16 | 
  17 | fn get_syntax_set() -> &'static SyntaxSet {
  18 |     static SYNTAX_SET: OnceLock<SyntaxSet> = OnceLock::new();
  19 |     SYNTAX_SET.get_or_init(SyntaxSet::load_defaults_newlines)
  20 | }
  21 | 
  22 | fn get_theme_set() -> &'static ThemeSet {
  23 |     static THEME_SET: OnceLock<ThemeSet> = OnceLock::new();
  24 |     THEME_SET.get_or_init(ThemeSet::load_defaults)
  25 | }
  26 | 
  27 | fn render_code_preview<'a>(
  28 |     content: &'a str,
  29 |     extension: &str,
  30 |     is_dark: bool,
  31 | ) -> Element<'a, Message> {
  32 |     let ps = get_syntax_set();
  33 |     let ts = get_theme_set();
  34 | 
  35 |     let syntax = ps
  36 |         .find_syntax_by_extension(extension)
  37 |         .unwrap_or_else(|| ps.find_syntax_plain_text());
  38 | 
  39 |     let theme_name = if is_dark {
  40 |         "base16-ocean.dark"
  41 |     } else {
  42 |         "base16-ocean.light"
  43 |     };
  44 |     let theme = &ts.themes[theme_name];
  45 | 
  46 |     let mut h = HighlightLines::new(syntax, theme);
  47 |     let mut spans: Vec<iced::widget::text::Span<'a, Message>> = Vec::new();
  48 | 
  49 |     // Limit to first 1000 lines to prevent UI freezing on massive files
  50 |     for line in LinesWithEndings::from(content).take(1000) {
  51 |         if let Ok(ranges) = h.highlight_line(line, ps) {
  52 |             for (style, text) in ranges {
  53 |                 spans.push(
  54 |                     span(text)
  55 |                         .size(13)
  56 |                         .font(Font {
  57 |                             family: font::Family::Monospace,
  58 |                             ..Font::default()
  59 |                         })
  60 |                         .color(iced::Color::from_rgb8(
  61 |                             style.foreground.r,
  62 |                             style.foreground.g,
  63 |                             style.foreground.b,
  64 |                         )),
  65 |                 );
  66 |             }
  67 |         } else {
  68 |             spans.push(span(line).size(13).font(Font {
  69 |                 family: font::Family::Monospace,
  70 |                 ..Font::default()
  71 |             }));
  72 |         }
  73 |     }
  74 | 
  75 |     if spans.is_empty() {
  76 |         return text(content).size(13).into();
  77 |     }
  78 | 
  79 |     rich_text(spans).into()
  80 | }
  81 | 
  82 | pub fn search_view(app: &App) -> Element<'_, Message> {
  83 |     column![top_navigation(app), main_layout(app), status_bar(app),]
  84 |         .width(Length::Fill)
  85 |         .height(Length::Fill)
  86 |         .into()
  87 | }

  89 | fn top_navigation(app: &App) -> Element<'_, Message> {
  90 |     let logo = row![
  91 |         load_icon_size("search", 20.0),
  92 |         text("Flash Search").size(18).font(Font {
  93 |             weight: font::Weight::Bold,
  94 |             ..Font::default()
  95 |         }),
  96 |     ]
  97 |     .spacing(12)
  98 |     .align_y(Alignment::Center);
  99 | 
 100 |     let search_bar = container(
 101 |         row![
 102 |             TextInput::new("Type to search everything...", &app.search_query)
 103 |                 .id(crate::iced_ui::get_search_input_id())
 104 |                 .on_input(Message::SearchQueryChanged)
 105 |                 .on_submit(Message::SearchSubmitted)
 106 |                 .padding(Padding::new(12.0))
 107 |                 .size(16)
 108 |                 .style(theme::search_input())
 109 |                 .width(Length::Fill),
 110 |             if app.is_searching {
 111 |                 Element::from(
 112 |                     container(text("Searching...").size(12).style(theme::dim_text_style()))
 113 |                         .padding(Padding::new(12.0)),
 114 |                 )
 115 |             } else {
 116 |                 Element::from(
 117 |                     button(load_icon("arrow-right"))
 118 |                         .on_press(Message::SearchSubmitted)
 119 |                         .style(theme::search_button())
 120 |                         .padding(Padding::new(10.0)),
 121 |                 )
 122 |             }
 123 |         ]
 124 |         .spacing(8)
 125 |         .align_y(Alignment::Center),
 126 |     )
 127 |     .style(theme::input_container)
 128 |     .width(Length::FillPortion(2))
 129 |     .max_width(800.0);
 130 | 
 131 |     let menu_items = row![
 132 |         button(load_icon_size("settings", 18.0))
 133 |             .on_press(Message::TabChanged(Tab::Settings))
 134 |             .style(theme::ghost_button())
 135 |             .padding(10.0),
 136 |     ]
 137 |     .spacing(8);
 138 | 
 139 |     container(
 140 |         row![
 141 |             logo,
 142 |             Space::new().width(Length::Fill),
 143 |             search_bar,
 144 |             Space::new().width(Length::Fill),
 145 |             menu_items,
 146 |         ]
 147 |         .padding(Padding {
 148 |             top: 12.0,
 149 |             bottom: 12.0,
 150 |             left: 20.0,
 151 |             right: 20.0,
 152 |         })
 153 |         .align_y(Alignment::Center),
 154 |     )
 155 |     .style(theme::header_container)
 156 |     .width(Length::Fill)
 157 |     .into()
 158 | }

 160 | fn main_layout(app: &App) -> Element<'_, Message> {
 161 |     let sidebar = if app.sidebar_collapsed {
 162 |         collapsed_sidebar(app)
 163 |     } else {
 164 |         left_sidebar(app)
 165 |     };
 166 | 
 167 |     row![
 168 |         sidebar,
 169 |         column![
 170 |             filter_chips(app),
 171 |             row![
 172 |                 results_panel(app).width(Length::FillPortion(2)),
 173 |                 container(right_panel(app)).width(Length::FillPortion(3)),
 174 |             ]
 175 |             .height(Length::Fill)
 176 |         ]
 177 |         .width(Length::Fill),
 178 |     ]
 179 |     .width(Length::Fill)
 180 |     .height(Length::Fill)
 181 |     .into()
 182 | }

 184 | fn filter_chips(app: &App) -> Element<'_, Message> {
 185 |     if app.filter_extensions.is_empty() {
 186 |         return Space::new().height(0).into();
 187 |     }
 188 | 
 189 |     let mut chips_row = row![].spacing(8).padding(Padding {
 190 |         top: 8.0,
 191 |         bottom: 8.0,
 192 |         left: 16.0,
 193 |         right: 16.0,
 194 |     });
 195 | 
 196 |     for ext in &app.filter_extensions {
 197 |         let ext_clone = ext.clone();
 198 |         chips_row = chips_row.push(
 199 |             container(
 200 |                 row![
 201 |                     text(ext).size(12),
 202 |                     mouse_area(load_icon_size("x", 12.0))
 203 |                         .on_press(Message::ToggleFilterExtension(ext_clone))
 204 |                 ]
 205 |                 .spacing(8)
 206 |                 .align_y(Alignment::Center),
 207 |             )
 208 |             .padding(Padding::from([4, 8]))
 209 |             .style(theme::badge_container),
 210 |         );
 211 |     }
 212 | 
 213 |     container(chips_row)
 214 |         .width(Length::Fill)
 215 |         .style(theme::header_container)
 216 |         .into()
 217 | }

 369 | fn results_panel(app: &App) -> iced::widget::Container<'_, Message> {
 370 |     if app.results.is_empty() {
 371 |         let (icon, msg) = if app.search_query.is_empty() {
 372 |             ("search", "Type something to begin searching...")
 373 |         } else {
 374 |             ("warning", "No results found for your query.")
 375 |         };
 376 | 
 377 |         return container(
 378 |             column![
 379 |                 load_icon_size(icon, 48.0),
 380 |                 text(msg).size(18).style(theme::dim_text_style()),
 381 |             ]
 382 |             .spacing(16)
 383 |             .align_x(Alignment::Center),
 384 |         )
 385 |         .center_x(Length::Fill)
 386 |         .center_y(Length::Fill);
 387 |     }
 388 | 
 389 |     let results = scrollable(column(
 390 |         app.results
 391 |             .iter()
 392 |             .enumerate()
 393 |             .map(|(i, res)| result_item_view(app, i, res))
 394 |             .collect::<Vec<Element<Message>>>(),
 395 |     ))
 396 |     .height(Length::Fill);
 397 | 
 398 |     container(results).width(Length::Fill).height(Length::Fill)
 399 | }

 401 | #[allow(clippy::too_many_lines)]
 402 | fn result_item_view<'a>(app: &App, i: usize, res: &'a super::FileItem) -> Element<'a, Message> {
 403 |     let is_selected = app.selected_index == Some(i);
 404 |     let is_hovered = app.hovered_item_index == Some(i);
 405 | 
 406 |     let mut actions_row = row![].spacing(10);
 407 |     if is_hovered || is_selected {
 408 |         actions_row = actions_row.push(
 409 |             row![
 410 |                 button(load_icon_size("external-link", 16.0))
 411 |                     .on_press(Message::OpenFile(res.path.clone()))
 412 |                     .style(theme::ghost_button())
 413 |                     .padding(Padding::new(6.0)),
 414 |                 button(load_icon_size("folder-open", 16.0))
 415 |                     .on_press(Message::OpenFolder(res.path.clone()))
 416 |                     .style(theme::ghost_button())
 417 |                     .padding(Padding::new(6.0)),
 418 |                 button(load_icon_size("copy", 16.0))
 419 |                     .on_press(Message::CopyPath(res.path.clone()))
 420 |                     .style(theme::ghost_button())
 421 |                     .padding(Padding::new(6.0)),
 422 |             ]
 423 |             .spacing(4),
 424 |         );
 425 |     }
 426 | 
 427 |     let card_content = column![
 428 |         row![
 429 |             load_icon_size(
 430 |                 if res.extension.as_deref() == Some("pdf") {
 431 |                     "file-text"
 432 |                 } else {
 433 |                     "file"
 434 |                 },
 435 |                 18.0
 436 |             ),
 437 |             text(&*res.title).size(15).font(Font {
 438 |                 weight: font::Weight::Bold,
 439 |                 ..Font::default()
 440 |             }),
 441 |             Space::new().width(Length::Fill),
 442 |             actions_row,
 443 |         ]
 444 |         .spacing(10)
 445 |         .align_y(Alignment::Center),
 446 |         text(&res.path).size(12).style(theme::dim_text_style()),
 447 |         row![
 448 |             container(
 449 |                 text(res.extension.as_deref().unwrap_or("FILE"))
 450 |                     .size(10)
 451 |                     .font(Font {
 452 |                         weight: font::Weight::Bold,
 453 |                         ..Font::default()
 454 |                     })
 455 |             )
 456 |             .padding(Padding::from([2, 6]))
 457 |             .style(theme::accent_badge_container),
 458 |             container(
 459 |                 text(
 460 |                     res.size
 461 |                         .map_or_else(|| "Unknown".to_string(), crate::iced_ui::format_size)
 462 |                 )
 463 |                 .size(10)
 464 |             )
 465 |             .padding(Padding::from([2, 6]))
 466 |             .style(theme::badge_container),
 467 |             container(
 468 |                 text(
 469 |                     res.modified
 470 |                         .map_or_else(|| "Unknown".to_string(), crate::iced_ui::format_date)
 471 |                 )
 472 |                 .size(10)
 473 |             )
 474 |             .padding(Padding::from([2, 6]))
 475 |             .style(theme::badge_container),
 476 |         ]
 477 |         .spacing(8),
 478 |         res.snippets.first().map_or_else(
 479 |             || Element::from(Space::new().height(0)),
 480 |             |snippet| {
 481 |                 Element::from(
 482 |                     container(parse_snippet(snippet))
 483 |                         .padding(Padding::new(8.0))
 484 |                         .width(Length::Fill)
 485 |                         .style(theme::hit_highlight_container),
 486 |                 )
 487 |             },
 488 |         ),
 489 |     ]
 490 |     .spacing(8);
 491 | 
 492 |     let mut item_area = container(card_content)
 493 |         .padding(Padding::new(16.0))
 494 |         .style(if is_selected {
 495 |             theme::result_card_selected
 496 |         } else {
 497 |             theme::result_card_normal
 498 |         })
 499 |         .width(Length::Fill);
 500 | 
 501 |     if is_hovered && !is_selected {
 502 |         item_area = item_area.style(theme::result_card_hover);
 503 |     }
 504 | 
 505 |     let mouse_wrapper = mouse_area(item_area)
 506 |         .on_press(Message::ResultSelected(i))
 507 |         .on_right_press(Message::ShowContextMenu(i))
 508 |         .on_enter(Message::ItemHovered(Some(i)))
 509 |         .on_exit(Message::ItemHovered(None));
 510 | 
 511 |     container(mouse_wrapper)
 512 |         .padding(Padding {
 513 |             top: 2.0,
 514 |             bottom: 2.0,
 515 |             left: 12.0,
 516 |             right: 12.0,
 517 |         })
 518 |         .into()
 519 | }
 520 | 
 521 | fn highlight_text<'a>(content: &'a str, terms: &[String]) -> Element<'a, Message> {
 522 |     if terms.is_empty() || content.is_empty() {
 523 |         return text(content).size(14).into();
 524 |     }
 525 | 
 526 |     let lower_content = content.to_lowercase();
 527 |     let mut matches = Vec::new();
 528 | 
 529 |     for term in terms {
 530 |         if term.is_empty() {
 531 |             continue;
 532 |         }
 533 |         let lower_term = term.to_lowercase();
 534 |         let mut start = 0;
 535 |         while let Some(idx) = lower_content[start..].find(&lower_term) {
 536 |             let abs_idx = start + idx;
 537 |             matches.push((abs_idx, abs_idx + term.len()));
 538 |             start = abs_idx + term.len();
 539 |         }
 540 |     }
 541 | 
 542 |     if matches.is_empty() {
 543 |         return text(content).size(14).into();
 544 |     }
 545 | 
 546 |     matches.sort_by_key(|m| m.0);
 547 |     let mut merged: Vec<(usize, usize)> = Vec::new();
 548 |     for m in matches {
 549 |         if let Some(last) = merged.last_mut()
 550 |             && m.0 <= last.1
 551 |         {
 552 |             last.1 = last.1.max(m.1);
 553 |             continue;
 554 |         }
 555 |         merged.push(m);
 556 |     }
 557 | 
 558 |     let mut spans: Vec<iced::widget::text::Span<'a, Message>> = Vec::new();
 559 |     let mut current = 0;
 560 | 
 561 |     for (start, end) in merged {
 562 |         if start > current {
 563 |             spans.push(span(&content[current..start]).size(14));
 564 |         }
 565 |         spans.push(
 566 |             span(&content[start..end])
 567 |                 .size(14)
 568 |                 .font(Font {
 569 |                     weight: font::Weight::Bold,
 570 |                     ..Font::default()
 571 |                 })
 572 |                 .color(iced::Color::from_rgb8(234, 179, 8)),
 573 |         );
 574 |         current = end;
 575 |     }
 576 | 
 577 |     if current < content.len() {
 578 |         spans.push(span(&content[current..]).size(14));
 579 |     }
 580 | 
 581 |     rich_text(spans).into()
 582 | }
 583 | 
 584 | fn parse_snippet<'a>(content: &'a str) -> Element<'a, Message> {
 585 |     let mut spans: Vec<iced::widget::text::Span<'a, Message>> = Vec::new();
 586 |     let mut current_pos = 0;
 587 | 
 588 |     while let Some(start) = content[current_pos..].find("<b>") {
 589 |         let absolute_start = current_pos + start;
 590 | 
 591 |         if absolute_start > current_pos {
 592 |             spans.push(span(&content[current_pos..absolute_start]).size(13));
 593 |         }
 594 | 
 595 |         current_pos = absolute_start + 3;
 596 | 
 597 |         if let Some(end) = content[current_pos..].find("</b>") {
 598 |             let absolute_end = current_pos + end;
 599 |             spans.push(
 600 |                 span(&content[current_pos..absolute_end])
 601 |                     .size(13)
 602 |                     .font(Font {
 603 |                         weight: font::Weight::Bold,
 604 |                         ..Font::default()
 605 |                     })
 606 |                     .color(iced::Color::from_rgb8(234, 179, 8)),
 607 |             );
 608 |             current_pos = absolute_end + 4;
 609 |         } else {
 610 |             spans.push(span(&content[current_pos..]).size(13).font(Font {
 611 |                 weight: font::Weight::Bold,
 612 |                 ..Font::default()
 613 |             }));
 614 |             current_pos = content.len();
 615 |             break;
 616 |         }
 617 |     }
 618 | 
 619 |     if current_pos < content.len() {
 620 |         spans.push(span(&content[current_pos..]).size(13));
 621 |     }
 622 | 
 623 |     if spans.is_empty() {
 624 |         return text(content).size(13).into();
 625 |     }
 626 | 
 627 |     rich_text(spans).into()
 628 | }
 629 | 
 630 | #[allow(clippy::too_many_lines)]
 631 | fn right_panel(app: &App) -> Element<'_, Message> {
 632 |     app.preview_result.as_ref().map_or_else(
 633 |         || {
 634 |             container(
 635 |                 column![
 636 |                     load_icon_size("file-text", 48.0),
 637 |                     text(if app.is_loading_preview {
 638 |                         "Loading document contents..."
 639 |                     } else {
 640 |                         "Select a file to preview"
 641 |                     })
 642 |                     .size(18)
 643 |                     .style(theme::dim_text_style()),
 644 |                 ]
 645 |                 .spacing(16)
 646 |                 .align_x(Alignment::Center),
 647 |             )
 648 |             .center_x(Length::Fill)
 649 |             .center_y(Length::Fill)
 650 |             .into()
 651 |         },
 652 |         |preview_result| {
 653 |             let ext = app
 654 |                 .selected_index
 655 |                 .and_then(|i| app.results.get(i))
 656 |                 .and_then(|r| r.extension.as_deref())
 657 |                 .unwrap_or("txt");
 658 | 
 659 |             let content = if preview_result.matched_terms.is_empty() {
 660 |                 render_code_preview(&preview_result.content, ext, app.is_dark)
 661 |             } else {
 662 |                 highlight_text(&preview_result.content, &preview_result.matched_terms)
 663 |             };
 664 | 
 665 |             let snippets: Element<'_, Message> = app
 666 |                 .selected_index
 667 |                 .and_then(|i| app.results.get(i))
 668 |                 .map_or_else(
 669 |                     || column![].into(),
 670 |                     |res| {
 671 |                         if res.snippets.is_empty() {
 672 |                             column![].into()
 673 |                         } else {
 674 |                             column![
 675 |                                 text("Context Highlights")
 676 |                                     .size(14)
 677 |                                     .font(Font {
 678 |                                         weight: font::Weight::Bold,
 679 |                                         ..Font::default()
 680 |                                     })
 681 |                                     .style(theme::dim_text_style()),
 682 |                                 column(
 683 |                                     res.snippets
 684 |                                         .iter()
 685 |                                         .enumerate()
 686 |                                         .map(|(i, s)| hit_row(i + 1, s))
 687 |                                 )
 688 |                                 .spacing(8)
 689 |                             ]
 690 |                             .spacing(12)
 691 |                             .into()

 751 | fn status_bar(app: &App) -> Element<'_, Message> {
 752 |     let mut status_row = row![
 753 |         text(format!("{} files indexed", app.files_indexed)).size(11),
 754 |         Space::new().width(Length::Fixed(16.0)),
 755 |         text(&app.index_size).size(11),
 756 |         Space::new().width(Length::Fill),
 757 |     ];
 758 | 
 759 |     if let Some(p) = app.rebuild_progress {
 760 |         status_row = status_row
 761 |             .push(container(iced::widget::progress_bar(0.0..=1.0, p)).width(Length::Fixed(100.0)));
 762 |         status_row = status_row.push(Space::new().width(Length::Fixed(8.0)));
 763 |     }
 764 | 
 765 |     if let Some(status) = &app.rebuild_status {
 766 |         status_row = status_row.push(text(status).size(11));
 767 |     }
 768 | 
 769 |     container(status_row.padding(Padding {
 770 |         top: 6.0,
 771 |         bottom: 6.0,
 772 |         left: 20.0,
 773 |         right: 20.0,
 774 |     }))
 775 |     .style(theme::top_bar_container)
 776 |     .width(Length::Fill)
 777 |     .into()
 778 | }

 789 | fn size_unit_button<'a>(unit: &'a str, app: &App) -> Element<'a, Message> {
 790 |     let is_active = app.size_unit == unit;
 791 |     button(text(unit).size(11).font(Font {
 792 |         weight: font::Weight::Bold,
 793 |         ..Font::default()
 794 |     }))
 795 |     .on_press(Message::SizeUnitChanged(unit.to_string()))
 796 |     .style(move |t: &iced::Theme, s| {
 797 |         if is_active {
 798 |             theme::primary_button()(t, s)
 799 |         } else {
 800 |             theme::secondary_button()(t, s)
 801 |         }
 802 |     })
 803 |     .padding(Padding::from([4, 10]))
 804 |     .into()
 805 | }
 806 |
```

```rust
   1 | use iced::{
   2 |     Background, Border, Color, Theme,
   3 |     border::Radius,

   7 | // --- Color Palette (Inspired by Zinc/Amber Premium Dark) ---
   8 | pub const SURFACE_DARK: Color = Color::from_rgb(0.06, 0.06, 0.07); // #0f1115
   9 | pub const PANEL_DARK: Color = Color::from_rgb(0.1, 0.11, 0.13); // #1a1c21
  10 | pub const BORDER_DARK: Color = Color::from_rgb(0.16, 0.17, 0.2); // #292c33
  11 | pub const ACCENT_BLUE: Color = Color::from_rgb(0.23, 0.51, 0.96); // #3b82f6
  12 | pub const HIT_AMBER: Color = Color::from_rgb(0.96, 0.62, 0.04); // #f59e0b
  13 |

  15 | pub const TEXT_MUTED: Color = Color::from_rgb(0.63, 0.64, 0.66);
  16 | pub const TEXT_DIM: Color = Color::from_rgb(0.40, 0.41, 0.43);
  17 | 
  18 | // --- Color Palette (Light) ---
  19 | pub const SURFACE_LIGHT: Color = Color::from_rgb(0.98, 0.98, 0.99); // #fafafa
  20 | pub const PANEL_LIGHT: Color = Color::from_rgb(0.94, 0.94, 0.96); // #f4f4f5
  21 | pub const BORDER_LIGHT: Color = Color::from_rgb(0.89, 0.90, 0.91); // #e4e4e7

  42 |
```

```rust
   1 | use crate::error::Result;
   2 | use arc_swap::ArcSwap;
   3 | use compact_str::CompactString;
   4 | use fst::automaton::Subsequence;
   5 | use fst::{IntoStreamer, Streamer};
   6 | use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};
   7 | use std::path::Path;
   8 | use std::sync::Arc;
   9 | 
  10 | #[derive(
  11 |     Serialize, Deserialize, Debug, Clone, rkyv::Archive, rkyv::Serialize, rkyv::Deserialize,
  12 | )]
  13 | pub struct FilenameEntry {
  14 |     pub path: String,
  15 |     pub name: CompactString,
  16 | }
  17 | 
  18 | #[derive(Serialize, Deserialize, Debug, Clone)]
  19 | pub struct FilenameSearchResult {
  20 |     pub file_path: String,
  21 |     pub file_name: CompactString,
  22 | }
  23 | 
  24 | #[derive(Serialize, Deserialize, Debug, Clone)]
  25 | pub struct FilenameIndexStats {
  26 |     pub total_files: usize,
  27 |     pub index_size_bytes: u64,
  28 | }
  29 | 
  30 | /// File extension for the binary index file
  31 | const INDEX_FILENAME: &str = "filenames.bin";
  32 | /// Legacy JSON filename for migration
  33 | const LEGACY_INDEX_FILENAME: &str = "filenames.json";
  34 | 
  35 | pub struct FilenameIndex {
  36 |     committed: ArcSwap<Vec<FilenameEntry>>,
  37 |     data_path: std::path::PathBuf,
  38 |     fst_map: ArcSwap<Arc<[u8]>>,
  39 |     staging: parking_lot::Mutex<Vec<FilenameEntry>>,
  40 | }
  41 | 
  42 | impl FilenameIndex {
  43 |     pub fn open(data_path: &Path) -> Result<Self> {
  44 |         let data_path = data_path.to_path_buf();
  45 | 
  46 |         let entries = if data_path.exists() {
  47 |             // Try rkyv first, then fall back to legacy JSON
  48 |             let bin_path = data_path.join(INDEX_FILENAME);
  49 |             let json_path = data_path.join(LEGACY_INDEX_FILENAME);
  50 | 
  51 |             if bin_path.exists() {
  52 |                 std::fs::read(&bin_path).map_or_else(
  53 |                     |_| Vec::new(),
  54 |                     |bytes| {
  55 |                         // Ensure byte alignment for rkyv
  56 |                         let mut aligned_bytes = rkyv::util::AlignedVec::<16>::new();
  57 |                         aligned_bytes.extend_from_slice(&bytes);
  58 | 
  59 |                         match rkyv::access::<rkyv::Archived<Vec<FilenameEntry>>, rkyv::rancor::Error>(
  60 |                             &aligned_bytes,
  61 |                         ) {
  62 |                             Ok(archived) => {
  63 |                                 let entries: Vec<FilenameEntry> =
  64 |                                     rkyv::deserialize::<Vec<FilenameEntry>, rkyv::rancor::Error>(
  65 |                                         archived,
  66 |                                     )
  67 |                                     .unwrap_or_default();
  68 |                                 tracing::info!(
  69 |                                     "Loaded {} filenames from rkyv index",
  70 |                                     entries.len()
  71 |                                 );
  72 |                                 entries
  73 |                             }
  74 |                             Err(e) => {
  75 |                                 tracing::warn!("Failed to parse rkyv filename index: {}", e);
  76 |                                 Vec::new()
  77 |                             }
  78 |                         }
  79 |                     },
  80 |                 )
  81 |             } else if json_path.exists() {
  82 |                 // Migrate from legacy JSON
  83 |                 std::fs::read_to_string(&json_path).map_or_else(
  84 |                     |_| Vec::new(),
  85 |                     |content| match serde_json::from_str::<Vec<FilenameEntry>>(&content) {
  86 |                         Ok(entries) => {
  87 |                             tracing::info!(
  88 |                                 "Migrated {} filenames from legacy JSON index",
  89 |                                 entries.len()
  90 |                             );
  91 |                             // Save as rkyv immediately and remove JSON
  92 |                             Self::save_to_disk_sync(&entries, &data_path);
  93 |                             let _ = std::fs::remove_file(&json_path);
  94 |                             entries
  95 |                         }
  96 |                         Err(e) => {
  97 |                             tracing::warn!("Failed to parse legacy JSON filename index: {}", e);
  98 |                             Vec::new()
  99 |                         }
 100 |                     },
 101 |                 )
 102 |             } else {
 103 |                 Vec::new()
 104 |             }
 105 |         } else {
 106 |             Vec::new()
 107 |         };
 108 | 
 109 |         let fst_map = ArcSwap::from_pointee(Arc::from(Self::build_fst(&entries)));
 110 | 
 111 |         Ok(Self {
 112 |             committed: ArcSwap::from_pointee(entries),
 113 |             data_path,
 114 |             fst_map,
 115 |             staging: parking_lot::Mutex::new(Vec::new()),
 116 |         })
 117 |     }
 118 | 
 119 |     pub fn add_file(&self, path: &str, name: &str) -> Result<()> {
 120 |         let entry = FilenameEntry {
 121 |             path: path.to_string(),
 122 |             name: CompactString::from(name),
 123 |         };
 124 | 
 125 |         self.staging.lock().push(entry);
 126 |         Ok(())
 127 |     }
 128 | 
 129 |     pub fn commit(&self) -> Result<()> {
 130 |         let mut staging = self.staging.lock();
 131 |         if staging.is_empty() {
 132 |             return Ok(());
 133 |         }
 134 | 
 135 |         let new_items = std::mem::take(&mut *staging);
 136 |         drop(staging);
 137 | 
 138 |         // Update committed list
 139 |         let mut current = self.committed.load().as_ref().clone();
 140 |         current.extend(new_items);
 141 | 
 142 |         // Rebuild FST map
 143 |         self.fst_map
 144 |             .store(Arc::new(Arc::from(Self::build_fst(&current))));
 145 | 
 146 |         let data_path = self.data_path.clone();
 147 |         let data_to_save = current.clone();
 148 | 
 149 |         self.committed.store(Arc::new(current));
 150 | 
 151 |         std::thread::spawn(move || {
 152 |             Self::save_to_disk_sync(&data_to_save, &data_path);
 153 |         });
 154 | 
 155 |         Ok(())
 156 |     }
 157 | 
 158 |     fn build_fst(entries: &[FilenameEntry]) -> Vec<u8> {
 159 |         let mut items: Vec<(String, u64)> = entries
 160 |             .iter()
 161 |             .enumerate()
 162 |             .map(|(i, e)| (format!("{}\0{}", e.name.to_lowercase(), i), i as u64))
 163 |             .collect();
 164 |         items.sort_by(|a, b| a.0.cmp(&b.0));
 165 | 
 166 |         let mut build = fst::MapBuilder::memory();
 167 |         for (k, v) in items {
 168 |             let _ = build.insert(k, v);
 169 |         }
 170 |         build.into_inner().unwrap_or_default()
 171 |     }
 172 | 
 173 |     /// Save entries to disk using rkyv (consolidated from bincode)
 174 |     fn save_to_disk_sync(entries: &Vec<FilenameEntry>, data_path: &std::path::Path) {
 175 |         match rkyv::to_bytes::<rkyv::rancor::Error>(entries) {
 176 |             Ok(bytes) => {
 177 |                 let _ = std::fs::write(data_path.join(INDEX_FILENAME), bytes.as_slice());
 178 |             }
 179 |             Err(e) => {
 180 |                 tracing::warn!("Failed to serialize filename index: {}", e);
 181 |             }
 182 |         }
 183 |     }
 184 | 
 185 |     pub fn search(&self, query: &str, limit: usize) -> Result<Vec<FilenameSearchResult>> {
 186 |         let fst_guard = self.fst_map.load();
 187 |         if fst_guard.is_empty() {
 188 |             return Ok(Vec::new());
 189 |         }
 190 | 
 191 |         // FST Map - use reference borrow from the guard
 192 |         let Ok(map) = fst::Map::new(&**fst_guard) else {
 193 |             return Ok(Vec::new());
 194 |         };
 195 | 
 196 |         // Fuzzy / Subsequence matching
 197 |         let query_lower = query.to_lowercase();
 198 |         let aut = Subsequence::new(&query_lower);
 199 | 
 200 |         let mut stream = map.search(aut).into_stream();
 201 | 
 202 |         let entries_lock = self.committed.load();
 203 | 
 204 |         let mut results = Vec::new();
 205 |         while let Some((_, v)) = stream.next() {
 206 |             if results.len() >= limit {
 207 |                 break;
 208 |             }
 209 |             if let Some(entry) = entries_lock.get(usize::try_from(v).unwrap_or(usize::MAX)) {
 210 |                 results.push(FilenameSearchResult {
 211 |                     file_path: entry.path.clone(),
 212 |                     file_name: entry.name.clone(),
 213 |                 });
 214 |             }
 215 |         }
 216 | 
 217 |         Ok(results)
 218 |     }
 219 | 
 220 |     pub fn clear(&self) -> Result<()> {
 221 |         self.committed.store(Arc::new(Vec::new()));
 222 |         self.fst_map
 223 |             .store(Arc::new(Arc::from(Vec::new().into_boxed_slice())));
 224 |         self.staging.lock().clear();
 225 | 
 226 |         let data_path = self.data_path.clone();
 227 |         std::thread::spawn(move || {
 228 |             let _ = std::fs::remove_file(data_path.join(INDEX_FILENAME));
 229 |             let _ = std::fs::remove_file(data_path.join(LEGACY_INDEX_FILENAME));
 230 |         });
 231 | 
 232 |         Ok(())
 233 |     }
 234 | 
 235 |     pub fn get_stats(&self) -> Result<FilenameIndexStats> {
 236 |         let entries = self.committed.load();
 237 | 
 238 |         let size: u64 = entries
 239 |             .iter()
 240 |             .map(|e| e.path.len() as u64 + e.name.len() as u64 + 32)
 241 |             .sum();
 242 | 
 243 |         Ok(FilenameIndexStats {
 244 |             total_files: entries.len(),
 245 |             index_size_bytes: size,
 246 |         })
 247 |     }
 248 | 
 249 |     pub fn rebuild_index(&self, paths: Vec<(String, String)>) -> Result<()> {
 250 |         let data_path = self.data_path.clone();
 251 |         let new_entries: Vec<FilenameEntry> = paths
 252 |             .into_iter()
 253 |             .map(|(path, name)| FilenameEntry {
 254 |                 path,
 255 |                 name: CompactString::from(name),
 256 |             })
 257 |             .collect();
 258 | 
 259 |         let data = new_entries.clone();
 260 | 
 261 |         self.fst_map
 262 |             .store(Arc::new(Arc::from(Self::build_fst(&new_entries))));
 263 |         self.committed.store(Arc::new(new_entries));
 264 |         self.staging.lock().clear();
 265 | 
 266 |         std::thread::spawn(move || {
 267 |             Self::save_to_disk_sync(&data, &data_path);
 268 |         });
 269 | 
 270 |         Ok(())
 271 |     }
 272 | }
```

### File: `src\indexer\query_parser.rs`

- Size: 10448 bytes
- Modified: SystemTime { intervals: 134209952494623780 }

```rust
   1 | use regex::Regex;
   2 | use std::sync::OnceLock;
   3 | 
   4 | static OPERATOR_REGEX: OnceLock<Regex> = OnceLock::new();
   5 | 
   6 | /// Parsed query with operators and search terms
   7 | #[derive(Debug, Clone)]
   8 | pub struct ParsedQuery {
   9 |     /// The original text query (for Tantivy)
  10 |     pub text_query: String,
  11 |     /// Extension filter (e.g., "pdf", "docx")
  12 |     pub extension: Option<String>,
  13 |     /// Path filter (search in specific path)
  14 |     pub path_filter: Option<String>,
  15 |     /// Title filter
  16 |     pub title_filter: Option<String>,
  17 |     /// Size filters
  18 |     pub min_size: Option<u64>,
  19 |     pub max_size: Option<u64>,
  20 |     /// Whether fuzzy matching is enabled
  21 |     pub fuzzy: bool,
  22 |     pub case_sensitive: bool,
  23 | }
  24 | 
  25 | impl ParsedQuery {
  26 |     #[must_use]
  27 |     pub fn new(query: &str, case_sensitive: bool) -> Self {
  28 |         Self::parse(query, case_sensitive)
  29 |     }
  30 | 
  31 |     #[allow(clippy::too_many_lines)]
  32 |     fn parse(input: &str, case_sensitive: bool) -> Self {
  33 |         let mut extension = None;
  34 |         let mut path_filter = None;
  35 |         let mut title_filter = None;
  36 |         let mut min_size = None;
  37 |         let mut max_size = None;
  38 |         let fuzzy = true;
  39 | 
  40 |         // Parse operators: ext:pdf, path:docs, title:report, size:>1MB
  41 |         let operator_regex = OPERATOR_REGEX.get_or_init(|| {
  42 |             Regex::new(r#"(?i)(ext|path|title|size):(?:"([^"]*)"|(\S+))"#).unwrap()
  43 |         });
  44 | 
  45 |         let size_regex = Regex::new(r"(?i)^([<>]?)(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)(MB|KB|GB|B)?$").unwrap();
  46 | 
  47 |         let mut remaining = input.to_string();
  48 | 
  49 |         // Process all operators
  50 |         for cap in operator_regex.captures_iter(input) {
  51 |             let operator = cap
  52 |                 .get(1)
  53 |                 .map(|m| m.as_str().to_lowercase())
  54 |                 .unwrap_or_default();
  55 |             let value = cap
  56 |                 .get(2)
  57 |                 .map(|m| m.as_str().to_string()) // Quoted value
  58 |                 .or_else(|| cap.get(3).map(|m| m.as_str().to_string())) // Unquoted value
  59 |                 .unwrap_or_default();
  60 | 
  61 |             match operator.as_str() {
  62 |                 "ext" => {
  63 |                     extension = Some(value.trim_start_matches('.').to_lowercase());
  64 |                     if let Some(m) = cap.get(0) {
  65 |                         remaining = remaining.replace(m.as_str(), "");
  66 |                     }
  67 |                 }
  68 |                 "path" => {
  69 |                     path_filter = Some(if case_sensitive {
  70 |                         value
  71 |                     } else {
  72 |                         value.to_lowercase()
  73 |                     });
  74 |                     if let Some(m) = cap.get(0) {
  75 |                         remaining = remaining.replace(m.as_str(), "");
  76 |                     }
  77 |                 }
  78 |                 "title" => {
  79 |                     title_filter = Some(if case_sensitive {
  80 |                         value
  81 |                     } else {
  82 |                         value.to_lowercase()
  83 |                     });
  84 |                     if let Some(m) = cap.get(0) {
  85 |                         remaining = remaining.replace(m.as_str(), "");
  86 |                     }
  87 |                 }
  88 |                 "size" => {
  89 |                     if let Some(scap) = size_regex.captures(&value) {
  90 |                         let op = scap.get(1).map_or("", |m| m.as_str());
  91 |                         if let Some(num_str) = scap.get(2)
  92 |                             && let Ok(num) = num_str.as_str().parse::<f64>()
  93 |                         {
  94 |                             let multiplier = scap.get(3).map_or(1, |m| {
  95 |                                 match m.as_str().to_uppercase().as_str() {
  96 |                                     "GB" => 1024 * 1024 * 1024,
  97 |                                     "MB" => 1024 * 1024,
  98 |                                     "KB" => 1024,
  99 |                                     _ => 1,
 100 |                                 }
 101 |                             });
 102 | 
 103 |                             #[allow(clippy::cast_possible_truncation, clippy::cast_sign_loss)]
 104 |                             let bytes = (num * f64::from(multiplier)).round() as u64;
 105 |                             match op {
 106 |                                 ">" => min_size = Some(bytes),
 107 |                                 "<" => max_size = Some(bytes),
 108 |                                 _ => {
 109 |                                     min_size = Some(bytes);
 110 |                                     max_size = Some(bytes);
 111 |                                 }
 112 |                             }
 113 |                         }
 114 |                     }
 115 |                     if let Some(m) = cap.get(0) {
 116 |                         remaining = remaining.replace(m.as_str(), "");
 117 |                     }
 118 |                 }
 119 |                 _ => {}
 120 |             }
 121 |         }
 122 | 
 123 |         // Clean up remaining text for full-text search
 124 |         let text_query = remaining
 125 |             .split_whitespace()
 126 |             .collect::<Vec<_>>()
 127 |             .join(" ")
 128 |             .trim()
 129 |             .to_string();
 130 | 
 131 |         Self {
 132 |             text_query: if text_query.is_empty() {
 133 |                 "*".to_string()
 134 |             } else {
 135 |                 text_query
 136 |             },
 137 |             extension,
 138 |             path_filter,
 139 |             title_filter,
 140 |             min_size,
 141 |             max_size,
 142 |             fuzzy,
 143 |             case_sensitive,
 144 |         }
 145 |     }
 146 | 
 147 |     /// Check if a path matches the extension filter
 148 |     #[must_use]
 149 |     pub fn matches_extension(&self, path: &str) -> bool {
 150 |         self.extension.as_ref().is_none_or(|ext| {
 151 |             let path_lower = path.to_lowercase();
 152 |             path_lower.ends_with(&format!(".{ext}"))
 153 |         })
 154 |     }
 155 | 
 156 |     /// Check if a path matches the path filter
 157 |     #[must_use]
 158 |     pub fn matches_path(&self, path: &str) -> bool {
 159 |         self.path_filter.as_ref().is_none_or(|filter| {
 160 |             if self.case_sensitive {
 161 |                 path.contains(filter)
 162 |             } else {
 163 |                 path.to_lowercase().contains(filter)
 164 |             }
 165 |         })
 166 |     }
 167 | 
 168 |     /// Check if a title matches the title filter
 169 |     #[must_use]
 170 |     pub fn matches_title(&self, title: Option<&str>) -> bool {
 171 |         self.title_filter.as_ref().is_none_or(|filter| {
 172 |             title.is_some_and(|t| {
 173 |                 if self.case_sensitive {
 174 |                     t.contains(filter)
 175 |                 } else {
 176 |                     t.to_lowercase().contains(filter)
 177 |                 }
 178 |             })
 179 |         })
 180 |     }
 181 | }
 182 | 
 183 | /// Extract search terms for highlighting from a query
 184 | #[must_use]
 185 | pub fn extract_highlight_terms(query: &str, case_sensitive: bool) -> Vec<String> {
 186 |     let parsed = ParsedQuery::new(query, case_sensitive);
 187 | 
 188 |     let mut terms: Vec<String> = parsed
 189 |         .text_query
 190 |         .split_whitespace()
 191 |         .filter(|t| *t != "*")
 192 |         .map(|t| {
 193 |             if case_sensitive {
 194 |                 t.to_string()
 195 |             } else {
 196 |                 t.to_lowercase()
 197 |             }
 198 |         })
 199 |         .collect();
 200 | 
 201 |     if terms.is_empty() && parsed.text_query == "*" {
 202 |         terms.push("*".to_string());
 203 |     }
 204 | 
 205 |     // Also add title filter terms
 206 |     if let Some(title) = parsed.title_filter {
 207 |         terms.push(title);
 208 |     }
 209 | 
 210 |     terms
 211 | }
```
