```rust
   1 | use tantivy::schema::{
   2 |     FAST, INDEXED, IndexRecordOption, STORED, STRING, Schema, TEXT, TextFieldIndexing, TextOptions,
   3 | };
   4 | 
   5 | /// Create Tantivy schema optimized for file search
   6 | #[must_use]
   7 | pub fn create_schema() -> Schema {
   8 |     let mut schema_builder = Schema::builder();
   9 | 
  10 |     // File path - stored for retrieval, indexed for exact matches
  11 |     schema_builder.add_text_field("file_path", STRING | STORED);
  12 | 
  13 |     // Content - indexed for search AND stored for fast preview retrieval
  14 |     // Storing content allows fast previews without re-parsing files
  15 |     let text_options = TextOptions::default().set_indexing_options(
  16 |         TextFieldIndexing::default()
  17 |             .set_tokenizer("default")
  18 |             .set_index_option(IndexRecordOption::WithFreqsAndPositions),
  19 |     );
  20 |     schema_builder.add_text_field("content", text_options);
  21 | 
  22 |     // Title - stored for display, indexed for search
  23 |     schema_builder.add_text_field("title", TEXT | STORED);
  24 | 
  25 |     // Modified timestamp - indexed for sorting
  26 |     schema_builder.add_date_field("modified", FAST | INDEXED);
  27 | 
  28 |     // File size - indexed for range queries
  29 |     schema_builder.add_u64_field("size", FAST | INDEXED);
  30 | 
  31 |     // File extension - indexed as keyword for fast filtering
  32 |     schema_builder.add_text_field("extension", STRING | STORED);
  33 | 
  34 |     // Language code - indexed as keyword for filtering (e.g., lang:eng)
  35 |     schema_builder.add_text_field("language", STRING | STORED);
  36 | 
  37 |     // Keywords - indexed and tokenized for search visibility
  38 |     let keywords_options = TextOptions::default()
  39 |         .set_indexing_options(
  40 |             TextFieldIndexing::default()
  41 |                 .set_tokenizer("default")
  42 |                 .set_index_option(IndexRecordOption::WithFreqsAndPositions),
  43 |         )
  44 |         .set_stored();
  45 |     schema_builder.add_text_field("keywords", keywords_options);
  46 | 
  47 |     // Optional advanced fields from Kreuzberg 4.8.0
  48 |     schema_builder.add_text_field("layout", STRING | STORED);
  49 |     schema_builder.add_text_field("code_metadata", STRING | STORED);
  50 | 
  51 |     schema_builder.build()
  52 | }
```

```rust
 104 | impl IndexSearcher {
 105 |     pub fn new(index: &Index, index_path: std::path::PathBuf) -> Result<Self> {
 106 |         let reader = index
 107 |             .reader_builder()
 108 |             .reload_policy(tantivy::ReloadPolicy::OnCommitWithDelay)
 109 |             .try_into()
 110 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::index(format!("Failed to create index reader: {e}")))?;
 111 | 
 112 |         let schema = index.schema();
 113 |         let path_field = schema
 114 |             .get_field("file_path")
 115 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("file_path", "Field not found"))?;
 116 |         let content_field = schema
 117 |             .get_field("content")
 118 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("content", "Field not found"))?;
 119 |         let title_field = schema
 120 |             .get_field("title")
 121 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("title", "Field not found"))?;
 122 |         let modified_field = schema
 123 |             .get_field("modified")
 124 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("modified", "Field not found"))?;
 125 |         let size_field = schema
 126 |             .get_field("size")
 127 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("size", "Field not found"))?;
 128 |         let extension_field = schema
 129 |             .get_field("extension")
 130 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("extension", "Field not found"))?;
 131 |

 135 |             cache: QueryCache::new(),
 136 |             path_field,

 138 |             title_field,
 139 |             modified_field,

 145 |     /// Search the index and return top results with optional filters
 146 |     pub async fn search(
 147 |         self: &std::sync::Arc<Self>,
 148 |         params: SearchParams<'_>,
 149 |     ) -> Result<Vec<SearchResult>> {
 150 |         let this = std::sync::Arc::clone(self);
 151 | 
 152 |         let query_owned = params.query.to_string();
 153 |         let extensions_owned: Option<Vec<String>> = params.file_extensions.map(<[String]>::to_vec);
 154 |         let limit = params.limit;
 155 |         let min_size = params.min_size;
 156 |         let max_size = params.max_size;
 157 |         let min_modified = params.min_modified;
 158 |         let case_sensitive = params.case_sensitive;
 159 | 
 160 |         tokio::task::spawn_blocking(move || {
 161 |             let params = SearchParams {
 162 |                 query: &query_owned,
 163 |                 limit,
 164 |                 min_size,
 165 |                 max_size,
 166 |                 min_modified,
 167 |                 file_extensions: extensions_owned.as_deref(),
 168 |                 case_sensitive,
 169 |             };
 170 |             this.search_sync(&params)
 171 |         })
 172 |         .await
 173 |         .map_err(|e| FlashError::search(params.query, format!("Search task failed: {e}")))?
 174 |     }
 175 | 
 176 |     /// Synchronous search implementation
 177 |     ///
 178 |     /// # Panics
 179 |     ///
 180 |     /// Panics if the phrase search regex fails to compile.
 181 |     #[allow(clippy::too_many_lines)]
 182 |     pub fn search_sync(&self, params: &SearchParams<'_>) -> Result<Vec<SearchResult>> {
 183 |         let file_extensions = params.file_extensions.map(|e| {
 184 |             e.iter()
 185 |                 .map(|s| CompactString::from(s.as_str()))
 186 |                 .collect::<smallvec::SmallVec<[CompactString; 8]>>()
 187 |         });
 188 | 
 189 |         // Create cache key
 190 |         let cache_key = CacheKey {
 191 |             query: params.query.to_string(),
 192 |             limit: params.limit,
 193 |             min_size: params.min_size,
 194 |             max_size: params.max_size,
 195 |             min_modified: params.min_modified,
 196 |             extensions: file_extensions.clone(),
 197 |             case_sensitive: params.case_sensitive,
 198 |         };
 199 | 
 200 |         // Check cache first
 201 |         if let Some(cached) = self.cache.get(&cache_key) {
 202 |             return Ok(cached);
 203 |         }
 204 | 
 205 |         let parsed = ParsedQuery::new(params.query, params.case_sensitive);
 206 |         let highlight_terms = extract_highlight_terms(params.query, params.case_sensitive);
 207 | 
 208 |         let searcher = self.reader.searcher();
 209 | 
 210 |         // Helper to run query with all filters
 211 |         #[allow(clippy::type_complexity)]
 212 |         let run_query = |text_query: Box<dyn tantivy::query::Query>,
 213 |                          limit: usize,
 214 |                          query_str: &str|
 215 |          -> Result<(
 216 |             Box<dyn tantivy::query::Query>,
 217 |             Vec<(f32, tantivy::DocAddress)>,
 218 |         )> {
 219 |             let mut combine: Vec<(Occur, Box<dyn tantivy::query::Query>)> =
 220 |                 vec![(Occur::Must, text_query)];
 221 | 
 222 |             if params.min_size.is_some() || params.max_size.is_some() {
 223 |                 let lower = Term::from_field_u64(self.size_field, params.min_size.unwrap_or(0));
 224 |                 let upper =
 225 |                     Term::from_field_u64(self.size_field, params.max_size.unwrap_or(u64::MAX));
 226 |                 let range = RangeQuery::new(Bound::Included(lower), Bound::Included(upper));
 227 |                 combine.push((Occur::Must, Box::new(range)));
 228 |             }
 229 | 
 230 |             if let Some(min_mod) = params.min_modified {
 231 |                 let lower = Term::from_field_date(
 232 |                     self.modified_field,
 233 |                     tantivy::DateTime::from_timestamp_secs(
 234 |                         i64::try_from(min_mod).unwrap_or(i64::MAX),
 235 |                     ),
 236 |                 );
 237 |                 let upper = Term::from_field_date(
 238 |                     self.modified_field,
 239 |                     tantivy::DateTime::from_timestamp_secs(i64::MAX / 1000),
 240 |                 );
 241 |                 let range = RangeQuery::new(Bound::Included(lower), Bound::Included(upper));
 242 |                 combine.push((Occur::Must, Box::new(range)));
 243 |             }
 244 | 
 245 |             if let Some(ref extensions) = file_extensions
 246 |                 && !extensions.is_empty()
 247 |             {
 248 |                 let extension_queries: Vec<_> = extensions
 249 |                     .iter()
 250 |                     .map(|ext| {
 251 |                         let ext_lower = ext.to_lowercase();
 252 |                         let term = tantivy::Term::from_field_text(self.extension_field, &ext_lower);
 253 |                         tantivy::query::TermQuery::new(term, IndexRecordOption::Basic)
 254 |                     })
 255 |                     .collect();
 256 | 
 257 |                 if !extension_queries.is_empty() {
 258 |                     let extension_bool_query = tantivy::query::BooleanQuery::new(
 259 |                         extension_queries
 260 |                             .into_iter()
 261 |                             .map(|q| (Occur::Should, Box::new(q) as Box<dyn tantivy::query::Query>))
 262 |                             .collect(),
 263 |                     );
 264 |                     combine.push((Occur::Must, Box::new(extension_bool_query)));
 265 |                 }
 266 |             }
 267 | 
 268 |             let final_query = tantivy::query::BooleanQuery::new(combine);
 269 |             let top_docs = searcher
 270 |                 .search(&final_query, &TopDocs::with_limit(limit))
 271 |                 .map_err(|e| FlashError::search(query_str, e.to_string()))?;
 272 | 
 273 |             Ok((Box::new(final_query), top_docs))
 274 |         };
 275 | 
 276 |         let (final_query, top_docs) = if parsed.text_query == "*" {
 277 |             run_query(
 278 |                 Box::new(tantivy::query::AllQuery),
 279 |                 params.limit,
 280 |                 params.query,
 281 |             )?
 282 |         } else {
 283 |             let mut query_parser =
 284 |                 tantivy::query::QueryParser::for_index(searcher.index(), vec![self.content_field]);
 285 |             query_parser.set_conjunction_by_default();
 286 | 
 287 |             let query_result = query_parser.parse_query(&parsed.text_query);
 288 | 
 289 |             if let Ok(q) = query_result {
 290 |                 run_query(q, params.limit, params.query)?
 291 |             } else {
 292 |                 let fuzzy_query = tantivy::query::FuzzyTermQuery::new(
 293 |                     Term::from_field_text(self.content_field, &parsed.text_query),
 294 |                     1,
 295 |                     true,
 296 |                 );
 297 |                 run_query(Box::new(fuzzy_query), params.limit, params.query)?
 298 |             }
 299 |         };
 300 | 
 301 |         if top_docs.len() < params.limit
 302 |             && !parsed.text_query.contains(' ')
 303 |             && parsed.text_query != "*"
 304 |         {
 305 |             let phrase_regex =
 306 |                 regex::Regex::new(r#""([^"]+)""#).expect("Invalid regex for phrase search");
 307 |             if !phrase_regex.is_match(&parsed.text_query) {
 308 |                 let fuzzy_query = tantivy::query::FuzzyTermQuery::new(
 309 |                     Term::from_field_text(self.content_field, &parsed.text_query),
 310 |                     1,
 311 |                     true,
 312 |                 );
 313 |                 if let Ok((_, fuzzy_docs)) =
 314 |                     run_query(Box::new(fuzzy_query), params.limit, params.query)
 315 |                 {
 316 |                     let mut combined = top_docs;
 317 |                     let existing_ids: std::collections::HashSet<_> =
 318 |                         combined.iter().map(|(_, addr)| *addr).collect();
 319 | 
 320 |                     for (score, addr) in fuzzy_docs {
 321 |                         if !existing_ids.contains(&addr) {
 322 |                             combined.push((score * 0.8, addr));
 323 |                         }
 324 |                     }
 325 |                     combined
 326 |                         .sort_by(|a, b| b.0.partial_cmp(&a.0).unwrap_or(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal));
 327 |                     return self.process_top_docs(
 328 |                         &searcher,
 329 |                         combined.into_iter().take(params.limit).collect(),
 330 |                         params.query,
 331 |                         &highlight_terms,
 332 |                         &*final_query,
 333 |                         &cache_key,
 334 |                     );
 335 |                 }
 336 |             }
 337 |         }
 338 | 
 339 |         self.process_top_docs(
 340 |             &searcher,
 341 |             top_docs,
 342 |             params.query,
 343 |             &highlight_terms,
 344 |             &*final_query,
 345 |             &cache_key,
 346 |         )
 347 |     }
 348 | 
 349 |     fn process_top_docs(
 350 |         &self,
 351 |         searcher: &tantivy::Searcher,
 352 |         top_docs: Vec<(f32, tantivy::DocAddress)>,
 353 |         query: &str,
 354 |         highlight_terms: &[String],
 355 |         final_query: &dyn tantivy::query::Query,
 356 |         cache_key: &CacheKey,
 357 |     ) -> Result<Vec<SearchResult>> {
 358 |         let mut results = Vec::with_capacity(top_docs.len().min(cache_key.limit));
 359 | 
 360 |         for (score, doc_address) in top_docs {
 361 |             match self.retrieve_result(searcher, query, score, doc_address, highlight_terms) {
 362 |                 Ok(mut result) => {
 363 |                     if let Ok(snippet_generator) = tantivy::snippet::SnippetGenerator::create(
 364 |                         searcher,
 365 |                         final_query,
 366 |                         self.content_field,
 367 |                     ) {
 368 |                         let doc: tantivy::TantivyDocument = searcher
 369 |                             .doc(doc_address)
 370 |                             .map_err(|e| FlashError::search(query, e.to_string()))?;
 371 |                         let snippet = snippet_generator.snippet_from_doc(&doc);
 372 |                         result.snippets = vec![snippet.to_html()];
 373 |                     }
 374 | 
 375 |                     results.push(result);
 376 |                 }
 377 |                 Err(e) => {
 378 |                     tracing::error!("Error retrieving result: {}", e);
 379 |                 }
 380 |             }
 381 | 
 382 |             if results.len() >= cache_key.limit {
 383 |                 break;
 384 |             }
 385 |         }
 386 | 
 387 |         self.cache.insert(cache_key.clone(), results.clone());
 388 |         Ok(results)
 389 |     }
 390 | 
 391 |     fn retrieve_result(
 392 |         &self,
 393 |         searcher: &tantivy::Searcher,
 394 |         query: &str,
 395 |         score: f32,
 396 |         doc_address: tantivy::DocAddress,
 397 |         highlight_terms: &[String],
 398 |     ) -> Result<SearchResult> {
 399 |         let tantivy_doc: tantivy::TantivyDocument = searcher
 400 |             .doc(doc_address)
 401 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::search(query, e.to_string()))?;
 402 | 
 403 |         let file_path = tantivy_doc
 404 |             .get_first(self.path_field)
 405 |             .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
 406 |             .unwrap_or_default()
 407 |             .to_string();
 408 | 
 409 |         let title = tantivy_doc
 410 |             .get_first(self.title_field)
 411 |             .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
 412 |             .map(CompactString::from);
 413 | 
 414 |         let extension = tantivy_doc
 415 |             .get_first(self.extension_field)
 416 |             .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
 417 |             .map(CompactString::from);
 418 | 
 419 |         let size = tantivy_doc
 420 |             .get_first(self.size_field)
 421 |             .and_then(|v| v.as_u64());
 422 | 
 423 |         let modified = searcher
 424 |             .segment_reader(doc_address.segment_ord)
 425 |             .fast_fields()
 426 |             .date("modified")
 427 |             .ok()
 428 |             .map(|f| {
 429 |                 let date = f.values.get_val(doc_address.doc_id);
 430 |                 u64::try_from(date.into_timestamp_secs()).unwrap_or(0)
 431 |             });
 432 | 
 433 |         Ok(SearchResult {
 434 |             file_path,
 435 |             score,
 436 |             title,
 437 |             extension,
 438 |             modified,
 439 |             size,
 440 |             matched_terms: highlight_terms.to_vec(),
 441 |             snippets: Vec::new(),
 442 |         })
 443 |     }
 444 | 
 445 |     pub fn get_statistics(&self) -> Result<IndexStatistics> {
 446 |         let searcher = self.reader.searcher();
 447 |         let total_docs = usize::try_from(searcher.num_docs()).unwrap_or(usize::MAX);
 448 | 
 449 |         let mut total_size = 0;
 450 |         if let Ok(entries) = std::fs::read_dir(&self.index_path) {
 451 |             for entry in entries.flatten() {
 452 |                 if let Ok(metadata) = entry.metadata()
 453 |                     && metadata.is_file()
 454 |                 {
 455 |                     total_size += metadata.len();
 456 |                 }
 457 |             }
 458 |         }
 459 | 
 460 |         Ok(IndexStatistics {
 461 |             total_documents: total_docs,
 462 |             total_size_bytes: total_size,
 463 |         })
 464 |     }
 465 | 
 466 |     pub fn get_recent_files(&self, limit: usize) -> Result<Vec<SearchResult>> {
 467 |         let searcher = self.reader.searcher();
 468 |         let query = tantivy::query::AllQuery;
 469 | 
 470 |         let top_docs = searcher
 471 |             .search(
 472 |                 &query,
 473 |                 &TopDocs::with_limit(limit)
 474 |                     .order_by_fast_field::<i64>("modified", tantivy::Order::Desc),
 475 |             )
 476 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::index(format!("Failed to get recent files: {e}")))?;
 477 | 
 478 |         let mut results = Vec::new();
 479 |         for (_score, doc_address) in top_docs {
 480 |             if let Ok(res) = self.retrieve_result(&searcher, "", 0.0, doc_address, &[]) {
 481 |                 results.push(res);
 482 |             }
 483 |         }
 484 | 
 485 |         Ok(results)
 486 |     }
 487 | 
 488 |     pub fn invalidate_cache(&self) {
 489 |         self.cache.invalidate();
 490 |     }
 491 | }
 492 |

 512 |             max_size: None,
 513 |             min_modified: None,
 514 |             extensions: None,
 515 |             case_sensitive: false,
```

```rust
   1 | use crate::error::{FlashError, Result};
   2 | use crate::parsers::ParsedDocument;
   3 | use parking_lot::Mutex;
   4 | use tantivy::schema::{Field, Schema};
   5 | use tantivy::{Index, IndexWriter, TantivyDocument};
   6 | use tracing::info;
   7 | 
   8 | /// Manages writing documents to the Tantivy index with batch support
   9 | pub struct IndexWriterManager {
  10 |     writer: Mutex<IndexWriter>,
  11 |     #[allow(dead_code)]
  12 |     schema: Schema,
  13 |     path_field: Field,
  14 |     content_field: Field,
  15 |     title_field: Field,
  16 |     modified_field: Field,
  17 |     size_field: Field,
  18 |     extension_field: Field,
  19 |     language_field: Field,
  20 |     keywords_field: Field,
  21 | }
  22 | 
  23 | impl IndexWriterManager {
  24 |     /// Calculate optimal heap size based on system resources
  25 |     /// Returns heap size in bytes (min 32MB, max 256MB)
  26 |     fn calculate_heap_size() -> usize {
  27 |         // Get system memory info (using sysinfo crate would be better, but this is lightweight)
  28 |         let available_memory = std::env::var("FLASH_SEARCH_MEMORY_MB")
  29 |             .ok()
  30 |             .and_then(|s| s.parse::<usize>().ok())
  31 |             .map_or_else(
  32 |                 || {
  33 |                     // Default calculation: use 5% of system memory, capped at 256MB
  34 |                     // This is a heuristic - in production, use sysinfo to get actual memory
  35 |                     let mut sys = sysinfo::System::new_with_specifics(
  36 |                         sysinfo::RefreshKind::nothing()
  37 |                             .with_memory(sysinfo::MemoryRefreshKind::everything()),
  38 |                     );
  39 |                     sys.refresh_memory();
  40 |                     let system_memory = usize::try_from(sys.total_memory()).unwrap_or(usize::MAX);
  41 | 
  42 |                     (system_memory / 20).clamp(32_000_000, 256_000_000)
  43 |                 },
  44 |                 |mb| mb * 1_000_000,
  45 |             );
  46 | 
  47 |         available_memory.clamp(32_000_000, 256_000_000)
  48 |     }
  49 | 
  50 |     pub fn new(index: &Index, memory_limit_mb: u32) -> Result<Self> {
  51 |         let schema = index.schema();
  52 | 
  53 |         // Use user-provided memory limit if it's within reasonable bounds,
  54 |         // otherwise fall back to adaptive calculation.
  55 |         let heap_size = if (32..=2048).contains(&memory_limit_mb) {
  56 |             info!(
  57 |                 "Using user-configured index writer heap size: {} MB",
  58 |                 memory_limit_mb
  59 |             );
  60 |             (memory_limit_mb as usize) * 1_000_000
  61 |         } else {
  62 |             let calculated = Self::calculate_heap_size();
  63 |             info!(
  64 |                 "Using calculated index writer heap size: {} MB (config: {} MB)",
  65 |                 calculated / 1_000_000,
  66 |                 memory_limit_mb
  67 |             );
  68 |             calculated
  69 |         };
  70 | 
  71 |         let writer = index
  72 |             .writer(heap_size)
  73 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::index(format!("Failed to create index writer: {e}")))?;
  74 | 
  75 |         let path_field = schema
  76 |             .get_field("file_path")
  77 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("file_path", "Field not found in schema"))?;
  78 |         let content_field = schema
  79 |             .get_field("content")
  80 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("content", "Field not found in schema"))?;
  81 |         let title_field = schema
  82 |             .get_field("title")
  83 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("title", "Field not found in schema"))?;
  84 |         let modified_field = schema
  85 |             .get_field("modified")
  86 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("modified", "Field not found in schema"))?;
  87 |         let size_field = schema
  88 |             .get_field("size")
  89 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("size", "Field not found in schema"))?;
  90 |         let extension_field = schema
  91 |             .get_field("extension")
  92 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("extension", "Field not found in schema"))?;
  93 |         let language_field = schema
  94 |             .get_field("language")
  95 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("language", "Field not found in schema"))?;
  96 |         let keywords_field = schema
  97 |             .get_field("keywords")
  98 |             .map_err(|_| FlashError::index_field("keywords", "Field not found in schema"))?;
  99 | 
 100 |         Ok(Self {
 101 |             writer: Mutex::new(writer),
 102 |             schema,
 103 |             path_field,
 104 |             content_field,
 105 |             title_field,
 106 |             modified_field,
 107 |             size_field,
 108 |             extension_field,
 109 |             language_field,
 110 |             keywords_field,
 111 |         })
 112 |     }
 113 | 
 114 |     /// Add a single document to the index
 115 |     /// Note: For better performance, use `add_documents_batch` for multiple docs
 116 |     pub fn add_document(&self, doc: &ParsedDocument, modified: u64, size: u64) -> Result<()> {
 117 |         let tantivy_doc = self.create_tantivy_document(doc, modified, size);
 118 | 
 119 |         self.writer
 120 |             .lock()
 121 |             .add_document(tantivy_doc)
 122 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::index(format!("Failed to add document: {e}")))?;
 123 | 
 124 |         Ok(())
 125 |     }
 126 | 
 127 |     /// Add multiple documents in a single lock acquisition (much more efficient)
 128 |     pub fn add_documents_batch(&self, docs: &[(ParsedDocument, u64, u64)]) -> Result<()> {
 129 |         if docs.is_empty() {
 130 |             return Ok(());
 131 |         }
 132 | 
 133 |         let writer = self.writer.lock();
 134 | 
 135 |         for (doc, modified, size) in docs {
 136 |             let tantivy_doc = self.create_tantivy_document(doc, *modified, *size);
 137 |             writer
 138 |                 .add_document(tantivy_doc)
 139 |                 .map_err(|e| FlashError::index(format!("Failed to add document: {e}")))?;
 140 |         }
 141 | 
 142 |         drop(writer);
 143 |         Ok(())
 144 |     }
 145 | 
 146 |     /// Create a Tantivy document from `ParsedDocument`
 147 |     #[inline]
 148 |     fn create_tantivy_document(
 149 |         &self,
 150 |         doc: &ParsedDocument,
 151 |         modified: u64,
 152 |         size: u64,
 153 |     ) -> TantivyDocument {
 154 |         let mut document = TantivyDocument::default();
 155 | 
 156 |         document.add_text(self.path_field, &doc.path);
 157 |         document.add_text(self.content_field, &doc.content);
 158 | 
 159 |         if let Some(ref title) = doc.title {
 160 |             document.add_text(self.title_field, title);
 161 |         }
 162 | 
 163 |         if let Some(ref language) = doc.language {
 164 |             document.add_text(self.language_field, language);
 165 |         }
 166 | 
 167 |         if let Some(ref keywords) = doc.keywords {
 168 |             document.add_text(self.keywords_field, keywords);
 169 |         }
 170 | 
 171 |         let modified_date =
 172 |             tantivy::DateTime::from_timestamp_secs(i64::try_from(modified).unwrap_or(i64::MAX));
 173 |         document.add_date(self.modified_field, modified_date);
 174 |         document.add_u64(self.size_field, size);
 175 | 
 176 |         // Index file extension for fast filtering
 177 |         if let Some(ext) = std::path::Path::new(&doc.path)
 178 |             .extension()
 179 |             .and_then(|e| e.to_str())
 180 |         {
 181 |             document.add_text(self.extension_field, ext.to_lowercase());
 182 |         }
 183 | 
 184 |         document
 185 |     }
 186 | 
 187 |     /// Remove a document from the index
 188 |     pub fn remove_document(&self, path: &str) -> Result<()> {
 189 |         let term = tantivy::Term::from_field_text(self.path_field, path);
 190 |         self.writer.lock().delete_term(term);
 191 | 
 192 |         Ok(())
 193 |     }
 194 | 
 195 |     /// Delete all documents from the index
 196 |     pub fn delete_all_documents(&self) -> Result<()> {
 197 |         self.writer
 198 |             .lock()
 199 |             .delete_all_documents()
 200 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::index(format!("Failed to delete all documents: {e}")))?;
 201 | 
 202 |         Ok(())
 203 |     }
 204 | 
 205 |     /// Commit pending changes to disk
 206 |     pub fn commit(&self) -> Result<()> {
 207 |         self.writer
 208 |             .lock()
 209 |             .commit()
 210 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::index(format!("Failed to commit index: {e}")))?;
 211 | 
 212 |         Ok(())
 213 |     }
 214 | }
```

```rust
   1 | use crate::error::{FlashError, Result};
   2 | use redb::{Database, ReadableTable, TableDefinition};
   3 | use rkyv;
   4 | use std::cmp::Reverse;
   5 | use std::collections::BinaryHeap;
   6 | use std::path::Path;
   7 | use std::sync::Arc;
   8 | use std::time::SystemTime;
   9 | 
  10 | const FILES_TABLE: TableDefinition<&str, &[u8]> = TableDefinition::new("files");
  11 | 
  12 | #[derive(Debug, Clone, rkyv::Archive, rkyv::Serialize, rkyv::Deserialize)]
  13 | pub struct FileMetadata {
  14 |     pub path: String,
  15 |     pub modified: u64,          // Unix timestamp
  16 |     pub size: u64,              // File size in bytes
  17 |     pub content_hash: [u8; 32], // Blake3 hash for content deduplication
  18 |     pub indexed_at: u64,        // When this file was last indexed
  19 | }
  20 | 
  21 | pub type RecentFileEntry = (String, Option<String>, u64, u64);
  22 | 
  23 | /// Manages file metadata database using redb
  24 | /// Implements connection pooling pattern for redb (even though it's embedded)
  25 | /// to ensure proper resource management and monitoring
  26 | pub struct MetadataDb {
  27 |     db: Arc<Database>,
  28 | }
  29 | 
  30 | impl MetadataDb {
  31 |     /// Open or create the metadata database
  32 |     pub fn open(db_path: &Path) -> Result<Self> {
  33 |         let db = match Database::create(db_path) {
  34 |             Ok(db) => Arc::new(db),
  35 |             Err(e) => {
  36 |                 tracing::warn!("Failed to open metadata database: {}. Forcing reset...", e);
  37 |                 let _ = std::fs::remove_file(db_path);
  38 |                 Arc::new(Database::create(db_path).map_err(|e| {
  39 |                     FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
  40 |                 })?)
  41 |             }
  42 |         };
  43 | 
  44 |         // Create table if it doesn't exist
  45 |         // Wrap this in a closure to easily catch errors and retry
  46 |         let init_table = |db: &Database| -> Result<()> {
  47 |             let txn = db.begin_write().map_err(|e| {
  48 |                 FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
  49 |             })?;
  50 |             {
  51 |                 let _table = txn.open_table(FILES_TABLE).map_err(|e| {
  52 |                     FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
  53 |                 })?;
  54 |             }
  55 |             txn.commit().map_err(|e| {
  56 |                 FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
  57 |             })
  58 |         };
  59 | 
  60 |         if let Err(e) = init_table(&db) {
  61 |             tracing::warn!(
  62 |                 "Failed to initialize database tables: {}. Wiping and recreating...",
  63 |                 e
  64 |             );
  65 |             drop(db); // Ensure file is not locked
  66 |             let _ = std::fs::remove_file(db_path);
  67 | 
  68 |             let db = Arc::new(Database::create(db_path).map_err(|e| {
  69 |                 FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
  70 |             })?);
  71 | 
  72 |             init_table(&db).map_err(|e| {
  73 |                 FlashError::database(
  74 |                     "database_operation",
  75 |                     "files_table",
  76 |                     format!("Retry failed: {e}"),
  77 |                 )
  78 |             })?;
  79 | 
  80 |             return Ok(Self { db });
  81 |         }
  82 | 
  83 |         Ok(Self { db })
  84 |     }
  85 | 
  86 |     /// Clone with shared state (for multi-threaded access)
  87 |     #[must_use]
  88 |     pub fn clone_for_thread(&self) -> Self {
  89 |         Self {
  90 |             db: Arc::clone(&self.db),
  91 |         }
  92 |     }
  93 | 
  94 |     /// Check if file needs reindexing based on modification time and hash
  95 |     pub fn needs_reindex(&self, path: &Path, modified: u64, size: u64) -> Result<bool> {
  96 |         let txn = self.db.begin_read().map_err(|e| {
  97 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
  98 |         })?;
  99 | 
 100 |         let table = txn.open_table(FILES_TABLE).map_err(|e| {
 101 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 102 |         })?;
 103 | 
 104 |         let path_str = path.to_str().unwrap_or("");
 105 | 
 106 |         let result = table
 107 |             .get(path_str)
 108 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string()))?
 109 |             .is_none_or(|metadata| {
 110 |                 let bytes = metadata.value();
 111 |                 // Zero-copy read and validate with byte alignment
 112 |                 let mut aligned_bytes = rkyv::util::AlignedVec::<16>::new();
 113 |                 aligned_bytes.extend_from_slice(bytes);
 114 | 
 115 |                 rkyv::access::<rkyv::Archived<FileMetadata>, rkyv::rancor::Error>(&aligned_bytes)
 116 |                     .ok()
 117 |                     .is_none_or(|meta| meta.modified != modified || meta.size != size)
 118 |             });
 119 | 
 120 |         Ok(result)
 121 |     }
 122 | 
 123 |     /// Update file metadata after indexing
 124 |     pub fn update_metadata(
 125 |         &self,
 126 |         path: &Path,
 127 |         modified: u64,
 128 |         size: u64,
 129 |         content_hash: [u8; 32],
 130 |     ) -> Result<()> {
 131 |         let txn = self.db.begin_write().map_err(|e| {
 132 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 133 |         })?;
 134 | 
 135 |         {
 136 |             let mut table = txn.open_table(FILES_TABLE).map_err(|e| {
 137 |                 FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 138 |             })?;
 139 | 
 140 |             let metadata = FileMetadata {
 141 |                 path: path.to_string_lossy().to_string(),
 142 |                 modified,
 143 |                 size,
 144 |                 content_hash,
 145 |                 indexed_at: SystemTime::now()
 146 |                     .duration_since(SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH)
 147 |                     .unwrap_or_default()
 148 |                     .as_secs(),
 149 |             };
 150 | 
 151 |             let bytes = rkyv::to_bytes::<rkyv::rancor::Error>(&metadata).map_err(|e| {
 152 |                 FlashError::database(
 153 |                     "database_operation",
 154 |                     "files_table",
 155 |                     format!("Serialization error: {e}"),
 156 |                 )
 157 |             })?;
 158 | 
 159 |             table
 160 |                 .insert(path.to_str().unwrap_or(""), bytes.as_slice())
 161 |                 .map_err(|e| {
 162 |                     FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 163 |                 })?;
 164 |         }
 165 | 
 166 |         txn.commit().map_err(|e| {
 167 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 168 |         })?;
 169 | 
 170 |         Ok(())
 171 |     }
 172 | 
 173 |     /// Remove a file from the metadata database
 174 |     pub fn remove_file(&self, path: &Path) -> Result<bool> {
 175 |         let txn = self.db.begin_write().map_err(|e| {
 176 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 177 |         })?;
 178 | 
 179 |         let existed = {
 180 |             let mut table = txn.open_table(FILES_TABLE).map_err(|e| {
 181 |                 FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 182 |             })?;
 183 | 
 184 |             let path_str = path.to_str().unwrap_or("");
 185 |             let removed = table.remove(path_str).map_err(|e| {
 186 |                 FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 187 |             })?;
 188 |             removed.is_some()
 189 |         };
 190 | 
 191 |         txn.commit().map_err(|e| {
 192 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 193 |         })?;
 194 | 
 195 |         Ok(existed)
 196 |     }
 197 | 
 198 |     /// Clear all metadata (nuke the table)
 199 |     pub fn clear(&self) -> Result<()> {
 200 |         let txn = self.db.begin_write().map_err(|e| {
 201 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 202 |         })?;
 203 | 
 204 |         {
 205 |             // Deleting the table is the fastest way to clear it
 206 |             txn.delete_table(FILES_TABLE).map_err(|e| {
 207 |                 FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 208 |             })?;
 209 |             // We must recreate it in the same transaction or next open?
 210 |             // Actually, open_table in next usage will recreate it if we create it here?
 211 |             // Safer to just open it again to ensure it exists empty.
 212 |             let _ = txn.open_table(FILES_TABLE).map_err(|e| {
 213 |                 FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 214 |             })?;
 215 |         }
 216 | 
 217 |         txn.commit().map_err(|e| {
 218 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 219 |         })?;
 220 | 
 221 |         Ok(())
 222 |     }
 223 | 
 224 |     /// Get metadata for a specific file
 225 |     pub fn get_metadata(&self, path: &Path) -> Result<Option<FileMetadata>> {
 226 |         let txn = self.db.begin_read().map_err(|e| {
 227 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 228 |         })?;
 229 | 
 230 |         let table = txn.open_table(FILES_TABLE).map_err(|e| {
 231 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 232 |         })?;
 233 | 
 234 |         let result = table
 235 |             .get(path.to_str().unwrap_or(""))
 236 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string()))?
 237 |             .and_then(|metadata| {
 238 |                 let bytes = metadata.value();
 239 |                 rkyv::access::<rkyv::Archived<FileMetadata>, rkyv::rancor::Error>(bytes)
 240 |                     .map_or(None, |meta| {
 241 |                         rkyv::deserialize::<FileMetadata, rkyv::rancor::Error>(meta).ok()
 242 |                     })
 243 |             });
 244 | 
 245 |         Ok(result)
 246 |     }
 247 | 
 248 |     /// Batch update metadata for multiple files (much more efficient)
 249 |     /// Updates all files in a single transaction to minimize I/O overhead
 250 |     pub fn batch_update_metadata(
 251 |         &self,
 252 |         entries: &[(String, u64, u64, [u8; 32])], // (path, modified, size, hash)
 253 |     ) -> Result<usize> {
 254 |         if entries.is_empty() {
 255 |             return Ok(0);
 256 |         }
 257 | 
 258 |         let txn = self.db.begin_write().map_err(|e| {
 259 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 260 |         })?;
 261 | 
 262 |         let indexed_at = SystemTime::now()
 263 |             .duration_since(SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH)
 264 |             .unwrap_or_default()
 265 |             .as_secs();
 266 | 
 267 |         {
 268 |             let mut table = txn.open_table(FILES_TABLE).map_err(|e| {
 269 |                 FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 270 |             })?;
 271 | 
 272 |             for (path, modified, size, content_hash) in entries {
 273 |                 let metadata = FileMetadata {
 274 |                     path: path.clone(),
 275 |                     modified: *modified,
 276 |                     size: *size,
 277 |                     content_hash: *content_hash,
 278 |                     indexed_at,
 279 |                 };
 280 | 
 281 |                 let bytes = rkyv::to_bytes::<rkyv::rancor::Error>(&metadata).map_err(|e| {
 282 |                     FlashError::database(
 283 |                         "database_operation",
 284 |                         "files_table",
 285 |                         format!("Serialization error: {e}"),
 286 |                     )
 287 |                 })?;
 288 | 
 289 |                 table.insert(path.as_str(), bytes.as_slice()).map_err(|e| {
 290 |                     FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 291 |                 })?;
 292 |             }
 293 |         }
 294 | 
 295 |         txn.commit().map_err(|e| {
 296 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 297 |         })?;
 298 | 
 299 |         Ok(entries.len())
 300 |     }
 301 | 
 302 |     /// Batch check which files need reindexing
 303 |     /// Returns a vector of booleans indicating if each file needs reindexing
 304 |     pub fn batch_needs_reindex(
 305 |         &self,
 306 |         entries: &[(String, u64, u64)], // (path, modified, size)
 307 |     ) -> Result<Vec<bool>> {
 308 |         if entries.is_empty() {
 309 |             return Ok(vec![]);
 310 |         }
 311 | 
 312 |         let txn = self.db.begin_read().map_err(|e| {
 313 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 314 |         })?;
 315 | 
 316 |         let table = txn.open_table(FILES_TABLE).map_err(|e| {
 317 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 318 |         })?;
 319 | 
 320 |         let results: Vec<bool> = entries
 321 |             .iter()
 322 |             .map(|(path, modified, size)| {
 323 |                 table.get(path.as_str()).ok().is_none_or(|opt_metadata| {
 324 |                     opt_metadata.is_none_or(|metadata| {
 325 |                         let bytes = metadata.value();
 326 |                         rkyv::access::<rkyv::Archived<FileMetadata>, rkyv::rancor::Error>(bytes)
 327 |                             .ok()
 328 |                             .is_none_or(|meta| meta.modified != *modified || meta.size != *size)
 329 |                     })
 330 |                 })
 331 |             })
 332 |             .collect();
 333 | 
 334 |         Ok(results)
 335 |     }
 336 | 
 337 |     /// Get recently modified files sorted by modification time
 338 |     /// Uses a bounded min-heap to avoid loading all files into memory.
 339 |     pub fn get_recent_files(&self, limit: usize) -> Result<Vec<RecentFileEntry>> {
 340 |         let txn = self.db.begin_read().map_err(|e| {
 341 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 342 |         })?;
 343 | 
 344 |         let table = txn.open_table(FILES_TABLE).map_err(|e| {
 345 |             FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 346 |         })?;
 347 | 
 348 |         // Use a min-heap to keep the top `limit` most recent files.
 349 |         // We store (modified, path, size) and the heap is ordered by modified (smallest at top).
 350 |         // We define a wrapper struct to have a min-heap based on modified time.
 351 |         // Since BinaryHeap is a max-heap, we invert the order by using Reverse.
 352 |         let mut heap: BinaryHeap<Reverse<(u64, String, u64)>> = BinaryHeap::new();
 353 | 
 354 |         for entry in table
 355 |             .iter()
 356 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string()))?
 357 |         {
 358 |             let (k, v) = entry.map_err(|e| {
 359 |                 FlashError::database("database_operation", "files_table", e.to_string())
 360 |             })?;
 361 |             let bytes = v.value();
 362 |             let (modified, size) =
 363 |                 rkyv::access::<rkyv::Archived<FileMetadata>, rkyv::rancor::Error>(bytes)
 364 |                     .map_or((0, 0), |meta| {
 365 |                         (meta.modified.to_native(), meta.size.to_native())
 366 |                     });
 367 |             let path = k.value().to_string();
 368 | 
 369 |             // Push the entry into the heap
 370 |             heap.push(Reverse((modified, path, size)));
 371 | 
 372 |             // If heap exceeds limit, remove the least recent (smallest modified)
 373 |             if heap.len() > limit {
 374 |                 heap.pop();
 375 |             }
 376 |         }
 377 | 
 378 |         // Extract the files from the heap.
 379 |         // They are in arbitrary order (heap order). We want them sorted by modified descending.
 380 |         let mut files: Vec<(String, u64, u64)> = heap
 381 |             .into_iter()
 382 |             .map(|Reverse(tuple)| {
 383 |                 let (modified, path, size) = tuple;
 384 |                 (path, modified, size)
 385 |             })
 386 |             .collect();
 387 | 
 388 |         // Sort by modified descending
 389 |         files.sort_by(|a, b| b.1.cmp(&a.1));
 390 | 
 391 |         // Convert to the expected format (without titles for now, can be enhanced)
 392 |         Ok(files
 393 |             .into_iter()
 394 |             .map(|(path, modified, size)| (path, None, modified, size))
 395 |             .collect())
 396 |     }
 397 | }
```

### File: `src\parsers\memory_map.rs`

- Size: 2198 bytes
- Modified: SystemTime { intervals: 134193676006324279 }

```rust
   1 | use crate::error::{FlashError, Result};
   2 | use memmap2::Mmap;
   3 | use std::fs::File;
   4 | use std::io::Read;
   5 | use std::path::Path;
   6 | 
   7 | const MMAP_THRESHOLD: u64 = 1024 * 1024; // 1MB
   8 | const MAX_FILE_SIZE: u64 = 100 * 1024 * 1024; // 100MB
   9 | 
  10 | pub fn read_file(path: &Path) -> Result<Vec<u8>> {
  11 |     let metadata = std::fs::metadata(path).map_err(|e| FlashError::Io(std::sync::Arc::new(e)))?;
  12 | 
  13 |     let file_size = metadata.len();
  14 | 
  15 |     if file_size > MAX_FILE_SIZE {
  16 |         return Err(FlashError::parse(
  17 |             path,
  18 |             format!("File too large: {file_size} bytes (max: {MAX_FILE_SIZE})"),
  19 |         ));
  20 |     }
  21 | 
  22 |     if file_size > MMAP_THRESHOLD {
  23 |         read_with_mmap(path)
  24 |     } else {
  25 |         read_with_buffer(path)
  26 |     }
  27 | }
  28 | 
  29 | pub fn read_file_as_string(path: &Path) -> Result<String> {
  30 |     let bytes = read_file(path)?;
  31 |     String::from_utf8(bytes).map_err(|e| FlashError::parse(path, format!("Invalid UTF-8: {e}")))
  32 | }
  33 | 
  34 | fn read_with_buffer(path: &Path) -> Result<Vec<u8>> {
  35 |     let mut file = File::open(path).map_err(|e| FlashError::Io(std::sync::Arc::new(e)))?;
  36 |     let mut bytes = Vec::new();
  37 |     file.read_to_end(&mut bytes)
  38 |         .map_err(|e| FlashError::Io(std::sync::Arc::new(e)))?;
  39 |     Ok(bytes)
  40 | }
  41 | 
  42 | fn read_with_mmap(path: &Path) -> Result<Vec<u8>> {
  43 |     let file = File::open(path)
  44 |         .map_err(|e| FlashError::parse(path, format!("Failed to open file: {e}")))?;
  45 | 
  46 |     // SAFETY: Memory mapping a file is unsafe because another process could modify it
  47 |     // while we are reading, potentially violating Rust's memory safety guarantees.
  48 |     // For a local desktop search engine, this risk is acceptable and typically results
  49 |     // in a process crash rather than an exploitable vulnerability.
  50 |     let mmap = unsafe {
  51 |         Mmap::map(&file)
  52 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::Io(std::sync::Arc::new(std::io::Error::other(e))))?
  53 |     };
  54 | 
  55 |     Ok(mmap.to_vec())
  56 | }
  57 | 
  58 | #[must_use]
  59 | pub fn is_mmap_applicable(path: &Path) -> bool {
  60 |     std::fs::metadata(path)
  61 |         .map(|m| m.len() > MMAP_THRESHOLD)
  62 |         .unwrap_or(false)
  63 | }
  64 | 
  65 | pub fn get_file_size(path: &Path) -> Result<u64> {
  66 |     std::fs::metadata(path)
  67 |         .map(|m| m.len())
  68 |         .map_err(|e| FlashError::Io(std::sync::Arc::new(e)))
  69 | }
```

```rust
  32 |     pub fn scan_volume(
  33 |         root: &Path,
  34 |         path_tx: &crossbeam_channel::Sender<PathBuf>,
  35 |         progress_tx: Option<&mpsc::Sender<ProgressEvent>>,
  36 |         total_count: &Arc<AtomicUsize>,

  42 |

  44 |             let handle = CreateFileW(

  54 | 
  55 |             let result = iterate_mft(
  56 |                 handle,
  57 |                 &drive_letter[..3],
  58 |                 path_tx,
  59 |                 progress_tx,
  60 |                 total_count,
  61 |             );
  62 |             let _ = CloseHandle(handle);
  63 |             result
  64 |         }
  65 |     }
  66 | 
  67 |     unsafe fn iterate_mft(
  68 |         handle: HANDLE,
  69 |         drive_root: &str,
  70 |         path_tx: &crossbeam_channel::Sender<PathBuf>,
  71 |         progress_tx: Option<&mpsc::Sender<ProgressEvent>>,
  72 |         total_count: &Arc<AtomicUsize>,
  73 |     ) -> Result<()> {
  74 |         unsafe {
  75 |             let mut journal_data = USN_JOURNAL_DATA_V0::default();
  76 |             let mut bytes_returned = 0u32;
  77 | 
  78 |             DeviceIoControl(
  79 |                 handle,
  80 |                 FSCTL_QUERY_USN_JOURNAL,
  81 |                 None,
  82 |                 0,
  83 |                 Some(std::ptr::addr_of_mut!(journal_data).cast()),
  84 |                 u32::try_from(std::mem::size_of::<USN_JOURNAL_DATA_V0>()).unwrap_or(u32::MAX),
  85 |                 Some(&raw mut bytes_returned),
  86 |                 None,
  87 |             )
  88 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::index(format!("Query USN Journal failed: {e}")))?;
  89 | 
  90 |             let mut mft_enum_data = MFT_ENUM_DATA_V0 {
  91 |                 StartFileReferenceNumber: 0,
  92 |                 LowUsn: 0,
  93 |                 HighUsn: journal_data.NextUsn,
  94 |             };
  95 | 
  96 |             let mut dir_map: HashMap<u64, DirInfo> = HashMap::with_capacity(100_000);
  97 |             let mut files: Vec<(CompactString, u64)> = Vec::with_capacity(500_000);
  98 |             // Use a Vec<u64> to ensure 8-byte alignment for USN records and avoid large stack allocation
  99 |             let mut buffer = vec![0u64; 8192]; // 8192 * 8 = 65536 bytes
 100 |             let buffer_ptr = buffer.as_mut_ptr().cast::<u8>();
 101 |             let buffer_len = u32::try_from(buffer.len() * 8).unwrap_or(u32::MAX);
 102 | 
 103 |             info!("Enumerating MFT records...");
 104 | 
 105 |             loop {
 106 |                 let mut bytes_returned = 0u32;
 107 |                 let success = DeviceIoControl(
 108 |                     handle,
 109 |                     FSCTL_ENUM_USN_DATA,
 110 |                     Some(std::ptr::addr_of!(mft_enum_data).cast()),
 111 |                     u32::try_from(std::mem::size_of::<MFT_ENUM_DATA_V0>()).unwrap_or(u32::MAX),
 112 |                     Some(buffer_ptr.cast()),
 113 |                     buffer_len,
 114 |                     Some(&raw mut bytes_returned),
 115 |                     None,
 116 |                 );
 117 | 
 118 |                 if success.is_err() || bytes_returned < 8 {
 119 |                     break;
 120 |                 }
 121 | 
 122 |                 let next_usn = buffer_ptr.cast::<i64>().read_unaligned();
 123 |                 mft_enum_data.StartFileReferenceNumber = u64::try_from(next_usn).unwrap_or(0);
 124 | 
 125 |                 let mut offset = 8;
 126 |                 while offset < bytes_returned as usize {
 127 |                     let record_ptr = buffer_ptr.add(offset);
 128 |                     #[allow(clippy::cast_ptr_alignment)]
 129 |                     let record = &*record_ptr.cast::<USN_RECORD_V2>();
 130 | 
 131 |                     // Skip system files to clean up the output and increase performance
 132 |                     if (record.FileAttributes & FILE_ATTRIBUTE_SYSTEM.0) == 0 {
 133 |                         #[allow(clippy::cast_ptr_alignment)]
 134 |                         let name_ptr = record_ptr.add(record.FileNameOffset as usize).cast::<u16>();
 135 |                         let name_len = (record.FileNameLength / 2) as usize;
 136 |                         let name = CompactString::from_utf16_lossy(std::slice::from_raw_parts(
 137 |                             name_ptr, name_len,
 138 |                         ));
 139 | 
 140 |                         let frn = record.FileReferenceNumber;
 141 |                         let parent_frn = record.ParentFileReferenceNumber;
 142 |                         let is_dir = (record.FileAttributes & 0x0000_0010) != 0; // FILE_ATTRIBUTE_DIRECTORY
 143 | 
 144 |                         if is_dir {
 145 |                             dir_map.insert(frn, DirInfo { name, parent_frn });
 146 |                         } else {
 147 |                             files.push((name, parent_frn));
 148 |                         }
 149 |                     }
 150 | 
 151 |                     offset += record.RecordLength as usize;
 152 |                 }
 153 |             }
 154 | 
 155 |             reconstruct_paths(
 156 |                 drive_root,
 157 |                 path_tx,
 158 |                 progress_tx,
 159 |                 total_count,
 160 |                 &dir_map,
 161 |                 files,
 162 |             );
 163 |             Ok(())
 164 |         }
 165 |     }
 166 | 
 167 |     fn reconstruct_paths(
 168 |         drive_root: &str,
 169 |         path_tx: &crossbeam_channel::Sender<PathBuf>,
 170 |         progress_tx: Option<&mpsc::Sender<ProgressEvent>>,
 171 |         total_count: &Arc<AtomicUsize>,
 172 |         dir_map: &HashMap<u64, DirInfo>,
 173 |         files: Vec<(CompactString, u64)>,
 174 |     ) {
 175 |         info!(
 176 |             "MFT Enumeration finished. Reconstructing paths for {} files...",
 177 |             files.len()
 178 |         );
 179 | 
 180 |         let mut count = 0;
 181 | 
 182 |         for (name, mut current_parent) in files {
 183 |             let mut path_parts: SmallVec<[&str; 16]> = SmallVec::new();
 184 |             path_parts.push(name.as_str());
 185 | 
 186 |             let mut depth = 0;
 187 |             let mut valid_path = true;
 188 | 
 189 |             // Trace back to root. In NTFS, root's parent is itself. FRN 5 is typically root.
 190 |             while depth < 50 {
 191 |                 if let Some(parent_info) = dir_map.get(&current_parent) {
 192 |                     path_parts.push(parent_info.name.as_str());
 193 |                     if current_parent == parent_info.parent_frn {
 194 |                         break; // Reached root
 195 |                     }
 196 |                     current_parent = parent_info.parent_frn;
 197 |                     depth += 1;
 198 |                 } else {
 199 |                     // Parent not found, orphaned or root not in map
 200 |                     valid_path = false;
 201 |                     break;
 202 |                 }
 203 |             }
 204 | 
 205 |             if valid_path {
 206 |                 let mut full_path = PathBuf::from(drive_root);
 207 |                 for part in path_parts.iter().rev() {
 208 |                     // Skip if it's the drive root name itself being reported
 209 |                     if !part.is_empty() && !part.contains(':') {
 210 |                         full_path.push(part);
 211 |                     }
 212 |                 }
 213 | 
 214 |                 let _ = path_tx.send(full_path.clone());
 215 |                 count += 1;
 216 | 
 217 |                 if count % 2000 == 0 {
 218 |                     total_count.store(count, Ordering::Relaxed);
 219 |                     if let Some(tx) = progress_tx {
 220 |                         let _ = tx.try_send(ProgressEvent {
 221 |                             ptype: ProgressType::Filename,
 222 |                             current_file: name.to_string(),
 223 |                             current_folder: String::new(),
 224 |                             processed: count,
 225 |                             total: 0,
 226 |                             status: format!("Reconstructing MFT: {count} files"),
 227 |                             eta_seconds: 0,
 228 |                             files_per_second: 0.0,
 229 |                         });
 230 |                     }
 231 |                 }
 232 |             }
 233 |         }
 234 | 
 235 |         total_count.store(count, Ordering::Relaxed);
 236 |     }
 237 | 
 238 |     pub fn watch_volume(
 239 |         root: &Path,
 240 |         tx: tokio::sync::mpsc::Sender<(PathBuf, crate::watcher::WatcherAction)>,
 241 |     ) {
 242 |         let drive_letter = root.to_string_lossy();
 243 |         let volume_path = format!("\\\\.\\{}", &drive_letter[..2]);
 244 |         let mut volume_wide: Vec<u16> = volume_path.encode_utf16().collect();
 245 |         volume_wide.push(0);
 246 | 
 247 |         let drive_root_str = drive_letter[..3].to_string();
 248 | 
 249 |         std::thread::spawn(move || {
 250 |             unsafe {
 251 |                 let handle = CreateFileW(
 252 |                     windows::core::PCWSTR(volume_wide.as_ptr()),
 253 |                     GENERIC_READ.0,
 254 |                     FILE_SHARE_READ | FILE_SHARE_WRITE,
 255 |                     None,
 256 |                     OPEN_EXISTING,
 257 |                     FILE_FLAG_BACKUP_SEMANTICS,
 258 |                     None,
 259 |                 )
 260 |                 .unwrap_or(HANDLE(std::ptr::null_mut()));
 261 | 
 262 |                 if handle == HANDLE(std::ptr::null_mut()) {
 263 |                     error!("Failed to open handle for USN monitoring.");
 264 |                     return;
 265 |                 }
 266 | 
 267 |                 let mut journal_data = USN_JOURNAL_DATA_V0::default();
 268 |                 let mut bytes_returned = 0u32;
 269 | 
 270 |                 let success = DeviceIoControl(
 271 |                     handle,
 272 |                     FSCTL_QUERY_USN_JOURNAL,
 273 |                     None,
 274 |                     0,
 275 |                     Some(std::ptr::addr_of_mut!(journal_data).cast()),
 276 |                     u32::try_from(std::mem::size_of::<USN_JOURNAL_DATA_V0>()).unwrap_or(u32::MAX),
 277 |                     Some(&raw mut bytes_returned),
 278 |                     None,
 279 |                 );
 280 | 
 281 |                 if success.is_err() {
 282 |                     let _ = CloseHandle(handle);
 283 |                     return;
 284 |                 }
 285 | 
 286 |                 let mut read_data = READ_USN_JOURNAL_DATA_V0 {
 287 |                     StartUsn: journal_data.NextUsn,
 288 |                     ReasonMask: 0xFFFF_FFFF,
 289 |                     ReturnOnlyOnClose: 1, // Only get events when file is closed (finished writing)
 290 |                     Timeout: 0,
 291 |                     BytesToWaitFor: 0,
 292 |                     UsnJournalID: journal_data.UsnJournalID,
 293 |                 };
 294 | 
 295 |                 // Use a Vec<u64> to ensure 8-byte alignment for USN records and avoid large stack allocation
 296 |                 let mut buffer = vec![0u64; 1024]; // 1024 * 8 = 8192 bytes
 297 |                 let buffer_ptr = buffer.as_mut_ptr().cast::<u8>();
 298 |                 let buffer_len = u32::try_from(buffer.len() * 8).unwrap_or(u32::MAX);
 299 | 
 300 |                 loop {
 301 |                     let mut bytes_returned = 0u32;
 302 |                     let success = DeviceIoControl(
 303 |                         handle,
 304 |                         FSCTL_READ_USN_JOURNAL,
 305 |                         Some(std::ptr::addr_of!(read_data).cast()),
 306 |                         u32::try_from(std::mem::size_of::<READ_USN_JOURNAL_DATA_V0>())
 307 |                             .unwrap_or(u32::MAX),
 308 |                         Some(buffer_ptr.cast()),
 309 |                         buffer_len,
 310 |                         Some(&raw mut bytes_returned),
 311 |                         None,
 312 |                     );
 313 | 
 314 |                     if success.is_ok() && bytes_returned >= 8 {
 315 |                         let next_usn = buffer_ptr.cast::<i64>().read_unaligned();
 316 |                         read_data.StartUsn = next_usn;
 317 | 
 318 |                         let mut offset = 8;
 319 |                         while offset < bytes_returned as usize {
 320 |                             let record_ptr = buffer_ptr.add(offset);
 321 |                             #[allow(clippy::cast_ptr_alignment)]
 322 |                             let record = &*record_ptr.cast::<USN_RECORD_V2>();
 323 | 
 324 |                             if (record.FileAttributes & FILE_ATTRIBUTE_SYSTEM.0) == 0 {
 325 |                                 #[allow(clippy::cast_ptr_alignment)]
 326 |                                 let name_ptr =
 327 |                                     record_ptr.add(record.FileNameOffset as usize).cast::<u16>();
 328 |                                 let name_len = (record.FileNameLength / 2) as usize;
 329 |                                 let name = String::from_utf16_lossy(std::slice::from_raw_parts(
 330 |                                     name_ptr, name_len,
 331 |                                 ));
 332 | 
 333 |                                 // Simplified path: In a full impl, we'd use the FRN map.
 334 |                                 // For now, we only support top-level changes or
 335 |                                 // we'd need to keep the fs_map in memory.
 336 |                                 // As a compromise for this prototype, we'll try to get the path
 337 |                                 // by using the parent FRN if we have a way to cache it.
 338 |                                 let mut changed_path = PathBuf::from(&drive_root_str);
 339 |                                 changed_path.push(name);
 340 | 
 341 |                                 let action = if (record.Reason & USN_REASON_FILE_DELETE) != 0 {
 342 |                                     crate::watcher::WatcherAction::Remove
 343 |                                 } else {
 344 |                                     crate::watcher::WatcherAction::Index
 345 |                                 };
 346 | 
 347 |                                 let _ = tx.blocking_send((changed_path, action));
 348 |                             }
 349 | 
 350 |                             offset += record.RecordLength as usize;
 351 |                         }
 352 |                     } else {
 353 |                         std::thread::sleep(std::time::Duration::from_millis(500));
 354 |                     }
 355 |                 }
 356 |             }
 357 |         });
 358 |     }
 359 | }
 360 |

 385 |         info!("Linux io_uring / parallel scan stub for {:?}", root);
 386 |         Ok(())
 387 |     }

 390 |         info!("Linux fanotify real-time monitoring stub for {:?}", root);
 391 |         Ok(())

 395 | use crate::error::Result;
 396 | use crate::scanner::{ProgressEvent, ProgressType};
 397 | use ignore::WalkBuilder;
 398 | use std::path::PathBuf;
 399 | use std::sync::Arc;
 400 | use std::sync::atomic::{AtomicUsize, Ordering};
 401 | use tokio::sync::mpsc;
 402 | use tracing::{info, warn};
 403 | 
 404 | pub trait DriveScanner: Send + Sync {
 405 |     fn scan(
 406 |         &self,
 407 |         root: PathBuf,
 408 |         exclude_patterns: Vec<String>,
 409 |         path_tx: crossbeam_channel::Sender<PathBuf>,
 410 |         progress_tx: Option<mpsc::Sender<ProgressEvent>>,
 411 |         total_count: Arc<AtomicUsize>,
 412 |     ) -> Result<()>;
 413 | 
 414 |     // Real-time hook for whole drives
 415 |     fn watch(
 416 |         &self,
 417 |         _root: std::path::PathBuf,
 418 |         _tx: tokio::sync::mpsc::Sender<(std::path::PathBuf, crate::watcher::WatcherAction)>,
 419 |     ) -> Result<()> {
 420 |         // Default no-op
 421 |         Ok(())
 422 |     }
 423 | }
 424 | 
 425 | pub struct DefaultDriveScanner;
 426 | 
 427 | impl DriveScanner for DefaultDriveScanner {
 428 |     fn scan(
 429 |         &self,
 430 |         root: PathBuf,
 431 |         exclude_patterns: Vec<String>,
 432 |         path_tx: crossbeam_channel::Sender<PathBuf>,
 433 |         progress_tx: Option<mpsc::Sender<ProgressEvent>>,
 434 |         total_count: Arc<AtomicUsize>,
 435 |     ) -> Result<()> {
 436 |         let mut builder = WalkBuilder::new(&root);
 437 | 
 438 |         let mut override_builder = ignore::overrides::OverrideBuilder::new(&root);
 439 |         for pattern in &exclude_patterns {
 440 |             let ignore_pattern = format!("!{pattern}");
 441 |             if let Err(e) = override_builder.add(&ignore_pattern) {
 442 |                 warn!("Invalid exclude pattern '{}': {}", pattern, e);
 443 |             }
 444 |         }
 445 |         if let Ok(overrides) = override_builder.build() {
 446 |             builder.overrides(overrides);
 447 |         }
 448 | 
 449 |         builder.follow_links(true).standard_filters(false);
 450 |         builder.max_depth(Some(20));
 451 | 
 452 |         info!("Starting DefaultDriveScanner for {}", root.display());
 453 |         let walker = builder.build_parallel();
 454 | 
 455 |         walker.run(|| {
 456 |             let path_tx = path_tx.clone();
 457 |             let progress_tx = progress_tx.clone();
 458 |             let total = total_count.clone();
 459 |             Box::new(move |entry| {
 460 |                 #[allow(clippy::collapsible_if)]
 461 |                 if let Ok(entry) = entry {
 462 |                     if entry.file_type().is_some_and(|ft| ft.is_file()) {
 463 |                         let path = entry.path().to_path_buf();
 464 |                         let _ = path_tx.send(path);
 465 |                         let count = total.fetch_add(1, Ordering::Relaxed);
 466 | 
 467 |                         #[allow(clippy::collapsible_if)]
 468 |                         if count.is_multiple_of(100) {
 469 |                             if let Some(tx) = &progress_tx {
 470 |                                 let _ = tx.try_send(ProgressEvent {
 471 |                                     ptype: ProgressType::Filename,
 472 |                                     current_file: entry.file_name().to_string_lossy().to_string(),
 473 |                                     current_folder: String::new(),
 474 |                                     processed: count,
 475 |                                     total: 0,
 476 |                                     status: "Scanning filenames...".to_string(),
 477 |                                     eta_seconds: 0,
 478 |                                     files_per_second: 0.0,
 479 |                                 });
 480 |                             }
 481 |                         }
 482 |                     }
 483 |                 }
 484 |                 ignore::WalkState::Continue
 485 |             })
 486 |         });
 487 | 
 488 |         let final_count = total_count.load(Ordering::Relaxed);
 489 |         if let Some(tx) = &progress_tx {
 490 |             let _ = tx.try_send(ProgressEvent {
 491 |                 ptype: ProgressType::Filename,
 492 |                 current_file: String::new(),
 493 |                 current_folder: String::new(),
 494 |                 processed: final_count,
 495 |                 total: final_count,
 496 |                 status: "Filename scan complete".to_string(),
 497 |                 eta_seconds: 0,
 498 |                 files_per_second: 0.0,
 499 |             });
 500 |         }
 501 | 
 502 |         Ok(())
 503 |     }
 504 | }
 505 | 
 506 | #[cfg(target_os = "windows")]
 507 | pub struct WindowsDriveScanner;
 508 | 
 509 | #[cfg(target_os = "windows")]
 510 | impl DriveScanner for WindowsDriveScanner {
 511 |     fn scan(
 512 |         &self,
 513 |         root: PathBuf,
 514 |         exclude_patterns: Vec<String>,
 515 |         path_tx: crossbeam_channel::Sender<PathBuf>,
 516 |         progress_tx: Option<mpsc::Sender<ProgressEvent>>,
 517 |         total_count: Arc<AtomicUsize>,
 518 |     ) -> Result<()> {
 519 |         let root_str = root.to_string_lossy();
 520 |         let is_unc = root_str.starts_with("\\\\");
 521 |         let is_root = root.parent().is_none() || root_str.len() <= 3;
 522 | 
 523 |         let mut is_local_drive = true;
 524 |         if is_root && !is_unc {
 525 |             unsafe {
 526 |                 let drive_root = format!("{}\\", &root_str[..2]);
 527 |                 let mut wide_root: Vec<u16> = drive_root.encode_utf16().collect();
 528 |                 wide_root.push(0);
 529 | 
 530 |                 let drive_type = windows::Win32::Storage::FileSystem::GetDriveTypeW(
 531 |                     windows::core::PCWSTR(wide_root.as_ptr()),
 532 |                 );
 533 | 
 534 |                 if drive_type == 3 {
 535 |                     // DRIVE_REMOTE
 536 |                     is_local_drive = false;
 537 |                 }
 538 |             }
 539 |         }
 540 | 
 541 |         if is_root && !is_unc && is_local_drive && root.exists() {
 542 |             info!(
 543 |                 "Whole local drive detected, attempting MFT scan for {:?}",
 544 |                 root
 545 |             );
 546 |             if let Err(e) =
 547 |                 windows_usn::scan_volume(&root, &path_tx, progress_tx.as_ref(), &total_count)
 548 |             {
 549 |                 warn!("MFT scan failed, falling back to parallel walk: {}", e);
 550 |             } else {
 551 |                 return Ok(());
 552 |             }
 553 |         } else if is_unc || !is_local_drive {
 554 |             info!(
 555 |                 "Network/Remote drive detected, using parallel fallback scanner for {:?}",
 556 |                 root
 557 |             );
 558 |         }
 559 | 
 560 |         let fallback = DefaultDriveScanner;
 561 |         fallback.scan(root, exclude_patterns, path_tx, progress_tx, total_count)
 562 |     }
 563 | 
 564 |     fn watch(
 565 |         &self,
 566 |         root: PathBuf,
 567 |         tx: tokio::sync::mpsc::Sender<(PathBuf, crate::watcher::WatcherAction)>,
 568 |     ) -> Result<()> {
 569 |         let root_str = root.to_string_lossy();
 570 |         let is_unc = root_str.starts_with("\\\\");
 571 |         let is_root = root.parent().is_none() || root_str.len() <= 3;
 572 | 
 573 |         let mut is_local_drive = true;
 574 |         if is_root && !is_unc {
 575 |             unsafe {
 576 |                 let drive_root = format!("{}\\", &root_str[..2]);
 577 |                 let mut wide_root: Vec<u16> = drive_root.encode_utf16().collect();
 578 |                 wide_root.push(0);
 579 | 
 580 |                 let drive_type = windows::Win32::Storage::FileSystem::GetDriveTypeW(
 581 |                     windows::core::PCWSTR(wide_root.as_ptr()),
 582 |                 );
 583 | 
 584 |                 if drive_type == 3 {
 585 |                     // DRIVE_REMOTE
 586 |                     is_local_drive = false;
 587 |                 }
 588 |             }
 589 |         }
 590 | 
 591 |         if is_root && !is_unc && is_local_drive && root.exists() {
 592 |             windows_usn::watch_volume(&root, tx);
 593 |         }
 594 | 
 595 |         Ok(())
 596 |     }
 597 | }
 598 | 
 599 | #[cfg(target_os = "macos")]
 600 | pub struct MacDriveScanner;
 601 | 
 602 | #[cfg(target_os = "macos")]
 603 | impl DriveScanner for MacDriveScanner {
 604 |     fn scan(
 605 |         &self,
 606 |         root: PathBuf,
 607 |         exclude_patterns: Vec<String>,
 608 |         path_tx: crossbeam_channel::Sender<PathBuf>,
 609 |         progress_tx: Option<mpsc::Sender<ProgressEvent>>,
 610 |         total_count: Arc<AtomicUsize>,
 611 |     ) -> Result<()> {
 612 |         let _ = macos_fsevents::scan_volume(&root);
 613 |         let fallback = DefaultDriveScanner;
 614 |         fallback.scan(root, exclude_patterns, path_tx, progress_tx, total_count)
 615 |     }
 616 | }
```

```rust
 206 | impl AppSettings {
 207 |     pub fn get_allowed_extensions(&self) -> &std::collections::HashSet<String> {
 208 |         self.allowed_extensions_cache.0.get_or_init(|| {
 209 |             let mut exts = std::collections::HashSet::new();
 210 |             for ext in COMMON_EXTENSIONS {
 211 |                 exts.insert((*ext).to_string());
 212 |             }
 213 |             for custom in self.custom_extensions.split(',') {
 214 |                 let trimmed = custom.trim().trim_start_matches('.').to_lowercase();
 215 |                 if !trimmed.is_empty() {
 216 |                     exts.insert(trimmed);
 217 |                 }
 218 |             }
 219 |             exts
 220 |         })
 221 |     }

 231 | 
 232 |     pub fn load(&self) -> Result<AppSettings> {
 233 |         let builder = Config::builder()
 234 |             // Start with default settings
 235 |             .add_source(ConfigFile::from_str(
 236 |                 &serde_json::to_string(&AppSettings::default())
 237 |                     .unwrap_or_else(|_| "{}".to_string()),
 238 |                 config::FileFormat::Json,
 239 |             ))
 240 |             // Add settings from file if it exists
 241 |             .add_source(ConfigFile::from(self.path.clone()).required(false))
 242 |             // Override with environment variables (e.g., FLASH_SEARCH_THEME=dark)
 243 |             .add_source(Environment::with_prefix("FLASH_SEARCH").separator("__"));
 244 | 
 245 |         match builder.build() {
 246 |             Ok(config) => config
 247 |                 .try_deserialize()
 248 |                 .map_err(|e| FlashError::config("parse_settings", e.to_string())),
 249 |             Err(e) => Err(FlashError::config("build_config", e.to_string())),
 250 |         }
 251 |     }
 252 | 
 253 |     pub fn save(&self, settings: &AppSettings) -> Result<()> {
 254 |         let content = serde_json::to_string_pretty(settings)
 255 |             .map_err(|e| FlashError::config("serialize_settings", e.to_string()))?;
 256 | 
 257 |         let tmp_path = self.path.with_extension("tmp");
 258 |         fs::write(&tmp_path, content).map_err(|e| FlashError::Io(std::sync::Arc::new(e)))?;
 259 |         fs::rename(&tmp_path, &self.path).map_err(|e| FlashError::Io(std::sync::Arc::new(e)))
 260 |     }
 261 | }
 262 | 
 263 | #[cfg(test)]
 264 | mod tests {
 265 |     use super::*;
 266 |     use tempfile::tempdir;
 267 | 
 268 |     #[test]
 269 |     fn test_settings_save_load() {
 270 |         let temp_dir = tempdir().unwrap();
 271 |         let manager = SettingsManager::new(temp_dir.path());
 272 | 
 273 |         let settings = AppSettings {
 274 |             max_results: 100,
 275 |             theme: Theme::Dark,
 276 |             ..Default::default()
 277 |         };
 278 | 
 279 |         manager.save(&settings).unwrap();
 280 |         let loaded = manager.load().unwrap();
 281 |         assert_eq!(loaded.max_results, 100);
 282 |         assert_eq!(loaded.theme, Theme::Dark);
```

```rust
  18 |         r"Software\Classes\Directory\shell\FlashSearch",

  33 |                 .map_err(|e| FlashError::config("context_menu", e.to_string()))?;
```
