 540 |             console.log(`Score: ${keyword.score}`);
 541 |             console.log(`Algorithm: ${keyword.algorithm}`);
 542 |         }
 543 |     }
 544 |     ```
 545 | 
 546 | ## Language Detection
 547 | 
 548 | Automatically detect the language(s) in documents using ISO 639-1 language codes.
 549 | 
 550 | === "Python"
 551 | 
 552 |     ```python
 553 |     from kreuzberg import (
 554 |         ExtractionConfig, LanguageDetectionConfig,
 555 |         extract_file_sync
 556 |     )
 557 | 
 558 |     # Enable language detection
 559 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 560 |         language_detection=LanguageDetectionConfig(
 561 |             enabled=True,
 562 |             min_confidence=0.8,
 563 |             detect_multiple=False
 564 |         )
 565 |     )
 566 | 
 567 |     result = extract_file_sync("multilingual.pdf", config=config)
 568 | 
 569 |     # Access detected languages
 570 |     if result.detected_languages:
 571 |         for lang_code in result.detected_languages:
 572 |             print(f"Detected language: {lang_code}")  # e.g., "en", "de", "fr"
 573 |     ```
 574 | 
 575 | === "TypeScript"
 576 | 
 577 |     ```typescript
 578 |     import {
 579 |         ExtractionConfig, LanguageDetectionConfig,
 580 |         extractFile
 581 |     } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 582 | 
 583 |     const config: ExtractionConfig = {
 584 |         languageDetection: {
 585 |             enabled: true,
 586 |             minConfidence: 0.8,
 587 |             detectMultiple: false
 588 |         }
 589 |     };
 590 | 
 591 |     const result = await extractFile("multilingual.pdf", null, config);
 592 | 
 593 |     // Access detected languages
 594 |     if (result.detectedLanguages) {
 595 |         for (const langCode of result.detectedLanguages) {
 596 |             console.log(`Detected language: ${langCode}`);  // e.g., "en", "de", "fr"
 597 |         }
 598 |     }
 599 |     ```
 600 | 
 601 | ## Token Reduction
 602 | 
 603 | Reduce the number of tokens in extracted content for cost optimization when working with LLM APIs. Higher modes are more aggressive but may lose more information.
 604 | 
 605 | === "Python"
 606 | 
 607 |     ```python
 608 |     from kreuzberg import (
 609 |         ExtractionConfig, TokenReductionConfig,
 610 |         extract_file_sync
 611 |     )
 612 | 
 613 |     # Light token reduction
 614 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 615 |         token_reduction=TokenReductionConfig(
 616 |             mode="light",
 617 |             preserve_important_words=True
 618 |         )
 619 |     )
 620 | 
 621 |     # Moderate reduction
 622 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 623 |         token_reduction=TokenReductionConfig(
 624 |             mode="moderate",
 625 |             preserve_important_words=True
 626 |         )
 627 |     )
 628 | 
 629 |     # Aggressive reduction
 630 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 631 |         token_reduction=TokenReductionConfig(
 632 |             mode="aggressive",
 633 |             preserve_important_words=True
 634 |         )
 635 |     )
 636 | 
 637 |     # Maximum reduction
 638 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 639 |         token_reduction=TokenReductionConfig(
 640 |             mode="maximum",
 641 |             preserve_important_words=True
 642 |         )
 643 |     )
 644 | 
 645 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 646 |     print(f"Reduced content length: {len(result.content)}")
 647 |     ```
 648 | 
 649 | === "TypeScript"
 650 | 
 651 |     ```typescript
 652 |     import {
 653 |         ExtractionConfig, TokenReductionConfig,
 654 |         extractFile
 655 |     } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 656 | 
 657 |     const config: ExtractionConfig = {
 658 |         tokenReduction: {
 659 |             mode: "moderate",
 660 |             preserveImportantWords: true
 661 |         }
 662 |     };
 663 | 
 664 |     const result = await extractFile("document.pdf", null, config);
 665 |     console.log(`Reduced content length: ${result.content.length}`);
 666 |     ```
 667 | 
 668 | **Token Reduction Modes:**
 669 | 
 670 | - `off`: No reduction (default)
 671 | - `light`: Remove extra whitespace and redundant punctuation
 672 | - `moderate`: Also remove common filler words and some formatting
 673 | - `aggressive`: Also remove longer stopwords and collapse similar phrases
 674 | - `maximum`: Maximum reduction while preserving semantic content
 675 | 
 676 | ## Page Extraction
 677 | 
 678 | Extract and track per-page content separately. Useful for multi-page documents where you need page-level granularity.
 679 | 
 680 | === "Python"
 681 | 
 682 |     ```python
 683 |     from kreuzberg import (
 684 |         ExtractionConfig, PageConfig,
 685 |         extract_file_sync
 686 |     )
 687 | 
 688 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 689 |         pages=PageConfig(
 690 |             extract_pages=True,
 691 |             insert_page_markers=True,
 692 |             marker_format="\n\n<!-- PAGE {page_num} -->\n\n"
 693 |         )
 694 |     )
 695 | 
 696 |     result = extract_file_sync("multi_page.pdf", config=config)
 697 | 
 698 |     # Access per-page content
 699 |     if result.pages:
 700 |         for page in result.pages:
 701 |             print(f"Page {page.page_number}:")
 702 |             print(f"Content: {page.content[:100]}...")
 703 |             print(f"Tables: {len(page.tables)}")
 704 |             print(f"Images: {len(page.images)}")
 705 |     ```
 706 | 
 707 | === "TypeScript"
 708 | 
 709 |     ```typescript
 710 |     import {
 711 |         ExtractionConfig, PageExtractionConfig,
 712 |         extractFile
 713 |     } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 714 | 
 715 |     const config: ExtractionConfig = {
 716 |         pages: {
 717 |             extractPages: true,
 718 |             insertPageMarkers: true,
 719 |             markerFormat: "\n\n<!-- PAGE {page_num} -->\n\n"
 720 |         }
 721 |     };
 722 | 
 723 |     const result = await extractFile("multi_page.pdf", null, config);
 724 | 
 725 |     // Access per-page content
 726 |     if (result.pages) {
 727 |         for (const page of result.pages) {
 728 |             console.log(`Page ${page.pageNumber}:`);
 729 |             console.log(`Content: ${page.content.substring(0, 100)}...`);
 730 |             console.log(`Tables: ${page.tables.length}`);
 731 |             console.log(`Images: ${page.images.length}`);
 732 |         }
 733 |     }
 734 |     ```
 735 | 
 736 | ## Element-Based Output
 737 | 
 738 | Extract semantic elements instead of unified content. This format is compatible with the Unstructured library and provides structured access to different content types (titles, headings, text, tables, images, etc.).
 739 | 
 740 | === "Python"
 741 | 
 742 |     ```python
 743 |     from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, ResultFormat, extract_file_sync
 744 | 
 745 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 746 |         result_format="element_based"
 747 |     )
 748 | 
 749 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 750 | 
 751 |     # Access semantic elements
 752 |     if result.elements:
 753 |         for element in result.elements:
 754 |             print(f"Type: {element.element_type}")  # title, heading, narrative_text, etc.
 755 |             print(f"Text: {element.text}")
 756 |             if element.metadata.get("page_number"):
 757 |                 print(f"Page: {element.metadata['page_number']}")
 758 |     ```
 759 | 
 760 | === "TypeScript"
 761 | 
 762 |     ```typescript
 763 |     import { ExtractionConfig, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 764 | 
 765 |     const config: ExtractionConfig = {
 766 |         resultFormat: "element_based"
 767 |     };
 768 | 
 769 |     const result = await extractFile("document.pdf", null, config);
 770 | 
 771 |     // Access semantic elements
 772 |     if (result.elements) {
 773 |         for (const element of result.elements) {
 774 |             console.log(`Type: ${element.elementType}`);
 775 |             console.log(`Text: ${element.text}`);
 776 |             if (element.metadata.pageNumber) {
 777 |                 console.log(`Page: ${element.metadata.pageNumber}`);
 778 |             }
 779 |         }
 780 |     }
 781 |     ```
 782 | 
 783 | **Element Types:**
 784 | 
 785 | - `title`: Document or section title
 786 | - `heading`: Section headings
 787 | - `narrative_text`: Regular paragraph text
 788 | - `list_item`: Items in bullet/numbered lists
 789 | - `table`: Table structures
 790 | - `image`: Images or figures
 791 | - `page_break`: Page boundaries
 792 | - `code_block`: Code snippets
 793 | - `block_quote`: Quoted text
 794 | - `footer`: Footer content
 795 | - `header`: Header content
 796 | 
 797 | ## Djot Content
 798 | 
 799 | Output extracted content in Djot markup format (a lighter alternative to Markdown with enhanced structure).
 800 | 
 801 | === "Python"
 802 | 
 803 |     ```python
 804 |     from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, OutputFormat, extract_file_sync
 805 | 
 806 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 807 |         output_format="djot"
 808 |     )
 809 | 
 810 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 811 |     print(result.content)  # Djot-formatted content
 812 | 
 813 |     # Access structured Djot content
 814 |     if result.djot_content:
 815 |         print(f"Plain text: {result.djot_content['plain_text']}")
 816 |         print(f"Blocks: {result.djot_content['blocks']}")
 817 |         print(f"Links: {result.djot_content['links']}")
 818 |         print(f"Images: {result.djot_content['images']}")
 819 |         print(f"Footnotes: {result.djot_content['footnotes']}")
 820 |     ```
 821 | 
 822 | === "TypeScript"
 823 | 
 824 |     ```typescript
 825 |     import { ExtractionConfig, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 826 | 
 827 |     const config: ExtractionConfig = {
 828 |         outputFormat: "djot"
 829 |     };
 830 | 
 831 |     const result = await extractFile("document.pdf", null, config);
 832 |     console.log(result.content);  // Djot-formatted content
 833 | 
 834 |     // Access structured Djot content (if available)
 835 |     if (result.djotContent) {
 836 |         console.log(`Plain text: ${result.djotContent.plain_text}`);
 837 |         console.log(`Blocks: ${result.djotContent.blocks}`);
 838 |         console.log(`Links: ${result.djotContent.links}`);
 839 |         console.log(`Images: ${result.djotContent.images}`);
 840 |         console.log(`Footnotes: ${result.djotContent.footnotes}`);
 841 |     }
 842 |     ```
 843 | 
 844 | ## API Server
 845 | 
 846 | Run Kreuzberg as an HTTP API server for integration with external services.
 847 | 
 848 | ```bash
 849 | # Start server on default port 8000
 850 | kreuzberg serve
 851 | 
 852 | # Custom host and port
 853 | kreuzberg serve --host 0.0.0.0 --port 9000
 854 | 
 855 | # Enable CORS and other options
 856 | kreuzberg serve --host localhost --port 8000
 857 | ```
 858 | 
 859 | **API Endpoints:**
 860 | 
 861 | - `POST /extract` - Extract from uploaded file
 862 | - `POST /batch` - Batch extraction
 863 | - `POST /detect` - Detect MIME type
 864 | 
 865 | **Example:**
 866 | 
 867 | ```bash
 868 | curl -X POST -F "file=@document.pdf" http://localhost:8000/extract
 869 | ```
 870 | 
 871 | ## MCP Server
 872 | 
 873 | Run Kreuzberg as a Model Context Protocol server for integration with Claude and other AI models.
 874 | 
 875 | ```bash
 876 | # Start MCP server with stdio transport
 877 | kreuzberg mcp --transport stdio
 878 | 
 879 | # Start MCP server with HTTP transport
 880 | kreuzberg mcp --transport http --host 127.0.0.1 --port 8001
 881 | ```
 882 | 
 883 | The MCP server exposes extraction functions to AI models, allowing them to process documents directly.
 884 | 
 885 | ## Security Limits
 886 | 
 887 | Set resource limits to prevent abuse and control memory/file size consumption.
 888 | 
 889 | === "Python"
 890 | 
 891 |     ```python
 892 |     from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, extract_file_sync
 893 | 
 894 |     config = ExtractionConfig(
 895 |         security_limits={
 896 |             "max_file_size": 100_000_000,      # 100 MB
 897 |             "max_archive_files": 1000,
 898 |             "max_text_length": 10_000_000,     # 10 MB of text
 899 |             "max_pages": 10000,
 900 |             "max_concurrent_extractions": 4
 901 |         }
 902 |     )
 903 | 
 904 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 905 |     ```
 906 | 
 907 | === "TypeScript"
 908 | 
 909 |     ```typescript
 910 |     import { ExtractionConfig, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 911 | 
 912 |     const config: ExtractionConfig = {
 913 |         securityLimits: {
 914 |             max_file_size: 100_000_000,        // 100 MB
 915 |             max_archive_files: 1000,
 916 |             max_text_length: 10_000_000,       // 10 MB of text
 917 |             max_pages: 10000,
 918 |             max_concurrent_extractions: 4
 919 |         }
 920 |     };
 921 | 
 922 |     const result = await extractFile("document.pdf", null, config);
 923 |     ```
 924 | 
 925 | **Common Limits:**
 926 | 
 927 | - `max_file_size`: Maximum input file size in bytes
 928 | - `max_archive_files`: Maximum files in archives (zip, tar, etc.)
 929 | - `max_text_length`: Maximum extracted text length
 930 | - `max_pages`: Maximum number of pages to process
 931 | - `max_concurrent_extractions`: Maximum concurrent extraction operations
 932 | 
 933 | ## Caching
 934 | 
 935 | Extraction results are cached by default to improve performance on repeated extractions of identical documents. Control caching behavior through configuration.
 936 | 
 937 | === "Python"
 938 | 
 939 |     ```python
 940 |     from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, extract_file_sync
 941 | 
 942 |     # Enable caching (default)
 943 |     config = ExtractionConfig(use_cache=True)
 944 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 945 | 
 946 |     # Disable caching for a specific extraction
 947 |     config = ExtractionConfig(use_cache=False)
 948 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 949 |     ```
 950 | 
 951 | === "TypeScript"
 952 | 
 953 |     ```typescript
 954 |     import { ExtractionConfig, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 955 | 
 956 |     // Enable caching (default)
 957 |     const config: ExtractionConfig = { useCache: true };
 958 |     const result = await extractFile("document.pdf", null, config);
 959 | 
 960 |     // Disable caching
 961 |     const config2: ExtractionConfig = { useCache: false };
 962 |     const result2 = await extractFile("document.pdf", null, config2);
 963 |     ```
 964 | 
 965 | **CLI Cache Management:**
 966 | 
 967 | ```bash
 968 | # View cache statistics
 969 | kreuzberg cache stats
 970 | 
 971 | # Clear all cached results
 972 | kreuzberg cache clear
 973 | ```
 974 | 
 975 | Caching is transparent and automatic—same input produces cached output instantly on subsequent extractions.
```

### File: `skills\kreuzberg\references\cli-reference.md`

- Size: 12274 bytes
- Modified: SystemTime { intervals: 134209877274128503 }

```markdown
   1 | # Kreuzberg CLI Reference
   2 | 
   3 | Comprehensive command-line interface for the Kreuzberg document intelligence library.
   4 | 
   5 | ## Installation
   6 | 
   7 | Install from crates.io:
   8 | 
   9 | ```bash
  10 | cargo install kreuzberg-cli
  11 | ```
  12 | 
  13 | Or download pre-built binaries from [GitHub Releases](https://github.com/lukasmwirth/kreuzberg/releases).
  14 | 
  15 | ## Commands
  16 | 
  17 | ### extract
  18 | 
  19 | Extract text and structure from a single document.
  20 | 
  21 | ```bash
  22 | kreuzberg extract <path> [FLAGS]
  23 | ```
  24 | 
  25 | **Positional Arguments**
  26 | 
  27 | - `<path>` — Path to the document file
  28 | 
  29 | **Flags**
  30 | 
  31 | - `-c, --config <path>` — Path to config file (TOML, YAML, or JSON). Auto-discovers `kreuzberg.{toml,yaml,json}` in current and parent directories if omitted.
  32 | - `--config-json <json>` — Inline JSON configuration (merged after config file, before CLI flags).
  33 | - `--config-json-base64 <base64>` — Base64-encoded JSON configuration.
  34 | - `-m, --mime-type <type>` — MIME type hint (auto-detected if not provided).
  35 | - `-f, --format <text|json>` — CLI output format (default: `text`). Controls how results display, not extraction content format.
  36 | - `--content-format <plain|markdown|djot|html>` — Extraction content format (default: `plain`). Controls format of extracted content. (Note: `--output-format` is a deprecated alias.)
  37 | - `--ocr <bool>` — Enable OCR processing.
  38 | - `--ocr-backend <BACKEND>` — OCR backend: `tesseract`, `paddle-ocr`, `easyocr`.
  39 | - `--ocr-language <LANG>` — OCR language code.
  40 | - `--ocr-auto-rotate <bool>` — Auto-rotate images before OCR.
  41 | - `--force-ocr <bool>` — Force OCR even if text extraction succeeds.
  42 | - `--disable-ocr <bool>` — Disable OCR entirely (even for images).
  43 | - `--no-cache <bool>` — Disable caching.
  44 | - `--chunk <bool>` — Enable text chunking.
  45 | - `--chunk-size <n>` — Chunk size in characters.
  46 | - `--chunk-overlap <n>` — Chunk overlap in characters.
  47 | - `--chunking-tokenizer <model>` — Tokenizer model for token-based sizing.
  48 | - `--include-structure <bool>` — Include hierarchical document structure.
  49 | - `--quality <bool>` — Enable quality processing.
  50 | - `--detect-language <bool>` — Enable language detection.
  51 | - `--layout` — Enable layout detection (RT-DETR v2). Use `--layout false` to disable.
  52 | - `--layout-confidence <float>` — Layout confidence threshold (0.0-1.0).
  53 | - `--layout-table-model <model>` — Table structure model: `tatr`, `slanet_wired`, `slanet_wireless`, `slanet_plus`, `slanet_auto`, `disabled`.
  54 | - `--acceleration <provider>` — ONNX execution provider: `auto`, `cpu`, `coreml`, `cuda`, `tensorrt`.
  55 | - `--extract-pages <bool>` — Extract pages as separate array.
  56 | - `--page-markers <bool>` — Insert page marker comments.
  57 | - `--extract-images <bool>` — Enable image extraction.
  58 | - `--target-dpi <n>` — Target DPI for images (36-2400).
  59 | - `--pdf-password <pass>` — Password for encrypted PDFs (repeatable).
  60 | - `--pdf-extract-images <bool>` — Extract images from PDF pages.
  61 | - `--pdf-extract-metadata <bool>` — Extract PDF metadata.
  62 | - `--token-reduction <level>` — Token reduction: `off`, `light`, `moderate`, `aggressive`, `maximum`.
  63 | - `--msg-codepage <n>` — Windows codepage fallback for MSG files.
  64 | - `--max-concurrent <n>` — Max parallel extractions in batch mode.
  65 | - `--max-threads <n>` — Cap all internal thread pools.
  66 | - `--cache-namespace <name>` — Cache namespace for tenant isolation.
  67 | - `--cache-ttl-secs <n>` — Per-request cache TTL in seconds.
  68 | 
  69 | **Examples**
  70 | 
  71 | ```bash
  72 | # Extract with default settings
  73 | kreuzberg extract document.pdf
  74 | 
  75 | # Extract with OCR enabled
  76 | kreuzberg extract scanned.pdf --ocr true
  77 | 
  78 | # Extract with specific output format
  79 | kreuzberg extract doc.docx --output-format markdown
  80 | 
  81 | # Extract with inline JSON config
  82 | kreuzberg extract file.pdf --config-json '{"ocr":{"backend":"tesseract"}}'
  83 | 
  84 | # Extract with base64-encoded config
  85 | kreuzberg extract file.pdf --config-json-base64 eyJvY3IiOnsiYmFja2VuZCI6InRlc3NlcmFjdCJ9fQ==
  86 | 
  87 | # Extract and output as JSON
  88 | kreuzberg extract doc.pdf --format json
  89 | 
  90 | # Extract with chunking
  91 | kreuzberg extract large-doc.pdf --chunk true --chunk-size 2000 --chunk-overlap 200
  92 | 
  93 | # Layout-aware markdown extraction
  94 | kreuzberg extract document.pdf --layout --content-format markdown
  95 | 
  96 | # With custom confidence threshold
  97 | kreuzberg extract document.pdf --layout-confidence 0.7 --content-format markdown
  98 | ```
  99 | 
 100 | ### batch
 101 | 
 102 | Batch extract from multiple documents in parallel.
 103 | 
 104 | ```bash
 105 | kreuzberg batch <paths...> [FLAGS]
 106 | ```
 107 | 
 108 | **Positional Arguments**
 109 | 
 110 | - `<paths...>` — One or more document file paths
 111 | 
 112 | **Flags**
 113 | 
 114 | - `-c, --config <path>` — Path to config file (TOML, YAML, or JSON). Auto-discovers `kreuzberg.{toml,yaml,json}` in current and parent directories if omitted.
 115 | - `--config-json <json>` — Inline JSON configuration (merged after config file, before CLI flags).
 116 | - `--config-json-base64 <base64>` — Base64-encoded JSON configuration.
 117 | - `-f, --format <text|json>` — CLI output format (default: `json`). Controls how results display, not extraction content format.
 118 | - All extraction override flags from `extract` are also supported (e.g., `--content-format`, `--ocr`, `--layout`, `--force-ocr`, `--no-cache`, `--quality`, `--acceleration`, etc.). See the `extract` command flags for the full list.
 119 | 
 120 | **Notes**
 121 | 
 122 | - Batch command defaults to JSON output format (unlike `extract` which defaults to text).
 123 | - Does not support `--mime-type` or `--detect-language` flags.
 124 | 
 125 | **Examples**
 126 | 
 127 | ```bash
 128 | # Batch extract multiple PDFs
 129 | kreuzberg batch document1.pdf document2.pdf document3.pdf
 130 | 
 131 | # Batch extract with glob patterns (shell expansion)
 132 | kreuzberg batch *.pdf
 133 | 
 134 | # Batch extract with custom output format
 135 | kreuzberg batch doc1.pdf doc2.pdf --output-format markdown
 136 | 
 137 | # Batch extract with OCR
 138 | kreuzberg batch scanned*.pdf --ocr true
 139 | 
 140 | # Batch extract with text output format
 141 | kreuzberg batch files*.docx --format text
 142 | ```
 143 | 
 144 | ### detect
 145 | 
 146 | Identify MIME type of a file.
 147 | 
 148 | ```bash
 149 | kreuzberg detect <path> [FLAGS]
 150 | ```
 151 | 
 152 | **Positional Arguments**
 153 | 
 154 | - `<path>` — Path to the file
 155 | 
 156 | **Flags**
 157 | 
 158 | - `-f, --format <text|json>` — Output format (default: `text`)
 159 | 
 160 | **Examples**
 161 | 
 162 | ```bash
 163 | # Detect MIME type (text output)
 164 | kreuzberg detect unknown-file.bin
 165 | 
 166 | # Detect MIME type (JSON output)
 167 | kreuzberg detect file.xyz --format json
 168 | ```
 169 | 
 170 | ### version
 171 | 
 172 | Display version information.
 173 | 
 174 | ```bash
 175 | kreuzberg version [FLAGS]
 176 | ```
 177 | 
 178 | **Flags**
 179 | 
 180 | - `-f, --format <text|json>` — Output format (default: `text`)
 181 | 
 182 | **Examples**
 183 | 
 184 | ```bash
 185 | # Show version as text
 186 | kreuzberg version
 187 | 
 188 | # Show version as JSON
 189 | kreuzberg version --format json
 190 | ```
 191 | 
 192 | ### cache
 193 | 
 194 | Manage extraction cache.
 195 | 
 196 | #### cache stats
 197 | 
 198 | Display cache statistics.
 199 | 
 200 | ```bash
 201 | kreuzberg cache stats [FLAGS]
 202 | ```
 203 | 
 204 | **Flags**
 205 | 
 206 | - `--cache-dir <path>` — Cache directory (default: `.kreuzberg` in current directory)
 207 | - `-f, --format <text|json>` — Output format (default: `text`)
 208 | 
 209 | **Examples**
 210 | 
 211 | ```bash
 212 | # Show cache stats
 213 | kreuzberg cache stats
 214 | 
 215 | # Show cache stats as JSON
 216 | kreuzberg cache stats --format json
 217 | 
 218 | # Show stats for specific cache directory
 219 | kreuzberg cache stats --cache-dir /tmp/my-cache
 220 | ```
 221 | 
 222 | #### cache clear
 223 | 
 224 | Clear all cached extractions.
 225 | 
 226 | ```bash
 227 | kreuzberg cache clear [FLAGS]
 228 | ```
 229 | 
 230 | **Flags**
 231 | 
 232 | - `--cache-dir <path>` — Cache directory (default: `.kreuzberg` in current directory)
 233 | - `-f, --format <text|json>` — Output format (default: `text`)
 234 | 
 235 | **Examples**
 236 | 
 237 | ```bash
 238 | # Clear cache
 239 | kreuzberg cache clear
 240 | 
 241 | # Clear specific cache directory
 242 | kreuzberg cache clear --cache-dir /tmp/my-cache
 243 | ```
 244 | 
 245 | ### serve
 246 | 
 247 | Start the API server (requires `api` feature).
 248 | 
 249 | ```bash
 250 | kreuzberg serve [FLAGS]
 251 | ```
 252 | 
 253 | **Flags**
 254 | 
 255 | - `-H, --host <host>` — Host to bind to (e.g., `127.0.0.1` or `0.0.0.0`). CLI arg overrides config file and environment variables.
 256 | - `-p, --port <port>` — Port to bind to. CLI arg overrides config file and environment variables.
 257 | - `-c, --config <path>` — Path to config file (TOML, YAML, or JSON). Auto-discovers `kreuzberg.{toml,yaml,json}` in current and parent directories if omitted.
 258 | 
 259 | **Configuration Precedence**
 260 | 
 261 | 1. CLI arguments (`--host`, `--port`)
 262 | 2. Environment variables (`KREUZBERG_HOST`, `KREUZBERG_PORT`)
 263 | 3. Config file (`[server]` section)
 264 | 4. Built-in defaults (`127.0.0.1:8000`)
 265 | 
 266 | **Examples**
 267 | 
 268 | ```bash
 269 | # Start server with defaults
 270 | kreuzberg serve
 271 | 
 272 | # Start server on specific host and port
 273 | kreuzberg serve --host 0.0.0.0 --port 3000
 274 | 
 275 | # Start server with config file
 276 | kreuzberg serve --config kreuzberg.toml
 277 | 
 278 | # Start server (environment variables override defaults)
 279 | KREUZBERG_HOST=192.168.1.100 KREUZBERG_PORT=8080 kreuzberg serve
 280 | ```
 281 | 
 282 | ### mcp
 283 | 
 284 | Start the Model Context Protocol (MCP) server (requires `mcp` feature).
 285 | 
 286 | ```bash
 287 | kreuzberg mcp [FLAGS]
 288 | ```
 289 | 
 290 | **Flags**
 291 | 
 292 | - `-c, --config <path>` — Path to config file (TOML, YAML, or JSON). Auto-discovers `kreuzberg.{toml,yaml,json}` in current and parent directories if omitted.
 293 | - `--transport <stdio|http>` — Transport mode (default: `stdio`)
 294 | - `--host <host>` — HTTP host for http transport (default: `127.0.0.1`)
 295 | - `--port <port>` — HTTP port for http transport (default: `8001`)
 296 | 
 297 | **Examples**
 298 | 
 299 | ```bash
 300 | # Start MCP server with stdio transport
 301 | kreuzberg mcp
 302 | 
 303 | # Start MCP server with HTTP transport
 304 | kreuzberg mcp --transport http
 305 | 
 306 | # Start MCP server on custom HTTP host/port
 307 | kreuzberg mcp --transport http --host 0.0.0.0 --port 9000
 308 | 
 309 | # Start MCP server with config file
 310 | kreuzberg mcp --config kreuzberg.toml
 311 | ```
 312 | 
 313 | ## Configuration
 314 | 
 315 | ### File Format
 316 | 
 317 | Configuration files support three formats with automatic detection:
 318 | 
 319 | - **TOML** — `.toml` extension (recommended)
 320 | - **YAML** — `.yaml` or `.yml` extension
 321 | - **JSON** — `.json` extension
 322 | 
 323 | ### Configuration Precedence
 324 | 
 325 | Settings are applied in order from highest to lowest priority:
 326 | 
 327 | 1. **Individual CLI flags** (e.g., `--ocr true`, `--output-format markdown`)
 328 | 2. **Inline JSON config** (`--config-json` or `--config-json-base64`)
 329 | 3. **Config file** (explicit `--config path.toml` or auto-discovered)
 330 | 4. **Default values** (built-in library defaults)
 331 | 
 332 | ### Auto-Discovery
 333 | 
 334 | When no config file is specified, Kreuzberg searches for configuration in this order:
 335 | 
 336 | 1. `kreuzberg.toml` in current directory
 337 | 2. `kreuzberg.yaml` in current directory
 338 | 3. `kreuzberg.json` in current directory
 339 | 4. Parent directories (same search pattern, up to filesystem root)
 340 | 
 341 | ### Example Configuration
 342 | 
 343 | ```toml
 344 | # Top-level extraction options
 345 | use_cache = true
 346 | enable_quality_processing = true
 347 | force_ocr = false
 348 | output_format = "markdown"
 349 | 
 350 | # OCR settings
 351 | [ocr]
 352 | backend = "tesseract"
 353 | language = "eng"
 354 | 
 355 | # Chunking settings
 356 | [chunking]
 357 | max_chars = 2000
 358 | max_overlap = 200
 359 | 
 360 | # Language detection
 361 | [language_detection]
 362 | enabled = true
 363 | 
 364 | # Server configuration (for serve command)
 365 | [server]
 366 | host = "127.0.0.1"
 367 | port = 8000
 368 | ```
 369 | 
 370 | ## Exit Codes
 371 | 
 372 | - `0` — Success
 373 | - Non-zero — Error (see stderr for details)
 374 | 
 375 | ## Error Handling
 376 | 
 377 | The CLI validates input and provides clear error messages:
 378 | 
 379 | - **File not found** — Verify path exists and is readable
 380 | - **Invalid MIME type** — Ensure file is accessible and format is supported
 381 | - **Invalid JSON** — Check `--config-json` syntax
 382 | - **Invalid config file** — Verify TOML/YAML/JSON format
 383 | - **Invalid chunk parameters** — Ensure chunk-size > 0 and overlap < chunk-size
 384 | 
 385 | ## Environment Variables
 386 | 
 387 | - `RUST_LOG` — Set logging level (e.g., `RUST_LOG=debug`)
 388 | - `KREUZBERG_HOST` — Server bind host (used by `serve` command)
 389 | - `KREUZBERG_PORT` — Server bind port (used by `serve` command)
 390 | 
 391 | ## Common Patterns
 392 | 
 393 | ### Extract with Custom Configuration
 394 | 
 395 | ```bash
 396 | kreuzberg extract document.pdf \
 397 |   --content-format markdown \
 398 |   --ocr true \
 399 |   --quality true
 400 | ```
 401 | 
 402 | ### Batch Process with Config File
 403 | 
 404 | ```bash
 405 | kreuzberg batch *.pdf --config extraction-config.toml
 406 | ```
 407 | 
 408 | ### CI/CD Integration
 409 | 
 410 | ```bash
 411 | # Extract to JSON for downstream processing
 412 | kreuzberg extract file.pdf --format json | jq '.content'
 413 | 
 414 | # Batch process with error handling
 415 | kreuzberg batch docs/*.pdf --format json || exit 1
 416 | ```
 417 | 
 418 | ### Performance Tuning
 419 | 
 420 | ```bash
 421 | # Disable cache for temporary processing
 422 | kreuzberg extract file.pdf --no-cache true
 423 | 
 424 | # Enable chunking for large documents
 425 | kreuzberg extract large-file.pdf \
 426 |   --chunk true \
 427 |   --chunk-size 5000 \
 428 |   --chunk-overlap 500
 429 | ```
 430 | 
 431 | ## Debugging
 432 | 
 433 | Enable detailed logging:
 434 | 
 435 | ```bash
 436 | RUST_LOG=debug kreuzberg extract document.pdf
 437 | ```
 438 | 
 439 | Check cache statistics:
 440 | 
 441 | ```bash
 442 | kreuzberg cache stats --format json
 443 | ```
 444 | 
 445 | Detect file MIME type:
 446 | 
 447 | ```bash
 448 | kreuzberg detect unknown-file --format json
 449 | ```
```

### File: `skills\kreuzberg\references\configuration.md`

- Size: 12826 bytes
- Modified: SystemTime { intervals: 134209877275277207 }

```markdown
   1 | # Configuration Reference
   2 | 
   3 | Kreuzberg uses a hierarchical configuration system supporting multiple formats and auto-discovery mechanisms. This reference covers all available configuration options, field names across programming languages, and loading strategies.
   4 | 
   5 | ## Supported Formats
   6 | 
   7 | Kreuzberg configurations can be defined in three formats:
   8 | 
   9 | - **TOML** (recommended): `kreuzberg.toml`
  10 | - **YAML**: `kreuzberg.yaml`
  11 | - **JSON**: `kreuzberg.json`
  12 | 
  13 | All formats support the same schema and configuration options.
  14 | 
  15 | ## Auto-Discovery
  16 | 
  17 | When no configuration file is explicitly specified, Kreuzberg searches for configuration files in the following order:
  18 | 
  19 | 1. Current working directory: `kreuzberg.toml`, `kreuzberg.yaml`, `kreuzberg.json`
  20 | 2. Parent directories (recursively up the tree, same file name pattern)
  21 | 
  22 | The first matching configuration file is loaded.
  23 | 
  24 | ## Programmatic Loading
  25 | 
  26 | ### Python
  27 | 
  28 | ```python
  29 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig
  30 | 
  31 | # Load from explicit path
  32 | config = ExtractionConfig.from_file("kreuzberg.toml")
  33 | 
  34 | # Auto-discover configuration
  35 | config = ExtractionConfig.discover()
  36 | ```
  37 | 
  38 | ### Node.js / TypeScript
  39 | 
  40 | ```typescript
  41 | import { ExtractionConfig } from '@kreuzberg/node';
  42 | 
  43 | // Load from explicit path
  44 | const config = ExtractionConfig.fromFile('kreuzberg.toml');
  45 | 
  46 | // Auto-discover configuration
  47 | const config = ExtractionConfig.discover();
  48 | ```
  49 | 
  50 | ### CLI
  51 | 
  52 | ```bash
  53 | # Explicit configuration file
  54 | kreuzberg extract --config kreuzberg.toml document.pdf
  55 | 
  56 | # Auto-discovery (searches default locations)
  57 | kreuzberg extract document.pdf
  58 | ```
  59 | 
  60 | ## Configuration Schema
  61 | 
  62 | The complete TOML schema with all available sections and options:
  63 | 
  64 | ### Top-Level Options
  65 | 
  66 | ```toml
  67 | use_cache = true
  68 | enable_quality_processing = true
  69 | force_ocr = false
  70 | output_format = "markdown"
  71 | result_format = "text"
  72 | max_concurrent_extractions = 4
  73 | ```
  74 | 
  75 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
  76 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
  77 | | `use_cache` | boolean | `true` | Enable caching of extraction results |
  78 | | `enable_quality_processing` | boolean | `true` | Enable post-processing for output quality |
  79 | | `force_ocr` | boolean | `false` | Force OCR processing even for searchable PDFs |
  80 | | `disable_ocr` | boolean | `false` | Disable OCR entirely — image files return empty content instead of errors (v4.7.0+) |
  81 | | `output_format` | string | `"markdown"` | Output format (markdown, html, text) |
  82 | | `result_format` | string | `"text"` | Result format for structured output |
  83 | | `max_concurrent_extractions` | integer | `4` | Maximum concurrent document extractions |
  84 | 
  85 | ### OCR Configuration
  86 | 
  87 | ```toml
  88 | [ocr]
  89 | backend = "tesseract"
  90 | language = "eng"
  91 | ```
  92 | 
  93 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
  94 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
  95 | | `backend` | string | `"tesseract"` | OCR backend (currently tesseract) |
  96 | | `language` | string | `"eng"` | ISO 639-3 language code (eng, deu, fra, etc.) |
  97 | 
  98 | #### Tesseract Configuration
  99 | 
 100 | ```toml
 101 | [ocr.tesseract_config]
 102 | psm = 3
 103 | oem = 3
 104 | min_confidence = 0.0
 105 | output_format = "text"
 106 | enable_table_detection = false
 107 | table_min_confidence = 0.5
 108 | table_column_threshold = 50
 109 | table_row_threshold_ratio = 0.5
 110 | use_cache = true
 111 | ```
 112 | 
 113 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 114 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 115 | | `psm` | integer | `3` | Page Segmentation Mode (0-13) |
 116 | | `oem` | integer | `3` | OCR Engine Mode (0-3) |
 117 | | `min_confidence` | float | `0.0` | Minimum OCR confidence threshold (0.0-1.0) |
 118 | | `output_format` | string | `"text"` | Output format from OCR |
 119 | | `enable_table_detection` | boolean | `false` | Enable table detection during OCR |
 120 | | `table_min_confidence` | float | `0.5` | Minimum confidence for table cells |
 121 | | `table_column_threshold` | integer | `50` | Pixel threshold for column detection |
 122 | | `table_row_threshold_ratio` | float | `0.5` | Row height ratio threshold |
 123 | | `use_cache` | boolean | `true` | Cache OCR results |
 124 | 
 125 | #### Tesseract Preprocessing
 126 | 
 127 | ```toml
 128 | [ocr.tesseract_config.preprocessing]
 129 | target_dpi = 300
 130 | auto_rotate = true
 131 | deskew = true
 132 | denoise = true
 133 | contrast_enhance = true
 134 | binarization_method = "otsu"
 135 | invert_colors = false
 136 | ```
 137 | 
 138 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 139 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 140 | | `target_dpi` | integer | `300` | Target DPI for preprocessing |
 141 | | `auto_rotate` | boolean | `true` | Automatically detect and correct page rotation |
 142 | | `deskew` | boolean | `true` | Correct skewed pages |
 143 | | `denoise` | boolean | `true` | Remove noise from images |
 144 | | `contrast_enhance` | boolean | `true` | Enhance image contrast |
 145 | | `binarization_method` | string | `"otsu"` | Method for image binarization |
 146 | | `invert_colors` | boolean | `false` | Invert image colors if needed |
 147 | 
 148 | ### PDF Options
 149 | 
 150 | ```toml
 151 | [pdf_options]
 152 | extract_images = true
 153 | extract_metadata = true
 154 | 
 155 | [pdf_options.hierarchy]
 156 | enabled = true
 157 | k_clusters = 6
 158 | include_bbox = true
 159 | ocr_coverage_threshold = 0.5
 160 | ```
 161 | 
 162 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 163 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 164 | | `extract_images` | boolean | `true` | Extract images from PDF documents |
 165 | | `extract_metadata` | boolean | `true` | Extract PDF metadata |
 166 | | `hierarchy.enabled` | boolean | `true` | Enable PDF hierarchy extraction (v4.0.0+) |
 167 | | `hierarchy.k_clusters` | integer | `6` | Number of clusters for hierarchy detection |
 168 | | `hierarchy.include_bbox` | boolean | `true` | Include bounding boxes in hierarchy |
 169 | | `hierarchy.ocr_coverage_threshold` | float | `0.5` | OCR coverage threshold for hierarchy (0.0-1.0) |
 170 | 
 171 | ### Image Processing
 172 | 
 173 | ```toml
 174 | [images]
 175 | extract_images = true
 176 | target_dpi = 300
 177 | max_image_dimension = 4096
 178 | auto_adjust_dpi = true
 179 | min_dpi = 72
 180 | max_dpi = 600
 181 | ```
 182 | 
 183 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 184 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 185 | | `extract_images` | boolean | `true` | Extract images from documents |
 186 | | `target_dpi` | integer | `300` | Target DPI for image processing |
 187 | | `max_image_dimension` | integer | `4096` | Maximum image dimension in pixels |
 188 | | `auto_adjust_dpi` | boolean | `true` | Automatically adjust DPI based on image size |
 189 | | `min_dpi` | integer | `72` | Minimum DPI threshold |
 190 | | `max_dpi` | integer | `600` | Maximum DPI threshold |
 191 | 
 192 | ### Chunking Configuration
 193 | 
 194 | ```toml
 195 | [chunking]
 196 | max_chars = 1000
 197 | max_overlap = 200
 198 | 
 199 | [chunking.embedding]
 200 | batch_size = 32
 201 | normalize = true
 202 | show_download_progress = true
 203 | cache_dir = "~/.cache/kreuzberg/embeddings"
 204 | 
 205 | [chunking.embedding.model]
 206 | type = "preset"
 207 | name = "balanced"
 208 | ```
 209 | 
 210 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 211 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 212 | | `max_chars` | integer | `1000` | Maximum characters per chunk |
 213 | | `max_overlap` | integer | `200` | Overlap between consecutive chunks |
 214 | | `embedding.batch_size` | integer | `32` | Batch size for embedding generation |
 215 | | `embedding.normalize` | boolean | `true` | Normalize embeddings to unit length |
 216 | | `embedding.show_download_progress` | boolean | `true` | Show progress when downloading models |
 217 | | `embedding.cache_dir` | string | `"~/.cache/kreuzberg/embeddings"` | Directory for caching embeddings |
 218 | | `embedding.model.type` | string | `"preset"` | Model type: preset, fastembed, or custom |
 219 | | `embedding.model.name` | string | `"balanced"` | Preset model name (balanced, fast, accurate, multilingual) |
 220 | | `embedding.model.model` | string | | FastEmbed model identifier |
 221 | | `embedding.model.model_id` | string | | Custom HuggingFace model ID |
 222 | | `embedding.model.dimensions` | integer | | Embedding dimensions |
 223 | 
 224 | ### Keywords Configuration
 225 | 
 226 | ```toml
 227 | [keywords]
 228 | algorithm = "yake"
 229 | max_keywords = 10
 230 | min_score = 0.0
 231 | ngram_range = [1, 3]
 232 | language = "en"
 233 | ```
 234 | 
 235 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 236 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 237 | | `algorithm` | string | `"yake"` | Keyword extraction algorithm (yake or rake) |
 238 | | `max_keywords` | integer | `10` | Maximum keywords to extract |
 239 | | `min_score` | float | `0.0` | Minimum relevance score for keywords |
 240 | | `ngram_range` | array | `[1, 3]` | N-gram size range [min, max] |
 241 | | `language` | string | `"en"` | Language code for keyword extraction |
 242 | 
 243 | ### Token Reduction
 244 | 
 245 | ```toml
 246 | [token_reduction]
 247 | mode = "off"
 248 | preserve_important_words = true
 249 | ```
 250 | 
 251 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 252 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 253 | | `mode` | string | `"off"` | Mode: off, aggressive, moderate, minimal |
 254 | | `preserve_important_words` | boolean | `true` | Preserve important words during reduction |
 255 | 
 256 | ### Language Detection
 257 | 
 258 | ```toml
 259 | [language_detection]
 260 | enabled = true
 261 | min_confidence = 0.8
 262 | detect_multiple = false
 263 | ```
 264 | 
 265 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 266 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 267 | | `enabled` | boolean | `true` | Enable automatic language detection |
 268 | | `min_confidence` | float | `0.8` | Minimum confidence threshold for detection |
 269 | | `detect_multiple` | boolean | `false` | Detect multiple languages in document |
 270 | 
 271 | ### Post-Processor
 272 | 
 273 | ```toml
 274 | [postprocessor]
 275 | enabled = true
 276 | ```
 277 | 
 278 | | Option | Type | Default | Description |
 279 | |--------|------|---------|-------------|
 280 | | `enabled` | boolean | `true` | Enable post-processing of extracted content |
 281 | 
 282 | ## FileExtractionConfig (Per-File Overrides)
 283 | 
 284 | Passed as an optional parameter to `batch_extract_file` / `batch_extract_bytes` (and their sync variants) to override settings per file in a batch. All fields optional — `None` = use batch default. The separate `_with_configs` functions were removed in v4.5.0.
 285 | 
 286 | **Overridable fields:** `enable_quality_processing`, `ocr`, `force_ocr`, `chunking`, `images`, `pdf_options`, `token_reduction`, `language_detection`, `pages`, `keywords`, `postprocessor`, `html_options`, `result_format`, `output_format`, `include_document_structure`, `layout`.
 287 | 
 288 | **Batch-level only (not overridable):** `max_concurrent_extractions`, `use_cache`, `acceleration`, `security_limits`.
 289 | 
 290 | **Merge semantics:** For each file, `FileExtractionConfig` fields are overlaid on the batch `ExtractionConfig`. `None` falls through to batch default; `Some(value)` replaces the batch default for that file.
 291 | 
 292 | ```toml
 293 | # FileExtractionConfig cannot be specified in config files —
 294 | # it is a programmatic API for per-file overrides at runtime.
 295 | ```
 296 | 
 297 | ## Naming Conventions
 298 | 
 299 | Kreuzberg uses consistent naming conventions across different contexts:
 300 | 
 301 | | Context | Convention | Example |
 302 | |---------|-----------|---------|
 303 | | Python | snake_case | `max_chars`, `pdf_options`, `use_cache` |
 304 | | Node.js / TypeScript | camelCase | `maxChars`, `pdfOptions`, `useCache` |
 305 | | Rust | snake_case | `max_chars`, `pdf_options`, `use_cache` |
 306 | | TOML / YAML / JSON | snake_case | `max_chars`, `pdf_options`, `use_cache` |
 307 | | CLI flags | kebab-case | `--max-chars`, `--pdf-options`, `--use-cache` |
 308 | 
 309 | When switching between languages, apply the appropriate conversion:
 310 | 
 311 | - Python → Node.js: `snake_case` to `camelCase`
 312 | - CLI → Python: `kebab-case` to `snake_case`
 313 | - TOML → Python: No conversion needed (both use `snake_case`)
 314 | 
 315 | ## Environment Variables
 316 | 
 317 | The following environment variables can override configuration:
 318 | 
 319 | | Variable | Purpose | Example |
 320 | |----------|---------|---------|
 321 | | `KREUZBERG_HOST` | Server bind address (serve command) | `127.0.0.1` |
 322 | | `KREUZBERG_PORT` | Server port (serve command) | `8080` |
 323 | 
 324 | ## Configuration Merging
 325 | 
 326 | Configuration sources are merged in priority order (highest to lowest):
 327 | 
 328 | 1. **CLI flags** (highest priority)
 329 | 2. **Inline JSON configuration** (programmatic)
 330 | 3. **Configuration file** (lowest priority)
 331 | 
 332 | Later sources override earlier ones. For example, a CLI flag `--max-chars 2000` overrides `max_chars = 1000` in the configuration file.
 333 | 
 334 | ## Example Configurations
 335 | 
 336 | ### Minimal Configuration
 337 | 
 338 | ```toml
 339 | use_cache = true
 340 | enable_quality_processing = true
 341 | 
 342 | [ocr]
 343 | backend = "tesseract"
 344 | language = "eng"
 345 | ```
 346 | 
 347 | ### High-Quality PDF Extraction
 348 | 
 349 | ```toml
 350 | use_cache = true
 351 | enable_quality_processing = true
 352 | force_ocr = false
 353 | 
 354 | [ocr]
 355 | backend = "tesseract"
 356 | language = "eng"
 357 | 
 358 | [ocr.tesseract_config]
 359 | psm = 3
 360 | oem = 3
 361 | enable_table_detection = true
 362 | table_min_confidence = 0.7
 363 | 
 364 | [pdf_options]
 365 | extract_images = true
 366 | extract_metadata = true
 367 | 
 368 | [pdf_options.hierarchy]
 369 | enabled = true
 370 | k_clusters = 6
 371 | 
 372 | [images]
 373 | extract_images = true
 374 | target_dpi = 300
 375 | ```
 376 | 
 377 | ### Semantic Search Configuration
 378 | 
 379 | ```toml
 380 | [chunking]
 381 | max_chars = 800
 382 | max_overlap = 150
 383 | 
 384 | [chunking.embedding]
 385 | batch_size = 32
 386 | normalize = true
 387 | cache_dir = "~/.cache/kreuzberg/embeddings"
 388 | 
 389 | [chunking.embedding.model]
 390 | type = "preset"
 391 | name = "accurate"
 392 | 
 393 | [keywords]
 394 | algorithm = "yake"
 395 | max_keywords = 15
 396 | ```
 397 | 
 398 | ## Field Name Reference
 399 | 
 400 | Critical field names to use in configuration files:
 401 | 
 402 | - `max_chars` (NOT `max_characters`)
 403 | - `max_overlap` (NOT `overlap`)
 404 | - `table_min_confidence`
 405 | - `table_column_threshold`
 406 | - `table_row_threshold_ratio`
 407 | - `ocr_coverage_threshold`
 408 | - `k_clusters`
 409 | - `include_bbox`
 410 | - `enable_table_detection`
 411 | - `auto_rotate`
 412 | - `auto_adjust_dpi`
 413 | - `show_download_progress`
 414 | - `min_confidence`
 415 | - `detect_multiple`
 416 | 
 417 | Always verify field names against the source configuration file when adding new options.
```

### File: `skills\kreuzberg\references\nodejs-api.md`

- Size: 34103 bytes
- Modified: SystemTime { intervals: 134209877278435550 }

```markdown
   1 | # Node.js/TypeScript API Reference
   2 | 
   3 | ## Overview
   4 | 
   5 | **Package**: `@kreuzberg/node` — A high-performance TypeScript SDK built on a Rust core for document intelligence and content extraction.
   6 | 
   7 | Supports both **ESM** (`import`) and **CommonJS** (`require`):
   8 | 
   9 | ```typescript
  10 | // ESM
  11 | import { extractFile, batchExtractFiles } from '@kreuzberg/node';
  12 | 
  13 | // CommonJS
  14 | const { extractFile, batchExtractFiles } = require('@kreuzberg/node');
  15 | ```
  16 | 
  17 | **Current Version**: 4.2.14
  18 | 
  19 | ---
  20 | 
  21 | ## Core Extraction Functions
  22 | 
  23 | All extraction functions return `ExtractionResult` containing extracted content, metadata, tables, and optional chunks/images.
  24 | 
  25 | ### Single File Extraction
  26 | 
  27 | #### `extractFile(filePath, mimeType?, config?): Promise<ExtractionResult>`
  28 | 
  29 | Extract content from a single file asynchronously.
  30 | 
  31 | ```typescript
  32 | import { extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
  33 | 
  34 | // Auto-detect MIME type from file extension
  35 | const result = await extractFile('document.pdf');
  36 | console.log(result.content);
  37 | 
  38 | // Explicit MIME type
  39 | const result2 = await extractFile('document.pdf', 'application/pdf');
  40 | 
  41 | // With configuration
  42 | const result3 = await extractFile('document.pdf', null, {
  43 |   chunking: {
  44 |     maxChars: 1000,
  45 |     maxOverlap: 200,
  46 |   },
  47 | });
  48 | ```
  49 | 
  50 | **Parameters**:
  51 | 
  52 | - `filePath: string` — Path to the file to extract
  53 | - `mimeType?: string | null` — Optional MIME type hint (auto-detect if null)
  54 | - `config?: ExtractionConfig` — Optional extraction configuration
  55 | 
  56 | **Returns**: `Promise<ExtractionResult>`
  57 | 
  58 | **Throws**: `ParsingError`, `OcrError`, `ValidationError`, `KreuzbergError`
  59 | 
  60 | #### `extractFileSync(filePath, mimeType?, config?): ExtractionResult`
  61 | 
  62 | Extract content from a single file synchronously.
  63 | 
  64 | ```typescript
  65 | import { extractFileSync } from '@kreuzberg/node';
  66 | 
  67 | const result = extractFileSync('document.pdf');
  68 | console.log(result.content);
  69 | ```
  70 | 
  71 | **Parameters**: Same as `extractFile()`
  72 | 
  73 | **Returns**: `ExtractionResult`
  74 | 
  75 | ---
  76 | 
  77 | ### Raw Bytes Extraction
  78 | 
  79 | #### `extractBytes(data, mimeType, config?): Promise<ExtractionResult>`
  80 | 
  81 | Extract content from raw bytes (Buffer or Uint8Array) asynchronously.
  82 | 
  83 | ```typescript
  84 | import { extractBytes } from '@kreuzberg/node';
  85 | import { readFile } from 'fs/promises';
  86 | 
  87 | const data = await readFile('document.pdf');
  88 | const result = await extractBytes(data, 'application/pdf');
  89 | console.log(result.content);
  90 | ```
  91 | 
  92 | **Parameters**:
  93 | 
  94 | - `data: Buffer | Uint8Array` — Raw file content
  95 | - `mimeType: string` — MIME type (required)
  96 | - `config?: ExtractionConfig` — Optional configuration
  97 | 
  98 | **Returns**: `Promise<ExtractionResult>`
  99 | 
 100 | #### `extractBytesSync(data, mimeType, config?): ExtractionResult`
 101 | 
 102 | Extract content from raw bytes synchronously.
 103 | 
 104 | ```typescript
 105 | import { extractBytesSync } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 106 | import { readFileSync } from 'fs';
 107 | 
 108 | const data = readFileSync('document.pdf');
 109 | const result = extractBytesSync(data, 'application/pdf');
 110 | ```
 111 | 
 112 | **Parameters**: Same as `extractBytes()`
 113 | 
 114 | **Returns**: `ExtractionResult`
 115 | 
 116 | ---
 117 | 
 118 | ### Batch Extraction (Recommended)
 119 | 
 120 | For processing multiple documents, batch APIs provide superior performance and memory management.
 121 | 
 122 | #### `batchExtractFiles(paths, config?): Promise<ExtractionResult[]>`
 123 | 
 124 | Extract content from multiple files in parallel (asynchronous).
 125 | 
 126 | ```typescript
 127 | import { batchExtractFiles } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 128 | 
 129 | const files = ['doc1.pdf', 'doc2.docx', 'doc3.xlsx'];
 130 | const results = await batchExtractFiles(files);
 131 | 
 132 | results.forEach((result, i) => {
 133 |   console.log(`${files[i]}: ${result.content.substring(0, 100)}...`);
 134 | });
 135 | ```
 136 | 
 137 | **Parameters**:
 138 | 
 139 | - `paths: string[]` — Array of file paths
 140 | - `config?: ExtractionConfig` — Configuration (applied to all files)
 141 | 
 142 | **Returns**: `Promise<ExtractionResult[]>` — Results in same order as input
 143 | 
 144 | #### `batchExtractFilesSync(paths, config?): ExtractionResult[]`
 145 | 
 146 | Extract content from multiple files synchronously.
 147 | 
 148 | ```typescript
 149 | import { batchExtractFilesSync } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 150 | 
 151 | const files = ['doc1.pdf', 'doc2.docx', 'doc3.xlsx'];
 152 | const results = batchExtractFilesSync(files);
 153 | ```
 154 | 
 155 | **Parameters**: Same as `batchExtractFiles()`
 156 | 
 157 | **Returns**: `ExtractionResult[]`
 158 | 
 159 | #### `batchExtractBytes(dataList, mimeTypes, config?): Promise<ExtractionResult[]>`
 160 | 
 161 | Extract content from multiple byte arrays in parallel (asynchronous).
 162 | 
 163 | ```typescript
 164 | import { batchExtractBytes } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 165 | import { readFile } from 'fs/promises';
 166 | 
 167 | const files = ['doc1.pdf', 'doc2.docx'];
 168 | const dataList = await Promise.all(files.map(f => readFile(f)));
 169 | const mimeTypes = ['application/pdf', 'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document'];
 170 | 
 171 | const results = await batchExtractBytes(dataList, mimeTypes);
 172 | ```
 173 | 
 174 | **Parameters**:
 175 | 
 176 | - `dataList: Uint8Array[]` — Array of file contents
 177 | - `mimeTypes: string[]` — MIME types (one per item, must match length)
 178 | - `config?: ExtractionConfig` — Configuration (applied to all items)
 179 | 
 180 | **Returns**: `Promise<ExtractionResult[]>`
 181 | 
 182 | #### `batchExtractBytesSync(dataList, mimeTypes, config?): ExtractionResult[]`
 183 | 
 184 | Extract content from multiple byte arrays synchronously.
 185 | 
 186 | ```typescript
 187 | import { batchExtractBytesSync } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 188 | import { readFileSync } from 'fs';
 189 | 
 190 | const dataList = ['doc1.pdf', 'doc2.docx'].map(f => readFileSync(f));
 191 | const mimeTypes = ['application/pdf', 'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document'];
 192 | 
 193 | const results = batchExtractBytesSync(dataList, mimeTypes);
 194 | ```
 195 | 
 196 | **Parameters**: Same as `batchExtractBytes()`
 197 | 
 198 | **Returns**: `ExtractionResult[]`
 199 | 
 200 | #### `batchExtractFilesWithConfigs(paths, fileConfigs, config?): Promise<ExtractionResult[]>`
 201 | 
 202 | Extract multiple files with per-file configuration overrides (asynchronous).
 203 | 
 204 | ```typescript
 205 | const results = await batchExtractFilesWithConfigs(
 206 |   ['report.pdf', 'scanned.pdf'],
 207 |   [null, { forceOcr: true, ocr: { backend: 'tesseract', language: 'deu' } }],
 208 | );
 209 | ```
 210 | 
 211 | **Parameters**:
 212 | 
 213 | - `paths: string[]` — File paths
 214 | - `fileConfigs: (FileExtractionConfig | null)[]` — Per-file configs (null = use batch defaults)
 215 | - `config?: ExtractionConfig` — Batch-level configuration
 216 | 
 217 | #### `batchExtractFilesWithConfigsSync(paths, fileConfigs, config?): ExtractionResult[]`
 218 | 
 219 | Synchronous variant.
 220 | 
 221 | #### `batchExtractBytesWithConfigs(dataList, mimeTypes, fileConfigs, config?): Promise<ExtractionResult[]>`
 222 | 
 223 | Extract multiple byte arrays with per-file overrides (asynchronous).
 224 | 
 225 | #### `batchExtractBytesWithConfigsSync(dataList, mimeTypes, fileConfigs, config?): ExtractionResult[]`
 226 | 
 227 | Synchronous variant.
 228 | 
 229 | ---
 230 | 
 231 | ## Worker Pool APIs
 232 | 
 233 | Worker pools enable concurrent extraction using Node.js worker threads for CPU-bound processing.
 234 | 
 235 | ### `createWorkerPool(size?): WorkerPool`
 236 | 
 237 | Create a worker pool for concurrent extraction.
 238 | 
 239 | ```typescript
 240 | import { createWorkerPool } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 241 | 
 242 | // Create pool with default size (number of CPU cores)
 243 | const pool = createWorkerPool();
 244 | 
 245 | // Create pool with specific size
 246 | const pool4 = createWorkerPool(4);
 247 | ```
 248 | 
 249 | **Parameters**:
 250 | 
 251 | - `size?: number` — Number of workers (defaults to CPU core count)
 252 | 
 253 | **Returns**: `WorkerPool` — Opaque handle for use with worker extraction functions
 254 | 
 255 | ### `extractFileInWorker(pool, filePath, mimeType?, config?): Promise<ExtractionResult>`
 256 | 
 257 | Extract a single file using a worker from the pool.
 258 | 
 259 | ```typescript
 260 | import { createWorkerPool, extractFileInWorker, closeWorkerPool } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 261 | 
 262 | const pool = createWorkerPool(4);
 263 | 
 264 | try {
 265 |   const files = ['doc1.pdf', 'doc2.docx', 'doc3.xlsx'];
 266 |   const results = await Promise.all(
 267 |     files.map(f => extractFileInWorker(pool, f))
 268 |   );
 269 | 
 270 |   results.forEach((r, i) => {
 271 |     console.log(`${files[i]}: ${r.content.substring(0, 100)}...`);
 272 |   });
 273 | } finally {
 274 |   await closeWorkerPool(pool);
 275 | }
 276 | ```
 277 | 
 278 | **Parameters**:
 279 | 
 280 | - `pool: WorkerPool` — Worker pool instance
 281 | - `filePath: string` — File path
 282 | - `mimeType?: string | null` — Optional MIME type
 283 | - `config?: ExtractionConfig` — Optional configuration
 284 | 
 285 | **Returns**: `Promise<ExtractionResult>`
 286 | 
 287 | ### `batchExtractFilesInWorker(pool, paths, config?): Promise<ExtractionResult[]>`
 288 | 
 289 | Extract multiple files using the worker pool for concurrent processing.
 290 | 
 291 | ```typescript
 292 | import { createWorkerPool, batchExtractFilesInWorker, closeWorkerPool } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 293 | 
 294 | const pool = createWorkerPool(4);
 295 | 
 296 | try {
 297 |   const files = ['invoice1.pdf', 'invoice2.pdf', 'invoice3.pdf'];
 298 |   const results = await batchExtractFilesInWorker(pool, files, {
 299 |     ocr: { backend: 'tesseract', language: 'eng' }
 300 |   });
 301 | 
 302 |   const total = results.reduce((sum, r) => sum + extractAmount(r.content), 0);
 303 |   console.log(`Total: $${total}`);
 304 | } finally {
 305 |   await closeWorkerPool(pool);
 306 | }
 307 | ```
 308 | 
 309 | **Parameters**:
 310 | 
 311 | - `pool: WorkerPool` — Worker pool instance
 312 | - `paths: string[]` — File paths
 313 | - `config?: ExtractionConfig` — Configuration (applied to all files)
 314 | 
 315 | **Returns**: `Promise<ExtractionResult[]>`
 316 | 
 317 | ### `getWorkerPoolStats(pool): WorkerPoolStats`
 318 | 
 319 | Get statistics about a worker pool.
 320 | 
 321 | ```typescript
 322 | import { createWorkerPool, getWorkerPoolStats } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 323 | 
 324 | const pool = createWorkerPool(4);
 325 | const stats = getWorkerPoolStats(pool);
 326 | 
 327 | console.log(`Pool size: ${stats.size}`);
 328 | console.log(`Active workers: ${stats.activeWorkers}`);
 329 | console.log(`Queued tasks: ${stats.queuedTasks}`);
 330 | ```
 331 | 
 332 | **Parameters**:
 333 | 
 334 | - `pool: WorkerPool` — Worker pool instance
 335 | 
 336 | **Returns**: `WorkerPoolStats`
 337 | 
 338 | ### `closeWorkerPool(pool): Promise<void>`
 339 | 
 340 | Close a worker pool and shut down all worker threads.
 341 | 
 342 | ```typescript
 343 | import { createWorkerPool, closeWorkerPool } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 344 | 
 345 | const pool = createWorkerPool(4);
 346 | 
 347 | try {
 348 |   // Use pool
 349 | } finally {
 350 |   await closeWorkerPool(pool);
 351 | }
 352 | ```
 353 | 
 354 | **Parameters**:
 355 | 
 356 | - `pool: WorkerPool` — Worker pool instance to close
 357 | 
 358 | **Returns**: `Promise<void>`
 359 | 
 360 | ---
 361 | 
 362 | ## Configuration Interface
 363 | 
 364 | ### `ExtractionConfig`
 365 | 
 366 | Main configuration object controlling extraction behavior.
 367 | 
 368 | ```typescript
 369 | interface ExtractionConfig {
 370 |   // Caching and processing
 371 |   useCache?: boolean;                            // Default: true
 372 |   enableQualityProcessing?: boolean;            // Default: false
 373 | 
 374 |   // OCR configuration
 375 |   ocr?: OcrConfig;                              // OCR settings
 376 |   forceOcr?: boolean;                           // Default: false
 377 | 
 378 |   // Document processing
 379 |   chunking?: ChunkingConfig;                    // Break into chunks
 380 |   images?: ImageExtractionConfig;               // Image extraction
 381 |   pdfOptions?: PdfConfig;                       // PDF-specific options
 382 |   tokenReduction?: TokenReductionConfig;        // Token optimization
 383 |   languageDetection?: LanguageDetectionConfig;  // Language detection
 384 |   postprocessor?: PostProcessorConfig;          // Post-processing
 385 |   htmlOptions?: HtmlConversionOptions;          // HTML conversion
 386 |   keywords?: KeywordConfig;                     // Keyword extraction
 387 |   pages?: PageExtractionConfig;                 // Page extraction
 388 | 
 389 |   // Output control
 390 |   maxConcurrentExtractions?: number;            // Default: 4
 391 |   outputFormat?: 'plain' | 'markdown' | 'djot' | 'html';  // Default: 'plain'
 392 |   resultFormat?: 'unified' | 'element_based';  // Default: 'unified'
 393 | }
 394 | ```
 395 | 
 396 | ### `FileExtractionConfig`
 397 | 
 398 | Per-file overrides for batch operations. All fields optional (omitted = use batch default).
 399 | 
 400 | ```typescript
 401 | interface FileExtractionConfig {
 402 |   enableQualityProcessing?: boolean;
 403 |   ocr?: OcrConfig;
 404 |   forceOcr?: boolean;
 405 |   chunking?: ChunkingConfig;
 406 |   images?: ImageExtractionConfig;
 407 |   pdfOptions?: PdfConfig;
 408 |   tokenReduction?: TokenReductionConfig;
 409 |   languageDetection?: LanguageDetectionConfig;
 410 |   pages?: PageExtractionConfig;
 411 |   keywords?: KeywordConfig;
 412 |   postprocessor?: PostProcessorConfig;
 413 |   outputFormat?: 'plain' | 'markdown' | 'djot' | 'html';
 414 |   resultFormat?: 'unified' | 'element_based';
 415 |   includeDocumentStructure?: boolean;
 416 | }
 417 | ```
 418 | 
 419 | Excluded (batch-level only): `maxConcurrentExtractions`, `useCache`, `securityLimits`.
 420 | 
 421 | ### `ChunkingConfig`
 422 | 
 423 | Configuration for breaking documents into chunks (useful for RAG and vector databases).
 424 | 
 425 | ```typescript
 426 | interface ChunkingConfig {
 427 |   maxChars?: number;          // Max characters per chunk (default: 4096)
 428 |   maxOverlap?: number;        // Overlap between chunks (default: 512)
 429 |   chunkSize?: number;         // Alternative unit (mutually exclusive with maxChars)
 430 |   chunkOverlap?: number;      // Alternative unit (mutually exclusive with maxOverlap)
 431 |   preset?: string;            // Named preset ('default', 'aggressive', 'minimal')
 432 |   embedding?: Record<string, unknown>;  // Embedding config
 433 |   enabled?: boolean;          // Enable chunking (default: true when config provided)
 434 | }
 435 | ```
 436 | 
 437 | **Key Point**: Use `maxChars` and `maxOverlap`, NOT `maxCharacters` or `overlap`.
 438 | 
 439 | ### `OcrConfig`
 440 | 
 441 | Configuration for optical character recognition.
 442 | 
 443 | ```typescript
 444 | interface OcrConfig {
 445 |   backend: string;              // OCR backend name (e.g., 'tesseract')
 446 |   language?: string;            // Language code (e.g., 'eng', 'deu')
 447 |   tesseractConfig?: TesseractConfig;
 448 | }
 449 | 
 450 | interface TesseractConfig {
 451 |   psm?: number;                 // Page Segmentation Mode (0-13)
 452 |   enableTableDetection?: boolean;
 453 |   tesseditCharWhitelist?: string;  // Character whitelist
 454 | }
 455 | ```
 456 | 
 457 | ### `ImageExtractionConfig`
 458 | 
 459 | Configuration for extracting and optimizing images.
 460 | 
 461 | ```typescript
 462 | interface ImageExtractionConfig {
 463 |   extractImages?: boolean;      // Default: true
 464 |   targetDpi?: number;          // Target DPI (default: 150)
 465 |   maxImageDimension?: number;  // Max width/height in pixels (default: 2000)
 466 |   autoAdjustDpi?: boolean;     // Auto-adjust DPI (default: true)
 467 |   minDpi?: number;             // Minimum DPI (default: 72)
 468 |   maxDpi?: number;             // Maximum DPI (default: 300)
 469 | }
 470 | ```
 471 | 
 472 | ### `PdfConfig`
 473 | 
 474 | PDF-specific extraction options.
 475 | 
 476 | ```typescript
 477 | interface PdfConfig {
 478 |   extractImages?: boolean;      // Default: true
 479 |   passwords?: string[];         // Passwords for encrypted PDFs
 480 |   extractMetadata?: boolean;    // Default: true
 481 |   hierarchy?: HierarchyConfig;  // Hierarchy extraction
 482 | }
 483 | ```
 484 | 
 485 | ### `LanguageDetectionConfig`
 486 | 
 487 | Configuration for automatic language detection.
 488 | 
 489 | ```typescript
 490 | interface LanguageDetectionConfig {
 491 |   enabled?: boolean;            // Default: true
 492 |   minConfidence?: number;       // Threshold 0.0-1.0 (default: 0.5)
 493 |   detectMultiple?: boolean;     // Detect multiple languages (default: false)
 494 | }
 495 | ```
 496 | 
 497 | ### `TokenReductionConfig`
 498 | 
 499 | Configuration for optimizing token usage.
 500 | 
 501 | ```typescript
 502 | interface TokenReductionConfig {
 503 |   mode?: string;                // 'aggressive' or 'conservative' (default: 'conservative')
 504 |   preserveImportantWords?: boolean;  // Default: true
 505 | }
 506 | ```
 507 | 
 508 | ### `KeywordConfig`
 509 | 
 510 | Configuration for keyword extraction.
 511 | 
 512 | ```typescript
 513 | interface KeywordConfig {
 514 |   algorithm?: 'yake' | 'rake';  // Default: 'yake'
 515 |   maxKeywords?: number;         // Maximum keywords (default: 10)
 516 |   minScore?: number;            // Minimum relevance score (default: 0.1)
 517 |   ngramRange?: [number, number];  // N-gram range (default: [1, 3])
 518 |   language?: string;            // Language code (default: 'en')
 519 |   yakeParams?: YakeParams;
 520 |   rakeParams?: RakeParams;
 521 | }
 522 | ```
 523 | 
 524 | ### `PageExtractionConfig`
 525 | 
 526 | Configuration for page-level content tracking.
 527 | 
 528 | ```typescript
 529 | interface PageExtractionConfig {
 530 |   extractPages?: boolean;       // Extract as separate pages array
 531 |   insertPageMarkers?: boolean;  // Insert page markers in content
 532 |   markerFormat?: string;        // Marker format with {page_num} placeholder
 533 | }
 534 | ```
 535 | 
 536 | ### `HtmlConversionOptions`
 537 | 
 538 | Configuration for HTML to Markdown conversion.
 539 | 
 540 | ```typescript
 541 | interface HtmlConversionOptions {
 542 |   headingStyle?: 'atx' | 'underlined' | 'atx_closed';
 543 |   listIndentType?: 'spaces' | 'tabs';
 544 |   listIndentWidth?: number;
 545 |   bullets?: string;
 546 |   strongEmSymbol?: string;
 547 |   escapeAsterisks?: boolean;
 548 |   escapeUnderscores?: boolean;
 549 |   escapeMisc?: boolean;
 550 |   escapeAscii?: boolean;
 551 |   codeLanguage?: string;
 552 |   autolinks?: boolean;
 553 |   defaultTitle?: boolean;
 554 |   brInTables?: boolean;
 555 |   hocrSpatialTables?: boolean;
 556 |   highlightStyle?: 'double_equal' | 'html' | 'bold' | 'none';
 557 |   extractMetadata?: boolean;
 558 |   whitespaceMode?: 'normalized' | 'strict';
 559 |   stripNewlines?: boolean;
 560 |   wrap?: boolean;
 561 |   wrapWidth?: number;
 562 |   convertAsInline?: boolean;
 563 |   subSymbol?: string;
 564 |   supSymbol?: string;
 565 |   newlineStyle?: 'spaces' | 'backslash';
 566 |   codeBlockStyle?: 'indented' | 'backticks' | 'tildes';
 567 |   keepInlineImagesIn?: string[];
 568 |   encoding?: string;
 569 |   debug?: boolean;
 570 |   stripTags?: string[];
 571 |   preserveTags?: string[];
 572 |   preprocessing?: HtmlPreprocessingOptions;
 573 | }
 574 | ```
 575 | 
 576 | ---
 577 | 
 578 | ## Result Types
 579 | 
 580 | ### `ExtractionResult`
 581 | 
 582 | Complete extraction result from document processing.
 583 | 
 584 | ```typescript
 585 | interface ExtractionResult {
 586 |   // Main content
 587 |   content: string;
 588 | 
 589 |   // Document type
 590 |   mimeType: string;
 591 | 
 592 |   // Metadata (format-specific)
 593 |   metadata: Metadata;
 594 | 
 595 |   // Extracted structures
 596 |   tables: Table[];
 597 | 
 598 |   // Optional processed data
 599 |   detectedLanguages: string[] | null;
 600 |   chunks: Chunk[] | null;        // From chunking config
 601 |   images: ExtractedImage[] | null;  // From image extraction
 602 |   elements?: Element[] | null;   // From element_based result format
 603 |   pages?: PageContent[] | null;  // From page extraction
 604 |   extractedKeywords?: ExtractedKeyword[] | null;  // Extracted keywords with scores
 605 |   qualityScore?: number | null;  // Overall extraction quality (0.0-1.0)
 606 |   processingWarnings?: ProcessingWarning[];  // Non-fatal warnings from pipeline
 607 | }
 608 | ```
 609 | 
 610 | ### `Table`
 611 | 
 612 | Extracted table data with cell structure.
 613 | 
 614 | ```typescript
 615 | interface Table {
 616 |   cells: string[][];    // 2D array of cell contents (rows × columns)
 617 |   markdown: string;     // Markdown representation
 618 |   pageNumber: number;   // 1-indexed page number
 619 | }
 620 | ```
 621 | 
 622 | ### `Chunk`
 623 | 
 624 | Text chunk for RAG or vector database indexing.
 625 | 
 626 | ```typescript
 627 | interface Chunk {
 628 |   content: string;
 629 |   embedding?: number[] | null;  // Vector embedding if computed
 630 |   metadata: ChunkMetadata;
 631 | }
 632 | 
 633 | interface ChunkMetadata {
 634 |   byteStart: number;      // UTF-8 byte offset in original text
 635 |   byteEnd: number;        // UTF-8 byte offset
 636 |   tokenCount?: number | null;
 637 |   chunkIndex: number;     // Zero-based index
 638 |   totalChunks: number;    // Total number of chunks
 639 |   firstPage?: number | null;   // 1-indexed, if page tracking enabled
 640 |   lastPage?: number | null;
 641 | }
 642 | ```
 643 | 
 644 | ### `ExtractedImage`
 645 | 
 646 | Image extracted from document.
 647 | 
 648 | ```typescript
 649 | interface ExtractedImage {
 650 |   data: Uint8Array;      // Raw image bytes
 651 |   format: string;        // Format (e.g., 'png', 'jpeg', 'tiff')
 652 |   imageIndex: number;    // Sequential index (0-indexed)
 653 |   pageNumber?: number | null;
 654 |   width?: number | null;
 655 |   height?: number | null;
 656 |   colorspace?: string | null;
 657 |   bitsPerComponent?: number | null;
 658 |   isMask: boolean;
 659 |   description?: string | null;
 660 |   ocrResult?: ExtractionResult | null;  // OCR result if processed
 661 | }
 662 | ```
 663 | 
 664 | ### `PageContent`
 665 | 
 666 | Per-page content when page extraction is enabled.
 667 | 
 668 | ```typescript
 669 | interface PageContent {
 670 |   pageNumber: number;    // 1-indexed
 671 |   content: string;       // Page text content
 672 |   tables: Table[];       // Tables on this page
 673 |   images: ExtractedImage[];  // Images on this page
 674 | }
 675 | ```
 676 | 
 677 | ### `ExtractedKeyword`
 678 | 
 679 | Extracted keyword with relevance score and position information.
 680 | 
 681 | ```typescript
 682 | interface ExtractedKeyword {
 683 |   text: string;           // Keyword text
 684 |   score: number;          // Relevance score (0.0-1.0)
 685 |   algorithm: string;      // Algorithm used ("tfidf", "textrank", "yake", etc.)
 686 |   positions?: number[] | null;  // Character positions in content (if available)
 687 | }
 688 | ```
 689 | 
 690 | ### `ProcessingWarning`
 691 | 
 692 | Non-fatal warning encountered during document processing.
 693 | 
 694 | ```typescript
 695 | interface ProcessingWarning {
 696 |   source: string;         // Component that generated the warning
 697 |   message: string;        // Warning message describing the issue
 698 | }
 699 | ```
 700 | 
 701 | ### `Metadata`
 702 | 
 703 | Extraction result metadata (format-specific).
 704 | 
 705 | ```typescript
 706 | interface Metadata {
 707 |   // Common fields
 708 |   language?: string | null;
 709 |   date?: string | null;
 710 |   subject?: string | null;
 711 |   format_type?: 'pdf' | 'excel' | 'email' | 'pptx' | 'archive' | 'image' | 'xml' | 'text' | 'html' | 'ocr';
 712 | 
 713 |   // PDF metadata
 714 |   title?: string | null;
 715 |   author?: string | null;
 716 |   creator?: string | null;
 717 |   producer?: string | null;
 718 |   creation_date?: string | null;
 719 |   modification_date?: string | null;
 720 |   page_count?: number;
 721 | 
 722 |   // Excel metadata
 723 |   sheet_count?: number;
 724 |   sheet_names?: string[];
 725 | 
 726 |   // Email metadata
 727 |   from_email?: string | null;
 728 |   from_name?: string | null;
 729 |   to_emails?: string[];
 730 |   cc_emails?: string[];
 731 |   bcc_emails?: string[];
 732 |   message_id?: string | null;
 733 |   attachments?: string[];
 734 | 
 735 |   // Image metadata
 736 |   width?: number;
 737 |   height?: number;
 738 |   exif?: Record<string, string>;
 739 | 
 740 |   // OCR metadata
 741 |   psm?: number;
 742 |   output_format?: string;
 743 |   table_count?: number;
 744 | 
 745 |   // HTML metadata
 746 |   canonical_url?: string | null;
 747 |   html_language?: string | null;
 748 |   text_direction?: 'ltr' | 'rtl' | 'auto' | null;
 749 |   open_graph?: Record<string, string>;
 750 |   twitter_card?: Record<string, string>;
 751 |   meta_tags?: Record<string, string>;
 752 |   html_headers?: HeaderMetadata[];
 753 |   html_links?: LinkMetadata[];
 754 |   html_images?: HtmlImageMetadata[];
 755 |   structured_data?: StructuredData[];
 756 | 
 757 |   // Text metadata
 758 |   line_count?: number;
 759 |   word_count?: number;
 760 |   character_count?: number;
 761 |   headers?: string[] | null;
 762 |   links?: [string, string][] | null;
 763 |   code_blocks?: [string, string][] | null;
 764 | 
 765 |   // Page structure
 766 |   page_structure?: PageStructure | null;
 767 | 
 768 |   // Additional typed fields
 769 |   category?: string | null;
 770 |   tags?: string[];
 771 |   document_version?: string | null;
 772 |   abstract_text?: string | null;
 773 | 
 774 |   // Custom fields from postprocessors
 775 |   [key: string]: unknown;
 776 | }
 777 | ```
 778 | 
 779 | ---
 780 | 
 781 | ## Error Handling
 782 | 
 783 | ### Error Classes
 784 | 
 785 | ```typescript
 786 | import {
 787 |   KreuzbergError,
 788 |   ParsingError,
 789 |   OcrError,           // Note: camelCase, not "OCRError"
 790 |   ValidationError,
 791 |   MissingDependencyError,
 792 |   CacheError,
 793 |   ImageProcessingError,
 794 |   PluginError,
 795 |   ErrorCode,
 796 | } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 797 | ```
 798 | 
 799 | **Error Hierarchy**:
 800 | 
 801 | - `KreuzbergError` — Base class for all Kreuzberg errors
 802 |   - `ParsingError` — Document format invalid or corrupted
 803 |   - `OcrError` — OCR processing failed
 804 |   - `ValidationError` — Extraction validation failed
 805 |   - `MissingDependencyError` — Required dependency unavailable
 806 |   - `CacheError` — Cache operation failed
 807 |   - `ImageProcessingError` — Image extraction or processing failed
 808 |   - `PluginError` — Plugin registration or execution failed
 809 | 
 810 | ### Error Diagnostics
 811 | 
 812 | ```typescript
 813 | import {
 814 |   classifyError,
 815 |   getErrorCodeDescription,
 816 |   getErrorCodeName,
 817 |   getLastErrorCode,
 818 |   getLastPanicContext,
 819 | } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 820 | 
 821 | try {
 822 |   const result = await extractFile('document.pdf');
 823 | } catch (error) {
 824 |   const classification = classifyError(error.message);
 825 |   console.log(`Error code: ${getErrorCodeName(classification.code)}`);
 826 |   console.log(`Description: ${getErrorCodeDescription(classification.code)}`);
 827 |   console.log(`Confidence: ${classification.confidence}`);
 828 | }
 829 | ```
 830 | 
 831 | ### `ErrorCode` Enum
 832 | 
 833 | ```typescript
 834 | enum ErrorCode {
 835 |   Success = 0,
 836 |   GenericError = 1,
 837 |   Panic = 2,
 838 |   InvalidArgument = 3,
 839 |   IoError = 4,
 840 |   ParsingError = 5,
 841 |   OcrError = 6,
 842 |   MissingDependency = 7,
 843 | }
 844 | ```
 845 | 
 846 | ---
 847 | 
 848 | ## Plugin System
 849 | 
 850 | ### Post-Processors
 851 | 
 852 | Custom post-processors can enrich extraction results without failing the extraction if they encounter errors.
 853 | 
 854 | #### `registerPostProcessor(processor): void`
 855 | 
 856 | Register a custom post-processor.
 857 | 
 858 | ```typescript
 859 | import { registerPostProcessor, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 860 | 
 861 | const processor = {
 862 |   name() {
 863 |     return 'my_processor';
 864 |   },
 865 | 
 866 |   async process(result) {
 867 |     // Enrich result with custom metadata
 868 |     result.metadata['custom_field'] = 'value';
 869 |     return result;
 870 |   },
 871 | 
 872 |   processingStage() {
 873 |     return 'late';  // 'early', 'middle', or 'late'
 874 |   },
 875 | 
 876 |   async initialize() {
 877 |     // Called once when registered
 878 |   },
 879 | 
 880 |   async shutdown() {
 881 |     // Called when unregistered
 882 |   },
 883 | };
 884 | 
 885 | registerPostProcessor(processor);
 886 | const result = await extractFile('document.pdf');
 887 | ```
 888 | 
 889 | #### `unregisterPostProcessor(name): void`
 890 | 
 891 | Remove a registered post-processor.
 892 | 
 893 | ```typescript
 894 | import { unregisterPostProcessor } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 895 | 
 896 | unregisterPostProcessor('my_processor');
 897 | ```
 898 | 
 899 | #### `listPostProcessors(): string[]`
 900 | 
 901 | List all registered post-processor names.
 902 | 
 903 | ```typescript
 904 | import { listPostProcessors } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 905 | 
 906 | const processors = listPostProcessors();
 907 | console.log('Registered processors:', processors);
 908 | ```
 909 | 
 910 | #### `clearPostProcessors(): void`
 911 | 
 912 | Unregister all post-processors.
 913 | 
 914 | ```typescript
 915 | import { clearPostProcessors } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 916 | 
 917 | clearPostProcessors();
 918 | ```
 919 | 
 920 | ### Validators
 921 | 
 922 | Custom validators check extraction results and fail the extraction if validation fails (unlike post-processors).
 923 | 
 924 | #### `registerValidator(validator): void`
 925 | 
 926 | Register a custom validator.
 927 | 
 928 | ```typescript
 929 | import { registerValidator, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 930 | 
 931 | const validator = {
 932 |   name() {
 933 |     return 'content_length_validator';
 934 |   },
 935 | 
 936 |   validate(result) {
 937 |     if (result.content.length < 10) {
 938 |       throw new Error('Content too short');
 939 |     }
 940 |   },
 941 | 
 942 |   priority() {
 943 |     return 100;  // Higher = runs first
 944 |   },
 945 | 
 946 |   shouldValidate(result) {
 947 |     return result.mimeType === 'application/pdf';  // Conditional validation
 948 |   },
 949 | 
 950 |   async initialize() {
 951 |     // Called once when registered
 952 |   },
 953 | 
 954 |   async shutdown() {
 955 |     // Called when unregistered
 956 |   },
 957 | };
 958 | 
 959 | registerValidator(validator);
 960 | const result = await extractFile('document.pdf');
 961 | ```
 962 | 
 963 | #### `unregisterValidator(name): void`
 964 | 
 965 | Remove a registered validator.
 966 | 
 967 | ```typescript
 968 | import { unregisterValidator } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 969 | 
 970 | unregisterValidator('content_length_validator');
 971 | ```
 972 | 
 973 | #### `listValidators(): string[]`
 974 | 
 975 | List all registered validator names.
 976 | 
 977 | ```typescript
 978 | import { listValidators } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 979 | 
 980 | const validators = listValidators();
 981 | ```
 982 | 
 983 | #### `clearValidators(): void`
 984 | 
 985 | Unregister all validators.
 986 | 
 987 | ```typescript
 988 | import { clearValidators } from '@kreuzberg/node';
 989 | 
 990 | clearValidators();
 991 | ```
 992 | 
 993 | ### OCR Backends
 994 | 
 995 | Custom OCR backends can be registered to handle image text extraction.
 996 | 
 997 | #### `registerOcrBackend(backend): void`
 998 | 
 999 | Register a custom OCR backend.
1000 | 
1001 | ```typescript
1002 | import { registerOcrBackend, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1003 | 
1004 | const backend = {
1005 |   name() {
1006 |     return 'my-ocr';
1007 |   },
1008 | 
1009 |   supportedLanguages() {
1010 |     return ['eng', 'deu', 'fra'];
1011 |   },
1012 | 
1013 |   async processImage(imageBytes, language) {
1014 |     // imageBytes: Uint8Array or Base64 string
1015 |     const buffer = typeof imageBytes === 'string'
1016 |       ? Buffer.from(imageBytes, 'base64')
1017 |       : Buffer.from(imageBytes);
1018 |
