1019 |     // Process and extract text
1020 |     return {
1021 |       content: 'extracted text',
1022 |       mime_type: 'text/plain',
1023 |       metadata: { confidence: 0.95, language },
1024 |       tables: [],
1025 |     };
1026 |   },
1027 | 
1028 |   async initialize() {
1029 |     // Load models, setup resources
1030 |   },
1031 | 
1032 |   async shutdown() {
1033 |     // Cleanup resources
1034 |   },
1035 | };
1036 | 
1037 | registerOcrBackend(backend);
1038 | ```
1039 | 
1040 | #### `GutenOcrBackend`
1041 | 
1042 | Built-in OCR backend implementation using Guten-OCR.
1043 | 
1044 | ```typescript
1045 | import { GutenOcrBackend, registerOcrBackend, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1046 | 
1047 | const backend = new GutenOcrBackend();
1048 | await backend.initialize();
1049 | registerOcrBackend(backend);
1050 | 
1051 | const result = await extractFile('scanned.pdf', null, {
1052 |   ocr: { backend: 'guten-ocr', language: 'eng' }
1053 | });
1054 | ```
1055 | 
1056 | #### `unregisterOcrBackend(name): void`
1057 | 
1058 | Remove a registered OCR backend.
1059 | 
1060 | ```typescript
1061 | import { unregisterOcrBackend } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1062 | 
1063 | unregisterOcrBackend('my-ocr');
1064 | ```
1065 | 
1066 | #### `listOcrBackends(): string[]`
1067 | 
1068 | List all registered OCR backend names.
1069 | 
1070 | ```typescript
1071 | import { listOcrBackends } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1072 | 
1073 | const backends = listOcrBackends();
1074 | ```
1075 | 
1076 | #### `clearOcrBackends(): void`
1077 | 
1078 | Unregister all OCR backends.
1079 | 
1080 | ```typescript
1081 | import { clearOcrBackends } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1082 | 
1083 | clearOcrBackends();
1084 | ```
1085 | 
1086 | ---
1087 | 
1088 | ## MIME Type Utilities
1089 | 
1090 | ### `detectMimeType(data): string | null`
1091 | 
1092 | Detect MIME type from file content (magic bytes).
1093 | 
1094 | ```typescript
1095 | import { detectMimeType } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1096 | import { readFileSync } from 'fs';
1097 | 
1098 | const data = readFileSync('document');
1099 | const mimeType = detectMimeType(data);
1100 | console.log(`Detected MIME type: ${mimeType}`);
1101 | ```
1102 | 
1103 | ### `detectMimeTypeFromPath(filePath): string | null`
1104 | 
1105 | Detect MIME type from file extension.
1106 | 
1107 | ```typescript
1108 | import { detectMimeTypeFromPath } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1109 | 
1110 | const mimeType = detectMimeTypeFromPath('document.pdf');
1111 | console.log(`MIME type: ${mimeType}`);  // 'application/pdf'
1112 | ```
1113 | 
1114 | ### `getExtensionsForMime(mimeType): string[]`
1115 | 
1116 | Get file extensions for a MIME type.
1117 | 
1118 | ```typescript
1119 | import { getExtensionsForMime } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1120 | 
1121 | const extensions = getExtensionsForMime('application/pdf');
1122 | console.log(`Extensions: ${extensions}`);  // ['.pdf']
1123 | ```
1124 | 
1125 | ### `validateMimeType(mimeType): boolean`
1126 | 
1127 | Check if a MIME type is valid.
1128 | 
1129 | ```typescript
1130 | import { validateMimeType } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1131 | 
1132 | if (validateMimeType('application/pdf')) {
1133 |   console.log('Valid MIME type');
1134 | }
1135 | ```
1136 | 
1137 | ---
1138 | 
1139 | ## Configuration Loading
1140 | 
1141 | ### `ExtractionConfig.fromFile(filePath): ExtractionConfig`
1142 | 
1143 | Load extraction configuration from a file (JSON, YAML, or TOML).
1144 | 
1145 | ```typescript
1146 | import { ExtractionConfig, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1147 | 
1148 | const config = ExtractionConfig.fromFile('./kreuzberg.toml');
1149 | const result = await extractFile('document.pdf', null, config);
1150 | ```
1151 | 
1152 | ### `ExtractionConfig.discover(): ExtractionConfig | null`
1153 | 
1154 | Auto-discover extraction configuration file in current and parent directories.
1155 | 
1156 | ```typescript
1157 | import { ExtractionConfig, extractFile } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1158 | 
1159 | // Searches for kreuzberg.{toml,yaml,json} in current directory and parents
1160 | const config = ExtractionConfig.discover();
1161 | if (config) {
1162 |   const result = await extractFile('document.pdf', null, config);
1163 | }
1164 | ```
1165 | 
1166 | ---
1167 | 
1168 | ## Embeddings
1169 | 
1170 | ### `getEmbeddingPreset(name): EmbeddingPreset | null`
1171 | 
1172 | Get a named embedding model preset.
1173 | 
1174 | ```typescript
1175 | import { getEmbeddingPreset } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1176 | 
1177 | const preset = getEmbeddingPreset('default');
1178 | if (preset) {
1179 |   console.log(`Model: ${preset.modelName}`);
1180 |   console.log(`Dimensions: ${preset.dimensions}`);
1181 | }
1182 | ```
1183 | 
1184 | ### `listEmbeddingPresets(): string[]`
1185 | 
1186 | List all available embedding presets.
1187 | 
1188 | ```typescript
1189 | import { listEmbeddingPresets } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1190 | 
1191 | const presets = listEmbeddingPresets();
1192 | console.log('Available presets:', presets);
1193 | ```
1194 | 
1195 | ### `EmbeddingPreset`
1196 | 
1197 | Type definition for embedding model presets.
1198 | 
1199 | ```typescript
1200 | interface EmbeddingPreset {
1201 |   name: string;           // Preset name (e.g., "fast", "balanced", "quality", "multilingual")
1202 |   chunkSize: number;      // Recommended chunk size in characters
1203 |   overlap: number;        // Recommended overlap in characters
1204 |   modelName: string;      // Model identifier (e.g., "AllMiniLML6V2Q", "BGEBaseENV15")
1205 |   dimensions: number;     // Embedding vector dimensions
1206 |   description: string;    // Human-readable description
1207 | }
1208 | ```
1209 | 
1210 | ---
1211 | 
1212 | ## Plugin Protocols
1213 | 
1214 | ### `PostProcessorProtocol`
1215 | 
1216 | Interface for custom post-processors.
1217 | 
1218 | ```typescript
1219 | interface PostProcessorProtocol {
1220 |   name(): string;
1221 | 
1222 |   process(result: ExtractionResult): ExtractionResult | Promise<ExtractionResult>;
1223 | 
1224 |   processingStage?(): ProcessingStage;  // 'early' | 'middle' | 'late'
1225 | 
1226 |   initialize?(): void | Promise<void>;
1227 | 
1228 |   shutdown?(): void | Promise<void>;
1229 | }
1230 | ```
1231 | 
1232 | ### `ValidatorProtocol`
1233 | 
1234 | Interface for custom validators.
1235 | 
1236 | ```typescript
1237 | interface ValidatorProtocol {
1238 |   name(): string;
1239 | 
1240 |   validate(result: ExtractionResult): void | Promise<void>;
1241 | 
1242 |   priority?(): number;  // Higher = runs first
1243 | 
1244 |   shouldValidate?(result: ExtractionResult): boolean;
1245 | 
1246 |   initialize?(): void | Promise<void>;
1247 | 
1248 |   shutdown?(): void | Promise<void>;
1249 | }
1250 | ```
1251 | 
1252 | ### `OcrBackendProtocol`
1253 | 
1254 | Interface for custom OCR backends.
1255 | 
1256 | ```typescript
1257 | interface OcrBackendProtocol {
1258 |   name(): string;
1259 | 
1260 |   supportedLanguages(): string[];
1261 | 
1262 |   processImage(
1263 |     imageBytes: Uint8Array | string,
1264 |     language: string,
1265 |   ): Promise<{
1266 |     content: string;
1267 |     mime_type: string;
1268 |     metadata: Record<string, unknown>;
1269 |     tables: unknown[];
1270 |   }>;
1271 | 
1272 |   initialize?(): void | Promise<void>;
1273 | 
1274 |   shutdown?(): void | Promise<void>;
1275 | }
1276 | ```
1277 | 
1278 | ---
1279 | 
1280 | ## Supported Document Formats
1281 | 
1282 | - **Documents**: PDF, DOCX, PPTX, XLSX, DOC, PPT
1283 | - **Text**: Markdown, Plain Text, XML, JSON, YAML, TOML
1284 | - **Web**: HTML (converted to Markdown)
1285 | - **Email**: EML, MSG
1286 | - **Images**: PNG, JPEG, TIFF (with OCR support)
1287 | - **Archives**: ZIP, TAR, GZIP (file listing)
1288 | 
1289 | ---

1299 |   clearDocumentExtractors,
1300 | } from '@kreuzberg/node';
1301 |

1312 | ---

1322 |   ExtractionConfig,
1323 |   ExtractionResult,

1325 |   KeywordConfig,
1326 |   LanguageDetectionConfig,

1328 |   OcrConfig,

1331 |   PdfConfig,

1333 |   Table,
1334 |   TokenReductionConfig,

1336 |   WorkerPool,
1337 |   WorkerPoolStats,
1338 |   EmbeddingPreset,
1339 |   // ... and many more
1340 | };
1341 | ```
1342 | 
1343 | ---
1344 | 
1345 | ## Best Practices
1346 | 
1347 | 1. **Use batch APIs for multiple documents**: `batchExtractFiles()` provides superior performance vs. calling `extractFile()` in a loop.
1348 | 
1349 | 2. **Enable chunking for RAG/vector DB**: Set `chunking` config to automatically break documents into overlapping chunks.
1350 | 
1351 | 3. **Use worker pools for high-concurrency scenarios**: Distribute CPU-bound work across multiple threads for 4+ concurrent extractions.
1352 | 
1353 | 4. **Configure language detection**: Enable automatic language detection for multilingual documents.
1354 | 
1355 | 5. **Register validators early**: Set up validators before calling extraction functions to catch quality issues immediately.
1356 | 
1357 | 6. **Use specific MIME types**: Provide explicit MIME types when available to avoid detection overhead.
1358 | 
1359 | 7. **Clean up resources**: Always call `closeWorkerPool()` when done to prevent resource leaks.
1360 | 
1361 | 8. **Handle extraction errors gracefully**: Catch specific error types (`ParsingError`, `OcrError`, etc.) for appropriate error handling.
1362 | 
1363 | ---
1364 | 
1365 | ## Version
1366 | 
1367 | **Package Version**: 4.2.14
```

```markdown
   1 | # Language Bindings Reference
   2 | 
   3 | Kreuzberg provides native bindings for multiple programming languages, each with precompiled binaries for x86_64 and aarch64 on Linux and macOS. This reference covers installation and basic usage for each binding.
   4 | 
   5 | ## Go
   6 | 
   7 | **Installation:**
   8 | 
   9 | ```bash
  10 | go get github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/packages/go/v4
  11 | ```
  12 | 
  13 | **Basic Extraction:**
  14 | 
  15 | ```go
  16 | package main
  17 | 
  18 | import (
  19 |     "context"
  20 |     "fmt"
  21 |     "github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/packages/go/v4/kreuzberg"
  22 | )
  23 | 
  24 | func main() {
  25 |     ctx := context.Background()
  26 |     result, err := kreuzberg.ExtractFile(ctx, "document.pdf", nil)
  27 |     if err != nil {
  28 |         panic(err)
  29 |     }
  30 |     fmt.Println(result.Content)
  31 | }
  32 | ```
  33 | 
  34 | See the [Go binding documentation](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/tree/main/packages/go) for complete API reference.
  35 | 
  36 | ## Ruby
  37 | 
  38 | **Installation:**
  39 | 
  40 | ```bash
  41 | gem install kreuzberg
  42 | ```
  43 | 
  44 | Or in your Gemfile:
  45 | 
  46 | ```ruby
  47 | gem 'kreuzberg'
  48 | ```
  49 | 
  50 | **Basic Extraction:**
  51 | 
  52 | ```ruby
  53 | require 'kreuzberg'
  54 | 
  55 | result = Kreuzberg.extract_file_sync('document.pdf')
  56 | puts result.content
  57 | ```
  58 | 
  59 | See the [Ruby binding documentation](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/tree/main/packages/ruby) for complete API reference.
  60 | 
  61 | ## Java
  62 | 
  63 | **Installation:**
  64 | Add to your Maven `pom.xml`:
  65 | 
  66 | ```xml
  67 | <dependency>
  68 |     <groupId>dev.kreuzberg</groupId>
  69 |     <artifactId>kreuzberg</artifactId>
  70 |     <version>4.2.x</version>
  71 | </dependency>
  72 | ```
  73 | 
  74 | **Basic Extraction:**
  75 | 
  76 | ```java
  77 | import dev.kreuzberg.Kreuzberg;
  78 | import dev.kreuzberg.ExtractionResult;
  79 | 
  80 | public class Example {
  81 |     public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
  82 |         ExtractionResult result = Kreuzberg.extractFile("document.pdf");
  83 |         System.out.println(result.getContent());
  84 |     }
  85 | }
  86 | ```
  87 | 
  88 | See the [Java binding documentation](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/tree/main/packages/java) for complete API reference.
  89 | 
  90 | ## C
  91 | 
  92 | **Installation:**
  93 | 
  94 | ```bash
  95 | dotnet add package Kreuzberg
  96 | ```
  97 | 
  98 | **Basic Extraction:**
  99 | 
 100 | ```csharp
 101 | using Kreuzberg;
 102 | 
 103 | var result = KreuzbergClient.ExtractFileSync("document.pdf");
 104 | Console.WriteLine(result.Content);
 105 | ```
 106 | 
 107 | See the [C# binding documentation](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/tree/main/packages/csharp) for complete API reference.
 108 | 
 109 | ## PHP
 110 | 
 111 | **Installation:**
 112 | 
 113 | ```bash
 114 | composer require kreuzberg/kreuzberg
 115 | ```
 116 | 
 117 | **Basic Extraction:**
 118 | 
 119 | ```php
 120 | <?php
 121 | require 'vendor/autoload.php';
 122 | 
 123 | use Kreuzberg\Kreuzberg;
 124 | 
 125 | $kreuzberg = new Kreuzberg();
 126 | $result = $kreuzberg->extractFile('document.pdf');
 127 | echo $result->content;
 128 | ```
 129 | 
 130 | See the [PHP binding documentation](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/tree/main/packages/php) for complete API reference.
 131 | 
 132 | ## Elixir
 133 | 
 134 | **Installation:**
 135 | Add to your `mix.exs` dependencies:
 136 | 
 137 | ```elixir
 138 | def deps do
 139 |   [
 140 |     kreuzberg: "~> 4.2"
 141 |   ]
 142 | end
 143 | ```
 144 | 
 145 | **Basic Extraction:**
 146 | 
 147 | ```elixir
 148 | {:ok, result} = Kreuzberg.extract_file("document.pdf")
 149 | IO.puts(result.content)
 150 | ```
 151 | 
 152 | See the [Elixir binding documentation](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/tree/main/packages/elixir) for complete API reference.
 153 | 
 154 | ## WebAssembly (WASM)
 155 | 
 156 | **Installation:**
 157 | 
 158 | ```bash
 159 | npm install @kreuzberg/wasm
 160 | ```
 161 | 
 162 | **Basic Extraction:**
 163 | 
 164 | ```typescript
 165 | import { extractBytes } from '@kreuzberg/wasm';
 166 | 
 167 | const fileData = await fs.promises.readFile('document.pdf');
 168 | const result = await extractBytes(fileData, 'application/pdf');
 169 | console.log(result.content);
 170 | ```
 171 | 
 172 | Supports browsers, Deno, and Cloudflare Workers.
 173 | 
 174 | See the [WASM binding documentation](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg/tree/main/packages/typescript) for complete API reference.
 175 | 
 176 | ## Docker
 177 | 
 178 | **Installation:**
 179 | Pull the official image from GitHub Container Registry:
 180 | 
 181 | ```bash
 182 | docker pull ghcr.io/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg
 183 | ```
 184 | 
 185 | **API Server Mode:**
 186 | 
 187 | ```bash
 188 | docker run -p 8000:8000 ghcr.io/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg serve --host 0.0.0.0
 189 | ```
 190 | 
 191 | **CLI Mode:**
 192 | 
 193 | ```bash
 194 | docker run -v $(pwd):/data ghcr.io/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg extract /data/document.pdf
 195 | ```
 196 | 
 197 | **MCP Server Mode:**
 198 | 
 199 | ```bash
 200 | docker run -i ghcr.io/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg mcp
 201 | ```
 202 | 
 203 | Image sizes:
 204 | 
 205 | - Core image: 1.0-1.3GB
 206 | - Full image: ~1.0-1.3GB
 207 | 
 208 | See the [Docker guide](https://docs.kreuzberg.dev/guides/docker/) for deployment details.
 209 | 
 210 | ## Platform Support
 211 | 
 212 | All language bindings include precompiled binaries for x86_64 and aarch64 on Linux and macOS. Windows support varies by binding. Refer to the main [README](https://github.com/kreuzberg-dev/kreuzberg) for platform compatibility matrix.
```

### File: `skills\kreuzberg\references\python-api.md`

- Size: 43298 bytes
- Modified: SystemTime { intervals: 134209877293832570 }

```markdown
   1 | # Kreuzberg Python API Reference
   2 | 
   3 | Comprehensive documentation for the Kreuzberg Python API. All extraction logic and heavy lifting is implemented in high-performance Rust, with Python adding OCR backends (EasyOCR, PaddleOCR) and custom post-processor support.
   4 | 
   5 | ## Extraction Functions
   6 | 
   7 | ### Synchronous File Extraction
   8 | 
   9 | ```python
  10 | def extract_file_sync(
  11 |     file_path: str | Path,
  12 |     mime_type: str | None = None,
  13 |     config: ExtractionConfig | None = None,
  14 |     *,
  15 |     easyocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
  16 |     paddleocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
  17 | ) -> ExtractionResult
  18 | ```
  19 | 
  20 | Extract content from a file (synchronous).
  21 | 
  22 | **Parameters:**
  23 | 
  24 | - `file_path` (str | Path): Path to the file
  25 | - `mime_type` (str | None): Optional MIME type hint (auto-detected if None)
  26 | - `config` (ExtractionConfig | None): Extraction configuration (uses defaults if None)
  27 | - `easyocr_kwargs` (dict | None): EasyOCR initialization options (languages, use_gpu, beam_width, etc.)
  28 | - `paddleocr_kwargs` (dict | None): PaddleOCR initialization options (lang, use_angle_cls, show_log, etc.)
  29 | 
  30 | **Returns:** ExtractionResult with content, metadata, and tables
  31 | 
  32 | **Example:**
  33 | 
  34 | ```python
  35 | from kreuzberg import extract_file_sync, ExtractionConfig, OcrConfig, TesseractConfig
  36 | 
  37 | # Basic usage
  38 | result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf")
  39 | 
  40 | # With Tesseract configuration
  41 | config = ExtractionConfig(
  42 |     ocr=OcrConfig(
  43 |         backend="tesseract",
  44 |         language="eng",
  45 |         tesseract_config=TesseractConfig(psm=6, enable_table_detection=True),
  46 |     )
  47 | )
  48 | result = extract_file_sync("invoice.pdf", config=config)
  49 | 
  50 | # With EasyOCR custom options
  51 | config = ExtractionConfig(ocr=OcrConfig(backend="easyocr", language="eng"))
  52 | result = extract_file_sync("scanned.pdf", config=config, easyocr_kwargs={"use_gpu": True})
  53 | ```
  54 | 
  55 | ### Asynchronous File Extraction
  56 | 
  57 | ```python
  58 | async def extract_file(
  59 |     file_path: str | Path,
  60 |     mime_type: str | None = None,
  61 |     config: ExtractionConfig | None = None,
  62 |     *,
  63 |     easyocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
  64 |     paddleocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
  65 | ) -> ExtractionResult
  66 | ```
  67 | 
  68 | Extract content from a file (asynchronous). Same parameters and behavior as `extract_file_sync`.
  69 | 
  70 | ### Synchronous Bytes Extraction
  71 | 
  72 | ```python
  73 | def extract_bytes_sync(
  74 |     data: bytes | bytearray,
  75 |     mime_type: str,
  76 |     config: ExtractionConfig | None = None,
  77 |     *,
  78 |     easyocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
  79 |     paddleocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
  80 | ) -> ExtractionResult
  81 | ```
  82 | 
  83 | Extract content from bytes (synchronous).
  84 | 
  85 | **Parameters:**
  86 | 
  87 | - `data` (bytes | bytearray): File content as bytes or bytearray
  88 | - `mime_type` (str): MIME type of the data (required for format detection)
  89 | - `config` (ExtractionConfig | None): Extraction configuration
  90 | - `easyocr_kwargs` (dict | None): EasyOCR initialization options
  91 | - `paddleocr_kwargs` (dict | None): PaddleOCR initialization options
  92 | 
  93 | **Returns:** ExtractionResult with content, metadata, and tables
  94 | 
  95 | ### Asynchronous Bytes Extraction
  96 | 
  97 | ```python
  98 | async def extract_bytes(
  99 |     data: bytes | bytearray,
 100 |     mime_type: str,
 101 |     config: ExtractionConfig | None = None,
 102 |     *,
 103 |     easyocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 104 |     paddleocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 105 | ) -> ExtractionResult
 106 | ```
 107 | 
 108 | Extract content from bytes (asynchronous). Same parameters and behavior as `extract_bytes_sync`.
 109 | 
 110 | ### Batch File Extraction
 111 | 
 112 | ```python
 113 | async def batch_extract_files(
 114 |     paths: list[str | Path],
 115 |     config: ExtractionConfig | None = None,
 116 |     *,
 117 |     easyocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 118 |     paddleocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 119 | ) -> list[ExtractionResult]
 120 | ```
 121 | 
 122 | Extract content from multiple files in parallel (asynchronous).
 123 | 
 124 | **Parameters:**
 125 | 
 126 | - `paths` (list[str | Path]): List of file paths
 127 | - `config` (ExtractionConfig | None): Extraction configuration
 128 | - `easyocr_kwargs` (dict | None): EasyOCR initialization options
 129 | - `paddleocr_kwargs` (dict | None): PaddleOCR initialization options
 130 | 
 131 | **Returns:** List of ExtractionResults (one per file)
 132 | 
 133 | ### Batch File Extraction (Synchronous)
 134 | 
 135 | ```python
 136 | def batch_extract_files_sync(
 137 |     paths: list[str | Path],
 138 |     config: ExtractionConfig | None = None,
 139 |     *,
 140 |     easyocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 141 |     paddleocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 142 | ) -> list[ExtractionResult]
 143 | ```
 144 | 
 145 | Extract content from multiple files in parallel (synchronous).
 146 | 
 147 | ### Batch Bytes Extraction
 148 | 
 149 | ```python
 150 | async def batch_extract_bytes(
 151 |     data_list: list[bytes | bytearray],
 152 |     mime_types: list[str],
 153 |     config: ExtractionConfig | None = None,
 154 |     *,
 155 |     easyocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 156 |     paddleocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 157 | ) -> list[ExtractionResult]
 158 | ```
 159 | 
 160 | Extract content from multiple byte arrays in parallel (asynchronous).
 161 | 
 162 | **Parameters:**
 163 | 
 164 | - `data_list` (list[bytes | bytearray]): List of file contents as bytes/bytearray
 165 | - `mime_types` (list[str]): List of MIME types (one per data item)
 166 | - `config` (ExtractionConfig | None): Extraction configuration
 167 | - `easyocr_kwargs` (dict | None): EasyOCR initialization options
 168 | - `paddleocr_kwargs` (dict | None): PaddleOCR initialization options
 169 | 
 170 | **Returns:** List of ExtractionResults (one per data item)
 171 | 
 172 | ### Batch Bytes Extraction (Synchronous)
 173 | 
 174 | ```python
 175 | def batch_extract_bytes_sync(
 176 |     data_list: list[bytes | bytearray],
 177 |     mime_types: list[str],
 178 |     config: ExtractionConfig | None = None,
 179 |     *,
 180 |     easyocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 181 |     paddleocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 182 | ) -> list[ExtractionResult]
 183 | ```
 184 | 
 185 | Extract content from multiple byte arrays in parallel (synchronous).
 186 | 
 187 | ### Per-File Config in Batch Functions
 188 | 
 189 | As of v4.5.0, per-file configuration overrides are passed as an optional `file_configs` parameter on the unified batch functions:
 190 | 
 191 | ```python
 192 | def batch_extract_files_sync(
 193 |     paths: list[str | Path],
 194 |     config: ExtractionConfig | None = None,
 195 |     *,
 196 |     file_configs: list[FileExtractionConfig | None] | None = None,
 197 |     easyocr_kwargs: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 198 | ) -> list[ExtractionResult]
 199 | ```
 200 | 
 201 | The `file_configs` list must have the same length as `paths`. Each element is either a `FileExtractionConfig` override or `None` to use batch defaults. The same parameter is available on `batch_extract_files`, `batch_extract_bytes_sync`, and `batch_extract_bytes`.
 202 | 
 203 | > **Note:** The separate `batch_extract_files_with_configs_sync` / `batch_extract_files_with_configs` / `batch_extract_bytes_with_configs_sync` / `batch_extract_bytes_with_configs` functions have been removed in v4.5.0.
 204 | 
 205 | ## Configuration Classes
 206 | 
 207 | ### ExtractionConfig
 208 | 
 209 | Main extraction configuration for document processing. All attributes are optional and use sensible defaults when not specified.
 210 | 
 211 | **Attributes:**
 212 | 
 213 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 214 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 215 | | `use_cache` | bool | True | Enable caching of extraction results to improve performance on repeated extractions |
 216 | | `enable_quality_processing` | bool | True | Enable quality post-processing to clean and normalize extracted text |
 217 | | `ocr` | OcrConfig \| None | None | OCR configuration for extracting text from images. None = OCR disabled |
 218 | | `force_ocr` | bool | False | Force OCR processing even for searchable PDFs that contain extractable text |
 219 | | `chunking` | ChunkingConfig \| None | None | Text chunking configuration for dividing content into manageable chunks. None = disabled |
 220 | | `images` | ImageExtractionConfig \| None | None | Image extraction configuration for extracting images FROM documents. None = no extraction |
 221 | | `pdf_options` | PdfConfig \| None | None | PDF-specific options like password handling and metadata extraction |
 222 | | `token_reduction` | TokenReductionConfig \| None | None | Token reduction configuration for reducing token count in extracted content |
 223 | | `language_detection` | LanguageDetectionConfig \| None | None | Language detection configuration for identifying document language(s) |
 224 | | `keywords` | KeywordConfig \| None | None | Keyword extraction configuration for identifying important terms and phrases |
 225 | | `postprocessor` | PostProcessorConfig \| None | None | Post-processor configuration for custom text processing |
 226 | | `max_concurrent_extractions` | int \| None | num_cpus * 2 | Maximum concurrent extractions in batch operations |
 227 | | `html_options` | HtmlConversionOptions \| None | None | HTML conversion options for converting documents to markdown |
 228 | | `pages` | PageConfig \| None | None | Page extraction configuration for tracking page boundaries |
 229 | | `security_limits` | dict[str, int] \| None | None | Security limits configuration |
 230 | | `result_format` | str | "unified" | Result format: "unified" or "element_based" |
 231 | | `output_format` | str | "plain" | Output content format: "plain", "markdown", "djot", or "html" |
 232 | 
 233 | **Example:**
 234 | 
 235 | ```python
 236 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, ChunkingConfig, OcrConfig
 237 | 
 238 | # Basic extraction with defaults
 239 | config = ExtractionConfig()
 240 | 
 241 | # Enable chunking with 512-char chunks and 100-char overlap
 242 | config = ExtractionConfig(chunking=ChunkingConfig(max_chars=512, max_overlap=100))
 243 | 
 244 | # Enable OCR with Tesseract
 245 | config = ExtractionConfig(ocr=OcrConfig(backend="tesseract", language="eng"))
 246 | 
 247 | # Multiple options
 248 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 249 |     use_cache=True,
 250 |     enable_quality_processing=True,
 251 |     output_format="markdown",
 252 |     result_format="unified"
 253 | )
 254 | ```
 255 | 
 256 | ### FileExtractionConfig
 257 | 
 258 | Per-file extraction overrides for batch operations. All fields optional (`None` = use batch default).
 259 | 
 260 | **Key fields:** `enable_quality_processing`, `ocr`, `force_ocr`, `chunking`, `images`, `pdf_options`, `token_reduction`, `language_detection`, `pages`, `keywords`, `postprocessor`, `html_options`, `result_format`, `output_format`, `include_document_structure`, `layout`.
 261 | 
 262 | Excluded (batch-level only): `max_concurrent_extractions`, `use_cache`, `acceleration`, `security_limits`.
 263 | 
 264 | ```python
 265 | per_file = FileExtractionConfig(
 266 |     force_ocr=True,
 267 |     ocr=OcrConfig(backend="tesseract", language="deu"),
 268 | )
 269 | ```
 270 | 
 271 | ### OcrConfig
 272 | 
 273 | OCR configuration for extracting text from images.
 274 | 
 275 | **Attributes:**
 276 | 
 277 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 278 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 279 | | `backend` | str | "tesseract" | OCR backend: "tesseract", "easyocr", or "paddleocr" |
 280 | | `language` | str | "eng" | Language code (ISO 639-3 three-letter: "eng", "deu", "fra" or ISO 639-1 two-letter: "en", "de", "fr") |
 281 | | `tesseract_config` | TesseractConfig \| None | None | Tesseract-specific configuration (only used when backend="tesseract") |
 282 | 
 283 | **Example:**
 284 | 
 285 | ```python
 286 | from kreuzberg import OcrConfig
 287 | 
 288 | # Tesseract with German language
 289 | config = OcrConfig(backend="tesseract", language="deu")
 290 | 
 291 | # EasyOCR for faster recognition
 292 | config = OcrConfig(backend="easyocr", language="eng")
 293 | 
 294 | # PaddleOCR for production deployments
 295 | config = OcrConfig(backend="paddleocr", language="chi_sim")
 296 | ```
 297 | 
 298 | ### TesseractConfig
 299 | 
 300 | Detailed Tesseract OCR configuration for advanced tuning. Fine-tune Tesseract OCR behavior for specific document types and quality levels.
 301 | 
 302 | **Attributes:**
 303 | 
 304 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 305 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 306 | | `language` | str | "eng" | OCR language (ISO 639-3 three-letter code) |
 307 | | `psm` | int | 3 | Page Segmentation Mode: 0 (detection only), 3 (auto), 6 (uniform block), 11 (sparse text) |
 308 | | `output_format` | str | "markdown" | Output format for OCR results |
 309 | | `oem` | int | 3 | OCR Engine Mode: 0 (legacy), 1 (LSTM), 2 (both), 3 (auto) |
 310 | | `min_confidence` | float | 0.0 | Minimum confidence threshold (0.0-1.0) for accepting OCR results |
 311 | | `preprocessing` | ImagePreprocessingConfig \| None | None | Image preprocessing configuration before OCR |
 312 | | `enable_table_detection` | bool | True | Enable automatic table detection and extraction |
 313 | | `table_min_confidence` | float | 0.0 | Minimum confidence for table detection (0.0-1.0) |
 314 | | `table_column_threshold` | int | 50 | Minimum pixel width between columns |
 315 | | `table_row_threshold_ratio` | float | 0.5 | Minimum row height ratio |
 316 | | `use_cache` | bool | True | Cache OCR results for improved performance |
 317 | | `classify_use_pre_adapted_templates` | bool | True | Use pre-adapted character templates |
 318 | | `language_model_ngram_on` | bool | False | Enable language model n-gram processing |
 319 | | `tessedit_dont_blkrej_good_wds` | bool | True | Don't block-reject good words |
 320 | | `tessedit_dont_rowrej_good_wds` | bool | True | Don't row-reject good words |
 321 | | `tessedit_enable_dict_correction` | bool | True | Enable dictionary-based spelling correction |
 322 | | `tessedit_char_whitelist` | str | "" | Whitelist of characters to recognize (empty = all) |
 323 | | `tessedit_char_blacklist` | str | "" | Blacklist of characters to ignore |
 324 | | `tessedit_use_primary_params_model` | bool | True | Use primary parameters model |
 325 | | `textord_space_size_is_variable` | bool | True | Allow variable space sizes |
 326 | | `thresholding_method` | bool | False | Thresholding method for binarization |
 327 | 
 328 | **Example:**
 329 | 
 330 | ```python
 331 | from kreuzberg import TesseractConfig, ImagePreprocessingConfig
 332 | 
 333 | # General document OCR
 334 | config = TesseractConfig(psm=3, oem=3)
 335 | 
 336 | # Invoice/form OCR with table detection
 337 | config = TesseractConfig(psm=6, oem=2, enable_table_detection=True, min_confidence=0.6)
 338 | 
 339 | # High-precision technical document OCR
 340 | config = TesseractConfig(
 341 |     psm=3,
 342 |     oem=2,
 343 |     preprocessing=ImagePreprocessingConfig(denoise=True, contrast_enhance=True, auto_rotate=True),
 344 |     min_confidence=0.7,
 345 |     tessedit_enable_dict_correction=True,
 346 | )
 347 | 
 348 | # Numeric-only OCR (for receipts, barcodes)
 349 | config = TesseractConfig(psm=6, tessedit_char_whitelist="0123456789.-,", min_confidence=0.8)
 350 | 
 351 | # Multiple language document
 352 | config = TesseractConfig(language="eng+fra+deu", psm=3, oem=2)
 353 | ```
 354 | 
 355 | ### ChunkingConfig
 356 | 
 357 | Text chunking configuration for dividing content into chunks. Chunking is useful for preparing content for embedding, indexing, or processing with length-limited systems (like LLM context windows).
 358 | 
 359 | **Attributes:**
 360 | 
 361 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 362 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 363 | | `max_chars` | int | 1000 | Maximum number of characters per chunk. Chunks larger than this will be split intelligently at sentence/paragraph boundaries |
 364 | | `max_overlap` | int | 200 | Overlap between consecutive chunks in characters. Creates context bridges between chunks for smoother processing |
 365 | | `embedding` | EmbeddingConfig \| None | None | Configuration for generating embeddings for each chunk using ONNX models. None = no embeddings |
 366 | | `preset` | str \| None | None | Use a preset chunking configuration (overrides individual settings if provided). Use list_embedding_presets() to see available presets |
 367 | 
 368 | **IMPORTANT:** The fields are `max_chars` and `max_overlap` (NOT `max_characters` or `overlap`).
 369 | 
 370 | **Example:**
 371 | 
 372 | ```python
 373 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, ChunkingConfig, EmbeddingConfig, EmbeddingModelType
 374 | 
 375 | # Basic chunking with defaults
 376 | config = ExtractionConfig(chunking=ChunkingConfig())
 377 | 
 378 | # Custom chunk size with overlap
 379 | config = ExtractionConfig(chunking=ChunkingConfig(max_chars=512, max_overlap=100))
 380 | 
 381 | # Chunking with embeddings
 382 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 383 |     chunking=ChunkingConfig(
 384 |         max_chars=512,
 385 |         embedding=EmbeddingConfig(model=EmbeddingModelType.preset("balanced"))
 386 |     )
 387 | )
 388 | 
 389 | # Using preset configuration
 390 | config = ExtractionConfig(chunking=ChunkingConfig(preset="semantic"))
 391 | ```
 392 | 
 393 | ### PdfConfig
 394 | 
 395 | PDF-specific extraction configuration.
 396 | 
 397 | **Attributes:**
 398 | 
 399 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 400 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 401 | | `extract_images` | bool | False | Extract images from PDF documents |
 402 | | `passwords` | list[str] \| None | None | List of passwords to try when opening encrypted PDFs. Try each password in order until one succeeds |
 403 | | `extract_metadata` | bool | True | Extract PDF metadata (title, author, creation date, etc.) |
 404 | | `hierarchy` | HierarchyConfig \| None | None | Document hierarchy detection configuration. None = no hierarchy detection |
 405 | 
 406 | **Example:**
 407 | 
 408 | ```python
 409 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, PdfConfig, HierarchyConfig
 410 | 
 411 | # Basic PDF configuration
 412 | config = ExtractionConfig(pdf_options=PdfConfig())
 413 | 
 414 | # Extract metadata and images from PDF
 415 | config = ExtractionConfig(pdf_options=PdfConfig(extract_images=True, extract_metadata=True))
 416 | 
 417 | # Handle encrypted PDFs
 418 | config = ExtractionConfig(pdf_options=PdfConfig(passwords=["password123", "fallback_password"]))
 419 | 
 420 | # Enable hierarchy detection
 421 | config = ExtractionConfig(pdf_options=PdfConfig(hierarchy=HierarchyConfig(k_clusters=6)))
 422 | ```
 423 | 
 424 | ### ImageExtractionConfig
 425 | 
 426 | Configuration for extracting images FROM documents. This is NOT for preprocessing images before OCR.
 427 | 
 428 | **Attributes:**
 429 | 
 430 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 431 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 432 | | `extract_images` | bool | True | Enable image extraction from documents |
 433 | | `target_dpi` | int | 300 | Target DPI for image normalization. Images are resampled to this DPI for consistency |
 434 | | `max_image_dimension` | int | 4096 | Maximum width or height for extracted images. Larger images are downscaled to fit |
 435 | | `auto_adjust_dpi` | bool | True | Automatically adjust DPI based on image content quality |
 436 | | `min_dpi` | int | 72 | Minimum DPI threshold. Images with lower DPI are upscaled |
 437 | | `max_dpi` | int | 600 | Maximum DPI threshold. Images with higher DPI are downscaled |
 438 | 
 439 | **Example:**
 440 | 
 441 | ```python
 442 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, ImageExtractionConfig
 443 | 
 444 | # Basic image extraction
 445 | config = ExtractionConfig(images=ImageExtractionConfig())
 446 | 
 447 | # Extract images with custom DPI settings
 448 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 449 |     images=ImageExtractionConfig(target_dpi=150, max_image_dimension=2048, auto_adjust_dpi=False)
 450 | )
 451 | ```
 452 | 
 453 | ### EmbeddingConfig
 454 | 
 455 | Embedding generation configuration for text chunks. Configures embedding generation using ONNX models via fastembed-rs.
 456 | 
 457 | **Attributes:**
 458 | 
 459 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 460 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 461 | | `model` | EmbeddingModelType | Preset "balanced" | The embedding model to use (preset, fastembed, or custom) |
 462 | | `normalize` | bool | True | Whether to normalize embedding vectors to unit length (recommended for cosine similarity) |
 463 | | `batch_size` | int | 32 | Number of texts to process simultaneously. Higher values use more memory but may be faster |
 464 | | `show_download_progress` | bool | False | Display progress during embedding model download |
 465 | | `cache_dir` | str \| None | None | Custom directory for caching downloaded models (defaults to ~/.cache/kreuzberg/embeddings/) |
 466 | 
 467 | **Example:**
 468 | 
 469 | ```python
 470 | from kreuzberg import EmbeddingConfig, EmbeddingModelType
 471 | 
 472 | # Basic preset embedding (recommended)
 473 | config = EmbeddingConfig()
 474 | 
 475 | # Specific preset with settings
 476 | config = EmbeddingConfig(
 477 |     model=EmbeddingModelType.preset("balanced"),
 478 |     normalize=True,
 479 |     batch_size=64
 480 | )
 481 | 
 482 | # Custom ONNX model
 483 | config = EmbeddingConfig(
 484 |     model=EmbeddingModelType.custom(model_id="sentence-transformers/all-MiniLM-L6-v2", dimensions=384)
 485 | )
 486 | 
 487 | # With custom cache directory
 488 | config = EmbeddingConfig(cache_dir="/path/to/model/cache")
 489 | ```
 490 | 
 491 | ### EmbeddingModelType
 492 | 
 493 | Embedding model type selector with multiple configurations.
 494 | 
 495 | **Static Methods:**
 496 | 
 497 | ```python
 498 | @staticmethod
 499 | def preset(name: str) -> EmbeddingModelType
 500 | ```
 501 | 
 502 | Use a preset configuration (recommended for most use cases). Available presets: balanced, compact, large.
 503 | 
 504 | ```python
 505 | @staticmethod
 506 | def fastembed(model: str, dimensions: int) -> EmbeddingModelType
 507 | ```
 508 | 
 509 | Use a specific fastembed model by name.
 510 | 
 511 | ```python
 512 | @staticmethod
 513 | def custom(model_id: str, dimensions: int) -> EmbeddingModelType
 514 | ```
 515 | 
 516 | Use a custom ONNX model from HuggingFace (e.g., sentence-transformers/*).
 517 | 
 518 | **Example:**
 519 | 
 520 | ```python
 521 | from kreuzberg import EmbeddingModelType, list_embedding_presets
 522 | 
 523 | # Using the balanced preset (recommended for general use)
 524 | model = EmbeddingModelType.preset("balanced")
 525 | 
 526 | # Using a specific fast embedding model
 527 | model = EmbeddingModelType.fastembed(model="BAAI/bge-small-en-v1.5", dimensions=384)
 528 | 
 529 | # Using a custom HuggingFace model
 530 | model = EmbeddingModelType.custom(
 531 |     model_id="sentence-transformers/all-MiniLM-L6-v2",
 532 |     dimensions=384
 533 | )
 534 | 
 535 | # Listing available presets
 536 | presets = list_embedding_presets()
 537 | print(f"Available presets: {presets}")
 538 | ```
 539 | 
 540 | ### TokenReductionConfig
 541 | 
 542 | Configuration for reducing token count in extracted content. Reduces token count to lower costs when working with LLM APIs.
 543 | 
 544 | **Attributes:**
 545 | 
 546 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 547 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 548 | | `mode` | str | "off" | Token reduction mode: "off", "light", "moderate", "aggressive", or "maximum" |
 549 | | `preserve_important_words` | bool | True | Preserve capitalized words, technical terms, and proper nouns even in aggressive reduction modes |
 550 | 
 551 | **Example:**
 552 | 
 553 | ```python
 554 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, TokenReductionConfig
 555 | 
 556 | # Moderate token reduction
 557 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 558 |     token_reduction=TokenReductionConfig(mode="moderate", preserve_important_words=True)
 559 | )
 560 | 
 561 | # Maximum reduction for large batches
 562 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 563 |     token_reduction=TokenReductionConfig(mode="maximum", preserve_important_words=True)
 564 | )
 565 | 
 566 | # No reduction (default)
 567 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 568 |     token_reduction=TokenReductionConfig(mode="off")
 569 | )
 570 | ```
 571 | 
 572 | ### LanguageDetectionConfig
 573 | 
 574 | Configuration for detecting document language(s).
 575 | 
 576 | **Attributes:**
 577 | 
 578 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 579 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 580 | | `enabled` | bool | True | Enable language detection for extracted content |
 581 | | `min_confidence` | float | 0.8 | Minimum confidence threshold (0.0-1.0) for language detection |
 582 | | `detect_multiple` | bool | False | Detect multiple languages in the document. When False, only the most confident language is returned |
 583 | 
 584 | **Example:**
 585 | 
 586 | ```python
 587 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, LanguageDetectionConfig, extract_file_sync
 588 | 
 589 | # Basic language detection
 590 | config = ExtractionConfig(language_detection=LanguageDetectionConfig())
 591 | 
 592 | # Detect multiple languages with lower confidence threshold
 593 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 594 |     language_detection=LanguageDetectionConfig(detect_multiple=True, min_confidence=0.6)
 595 | )
 596 | 
 597 | # Access detected languages in result
 598 | result = extract_file_sync("multilingual.pdf", config=config)
 599 | print(f"Languages: {result.detected_languages}")
 600 | ```
 601 | 
 602 | ### KeywordConfig
 603 | 
 604 | Keyword extraction configuration.
 605 | 
 606 | **Attributes:**
 607 | 
 608 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 609 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 610 | | `algorithm` | KeywordAlgorithm | - | Keyword extraction algorithm (KeywordAlgorithm.Yake or KeywordAlgorithm.Rake) |
 611 | | `max_keywords` | int | 10 | Maximum number of keywords to extract |
 612 | | `min_score` | float | 0.0 | Minimum score threshold |
 613 | | `ngram_range` | tuple[int, int] | (1, 3) | N-gram range for keyword extraction |
 614 | | `language` | str \| None | "en" | Optional language hint |
 615 | | `yake_params` | YakeParams \| None | None | YAKE-specific tuning parameters |
 616 | | `rake_params` | RakeParams \| None | None | RAKE-specific tuning parameters |
 617 | 
 618 | ### PageConfig
 619 | 
 620 | Page extraction and tracking configuration.
 621 | 
 622 | **Attributes:**
 623 | 
 624 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 625 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 626 | | `extract_pages` | bool | False | Enable page tracking and per-page extraction |
 627 | | `insert_page_markers` | bool | False | Insert page markers into content |
 628 | | `marker_format` | str | "\\n\\n<!-- PAGE {page_num} -->\\n\\n" | Marker template containing {page_num} |
 629 | 
 630 | **Example:**
 631 | 
 632 | ```python
 633 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, PageConfig
 634 | 
 635 | config = ExtractionConfig(pages=PageConfig(extract_pages=True))
 636 | ```
 637 | 
 638 | ### PostProcessorConfig
 639 | 
 640 | Configuration for post-processors in the extraction pipeline.
 641 | 
 642 | **Attributes:**
 643 | 
 644 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 645 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 646 | | `enabled` | bool | True | Enable post-processors in the extraction pipeline |
 647 | | `enabled_processors` | list[str] \| None | None | Whitelist of processor names to run. None = run all enabled |
 648 | | `disabled_processors` | list[str] \| None | None | Blacklist of processor names to skip. None = none disabled |
 649 | 
 650 | **Example:**
 651 | 
 652 | ```python
 653 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, PostProcessorConfig
 654 | 
 655 | # Basic post-processing with defaults
 656 | config = ExtractionConfig(postprocessor=PostProcessorConfig())
 657 | 
 658 | # Enable only specific processors
 659 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 660 |     postprocessor=PostProcessorConfig(
 661 |         enabled=True,
 662 |         enabled_processors=["normalize_whitespace", "fix_encoding"]
 663 |     )
 664 | )
 665 | 
 666 | # Disable specific processors
 667 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 668 |     postprocessor=PostProcessorConfig(
 669 |         enabled=True,
 670 |         disabled_processors=["experimental_cleanup"]
 671 |     )
 672 | )
 673 | 
 674 | # Disable all post-processing
 675 | config = ExtractionConfig(postprocessor=PostProcessorConfig(enabled=False))
 676 | ```
 677 | 
 678 | ### ImagePreprocessingConfig
 679 | 
 680 | Configuration for preprocessing images before OCR. This is NOT for extracting images from documents.
 681 | 
 682 | **Attributes:**
 683 | 
 684 | | Field | Type | Default | Description |
 685 | |-------|------|---------|-------------|
 686 | | `target_dpi` | int | 300 | Target DPI for image normalization before OCR |
 687 | | `auto_rotate` | bool | True | Automatically detect and correct image rotation |
 688 | | `deskew` | bool | True | Correct skewed images to improve OCR accuracy |
 689 | | `denoise` | bool | False | Apply denoising filters to reduce noise in images |
 690 | | `contrast_enhance` | bool | False | Enhance contrast to improve text readability |
 691 | | `binarization_method` | str | "otsu" | Method for converting images to black and white |
 692 | | `invert_colors` | bool | False | Invert colors (white text on black background) |
 693 | 
 694 | **Example:**
 695 | 
 696 | ```python
 697 | from kreuzberg import TesseractConfig, ImagePreprocessingConfig
 698 | 
 699 | # Basic preprocessing for OCR
 700 | config = TesseractConfig(preprocessing=ImagePreprocessingConfig())
 701 | 
 702 | # Aggressive preprocessing for low-quality scans
 703 | config = TesseractConfig(
 704 |     preprocessing=ImagePreprocessingConfig(
 705 |         target_dpi=300,
 706 |         denoise=True,
 707 |         contrast_enhance=True,
 708 |         auto_rotate=True,
 709 |         deskew=True
 710 |     )
 711 | )
 712 | ```
 713 | 
 714 | ## ExtractionResult
 715 | 
 716 | Result object returned by extraction functions.
 717 | 
 718 | **Attributes:**
 719 | 
 720 | | Field | Type | Description |
 721 | |-------|------|-------------|
 722 | | `content` | str | Main extracted text content in the specified output_format |
 723 | | `mime_type` | str | MIME type of the processed document |
 724 | | `metadata` | Metadata | Extracted document metadata (title, author, created_at, format_type, etc.) |
 725 | | `tables` | list[ExtractedTable] | Extracted tables from the document |
 726 | | `detected_languages` | list[str] \| None | Detected language codes (e.g., ["en", "de"]) if language detection is enabled |
 727 | | `chunks` | list[Chunk] \| None | Text chunks if chunking is enabled (each chunk has content, embedding, metadata) |
 728 | | `images` | list[ExtractedImage] \| None | Extracted images if image extraction is enabled |
 729 | | `pages` | list[PageContent] \| None | Per-page content and metadata if page extraction is enabled |
 730 | | `elements` | list[Element] \| None | Semantic elements if result_format="element_based" |
 731 | | `output_format` | str \| None | Format of the content field (plain, markdown, djot, html) |
 732 | | `result_format` | str \| None | Result format used (unified or element_based) |
 733 | | `extracted_keywords` | list[ExtractedKeyword] \| None | Extracted keywords with relevance scores if keyword extraction enabled |
 734 | | `quality_score` | float \| None | Overall quality score for the extraction result (0.0-1.0) |
 735 | | `processing_warnings` | list[ProcessingWarning] | Non-fatal warnings encountered during extraction pipeline |
 736 | 
 737 | **Methods:**
 738 | 
 739 | ```python
 740 | def get_page_count(self) -> int
 741 | ```
 742 | 
 743 | Get the total number of pages in the document.
 744 | 
 745 | ```python
 746 | def get_chunk_count(self) -> int
 747 | ```
 748 | 
 749 | Get the total number of chunks if chunking is enabled.
 750 | 
 751 | ```python
 752 | def get_detected_language(self) -> str | None
 753 | ```
 754 | 
 755 | Get the most confident detected language code.
 756 | 
 757 | ```python
 758 | def get_metadata_field(self, field_name: str) -> Any | None
 759 | ```
 760 | 
 761 | Get a specific metadata field by name.
 762 | 
 763 | **Example:**
 764 | 
 765 | ```python
 766 | from kreuzberg import extract_file_sync, ExtractionConfig, ChunkingConfig
 767 | 
 768 | config = ExtractionConfig(
 769 |     chunking=ChunkingConfig(max_chars=512),
 770 |     output_format="markdown"
 771 | )
 772 | result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 773 | 
 774 | print(f"Content preview: {result.content[:200]}")
 775 | print(f"MIME type: {result.mime_type}")
 776 | print(f"Page count: {result.get_page_count()}")
 777 | print(f"Chunk count: {result.get_chunk_count()}")
 778 | print(f"Detected language: {result.get_detected_language()}")
 779 | 
 780 | if result.tables:
 781 |     print(f"Found {len(result.tables)} tables")
 782 | 
 783 | if result.chunks:
 784 |     first_chunk = result.chunks[0]
 785 |     print(f"First chunk: {first_chunk.content[:100]}")
 786 |     if first_chunk.embedding:
 787 |         print(f"Embedding dimensions: {len(first_chunk.embedding)}")
 788 | ```
 789 | 
 790 | ## Error Classes
 791 | 
 792 | All exceptions inherit from `KreuzbergError`, the base exception class.
 793 | 
 794 | ### KreuzbergError
 795 | 
 796 | Base exception class for all Kreuzberg errors.
 797 | 
 798 | ```python
 799 | class KreuzbergError(Exception):
 800 |     """Base exception for all Kreuzberg errors."""
 801 | ```
 802 | 
 803 | ### ParsingError
 804 | 
 805 | Raised when document parsing fails.
 806 | 
 807 | ```python
 808 | class ParsingError(KreuzbergError):
 809 |     """Document parsing failed (corrupt, malformed, etc.)."""
 810 | ```
 811 | 
 812 | ### OCRError
 813 | 
 814 | Raised when OCR processing fails.
 815 | 
 816 | ```python
 817 | class OCRError(KreuzbergError):
 818 |     """OCR operation failed."""
 819 | ```
 820 | 
 821 | ### ValidationError
 822 | 
 823 | Raised when validation fails.
 824 | 
 825 | ```python
 826 | class ValidationError(KreuzbergError):
 827 |     """Validation failed (invalid parameters, constraints, format mismatches)."""
 828 | ```
 829 | 
 830 | ### MissingDependencyError
 831 | 
 832 | Raised when required dependencies are not available.
 833 | 
 834 | ```python
 835 | class MissingDependencyError(KreuzbergError):
 836 |     """Required dependency not available (easyocr, paddleocr, tesseract, etc.)."""
 837 | 
 838 |     @staticmethod
 839 |     def create_for_package(dependency_group: str, functionality: str, package_name: str) -> MissingDependencyError
 840 | ```
 841 | 
 842 | **Example:**
 843 | 
 844 | ```python
 845 | from kreuzberg import extract_file_sync, MissingDependencyError, OCRError, ParsingError
 846 | 
 847 | try:
 848 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf")
 849 | except ParsingError as e:
 850 |     print(f"Failed to parse document: {e}")
 851 | except OCRError as e:
 852 |     print(f"OCR failed: {e}")
 853 | except MissingDependencyError as e:
 854 |     print(f"Missing dependency: {e}")
 855 | ```
 856 | 
 857 | ## Utility Functions
 858 | 
 859 | ### MIME Type Detection
 860 | 
 861 | ```python
 862 | def detect_mime_type(data: bytes | bytearray) -> str
 863 | ```
 864 | 
 865 | Detect MIME type from file bytes using magic number detection.
 866 | 
 867 | **Parameters:**
 868 | 
 869 | - `data` (bytes | bytearray): File content as bytes or bytearray
 870 | 
 871 | **Returns:** Detected MIME type (e.g., "application/pdf", "image/png")
 872 | 
 873 | ```python
 874 | def detect_mime_type_from_path(path: str | Path) -> str
 875 | ```
 876 | 
 877 | Detect MIME type from file path by reading the file and detecting its MIME type.
 878 | 
 879 | **Parameters:**
 880 | 
 881 | - `path` (str | Path): Path to the file
 882 | 
 883 | **Returns:** Detected MIME type
 884 | 
 885 | **Raises:**
 886 | 
 887 | - `OSError`: If file cannot be read (file not found, permission denied, etc.)
 888 | - `RuntimeError`: If MIME type detection fails
 889 | 
 890 | **Example:**
 891 | 
 892 | ```python
 893 | from kreuzberg import detect_mime_type, detect_mime_type_from_path
 894 | 
 895 | # From bytes
 896 | pdf_bytes = b"%PDF-1.4\n"
 897 | mime_type = detect_mime_type(pdf_bytes)
 898 | 
 899 | # From path
 900 | mime_type = detect_mime_type_from_path("document.pdf")
 901 | ```
 902 | 
 903 | ### MIME Type Validation
 904 | 
 905 | ```python
 906 | def validate_mime_type(mime_type: str) -> str
 907 | ```
 908 | 
 909 | Validate a MIME type string and return the canonical form.
 910 | 
 911 | ```python
 912 | def get_extensions_for_mime(mime_type: str) -> list[str]
 913 | ```
 914 | 
 915 | Get file extensions associated with a MIME type.
 916 | 
 917 | **Example:**
 918 | 
 919 | ```python
 920 | from kreuzberg import validate_mime_type, get_extensions_for_mime
 921 | 
 922 | canonical = validate_mime_type("application/pdf")
 923 | extensions = get_extensions_for_mime("application/pdf")  # Returns ["pdf"]
 924 | ```
 925 | 
 926 | ### Configuration Loading
 927 | 
 928 | ```python
 929 | def load_extraction_config_from_file(path: str | Path) -> ExtractionConfig
 930 | ```
 931 | 
 932 | Load extraction configuration from a specific file.
 933 | 
 934 | **Parameters:**
 935 | 
 936 | - `path` (str | Path): Path to the configuration file (.toml, .yaml, or .json)
 937 | 
 938 | **Returns:** ExtractionConfig parsed from the file
 939 | 
 940 | **Raises:**
 941 | 
 942 | - `FileNotFoundError`: If the configuration file does not exist
 943 | - `RuntimeError`: If the file cannot be read or parsed
 944 | - `ValueError`: If the file format is invalid or unsupported
 945 | 
 946 | ```python
 947 | def discover_extraction_config() -> ExtractionConfig | None
 948 | ```
 949 | 
 950 | Discover extraction configuration from the environment (deprecated).
 951 | 
 952 | Attempts to locate a Kreuzberg configuration file using:
 953 | 
 954 | 1. KREUZBERG_CONFIG_PATH environment variable
 955 | 2. Search for kreuzberg.toml, kreuzberg.yaml, or kreuzberg.json in current and parent directories
 956 | 
 957 | **Returns:** ExtractionConfig if found, None otherwise
 958 | 
 959 | **Note:** Deprecated in favor of `load_extraction_config_from_file` for more predictable behavior.
 960 | 
 961 | **Example:**
 962 | 
 963 | ```python
 964 | from kreuzberg import load_extraction_config_from_file, extract_file_sync
 965 | 
 966 | # Load from specific file
 967 | config = load_extraction_config_from_file("kreuzberg.toml")
 968 | result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", config=config)
 969 | 
 970 | # Auto-discover configuration
 971 | import os
 972 | os.environ["KREUZBERG_CONFIG_PATH"] = "config/kreuzberg.yaml"
 973 | # Then extraction will use the discovered config
 974 | ```
 975 | 
 976 | ## Plugin System
 977 | 
 978 | ### Registering Post-Processors
 979 | 
 980 | ```python
 981 | def register_post_processor(processor: Any) -> None
 982 | ```
 983 | 
 984 | Register a Python PostProcessor with the Rust core. Once registered, the processor will be called automatically after extraction to enrich results.
 985 | 
 986 | **Required Methods:**
 987 | 
 988 | - `name() -> str`: Return processor name (must be non-empty)
 989 | - `process(result: ExtractionResult) -> ExtractionResult`: Process and enrich the extraction result
 990 | - `processing_stage() -> str`: Return "early", "middle", or "late"
 991 | 
 992 | **Optional Methods:**
 993 | 
 994 | - `initialize() -> None`: Called when processor is registered
 995 | - `shutdown() -> None`: Called when processor is unregistered
 996 | 
 997 | **Example:**
 998 | 
 999 | ```python
1000 | from kreuzberg import register_post_processor, ExtractionResult
1001 | 
1002 | class EntityExtractor:
1003 |     def name(self) -> str:
1004 |         return "entity_extraction"
1005 | 
1006 |     def processing_stage(self) -> str:
1007 |         return "early"
1008 | 
1009 |     def process(self, result: ExtractionResult) -> ExtractionResult:
1010 |         entities = {"PERSON": ["John Doe"], "ORG": ["Microsoft"]}
1011 |         result.metadata["entities"] = entities
1012 |         return result
1013 | 
1014 | register_post_processor(EntityExtractor())
1015 | ```
1016 | 
1017 | ### Registering OCR Backends
1018 | 
1019 | ```python
1020 | def register_ocr_backend(backend: Any) -> None
1021 | ```
1022 | 
1023 | Register a Python OCR backend with the Rust core.
1024 | 
1025 | **Required Methods:**
1026 | 
1027 | - `name() -> str`: Return backend name (must be non-empty)
1028 | - `supported_languages() -> list[str]`: Return list of supported language codes
1029 | - `process_image(image_bytes: bytes, language: str) -> OcrResult`: Process image and return OCR result
1030 | - `process_file(path: str, language: str) -> OcrResult`: Process file and return OCR result
1031 | - `initialize() -> None`: Called when backend is registered
1032 | - `shutdown() -> None`: Called when backend is unregistered
1033 | - `version() -> str`: Return backend version string
1034 | 
1035 | **Example:**
1036 | 
1037 | ```python
1038 | from kreuzberg import register_ocr_backend
1039 | 
1040 | class MyOcrBackend:
1041 |     def name(self) -> str:
1042 |         return "my-ocr"
1043 | 
1044 |     def supported_languages(self) -> list[str]:
1045 |         return ["eng", "deu", "fra"]
1046 | 
1047 |     def process_image(self, image_bytes: bytes, language: str) -> dict:
1048 |         return {
1049 |             "content": "extracted text",
1050 |             "metadata": {"confidence": 0.95},
1051 |             "tables": []
1052 |         }
1053 | 
1054 | register_ocr_backend(MyOcrBackend())
1055 | ```
1056 | 
1057 | ### Registering Validators
1058 | 
1059 | ```python
1060 | def register_validator(validator: Any) -> None
1061 | ```
1062 | 
1063 | Register a Python Validator with the Rust core. Validators are called automatically after extraction to validate results.
1064 | 
1065 | **Required Methods:**
1066 | 
1067 | - `name() -> str`: Return validator name (must be non-empty)
1068 | - `validate(result: ExtractionResult) -> None`: Validate the extraction result (raise error to fail)
1069 | 
1070 | **Optional Methods:**
1071 | 
1072 | - `should_validate(result: ExtractionResult) -> bool`: Check if validator should run (defaults to True)
1073 | - `priority() -> int`: Return priority (defaults to 50, higher runs first)
1074 | 
1075 | **Example:**
1076 | 
1077 | ```python
1078 | from kreuzberg import register_validator, ValidationError, ExtractionResult
1079 | 
1080 | class MinLengthValidator:
1081 |     def name(self) -> str:
1082 |         return "min_length_validator"
1083 | 
1084 |     def priority(self) -> int:
1085 |         return 100
1086 | 
1087 |     def validate(self, result: ExtractionResult) -> None:
1088 |         if len(result.content) < 100:
1089 |             raise ValidationError("Content too short")
1090 | 
1091 | register_validator(MinLengthValidator())
1092 | ```
1093 |

1150 | ## Format Enums
1151 | 
1152 | ### OutputFormat
1153 | 
1154 | Output format for extraction results.
1155 | 
1156 | ```python
1157 | class OutputFormat(str, Enum):
1158 |     PLAIN = "plain"         # Plain text format
1159 |     MARKDOWN = "markdown"   # Markdown format
1160 |     DJOT = "djot"          # Djot lightweight markup format
1161 |     HTML = "html"          # HTML format
1162 | ```
1163 | 
1164 | ### ResultFormat
1165 | 
1166 | Result format controlling extraction output structure.
1167 | 
1168 | ```python
1169 | class ResultFormat(str, Enum):
1170 |     UNIFIED = "unified"                # All content in `content` field
1171 |     ELEMENT_BASED = "element_based"   # Unstructured-compatible output with semantic elements
1172 | ```
1173 | 
1174 | ## Error Handling
1175 | 
1176 | ### Error Code Functions
1177 | 
1178 | ```python
1179 | def get_last_error_code() -> int
1180 | ```
1181 | 
1182 | Get the last error code from the FFI layer.
1183 | 
1184 | **Returns:**
1185 | 
1186 | - 0 (SUCCESS): No error occurred
1187 | - 1 (GENERIC_ERROR): Generic unspecified error
1188 | - 2 (PANIC): A panic occurred in the Rust core
1189 | - 3 (INVALID_ARGUMENT): Invalid argument provided
1190 | - 4 (IO_ERROR): I/O operation failed
1191 | - 5 (PARSING_ERROR): Document parsing failed
1192 | - 6 (OCR_ERROR): OCR operation failed
1193 | - 7 (MISSING_DEPENDENCY): Required dependency not available
1194 | 
1195 | ```python
1196 | def get_error_details() -> dict[str, Any]
1197 | ```
1198 | 
1199 | Get detailed error information from the FFI layer.
1200 | 
1201 | **Returns:** dict with keys:
1202 | 
1203 | - `message` (str): Human-readable error message
1204 | - `error_code` (int): Numeric error code (0-7)
1205 | - `error_type` (str): Error type name (e.g., "validation", "ocr")
1206 | - `source_file` (str | None): Source file path if available
1207 | - `source_function` (str | None): Function name if available
1208 | - `source_line` (int): Line number (0 if unknown)
1209 | - `context_info` (str | None): Additional context if available
1210 | - `is_panic` (bool): Whether error came from a panic
1211 | 
1212 | ```python
1213 | def classify_error(message: str) -> int
1214 | ```
1215 | 
1216 | Classify an error message into a Kreuzberg error code.
1217 | 
1218 | **Parameters:**
1219 | 
1220 | - `message` (str): The error message to classify
1221 | 
1222 | **Returns:** int error code (0-7) representing the classification
1223 | 
1224 | ```python
1225 | def error_code_name(code: int) -> str
1226 | ```
1227 | 
1228 | Get the human-readable name of an error code.
1229 | 
1230 | **Parameters:**
1231 | 
1232 | - `code` (int): Numeric error code (0-7)
1233 | 
1234 | **Returns:** Human-readable error code name (e.g., "validation", "ocr")
1235 | 
1236 | **Example:**
1237 | 
1238 | ```python
1239 | from kreuzberg import get_error_details, get_last_error_code, error_code_name, classify_error
1240 | 
1241 | try:
1242 |     result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf")
1243 | except Exception as e:
1244 |     code = get_last_error_code()
1245 |     if code:
1246 |         print(f"Error code: {code} ({error_code_name(code)})")
1247 | 
1248 |     details = get_error_details()
1249 |     print(f"Error: {details['message']}")
1250 |     print(f"Type: {details['error_type']}")
1251 | 
1252 |     classified = classify_error(str(e))
1253 |     print(f"Classified as: {error_code_name(classified)}")
1254 | ```

1347 | def list_embedding_presets() -> list[str]
1348 | ```

1351 |

1354 | ```
1355 |

1359 |

1362 |     validate_dpi,
1363 |     get_valid_binarization_methods,
1364 |     list_embedding_presets,
1365 |     get_embedding_preset
1366 | )
1367 | 
1368 | # Validate parameters
1369 | if not validate_dpi(300):
1370 |     print("Invalid DPI")
1371 | 
1372 | # List valid values
1373 | binarization_methods = get_valid_binarization_methods()
1374 | presets = list_embedding_presets()
1375 | 
1376 | # Get preset details
1377 | preset = get_embedding_preset("balanced")
1378 | if preset:
1379 |     print(f"Balanced preset: {preset.description}")
1380 |     print(f"Dimensions: {preset.dimensions}")
1381 |     print(f"Recommended chunk size: {preset.chunk_size}")
1382 | ```

1384 | ## Configuration Utilities
1385 | 
1386 | ### Config Manipulation
1387 | 
1388 | ```python
1389 | def config_to_json(config: ExtractionConfig) -> str
1390 | ```
1391 | 
1392 | Convert ExtractionConfig to JSON string.
1393 | 
1394 | ```python
1395 | def config_get_field(config: ExtractionConfig, field_name: str) -> Any | None
1396 | ```
1397 | 
1398 | Get a specific field value from ExtractionConfig.
1399 | 
1400 | ```python
1401 | def config_merge(base: ExtractionConfig, override: ExtractionConfig) -> None
1402 | ```
1403 | 
1404 | Merge override config into base config (mutates base).
1405 | 
1406 | **Example:**
1407 | 
1408 | ```python
1409 | from kreuzberg import ExtractionConfig, config_to_json, config_get_field, config_merge
1410 | 
1411 | config = ExtractionConfig(use_cache=True, enable_quality_processing=False)
1412 | 
1413 | # Convert to JSON
1414 | json_str = config_to_json(config)
1415 | print(json_str)
1416 | 
1417 | # Get field
1418 | use_cache = config_get_field(config, "use_cache")
1419 | print(f"use_cache: {use_cache}")
1420 | 
1421 | # Merge configs
1422 | override = ExtractionConfig(use_cache=False)
1423 | config_merge(config, override)
1424 | ```
