```markdown
   1 | # Kreuzberg Rust API Reference
   2 | 
   3 | Complete API reference for the Kreuzberg document extraction library in Rust.
   4 | 
   5 | ## Setup
   6 | 
   7 | Add to your `Cargo.toml`:
   8 | 
   9 | ```toml
  10 | [dependencies]
  11 | kreuzberg = { version = "4", features = [
  12 |     "tokio-runtime",
  13 |     "pdf",
  14 |     "ocr",
  15 |     "chunking",
  16 |     "embeddings",
  17 |     "language-detection",
  18 |     "keywords-yake",
  19 |     "keywords-rake",
  20 |     "api",
  21 |     "mcp"
  22 | ] }
  23 | tokio = { version = "1", features = ["full"] }
  24 | ```
  25 | 
  26 | ### Core Features
  27 | 
  28 | - **tokio-runtime**: Enables async/sync extraction (default). Required for `extract_file_sync`, `batch_extract_file_sync`, `batch_extract_file`
  29 | - **pdf**: PDF extraction with PDFium
  30 | - **ocr**: Tesseract-based OCR for scanned documents
  31 | - **chunking**: Text chunking for RAG pipelines
  32 | - **embeddings**: Vector embeddings generation
  33 | - **language-detection**: Detect document language
  34 | - **keywords-yake** / **keywords-rake**: Extract keywords using YAKE or RAKE
  35 | - **api**: HTTP API with Axum
  36 | - **mcp**: Model Context Protocol support
  37 | 
  38 | ---
  39 | 
  40 | ## Core Extraction Functions
  41 | 
  42 | ### `extract_file` (async)
  43 | 
  44 | Extract content from a file path.
  45 | 
  46 | ```rust
  47 | pub async fn extract_file(
  48 |     path: impl AsRef<Path>,
  49 |     mime_type: Option<&str>,
  50 |     config: &ExtractionConfig,
  51 | ) -> Result<ExtractionResult>
  52 | ```
  53 | 
  54 | **Always available.** Requires async context (`#[tokio::main]`, `tokio::spawn`, etc.).
  55 | 
  56 | ```rust
  57 | use kreuzberg::{extract_file, ExtractionConfig};
  58 | use std::path::Path;
  59 | 
  60 | #[tokio::main]
  61 | async fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
  62 |     let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
  63 |     let result = extract_file("document.pdf", None, &config).await?;
  64 |     println!("Content: {}", result.content);
  65 |     Ok(())
  66 | }
  67 | ```
  68 | 
  69 | ### `extract_bytes` (async)
  70 | 
  71 | Extract content from byte data.
  72 | 
  73 | ```rust
  74 | pub async fn extract_bytes(
  75 |     data: &[u8],
  76 |     mime_type: &str,
  77 |     config: &ExtractionConfig,
  78 | ) -> Result<ExtractionResult>
  79 | ```
  80 | 
  81 | **Always available.** Requires async context.
  82 | 
  83 | ```rust
  84 | #[tokio::main]
  85 | async fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
  86 |     let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
  87 |     let pdf_bytes = std::fs::read("document.pdf")?;
  88 |     let result = extract_bytes(&pdf_bytes, "application/pdf", &config).await?;
  89 |     Ok(())
  90 | }
  91 | ```
  92 | 
  93 | ### `extract_file_sync` (sync)
  94 | 
  95 | Synchronous wrapper around `extract_file`.
  96 | 
  97 | ```rust
  98 | pub fn extract_file_sync(
  99 |     path: impl AsRef<Path>,
 100 |     mime_type: Option<&str>,
 101 |     config: &ExtractionConfig,
 102 | ) -> Result<ExtractionResult>
 103 | ```
 104 | 
 105 | **Requires tokio-runtime feature.** Blocks the current thread using a global Tokio runtime.
 106 | 
 107 | ```rust
 108 | use kreuzberg::{extract_file_sync, ExtractionConfig};
 109 | 
 110 | fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
 111 |     let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
 112 |     let result = extract_file_sync("document.pdf", None, &config)?;
 113 |     println!("Content: {}", result.content);
 114 |     Ok(())
 115 | }
 116 | ```
 117 | 
 118 | ### `extract_bytes_sync` (sync)
 119 | 
 120 | Synchronous wrapper around `extract_bytes`.
 121 | 
 122 | ```rust
 123 | pub fn extract_bytes_sync(
 124 |     content: &[u8],
 125 |     mime_type: &str,
 126 |     config: &ExtractionConfig,
 127 | ) -> Result<ExtractionResult>
 128 | ```
 129 | 
 130 | **Always available.** Works in sync and async contexts.
 131 | 
 132 | ```rust
 133 | fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
 134 |     let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
 135 |     let bytes = b"Hello, world!";
 136 |     let result = extract_bytes_sync(bytes, "text/plain", &config)?;
 137 |     Ok(())
 138 | }
 139 | ```
 140 | 
 141 | ### `batch_extract_file` (async, parallel)
 142 | 
 143 | Extract multiple files concurrently.
 144 | 
 145 | ```rust
 146 | pub async fn batch_extract_file(
 147 |     paths: Vec<impl AsRef<Path>>,
 148 |     config: &ExtractionConfig,
 149 | ) -> Result<Vec<ExtractionResult>>
 150 | ```
 151 | 
 152 | **Requires tokio-runtime feature.** Processes files in parallel with automatic concurrency management (defaults to `num_cpus * 1.5`).
 153 | 
 154 | ```rust
 155 | #[tokio::main]
 156 | async fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
 157 |     let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
 158 |     let paths = vec!["doc1.pdf", "doc2.pdf", "doc3.pdf"];
 159 |     let results = batch_extract_file(paths, &config).await?;
 160 |     println!("Processed {} files", results.len());
 161 |     Ok(())
 162 | }
 163 | ```
 164 | 
 165 | ### `batch_extract_bytes` (async, parallel)
 166 | 
 167 | Extract multiple byte arrays concurrently.
 168 | 
 169 | ```rust
 170 | pub async fn batch_extract_bytes(
 171 |     contents: Vec<(Vec<u8>, String)>,
 172 |     config: &ExtractionConfig,
 173 | ) -> Result<Vec<ExtractionResult>>
 174 | ```
 175 | 
 176 | **Requires tokio-runtime feature.** Each tuple is `(bytes, mime_type)`.
 177 | 
 178 | ```rust
 179 | #[tokio::main]
 180 | async fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
 181 |     let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
 182 |     let contents = vec![
 183 |         (b"PDF content".to_vec(), "application/pdf".to_string()),
 184 |         (b"Text content".to_vec(), "text/plain".to_string()),
 185 |     ];
 186 |     let results = batch_extract_bytes(contents, &config).await?;
 187 |     Ok(())
 188 | }
 189 | ```
 190 | 
 191 | ### `batch_extract_file_sync` (sync, parallel)
 192 | 
 193 | Synchronous wrapper for batch file extraction.
 194 | 
 195 | ```rust
 196 | pub fn batch_extract_file_sync(
 197 |     paths: Vec<impl AsRef<Path>>,
 198 |     config: &ExtractionConfig,
 199 | ) -> Result<Vec<ExtractionResult>>
 200 | ```
 201 | 
 202 | **Requires tokio-runtime feature.** Uses global runtime for concurrency.
 203 | 
 204 | ```rust
 205 | fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
 206 |     let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
 207 |     let paths = vec!["doc1.pdf", "doc2.pdf"];
 208 |     let results = batch_extract_file_sync(paths, &config)?;
 209 |     Ok(())
 210 | }
 211 | ```
 212 | 
 213 | ### `batch_extract_bytes_sync` (sync, parallel)
 214 | 
 215 | Synchronous wrapper for batch byte extraction.
 216 | 
 217 | ```rust
 218 | pub fn batch_extract_bytes_sync(
 219 |     contents: Vec<(Vec<u8>, String)>,
 220 |     config: &ExtractionConfig,
 221 | ) -> Result<Vec<ExtractionResult>>
 222 | ```
 223 | 
 224 | **Always available.** Each tuple is `(bytes, mime_type)`.
 225 | 
 226 | ```rust
 227 | fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
 228 |     let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
 229 |     let contents = vec![
 230 |         (b"content 1".to_vec(), "text/plain".to_string()),
 231 |         (b"content 2".to_vec(), "text/plain".to_string()),
 232 |     ];
 233 |     let results = batch_extract_bytes_sync(contents, &config)?;
 234 |     Ok(())
 235 | }
 236 | ```
 237 | 
 238 | ### `FileExtractionConfig`
 239 | 
 240 | Per-file overrides for batch operations, passed as an optional parameter to `batch_extract_file` / `batch_extract_bytes` (and their sync variants). All fields `Option<T>` — `None` = use batch default.
 241 | 
 242 | > **Note (v4.5.0):** The separate `batch_extract_file_with_configs` / `batch_extract_bytes_with_configs` functions have been removed. Per-file configs are now an optional parameter on the unified batch functions.
 243 | 
 244 | ```rust
 245 | pub struct FileExtractionConfig {
 246 |     pub enable_quality_processing: Option<bool>,
 247 |     pub ocr: Option<OcrConfig>,
 248 |     pub force_ocr: Option<bool>,
 249 |     pub chunking: Option<ChunkingConfig>,
 250 |     pub images: Option<ImageExtractionConfig>,
 251 |     pub pdf_options: Option<PdfConfig>,
 252 |     pub token_reduction: Option<TokenReductionConfig>,
 253 |     pub language_detection: Option<LanguageDetectionConfig>,
 254 |     pub pages: Option<PageConfig>,
 255 |     pub postprocessor: Option<PostProcessorConfig>,
 256 |     pub output_format: Option<OutputFormat>,
 257 |     pub include_document_structure: Option<bool>,
 258 | }
 259 | ```
 260 | 
 261 | Excluded batch-level fields: `max_concurrent_extractions`, `use_cache`, `acceleration`, `security_limits`.
 262 | 
 263 | ---
 264 | 
 265 | ## Configuration
 266 | 
 267 | ### `ExtractionConfig`
 268 | 
 269 | Main configuration struct for all extraction operations.
 270 | 
 271 | ```rust
 272 | pub struct ExtractionConfig {
 273 |     /// Enable caching (default: true)
 274 |     pub use_cache: bool,
 275 | 
 276 |     /// Enable quality post-processing (default: true)
 277 |     pub enable_quality_processing: bool,
 278 | 
 279 |     /// OCR configuration (None = OCR disabled)
 280 |     pub ocr: Option<OcrConfig>,
 281 | 
 282 |     /// Force OCR even for searchable PDFs (default: false)
 283 |     pub force_ocr: bool,
 284 | 
 285 |     /// Text chunking configuration (None = disabled)
 286 |     pub chunking: Option<ChunkingConfig>,
 287 | 
 288 |     /// Image extraction configuration (None = disabled)
 289 |     pub images: Option<ImageExtractionConfig>,
 290 | 
 291 |     /// PDF-specific options (requires pdf feature)
 292 |     #[cfg(feature = "pdf")]
 293 |     pub pdf_options: Option<PdfConfig>,
 294 | 
 295 |     /// Token reduction configuration (None = disabled)
 296 |     pub token_reduction: Option<TokenReductionConfig>,
 297 | 
 298 |     /// Language detection configuration (None = disabled)
 299 |     pub language_detection: Option<LanguageDetectionConfig>,
 300 | 
 301 |     /// Page extraction configuration (None = disabled)
 302 |     pub pages: Option<PageConfig>,
 303 | 
 304 |     /// Keyword extraction configuration (requires keywords-yake or keywords-rake)
 305 |     #[cfg(any(feature = "keywords-yake", feature = "keywords-rake"))]
 306 |     pub keywords: Option<KeywordConfig>,
 307 | 
 308 |     /// Post-processor configuration (None = use defaults)
 309 |     pub postprocessor: Option<PostProcessorConfig>,
 310 | 
 311 |     /// HTML to Markdown conversion options (requires html feature)
 312 |     #[cfg(feature = "html")]
 313 |     pub html_options: Option<ConversionOptions>,
 314 | 
 315 |     /// Maximum concurrent extractions in batch (None = num_cpus * 1.5)
 316 |     pub max_concurrent_extractions: Option<usize>,
 317 | 
 318 |     /// Result structure format (default: Unified)
 319 |     /// Uses types::OutputFormat (Unified | ElementBased)
 320 |     pub result_format: types::OutputFormat,
 321 | 
 322 |     /// Security limits for archives (requires archives feature)
 323 |     #[cfg(feature = "archives")]
 324 |     pub security_limits: Option<SecurityLimits>,
 325 | 
 326 |     /// Content output format (default: Plain)
 327 |     /// Uses config::OutputFormat (Plain | Markdown | Djot | Html)
 328 |     pub output_format: OutputFormat,
 329 | }
 330 | ```
 331 | 
 332 | #### Creating Configs
 333 | 
 334 | ```rust
 335 | use kreuzberg::{ExtractionConfig, OcrConfig, ChunkingConfig, OutputFormat};
 336 | 
 337 | // Default configuration
 338 | let config = ExtractionConfig::default();
 339 | 
 340 | // With OCR
 341 | let config = ExtractionConfig {
 342 |     ocr: Some(OcrConfig {
 343 |         backend: "tesseract".to_string(),
 344 |         ..Default::default()
 345 |     }),
 346 |     ..Default::default()
 347 | };
 348 | 
 349 | // With chunking
 350 | let config = ExtractionConfig {
 351 |     chunking: Some(ChunkingConfig {
 352 |         max_characters: 512,
 353 |         overlap: 50,
 354 |         ..Default::default()
 355 |     }),
 356 |     output_format: OutputFormat::Markdown,
 357 |     ..Default::default()
 358 | };
 359 | ```
 360 | 
 361 | ---
 362 | 
 363 | ## Output Formats
 364 | 
 365 | There are two separate enums both named `OutputFormat` in different modules:
 366 | 
 367 | ### Content `OutputFormat` (`core::config::formats::OutputFormat`)
 368 | 
 369 | Controls the format of the `content` field text. Used by `ExtractionConfig::output_format`.
 370 | 
 371 | ```rust
 372 | pub enum OutputFormat {
 373 |     /// Plain text (default)
 374 |     Plain,
 375 |     /// Markdown formatted
 376 |     Markdown,
 377 |     /// Djot markup format
 378 |     Djot,
 379 |     /// HTML format
 380 |     Html,
 381 | }
 382 | ```
 383 | 
 384 | ### Result `OutputFormat` (`types::extraction::OutputFormat`)
 385 | 
 386 | Controls the result structure. Used by `ExtractionConfig::result_format`.
 387 | 
 388 | ```rust
 389 | pub enum OutputFormat {
 390 |     /// Unified format with all content in `content` field (default)
 391 |     Unified,
 392 |     /// Element-based format with semantic element extraction
 393 |     ElementBased,
 394 | }
 395 | ```
 396 | 
 397 | ```rust
 398 | use kreuzberg::{ExtractionConfig, OutputFormat};
 399 | 
 400 | let config = ExtractionConfig {
 401 |     output_format: OutputFormat::Markdown,  // content format (Plain/Markdown/Djot/Html)
 402 |     // result_format uses types::OutputFormat (Unified/ElementBased) — defaults to Unified
 403 |     ..Default::default()
 404 | };
 405 | ```
 406 | 
 407 | ---
 408 | 
 409 | ## Extraction Result
 410 | 
 411 | ### `ExtractionResult`
 412 | 
 413 | Result returned by all extraction functions.
 414 | 
 415 | ```rust
 416 | pub struct ExtractionResult {
 417 |     /// Main extracted content
 418 |     pub content: String,
 419 | 
 420 |     /// Document MIME type
 421 |     pub mime_type: Cow<'static, str>,
 422 | 
 423 |     /// Metadata about extraction
 424 |     pub metadata: Metadata,
 425 | 
 426 |     /// Extracted tables (HTML/Markdown)
 427 |     pub tables: Vec<Table>,
 428 | 
 429 |     /// Detected languages (if language-detection enabled)
 430 |     pub detected_languages: Option<Vec<String>>,
 431 | 
 432 |     /// Text chunks (if chunking enabled)
 433 |     pub chunks: Option<Vec<Chunk>>,
 434 | 
 435 |     /// Extracted images (if image extraction enabled)
 436 |     pub images: Option<Vec<ExtractedImage>>,
 437 | 
 438 |     /// Per-page content (if page extraction enabled)
 439 |     pub pages: Option<Vec<PageContent>>,
 440 | 
 441 |     /// Semantic elements (if element-based format enabled)
 442 |     pub elements: Option<Vec<Element>>,
 443 | 
 444 |     /// Djot document structure (if extracting Djot)
 445 |     pub djot_content: Option<DjotContent>,
 446 | 
 447 |     /// Extracted keywords with relevance scores (if keyword extraction enabled)
 448 |     pub extracted_keywords: Option<Vec<ExtractedKeyword>>,
 449 | 
 450 |     /// Quality score for extraction result (0.0-1.0)
 451 |     pub quality_score: Option<f64>,
 452 | 
 453 |     /// Non-fatal warnings during processing pipeline
 454 |     pub processing_warnings: Vec<ProcessingWarning>,
 455 | }
 456 | ```
 457 | 
 458 | ### `ExtractedKeyword`
 459 | 
 460 | Extracted keyword with relevance score and position information.
 461 | 
 462 | ```rust
 463 | pub struct ExtractedKeyword {
 464 |     /// Keyword text
 465 |     pub text: String,
 466 | 
 467 |     /// Relevance score (0.0-1.0)
 468 |     pub score: f32,
 469 | 
 470 |     /// Algorithm used for extraction ("tfidf", "textrank", "yake", etc.)
 471 |     pub algorithm: String,
 472 | 
 473 |     /// Character positions in content (if available)
 474 |     pub positions: Option<Vec<usize>>,
 475 | }
 476 | ```
 477 | 
 478 | ### `ProcessingWarning`
 479 | 
 480 | Non-fatal warning encountered during document processing.
 481 | 
 482 | ```rust
 483 | pub struct ProcessingWarning {
 484 |     /// Component that generated the warning
 485 |     pub source: String,
 486 | 
 487 |     /// Warning message describing the issue
 488 |     pub message: String,
 489 | }
 490 | ```
 491 | 
 492 | ### `Chunk`
 493 | 
 494 | Text chunk with optional embedding.
 495 | 
 496 | ```rust
 497 | pub struct Chunk {
 498 |     /// Chunk text content
 499 |     pub content: String,
 500 | 
 501 |     /// Optional embedding vector
 502 |     pub embedding: Option<Vec<f32>>,
 503 | 
 504 |     /// Chunk metadata
 505 |     pub metadata: ChunkMetadata,
 506 | }
 507 | 
 508 | pub struct ChunkMetadata {
 509 |     pub byte_start: usize,
 510 |     pub byte_end: usize,
 511 |     pub token_count: Option<usize>,
 512 |     pub chunk_index: usize,
 513 |     pub total_chunks: usize,
 514 |     pub first_page: Option<usize>,
 515 |     pub last_page: Option<usize>,
 516 | }
 517 | ```
 518 | 
 519 | ### `ExtractedImage`
 520 | 
 521 | Image extracted from document.
 522 | 
 523 | ```rust
 524 | pub struct ExtractedImage {
 525 |     /// Raw image bytes
 526 |     pub data: Bytes,
 527 | 
 528 |     /// Format: "jpeg", "png", "webp", etc.
 529 |     pub format: Cow<'static, str>,
 530 | 
 531 |     /// Zero-indexed position
 532 |     pub image_index: usize,
 533 | 
 534 |     /// Page number (1-indexed)
 535 |     pub page_number: Option<usize>,
 536 | 
 537 |     /// Image dimensions
 538 |     pub width: Option<u32>,
 539 |     pub height: Option<u32>,
 540 | 
 541 |     /// Colorspace: "RGB", "CMYK", "Gray"
 542 |     pub colorspace: Option<String>,
 543 | 
 544 |     /// Bits per component
 545 |     pub bits_per_component: Option<u32>,
 546 | 
 547 |     /// Whether this is a mask image
 548 |     pub is_mask: bool,
 549 | 
 550 |     /// Image description
 551 |     pub description: Option<String>,
 552 | 
 553 |     /// Nested OCR result (if OCRed)
 554 |     pub ocr_result: Option<Box<ExtractionResult>>,
 555 | }
 556 | ```
 557 | 
 558 | ---
 559 | 
 560 | ## Error Handling
 561 | 
 562 | ### `KreuzbergError` enum
 563 | 
 564 | ```rust
 565 | pub enum KreuzbergError {
 566 |     /// File system errors (always bubble up)
 567 |     Io(std::io::Error),
 568 | 
 569 |     /// Document parsing errors
 570 |     Parsing {
 571 |         message: String,
 572 |         source: Option<Box<dyn std::error::Error + Send + Sync>>,
 573 |     },
 574 | 
 575 |     /// OCR processing errors
 576 |     Ocr {
 577 |         message: String,
 578 |         source: Option<Box<dyn std::error::Error + Send + Sync>>,
 579 |     },
 580 | 
 581 |     /// Configuration/input validation errors
 582 |     Validation {
 583 |         message: String,
 584 |         source: Option<Box<dyn std::error::Error + Send + Sync>>,
 585 |     },
 586 | 
 587 |     /// Cache operation errors
 588 |     Cache {
 589 |         message: String,
 590 |         source: Option<Box<dyn std::error::Error + Send + Sync>>,
 591 |     },
 592 | 
 593 |     /// Image processing errors
 594 |     ImageProcessing {
 595 |         message: String,
 596 |         source: Option<Box<dyn std::error::Error + Send + Sync>>,
 597 |     },
 598 | 
 599 |     /// Serialization errors (JSON, MessagePack)
 600 |     Serialization {
 601 |         message: String,
 602 |         source: Option<Box<dyn std::error::Error + Send + Sync>>,
 603 |     },
 604 | 
 605 |     /// Missing system dependency (e.g. Tesseract)
 606 |     MissingDependency(String),
 607 | 
 608 |     /// Plugin-specific errors
 609 |     Plugin {
 610 |         message: String,
 611 |         plugin_name: String,
 612 |     },
 613 | 
 614 |     /// Mutex/RwLock poisoning
 615 |     LockPoisoned(String),
 616 | 
 617 |     /// Unsupported MIME type or format
 618 |     UnsupportedFormat(String),
 619 | 
 620 |     /// Other errors
 621 |     Other(String),
 622 | }
 623 | ```
 624 | 
 625 | #### Error Constructors
 626 | 
 627 | ```rust
 628 | use kreuzberg::KreuzbergError;
 629 | 
 630 | // Create errors
 631 | let err = KreuzbergError::parsing("invalid PDF");
 632 | let err = KreuzbergError::ocr("Tesseract failed");
 633 | let err = KreuzbergError::validation("config invalid");
 634 | let err = KreuzbergError::unsupported_format("application/unknown");
 635 | let err = KreuzbergError::missing_dependency("tesseract");
 636 | 
 637 | // With source
 638 | let source = std::io::Error::new(std::io::ErrorKind::NotFound, "file missing");
 639 | let err = KreuzbergError::parsing_with_source("corrupt PDF", source);
 640 | ```
 641 | 
 642 | #### Handling Errors
 643 | 
 644 | ```rust
 645 | use kreuzberg::extract_file;
 646 | 
 647 | match extract_file("doc.pdf", None, &config).await {
 648 |     Ok(result) => println!("Success: {}", result.content),
 649 |     Err(kreuzberg::KreuzbergError::Io(e)) => {
 650 |         println!("File error: {}", e);
 651 |     }
 652 |     Err(kreuzberg::KreuzbergError::UnsupportedFormat(fmt)) => {
 653 |         println!("Unsupported: {}", fmt);
 654 |     }
 655 |     Err(e) => println!("Other error: {}", e),
 656 | }
 657 | ```
 658 | 
 659 | ---
 660 | 
 661 | ## MIME Type Detection
 662 | 
 663 | ### `detect_mime_type`
 664 | 
 665 | Detect MIME type from file path.
 666 | 
 667 | ```rust
 668 | pub fn detect_mime_type(path: impl AsRef<Path>) -> Result<String>
 669 | ```
 670 | 
 671 | ```rust
 672 | use kreuzberg::detect_mime_type;
 673 | 
 674 | let mime = detect_mime_type("document.pdf")?;
 675 | assert_eq!(mime, "application/pdf");
 676 | ```
 677 | 
 678 | ### `detect_mime_type_from_bytes`
 679 | 
 680 | Detect MIME type from byte data.
 681 | 
 682 | ```rust
 683 | pub fn detect_mime_type_from_bytes(data: &[u8]) -> Result<String>
 684 | ```
 685 | 
 686 | ### `validate_mime_type`
 687 | 
 688 | Check if a MIME type is supported.
 689 | 
 690 | ```rust
 691 | pub fn validate_mime_type(mime_type: &str) -> Result<()>
 692 | ```
 693 | 
 694 | ```rust
 695 | use kreuzberg::validate_mime_type;
 696 | 
 697 | validate_mime_type("application/pdf")?;  // OK
 698 | validate_mime_type("application/unknown")?;  // Error
 699 | ```
 700 | 
 701 | ### `get_extensions_for_mime`
 702 | 
 703 | Get file extensions for a MIME type.
 704 | 
 705 | ```rust
 706 | pub fn get_extensions_for_mime(mime_type: &str) -> Vec<String>
 707 | ```
 708 | 
 709 | ```rust
 710 | use kreuzberg::get_extensions_for_mime;
 711 | 
 712 | let exts = get_extensions_for_mime("application/pdf");
 713 | // ["pdf"]
 714 | 
 715 | let exts = get_extensions_for_mime("text/plain");
 716 | // ["txt", "text"]
 717 | ```
 718 | 
 719 | ### MIME Type Constants
 720 | 
 721 | ```rust
 722 | use kreuzberg::{
 723 |     PDF_MIME_TYPE,
 724 |     PLAIN_TEXT_MIME_TYPE,
 725 |     HTML_MIME_TYPE,
 726 |     MARKDOWN_MIME_TYPE,
 727 |     JSON_MIME_TYPE,
 728 |     XML_MIME_TYPE,
 729 |     DOCX_MIME_TYPE,
 730 |     POWER_POINT_MIME_TYPE,
 731 |     EXCEL_MIME_TYPE,
 732 | };
 733 | 
 734 | assert_eq!(PDF_MIME_TYPE, "application/pdf");
 735 | assert_eq!(PLAIN_TEXT_MIME_TYPE, "text/plain");
 736 | ```
 737 | 
 738 | ---
 739 | 
 740 | ## Plugin Registry
 741 | 
 742 | Access extractors, OCR backends, and validators.
 743 | 
 744 | ### `get_document_extractor_registry`
 745 | 
 746 | Get all available document extractors.
 747 | 
 748 | ```rust
 749 | pub fn get_document_extractor_registry() -> Arc<RwLock<DocumentExtractorRegistry>>
 750 | ```
 751 | 
 752 | ### `get_ocr_backend_registry`
 753 | 
 754 | Get all available OCR backends.
 755 | 
 756 | ```rust
 757 | pub fn get_ocr_backend_registry() -> Arc<RwLock<OcrBackendRegistry>>
 758 | ```
 759 | 
 760 | ### `get_post_processor_registry`
 761 | 
 762 | Get all available post-processors.
 763 | 
 764 | ```rust
 765 | pub fn get_post_processor_registry() -> Arc<RwLock<PostProcessorRegistry>>
 766 | ```
 767 | 
 768 | ### `get_validator_registry`
 769 | 
 770 | Get all available validators.
 771 | 
 772 | ```rust
 773 | pub fn get_validator_registry() -> Arc<RwLock<ValidatorRegistry>>
 774 | ```
 775 | 
 776 | ---
 777 | 
 778 | ## Complete Example
 779 | 
 780 | ```rust
 781 | use kreuzberg::{
 782 |     extract_file, ExtractionConfig, OutputFormat,
 783 |     ChunkingConfig, OcrConfig, LanguageDetectionConfig,
 784 | };
 785 | 
 786 | #[tokio::main]
 787 | async fn main() -> kreuzberg::Result<()> {
 788 |     // Configure extraction
 789 |     let config = ExtractionConfig {
 790 |         output_format: OutputFormat::Markdown,
 791 |         chunking: Some(ChunkingConfig {
 792 |             max_characters: 512,
 793 |             overlap: 50,
 794 |             ..Default::default()
 795 |         }),
 796 |         language_detection: Some(LanguageDetectionConfig::default()),
 797 |         ocr: Some(OcrConfig {
 798 |             backend: "tesseract".to_string(),
 799 |             ..Default::default()
 800 |         }),
 801 |         force_ocr: false,
 802 |         ..Default::default()
 803 |     };
 804 | 
 805 |     // Extract from file
 806 |     let result = extract_file("document.pdf", None, &config).await?;
 807 | 
 808 |     // Use results
 809 |     println!("Content:\n{}", result.content);
 810 |     println!("MIME: {}", result.mime_type);
 811 | 
 812 |     if let Some(langs) = result.detected_languages {
 813 |         println!("Languages: {:?}", langs);
 814 |     }
 815 | 
 816 |     if let Some(chunks) = result.chunks {
 817 |         println!("Chunks: {}", chunks.len());
 818 |         for chunk in chunks {
 819 |             println!("  - {}", &chunk.content[..50.min(chunk.content.len())]);
 820 |         }
 821 |     }
 822 | 
 823 |     if let Some(images) = result.images {
 824 |         println!("Images: {}", images.len());
 825 |     }
 826 | 
 827 |     if let Some(pages) = result.pages {
 828 |         println!("Pages: {}", pages.len());
 829 |     }
 830 | 
 831 |     Ok(())
 832 | }
 833 | ```
 834 | 
 835 | ---
 836 | 
 837 | ## Result Type Alias
 838 | 
 839 | ```rust
 840 | pub type Result<T> = std::result::Result<T, KreuzbergError>;
 841 | ```
 842 | 
 843 | All fallible operations return `Result<T>` where errors are `KreuzbergError`.
 844 | 
 845 | ---
 846 | 
 847 | ## Feature Flags Summary
 848 | 
 849 | | Feature | Availability | Dependencies |
 850 | |---------|--------------|--------------|
 851 | | tokio-runtime | Default | Tokio runtime for async/sync |
 852 | | pdf | Default | PDFium |
 853 | | ocr | Optional | Tesseract |
 854 | | chunking | Optional | text-splitter |
 855 | | embeddings | Optional | FastEmbed, requires tokio-runtime |
 856 | | language-detection | Optional | whatlang |
 857 | | keywords-yake | Optional | yake-rust |
 858 | | keywords-rake | Optional | rake |
 859 | | api | Optional | Axum, requires tokio-runtime |
 860 | | mcp | Optional | Model Context Protocol, requires tokio-runtime |
 861 | 
 862 | ---
 863 | 
 864 | ## Version
 865 | 
 866 | This reference is for Kreuzberg 4.x.
```

### File: `skills\kreuzberg\references\supported-formats.md`

- Size: 12057 bytes

```markdown
   1 | # Supported Formats Reference
   2 | 
   3 | Kreuzberg supports 91+ file formats across 8 major categories with intelligent format detection and comprehensive metadata extraction. All formats support text and metadata extraction. Additional capabilities like OCR and table detection are noted per format.
   4 | 
   5 | ## Office Documents
   6 | 
   7 | ### Word Processing
   8 | 
   9 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  10 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  11 | | Microsoft Word | `.docx` | `application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document` | Full text extraction, tables, embedded images, metadata, styles |
  12 | | Word Macro-Enabled | `.docm` | `application/vnd.ms-word.document.macroEnabled.12` | Macro-enabled document extraction, metadata |
  13 | | Word Template | `.dotx`, `.dotm`, `.dot` | Various Word template MIME types | Template document extraction, metadata |
  14 | | OpenDocument Text | `.odt` | `application/vnd.oasis.opendocument.text` | Full text extraction, tables, embedded images, metadata, styles |
  15 | 
  16 | ### Spreadsheets
  17 | 
  18 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  19 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  20 | | Excel Workbook | `.xlsx` | `application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet` | Sheet data, cell values, formulas, cell metadata, charts |
  21 | | Excel Macro-Enabled | `.xlsm` | `application/vnd.ms-excel.sheet.macroEnabled.12` | Sheet data, formulas, macros (text only), metadata |
  22 | | Excel Binary | `.xlsb` | `application/vnd.ms-excel.sheet.binary.macroEnabled.12` | Binary sheet data extraction, metadata |
  23 | | Excel Legacy | `.xls` | `application/vnd.ms-excel` | Legacy sheet data extraction, metadata |
  24 | | Excel Add-in | `.xla` | `application/vnd.ms-excel` | Add-in data extraction |
  25 | | Excel Macro Add-in | `.xlam` | `application/vnd.ms-excel.addin.macroEnabled.12` | Macro add-in metadata |
  26 | | Excel Template | `.xltm` | `application/vnd.ms-excel.template.macroEnabled.12` | Template data and metadata |
  27 | | Excel Template (XML) | `.xltx` | `application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.template` | XML template data and metadata |
  28 | | Excel Template (Legacy) | `.xlt` | `application/vnd.ms-excel` | Legacy template data extraction |
  29 | | OpenDocument Spreadsheet | `.ods` | `application/vnd.oasis.opendocument.spreadsheet` | Sheet data, cell values, formulas, metadata |
  30 | 
  31 | ### Presentations
  32 | 
  33 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  34 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  35 | | PowerPoint Presentation | `.pptx` | `application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.presentationml.presentation` | Slide text, speaker notes, embedded images, metadata |
  36 | | PowerPoint Legacy | `.ppt` | `application/vnd.ms-powerpoint` | Legacy slide text extraction, metadata |
  37 | | PowerPoint Slideshow | `.ppsx` | `application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.presentationml.slideshow` | Slideshow content, speaker notes, metadata |
  38 | | PowerPoint Template | `.potx`, `.potm`, `.pot` | Various PowerPoint template MIME types | Template slide extraction, metadata |
  39 | 
  40 | ### PDF
  41 | 
  42 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  43 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  44 | | Portable Document Format | `.pdf` | `application/pdf` | Text extraction, tables, embedded images, metadata, OCR (when needed), password protection support |
  45 | 
  46 | ### eBooks
  47 | 
  48 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  49 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  50 | | EPUB | `.epub` | `application/epub+zip` | Chapter text, metadata, embedded resources, navigation |
  51 | | FictionBook | `.fb2` | `application/x-fictionbook+xml` | Book content, metadata, chapter structure |
  52 | 
  53 | ### Database
  54 | 
  55 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  56 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  57 | | dBASE | `.dbf` | `application/x-dbf` | Table data extraction as markdown, field type support |
  58 | 
  59 | ### Hangul
  60 | 
  61 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  62 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  63 | | Hangul Word Processor | `.hwp`, `.hwpx` | `application/x-hwp`, `application/haansofthwpx` | Korean document format, text extraction |
  64 | 
  65 | ## Images (OCR-Enabled)
  66 | 
  67 | ### Raster Images
  68 | 
  69 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  70 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  71 | | PNG | `.png` | `image/png` | OCR text extraction, table detection, EXIF metadata, dimensions, color space |
  72 | | JPEG | `.jpg`, `.jpeg` | `image/jpeg` | OCR text extraction, table detection, EXIF metadata, color profile |
  73 | | GIF | `.gif` | `image/gif` | OCR text extraction, animation metadata, dimensions |
  74 | | WebP | `.webp` | `image/webp` | OCR text extraction, metadata, lossy/lossless detection |
  75 | | Bitmap | `.bmp` | `image/bmp` | OCR text extraction, dimensions, color depth |
  76 | | TIFF | `.tiff`, `.tif` | `image/tiff` | OCR text extraction, multi-page support, EXIF metadata, compression info |
  77 | 
  78 | ### Advanced Image Formats
  79 | 
  80 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  81 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  82 | | JPEG 2000 | `.jp2` | `image/jp2` | OCR via pure Rust decoder (hayro-jpeg2000), table detection, resolution metadata |
  83 | | JPEG 2000 Extended | `.jpx` | `image/jpx` | Advanced JPEG 2000 features, high-resolution content, metadata |
  84 | | JPEG 2000 Compound | `.jpm` | `image/jpm` | Compound image support, mixed content |
  85 | | Motion JPEG 2000 | `.mj2` | `video/mj2` | JPEG 2000 video/sequence metadata |
  86 | | JBIG2 | `.jbig2`, `.jb2` | `image/jbig2` | Bi-level image OCR, high compression, technical documents |
  87 | | Portable PixMap | `.pnm`, `.pbm`, `.pgm`, `.ppm` | `image/x-portable-pixmap` | OCR for plain image formats, raw pixel data |
  88 | 
  89 | ### Vector Graphics
  90 | 
  91 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
  92 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
  93 | | Scalable Vector Graphics | `.svg` | `image/svg+xml` | DOM parsing, embedded text extraction, graphics metadata, vector elements |
  94 | 
  95 | ## Web & Data
  96 | 
  97 | ### Markup & Structured Text
  98 | 
  99 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
 100 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
 101 | | HyperText Markup | `.html`, `.htm` | `text/html` | DOM parsing, text extraction, metadata (Open Graph, Twitter Card), link extraction |
 102 | | XHTML | `.xhtml` | `application/xhtml+xml` | XHTML parsing, metadata extraction, semantic structure |
 103 | | XML | `.xml` | `application/xml` | DOM parsing, namespace handling, text extraction, structure analysis |
 104 | 
 105 | ### Structured Data Formats
 106 | 
 107 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
 108 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
 109 | | JSON | `.json` | `application/json` | Schema detection, nested structure parsing, validation |
 110 | | YAML | `.yaml`, `.yml` | `application/x-yaml` | Hierarchical data parsing, custom tags, nested structures |
 111 | | TOML | `.toml` | `application/toml` | Configuration parsing, table structures, type preservation |
 112 | | CSV | `.csv` | `text/csv` | Delimiter detection, header inference, type detection |
 113 | | TSV | `.tsv` | `text/tab-separated-values` | Tab-separated value parsing, header detection |
 114 | 
 115 | ### Text & Markup Languages
 116 | 
 117 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
 118 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
 119 | | Plain Text | `.txt` | `text/plain` | Raw text extraction, encoding detection |
 120 | | Markdown | `.md`, `.markdown` | `text/markdown` | CommonMark parsing, GFM extensions, front matter |
 121 | | Djot | `.djot` | `text/djot` | Djot format parsing, semantic structure |
 122 | | reStructuredText | `.rst` | `text/x-rst` | RST parsing, directive handling, role extraction |
 123 | | Org Mode | `.org` | `text/org` | Org mode structure, outline parsing, metadata |
 124 | | Rich Text Format | `.rtf` | `application/rtf` | Text with formatting extraction, font information |
 125 | 
 126 | ## Email & Archives
 127 | 
 128 | ### Email Formats
 129 | 
 130 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
 131 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
 132 | | Email Message | `.eml` | `message/rfc822` | Headers (from, to, subject, date), body (HTML/plain text), attachments, threading info |
 133 | | Microsoft Outlook | `.msg` | `application/vnd.ms-outlook` | Outlook headers, body content, attachments, recipient metadata |
 134 | 
 135 | ### Archive Formats
 136 | 
 137 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
 138 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
 139 | | ZIP Archive | `.zip` | `application/zip` | File listing, nested archive support, compression metadata |
 140 | | Tar Archive | `.tar` | `application/x-tar` | File listing, permission metadata, nested archives |
 141 | | Gzip Tar | `.tgz` | `application/gzip` | Compressed archive listing, metadata |
 142 | | Gzip | `.gz` | `application/gzip` | Compressed file metadata |
 143 | | 7-Zip | `.7z` | `application/x-7z-compressed` | File listing, compression info, nested archives |
 144 | 
 145 | ## Academic & Scientific
 146 | 
 147 | ### Citation Formats
 148 | 
 149 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
 150 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
 151 | | BibTeX | `.bib` | `text/bibtex` | Structured parsing, entry types, field extraction |
 152 | | BibLaTeX | `.biblatex` | `text/bibtex` | Extended BibTeX format, advanced field support |
 153 | | RIS | `.ris` | `application/x-research-info-systems` | Structured RIS format parsing, type detection |
 154 | | NIH RIS | `.nbib` | `application/x-research-info-systems` | NIH/PubMed format, structured citation data |
 155 | | EndNote | `.enw` | `application/x-endnote` | EndNote XML format, citation metadata |
 156 | | Citation Style Language | `.csl` | `application/vnd.citationstyles.csl+xml` | CSL JSON/XML parsing, style definitions |
 157 | 
 158 | ### Scientific & Technical Formats
 159 | 
 160 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
 161 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
 162 | | LaTeX | `.tex`, `.latex` | `application/x-latex` | LaTeX source parsing, commands, document structure |
 163 | | Typst | `.typ` | `text/plain` | Typst markup parsing, document structure |
 164 | | JATS XML | `.jats` | `application/xml` | PubMed JATS parsing, article structure, metadata |
 165 | | Jupyter Notebook | `.ipynb` | `application/x-ipynb+json` | Cell extraction (code + markdown), output parsing, metadata |
 166 | | DocBook | `.docbook` | `application/docbook+xml` | DocBook XML parsing, semantic structure |
 167 | 
 168 | ### Documentation Formats
 169 | 
 170 | | Format | Extensions | MIME Type | Capabilities |
 171 | |--------|-----------|-----------|--------------|
 172 | | OPML | `.opml` | `application/x-opml+xml` | Outline parsing, hierarchy extraction, metadata |
 173 | | Perl POD | `.pod` | `text/x-pod` | Perl documentation parsing, section extraction |
 174 | | Manual Page | `.mdoc` | `text/plain` | UNIX manual page parsing, section structure |
 175 | | Troff/Groff | `.troff` | `text/troff` | Typesetting markup parsing, document structure |
 176 | 
 177 | ## Format Capabilities Summary
 178 | 
 179 | ### Text Extraction
 180 | 
 181 | All 85+ formats support full or partial text extraction. Document structure and encoding are automatically detected.
 182 | 
 183 | ### Metadata Support
 184 | 
 185 | Comprehensive metadata extraction includes:
 186 | 
 187 | - Document properties (title, author, subject, creation date, modification date)
 188 | - Format-specific metadata (page count, dimensions, encoding, language)
 189 | - EXIF data (for images)
 190 | - Document statistics (word count, character count)
 191 | 
 192 | ### OCR (Optical Character Recognition)
 193 | 
 194 | OCR is available for image formats:
 195 | 
 196 | - **Raster Images**: PNG, JPEG, GIF, WebP, BMP, TIFF
 197 | - **Advanced Formats**: JPEG 2000, JBIG2, PNM/PBM/PGM/PPM
 198 | - **Configurable Backends**: Tesseract (all languages), EasyOCR, PaddleOCR (Python), Guten (Node.js)
 199 | 
 200 | ### Table Detection
 201 | 
 202 | Smart table detection and reconstruction available for:
 203 | 
 204 | - PDF documents (native tables and scanned content with OCR)
 205 | - Office documents (Excel, Word)
 206 | - Images (via OCR backends)
 207 | - HTML/XML (from markup structure)
 208 | 
 209 | ### Archive & Nested Document Support
 210 | 
 211 | Archives and nested formats support file listing and sequential extraction:
 212 | 
 213 | - ZIP, TAR, TGZ, 7Z archives
 214 | - Email attachments
 215 | - Nested archives within archives
 216 | 
 217 | ## Getting Started
 218 | 
 219 | For language-specific examples and detailed API documentation, see the [API Reference](https://docs.kreuzberg.dev/reference/api-python/).
 220 | 
 221 | For OCR configuration and backend selection, see the [OCR Backends Guide](https://docs.kreuzberg.dev/guides/ocr/).
 222 | 
 223 | For comprehensive format details and format detection, see the [Complete Format Reference](https://docs.kreuzberg.dev/reference/formats/).
```
